BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP kathito vaṃśavistāro bhavatā somasūryayoḥ
BhP rājñāṃ cobhayavaṃśyānāṃ caritaṃ paramādbhutam
BhP yadoś ca dharmaśīlasya nitarāṃ munisattama
BhP tatrāṃśenāvatīrṇasya viṣṇor vīryāṇi śaṃsa naḥ
BhP avatīrya yador vaṃśe bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ
BhP kṛtavān yāni viśvātmā tāni no vada vistarāt
BhP nivṛttatarṣair upagīyamānād bhavauṣadhāc chrotramano'bhirāmāt
BhP ka uttamaślokaguṇānuvādāt pumān virajyeta vinā paśughnāt
BhP pitāmahā me samare 'marañjayair devavratādyātirathais timiṅgilaiḥ
BhP duratyayaṃ kauravasainyasāgaraṃ kṛtvātaran vatsapadaṃ sma yatplavāḥ
BhP drauṇyastravipluṣṭam idaṃ madaṅgaṃ santānabījaṃ kurupāṇḍavānām
BhP jugopa kukṣiṃ gata āttacakro mātuś ca me yaḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāyāḥ
BhP vīryāṇi tasyākhiladehabhājām antar bahiḥ pūruṣakālarūpaiḥ
BhP prayacchato mṛtyum utāmṛtaṃ ca māyāmanuṣyasya vadasva vidvan
BhP rohiṇyās tanayaḥ prokto rāmaḥ saṅkarṣaṇas tvayā
BhP devakyā garbhasambandhaḥ kuto dehāntaraṃ vinā
BhP kasmān mukundo bhagavān pitur gehād vrajaṃ gataḥ
BhP kva vāsaṃ jñātibhiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛtavān sātvatāṃ patiḥ
BhP vraje vasan kim akaron madhupuryāṃ ca keśavaḥ
BhP bhrātaraṃ cāvadhīt kaṃsaṃ mātur addhātadarhaṇam
BhP dehaṃ mānuṣam āśritya kati varṣāṇi vṛṣṇibhiḥ
BhP yadupuryāṃ sahāvātsīt patnyaḥ katy abhavan prabhoḥ
BhP etad anyac ca sarvaṃ me mune kṛṣṇaviceṣṭitam
BhP vaktum arhasi sarvajña śraddadhānāya vistṛtam
BhP naiṣātiduḥsahā kṣun māṃ tyaktodam api bādhate
BhP pibantaṃ tvanmukhāmbhoja cyutaṃ harikathāmṛtam
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP evaṃ niśamya bhṛgunandana sādhuvādaṃ
BhP vaiyāsakiḥ sa bhagavān atha viṣṇurātam
BhP pratyarcya kṛṣṇacaritaṃ kalikalmaṣaghnaṃ
BhP vyāhartum ārabhata bhāgavatapradhānaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP samyag vyavasitā buddhis tava rājarṣisattama
BhP vāsudevakathāyāṃ te yaj jātā naiṣṭhikī ratiḥ
BhP vāsudevakathāpraśnaḥ puruṣāṃs trīn punāti hi
BhP vaktāraṃ pracchakaṃ śrotṝṃs tatpādasalilaṃ yathā
BhP bhūmir dṛptanṛpavyāja daityānīkaśatāyutaiḥ
BhP ākrāntā bhūribhāreṇa brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau
BhP gaur bhūtvāśrumukhī khinnā krandantī karuṇaṃ vibhoḥ
BhP upasthitāntike tasmai vyasanaṃ samavocata
BhP brahmā tadupadhāryātha saha devais tayā saha
BhP jagāma satrinayanas tīraṃ kṣīrapayonidheḥ
BhP tatra gatvā jagannāthaṃ devadevaṃ vṛṣākapim
BhP puruṣaṃ puruṣasūktena upatasthe samāhitaḥ
BhP giraṃ samādhau gagane samīritāṃ niśamya vedhās tridaśān uvāca ha
BhP gāṃ pauruṣīṃ me śṛṇutāmarāḥ punar vidhīyatām āśu tathaiva mā ciram
BhP puraiva puṃsāvadhṛto dharājvaro bhavadbhir aṃśair yaduṣūpajanyatām
BhP sa yāvad urvyā bharam īśvareśvaraḥ svakālaśaktyā kṣapayaṃś cared bhuvi
BhP vasudevagṛhe sākṣād bhagavān puruṣaḥ paraḥ
BhP janiṣyate tatpriyārthaṃ sambhavantu surastriyaḥ
BhP vāsudevakalānantaḥ sahasravadanaḥ svarāṭ
BhP agrato bhavitā devo hareḥ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP viṣṇor māyā bhagavatī yayā sammohitaṃ jagat
BhP ādiṣṭā prabhuṇāṃśena kāryārthe sambhaviṣyati
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity ādiśyāmaragaṇān prajāpatipatir vibhuḥ
BhP āśvāsya ca mahīṃ gīrbhiḥ svadhāma paramaṃ yayau
BhP śūraseno yadupatir mathurām āvasan purīm
BhP māthurāñ chūrasenāṃś ca viṣayān bubhuje purā
BhP rājadhānī tataḥ sābhūt sarvayādavabhūbhujām
BhP mathurā bhagavān yatra nityaṃ sannihito hariḥ
BhP tasyāṃ tu karhicic chaurir vasudevaḥ kṛtodvahaḥ
BhP devakyā sūryayā sārdhaṃ prayāṇe ratham āruhat
BhP ugrasenasutaḥ kaṃsaḥ svasuḥ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP raśmīn hayānāṃ jagrāha raukmai rathaśatair vṛtaḥ
BhP catuḥśataṃ pāribarhaṃ gajānāṃ hemamālinām
BhP aśvānām ayutaṃ sārdhaṃ rathānāṃ ca triṣaṭśatam
BhP dāsīnāṃ sukumārīṇāṃ dve śate samalaṅkṛte
BhP duhitre devakaḥ prādād yāne duhitṛvatsalaḥ
BhP śaṅkhatūryamṛdaṅgāś ca nedur dundubhayaḥ samam
BhP prayāṇaprakrame tāta varavadhvoḥ sumaṅgalam
BhP pathi pragrahiṇaṃ kaṃsam ābhāṣyāhāśarīravāk
BhP asyās tvām aṣṭamo garbho hantā yāṃ vahase 'budha
BhP ity uktaḥ sa khalaḥ pāpo bhojānāṃ kulapāṃsanaḥ
BhP bhaginīṃ hantum ārabdhaṃ khaḍgapāṇiḥ kace 'grahīt
BhP taṃ jugupsitakarmāṇaṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ nirapatrapam
BhP vasudevo mahābhāga uvāca parisāntvayan
BhP śrīvasudeva uvāca
BhP ślāghanīyaguṇaḥ śūrair bhavān bhojayaśaskaraḥ
BhP sa kathaṃ bhaginīṃ hanyāt striyam udvāhaparvaṇi
BhP mṛtyur janmavatāṃ vīra dehena saha jāyate
BhP adya vābdaśatānte vā mṛtyur vai prāṇināṃ dhruvaḥ
BhP dehe pañcatvam āpanne dehī karmānugo 'vaśaḥ
BhP dehāntaram anuprāpya prāktanaṃ tyajate vapuḥ
BhP vrajaṃs tiṣṭhan padaikena yathaivaikena gacchati
BhP yathā tṛṇajalaukaivaṃ dehī karmagatiṃ gataḥ
BhP svapne yathā paśyati deham īdṛśaṃ manorathenābhiniviṣṭacetanaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭaśrutābhyāṃ manasānucintayan prapadyate tat kim api hy apasmṛtiḥ
BhP yato yato dhāvati daivacoditaṃ mano vikārātmakam āpa pañcasu
BhP guṇeṣu māyārociteṣu dehy asau prapadyamānaḥ saha tena jāyate
BhP jyotir yathaivodakapārthiveṣv adaḥ
BhP samīravegānugataṃ vibhāvyate
BhP evaṃ svamāyāraciteṣv asau pumān
BhP guṇeṣu rāgānugato vimuhyati
BhP tasmān na kasyacid droham ācaret sa tathāvidhaḥ
BhP ātmanaḥ kṣemam anvicchan drogdhur vai parato bhayam
BhP eṣā tavānujā bālā kṛpaṇā putrikopamā
BhP hantuṃ nārhasi kalyāṇīm imāṃ tvaṃ dīnavatsalaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ sa sāmabhir bhedair bodhyamāno 'pi dāruṇaḥ
BhP na nyavartata kauravya puruṣādān anuvrataḥ
BhP nirbandhaṃ tasya taṃ jñātvā vicintyānakadundubhiḥ
BhP prāptaṃ kālaṃ prativyoḍhum idaṃ tatrānvapadyata
BhP mṛtyur buddhimatāpohyo yāvad buddhibalodayam
BhP yady asau na nivarteta nāparādho 'sti dehinaḥ
BhP pradāya mṛtyave putrān mocaye kṛpaṇām imām
BhP sutā me yadi jāyeran mṛtyur vā na mriyeta cet
BhP viparyayo vā kiṃ na syād gatir dhātur duratyayā
BhP upasthito nivarteta nivṛttaḥ punar āpatet
BhP agner yathā dāruviyogayogayor adṛṣṭato 'nyan na nimittam asti
BhP evaṃ hi jantor api durvibhāvyaḥ śarīrasaṃyogaviyogahetuḥ
BhP evaṃ vimṛśya taṃ pāpaṃ yāvadātmanidarśanam
BhP pūjayām āsa vai śaurir bahumānapuraḥsaram
BhP prasannavadanāmbhojo nṛśaṃsaṃ nirapatrapam
BhP manasā dūyamānena vihasann idam abravīt
BhP śrīvasudeva uvāca
BhP na hy asyās te bhayaṃ saumya yad vai sāhāśarīravāk
BhP putrān samarpayiṣye 'syā yatas te bhayam utthitam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP svasur vadhān nivavṛte kaṃsas tadvākyasāravit
BhP vasudevo 'pi taṃ prītaḥ praśasya prāviśad gṛham
BhP atha kāla upāvṛtte devakī sarvadevatā
BhP putrān prasuṣuve cāṣṭau kanyāṃ caivānuvatsaram
BhP kīrtimantaṃ prathamajaṃ kaṃsāyānakadundubhiḥ
BhP arpayām āsa kṛcchreṇa so 'nṛtād ativihvalaḥ
BhP kiṃ duḥsahaṃ nu sādhūnāṃ viduṣāṃ kim apekṣitam
BhP kim akāryaṃ kadaryāṇāṃ dustyajaṃ kiṃ dhṛtātmanām
BhP dṛṣṭvā samatvaṃ tac chaureḥ satye caiva vyavasthitim
BhP kaṃsas tuṣṭamanā rājan prahasann idam abravīt
BhP pratiyātu kumāro 'yaṃ na hy asmād asti me bhayam
BhP aṣṭamād yuvayor garbhān mṛtyur me vihitaḥ kila
BhP tatheti sutam ādāya yayāv ānakadundubhiḥ
BhP nābhyanandata tadvākyam asato 'vijitātmanaḥ
BhP nandādyā ye vraje gopā yāś cāmīṣāṃ ca yoṣitaḥ
BhP vṛṣṇayo vasudevādyā devakyādyā yadustriyaḥ
BhP sarve vai devatāprāyā ubhayor api bhārata
BhP jñātayo bandhusuhṛdo ye ca kaṃsam anuvratāḥ
BhP etat kaṃsāya bhagavāñ chaśaṃsābhyetya nāradaḥ
BhP bhūmer bhārāyamāṇānāṃ daityānāṃ ca vadhodyamam
BhP ṛṣer vinirgame kaṃso yadūn matvā surān iti
BhP devakyā garbhasambhūtaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca svavadhaṃ prati
BhP devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca nigṛhya nigaḍair gṛhe
BhP jātaṃ jātam ahan putraṃ tayor ajanaśaṅkayā
BhP mātaraṃ pitaraṃ bhrātṝn sarvāṃś ca suhṛdas tathā
BhP ghnanti hy asutṛpo lubdhā rājānaḥ prāyaśo bhuvi
BhP ātmānam iha sañjātaṃ jānan prāg viṣṇunā hatam
BhP mahāsuraṃ kālanemiṃ yadubhiḥ sa vyarudhyata
BhP ugrasenaṃ ca pitaraṃ yadubhojāndhakādhipam
BhP svayaṃ nigṛhya bubhuje śūrasenān mahābalaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP pralambabakacāṇūra tṛṇāvartamahāśanaiḥ
BhP muṣṭikāriṣṭadvivida pūtanākeśīdhenukaiḥ
BhP anyaiś cāsurabhūpālair bāṇabhaumādibhir yutaḥ
BhP yadūnāṃ kadanaṃ cakre balī māgadhasaṃśrayaḥ
BhP te pīḍitā niviviśuḥ kurupañcālakekayān
BhP śālvān vidarbhān niṣadhān videhān kośalān api
BhP eke tam anurundhānā jñātayaḥ paryupāsate
BhP hateṣu ṣaṭsu bāleṣu devakyā augraseninā
BhP saptamo vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma yam anantaṃ pracakṣate
BhP garbho babhūva devakyā harṣaśokavivardhanaḥ
BhP bhagavān api viśvātmā viditvā kaṃsajaṃ bhayam
BhP yadūnāṃ nijanāthānāṃ yogamāyāṃ samādiśat
BhP gaccha devi vrajaṃ bhadre gopagobhir alaṅkṛtam
BhP rohiṇī vasudevasya bhāryāste nandagokule
BhP anyāś ca kaṃsasaṃvignā vivareṣu vasanti hi
BhP devakyā jaṭhare garbhaṃ śeṣākhyaṃ dhāma māmakam
BhP tat sannikṛṣya rohiṇyā udare sanniveśaya
BhP athāham aṃśabhāgena devakyāḥ putratāṃ śubhe
BhP prāpsyāmi tvaṃ yaśodāyāṃ nandapatnyāṃ bhaviṣyasi
BhP arciṣyanti manuṣyās tvāṃ sarvakāmavareśvarīm
BhP dhūpopahārabalibhiḥ sarvakāmavarapradām
BhP nāmadheyāni kurvanti sthānāni ca narā bhuvi
BhP durgeti bhadrakālīti vijayā vaiṣṇavīti ca
BhP kumudā caṇḍikā kṛṣṇā mādhavī kanyaketi ca
BhP māyā nārāyaṇīśānī śāradety ambiketi ca
BhP garbhasaṅkarṣaṇāt taṃ vai prāhuḥ saṅkarṣaṇaṃ bhuvi
BhP rāmeti lokaramaṇād balabhadraṃ balocchrayāt
BhP sandiṣṭaivaṃ bhagavatā tathety om iti tadvacaḥ
BhP pratigṛhya parikramya gāṃ gatā tat tathākarot
BhP garbhe praṇīte devakyā rohiṇīṃ yoganidrayā
BhP aho visraṃsito garbha iti paurā vicukruśuḥ
BhP bhagavān api viśvātmā bhaktānām abhayaṅkaraḥ
BhP āviveśāṃśabhāgena mana ānakadundubheḥ
BhP sa bibhrat pauruṣaṃ dhāma bhrājamāno yathā raviḥ
BhP durāsado 'tidurdharṣo bhūtānāṃ sambabhūva ha
BhP tato jaganmaṅgalam acyutāṃśaṃ samāhitaṃ śūrasutena devī
BhP dadhāra sarvātmakam ātmabhūtaṃ kāṣṭhā yathānandakaraṃ manastaḥ
BhP sā devakī sarvajagannivāsa nivāsabhūtā nitarāṃ na reje
BhP bhojendragehe 'gniśikheva ruddhā sarasvatī jñānakhale yathā satī
BhP tāṃ vīkṣya kaṃsaḥ prabhayājitāntarāṃ
BhP virocayantīṃ bhavanaṃ śucismitām
BhP āhaiṣa me prāṇaharo harir guhāṃ
BhP dhruvaṃ śrito yan na pureyam īdṛśī
BhP kim adya tasmin karaṇīyam āśu me yad arthatantro na vihanti vikramam
BhP striyāḥ svasur gurumatyā vadho 'yaṃ yaśaḥ śriyaṃ hanty anukālam āyuḥ
BhP sa eṣa jīvan khalu sampareto varteta yo 'tyantanṛśaṃsitena
BhP dehe mṛte taṃ manujāḥ śapanti gantā tamo 'ndhaṃ tanumānino dhruvam
BhP iti ghoratamād bhāvāt sannivṛttaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ
BhP āste pratīkṣaṃs tajjanma harer vairānubandhakṛt
BhP āsīnaḥ saṃviśaṃs tiṣṭhan bhuñjānaḥ paryaṭan mahīm
BhP cintayāno hṛṣīkeśam apaśyat tanmayaṃ jagat
BhP brahmā bhavaś ca tatraitya munibhir nāradādibhiḥ
BhP devaiḥ sānucaraiḥ sākaṃ gīrbhir vṛṣaṇam aiḍayan
BhP satyavrataṃ satyaparaṃ trisatyaṃ
BhP satyasya yoniṃ nihitaṃ ca satye
BhP satyasya satyam ṛtasatyanetraṃ
BhP satyātmakaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannāḥ
BhP ekāyano 'sau dviphalas trimūlaś catūrasaḥ pañcavidhaḥ ṣaḍātmā
BhP saptatvag aṣṭaviṭapo navākṣo daśacchadī dvikhago hy ādivṛkṣaḥ
BhP tvam eka evāsya sataḥ prasūtis tvaṃ sannidhānaṃ tvam anugrahaś ca
BhP tvanmāyayā saṃvṛtacetasas tvāṃ paśyanti nānā na vipaścito ye
BhP bibharṣi rūpāṇy avabodha ātmā kṣemāya lokasya carācarasya
BhP sattvopapannāni sukhāvahāni satām abhadrāṇi muhuḥ khalānām
BhP tvayy ambujākṣākhilasattvadhāmni samādhināveśitacetasaike
BhP tvatpādapotena mahatkṛtena kurvanti govatsapadaṃ bhavābdhim
BhP svayaṃ samuttīrya sudustaraṃ dyuman
BhP bhavārṇavaṃ bhīmam adabhrasauhṛdāḥ
BhP bhavatpadāmbhoruhanāvam atra te
BhP nidhāya yātāḥ sadanugraho bhavān
BhP ye 'nye 'ravindākṣa vimuktamāninas
BhP tvayy astabhāvād aviśuddhabuddhayaḥ
BhP āruhya kṛcchreṇa paraṃ padaṃ tataḥ
BhP patanty adho 'nādṛtayuṣmadaṅghrayaḥ
BhP tathā na te mādhava tāvakāḥ kvacid bhraśyanti mārgāt tvayi baddhasauhṛdāḥ
BhP tvayābhiguptā vicaranti nirbhayā vināyakānīkapamūrdhasu prabho
BhP sattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ śrayate bhavān sthitau
BhP śarīriṇāṃ śreyaupāyanaṃ vapuḥ
BhP vedakriyāyogatapaḥsamādhibhis
BhP tavārhaṇaṃ yena janaḥ samīhate
BhP sattvaṃ na ced dhātar idaṃ nijaṃ bhaved
BhP vijñānam ajñānabhidāpamārjanam
BhP guṇaprakāśair anumīyate bhavān
BhP prakāśate yasya ca yena vā guṇaḥ
BhP na nāmarūpe guṇajanmakarmabhir nirūpitavye tava tasya sākṣiṇaḥ
BhP manovacobhyām anumeyavartmano deva kriyāyāṃ pratiyanty athāpi hi
BhP śṛṇvan gṛṇan saṃsmarayaṃś ca cintayan
BhP nāmāni rūpāṇi ca maṅgalāni te
BhP kriyāsu yas tvaccaraṇāravindayor
BhP āviṣṭacetā na bhavāya kalpate
BhP diṣṭyā hare 'syā bhavataḥ pado bhuvo
BhP bhāro 'panītas tava janmaneśituḥ
BhP diṣṭyāṅkitāṃ tvatpadakaiḥ suśobhanair
BhP drakṣyāma gāṃ dyāṃ ca tavānukampitām
BhP na te 'bhavasyeśa bhavasya kāraṇaṃ vinā vinodaṃ bata tarkayāmahe
BhP bhavo nirodhaḥ sthitir apy avidyayā kṛtā yatas tvayy abhayāśrayātmani
BhP matsyāśvakacchapanṛsiṃhavarāhahaṃsa
BhP rājanyavipravibudheṣu kṛtāvatāraḥ
BhP tvaṃ pāsi nas tribhuvanaṃ ca yathādhuneśa
BhP bhāraṃ bhuvo hara yadūttama vandanaṃ te
BhP diṣṭyāmba te kukṣigataḥ paraḥ pumān
BhP aṃśena sākṣād bhagavān bhavāya naḥ
BhP mābhūd bhayaṃ bhojapater mumūrṣor
BhP goptā yadūnāṃ bhavitā tavātmajaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity abhiṣṭūya puruṣaṃ yadrūpam anidaṃ yathā
BhP brahmeśānau purodhāya devāḥ pratiyayur divam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP atha sarvaguṇopetaḥ kālaḥ paramaśobhanaḥ
BhP yarhy evājanajanmarkṣaṃ śāntarkṣagrahatārakam
BhP diśaḥ prasedur gaganaṃ nirmaloḍugaṇodayam
BhP mahī maṅgalabhūyiṣṭha puragrāmavrajākarā
BhP nadyaḥ prasannasalilā hradā jalaruhaśriyaḥ
BhP dvijālikulasannāda stavakā vanarājayaḥ
BhP vavau vāyuḥ sukhasparśaḥ puṇyagandhavahaḥ śuciḥ
BhP agnayaś ca dvijātīnāṃ śāntās tatra samindhata
BhP manāṃsy āsan prasannāni sādhūnām asuradruhām
BhP jāyamāne 'jane tasmin nedur dundubhayaḥ samam
BhP jaguḥ kinnaragandharvās tuṣṭuvuḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
BhP vidyādharyaś ca nanṛtur apsarobhiḥ samaṃ mudā
BhP mumucur munayo devāḥ sumanāṃsi mudānvitāḥ
BhP mandaṃ mandaṃ jaladharā jagarjur anusāgaram
BhP niśīthe tamaudbhūte jāyamāne janārdane
BhP devakyāṃ devarūpiṇyāṃ viṣṇuḥ sarvaguhāśayaḥ
BhP āvirāsīd yathā prācyāṃ diśīndur iva puṣkalaḥ
BhP tam adbhutaṃ bālakam ambujekṣaṇaṃ caturbhujaṃ śaṅkhagadādyudāyudham
BhP śrīvatsalakṣmaṃ galaśobhikaustubhaṃ pītāmbaraṃ sāndrapayodasaubhagam
BhP mahārhavaidūryakirīṭakuṇḍala tviṣā pariṣvaktasahasrakuntalam
BhP uddāmakāñcyaṅgadakaṅkaṇādibhir virocamānaṃ vasudeva aikṣata
BhP sa vismayotphullavilocano hariṃ sutaṃ vilokyānakadundubhis tadā
BhP kṛṣṇāvatārotsavasambhramo 'spṛśan mudā dvijebhyo 'yutam āpluto gavām
BhP athainam astaud avadhārya pūruṣaṃ paraṃ natāṅgaḥ kṛtadhīḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
BhP svarociṣā bhārata sūtikāgṛhaṃ virocayantaṃ gatabhīḥ prabhāvavit
BhP śrīvasudeva uvāca
BhP vidito 'si bhavān sākṣāt puruṣaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ
BhP kevalānubhavānanda svarūpaḥ sarvabuddhidṛk
BhP sa eva svaprakṛtyedaṃ sṛṣṭvāgre triguṇātmakam
BhP tad anu tvaṃ hy apraviṣṭaḥ praviṣṭa iva bhāvyase
BhP yatheme 'vikṛtā bhāvās tathā te vikṛtaiḥ saha
BhP nānāvīryāḥ pṛthagbhūtā virājaṃ janayanti hi
BhP sannipatya samutpādya dṛśyante 'nugatā iva
BhP prāg eva vidyamānatvān na teṣām iha sambhavaḥ
BhP evaṃ bhavān buddhyanumeyalakṣaṇair grāhyair guṇaiḥ sann api tadguṇāgrahaḥ
BhP anāvṛtatvād bahir antaraṃ na te sarvasya sarvātmana ātmavastunaḥ
BhP ya ātmano dṛśyaguṇeṣu sann iti vyavasyate svavyatirekato 'budhaḥ
BhP vinānuvādaṃ na ca tan manīṣitaṃ samyag yatas tyaktam upādadat pumān
BhP tvatto 'sya janmasthitisaṃyamān vibho
BhP vadanty anīhād aguṇād avikriyāt
BhP tvayīśvare brahmaṇi no virudhyate
BhP tvadāśrayatvād upacaryate guṇaiḥ
BhP sa tvaṃ trilokasthitaye svamāyayā
BhP bibharṣi śuklaṃ khalu varṇam ātmanaḥ
BhP sargāya raktaṃ rajasopabṛṃhitaṃ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ ca varṇaṃ tamasā janātyaye
BhP tvam asya lokasya vibho rirakṣiṣur gṛhe 'vatīrṇo 'si mamākhileśvara
BhP rājanyasaṃjñāsurakoṭiyūthapair nirvyūhyamānā nihaniṣyase camūḥ
BhP ayaṃ tv asabhyas tava janma nau gṛhe
BhP śrutvāgrajāṃs te nyavadhīt sureśvara
BhP sa te 'vatāraṃ puruṣaiḥ samarpitaṃ
BhP śrutvādhunaivābhisaraty udāyudhaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP athainam ātmajaṃ vīkṣya mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇam
BhP devakī tam upādhāvat kaṃsād bhītā suvismitā
BhP śrīdevaky uvāca
BhP rūpaṃ yat tat prāhur avyaktam ādyaṃ
BhP brahma jyotir nirguṇaṃ nirvikāram
BhP sattāmātraṃ nirviśeṣaṃ nirīhaṃ
BhP sa tvaṃ sākṣād viṣṇur adhyātmadīpaḥ
BhP naṣṭe loke dviparārdhāvasāne mahābhūteṣv ādibhūtaṃ gateṣu
BhP vyakte 'vyaktaṃ kālavegena yāte bhavān ekaḥ śiṣyate 'śeṣasaṃjñaḥ
BhP yo 'yaṃ kālas tasya te 'vyaktabandho
BhP ceṣṭām āhuś ceṣṭate yena viśvam
BhP nimeṣādir vatsarānto mahīyāṃs
BhP taṃ tveśānaṃ kṣemadhāma prapadye
BhP martyo mṛtyuvyālabhītaḥ palāyan lokān sarvān nirbhayaṃ nādhyagacchat
BhP tvat pādābjaṃ prāpya yadṛcchayādya susthaḥ śete mṛtyur asmād apaiti
BhP sa tvaṃ ghorād ugrasenātmajān nas trāhi trastān bhṛtyavitrāsahāsi
BhP rūpaṃ cedaṃ pauruṣaṃ dhyānadhiṣṇyaṃ mā pratyakṣaṃ māṃsadṛśāṃ kṛṣīṣṭhāḥ
BhP janma te mayy asau pāpo mā vidyān madhusūdana
BhP samudvije bhavaddhetoḥ kaṃsād aham adhīradhīḥ
BhP upasaṃhara viśvātmann ado rūpam alaukikam
BhP śaṅkhacakragadāpadma śriyā juṣṭaṃ caturbhujam
BhP viśvaṃ yad etat svatanau niśānte yathāvakāśaṃ puruṣaḥ paro bhavān
BhP bibharti so 'yaṃ mama garbhago 'bhūd aho nṛlokasya viḍambanaṃ hi tat
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP tvam eva pūrvasarge 'bhūḥ pṛśniḥ svāyambhuve sati
BhP tadāyaṃ sutapā nāma prajāpatir akalmaṣaḥ
BhP yuvāṃ vai brahmaṇādiṣṭau prajāsarge yadā tataḥ
BhP sanniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ tepāthe paramaṃ tapaḥ
BhP varṣavātātapahima gharmakālaguṇān anu
BhP sahamānau śvāsarodha vinirdhūtamanomalau
BhP śīrṇaparṇānilāhārāv upaśāntena cetasā
BhP mattaḥ kāmān abhīpsantau madārādhanam īhatuḥ
BhP evaṃ vāṃ tapyatos tīvraṃ tapaḥ paramaduṣkaram
BhP divyavarṣasahasrāṇi dvādaśeyur madātmanoḥ
BhP tadā vāṃ parituṣṭo 'ham amunā vapuṣānaghe
BhP tapasā śraddhayā nityaṃ bhaktyā ca hṛdi bhāvitaḥ
BhP prādurāsaṃ varadarāḍ yuvayoḥ kāmaditsayā
BhP vriyatāṃ vara ity ukte mādṛśo vāṃ vṛtaḥ sutaḥ
BhP ajuṣṭagrāmyaviṣayāv anapatyau ca dampatī
BhP na vavrāthe 'pavargaṃ me mohitau devamāyayā
BhP gate mayi yuvāṃ labdhvā varaṃ matsadṛśaṃ sutam
BhP grāmyān bhogān abhuñjāthāṃ yuvāṃ prāptamanorathau
BhP adṛṣṭvānyatamaṃ loke śīlaudāryaguṇaiḥ samam
BhP ahaṃ suto vām abhavaṃ pṛśnigarbha iti śrutaḥ
BhP tayor vāṃ punar evāham adityām āsa kaśyapāt
BhP upendra iti vikhyāto vāmanatvāc ca vāmanaḥ
BhP tṛtīye 'smin bhave 'haṃ vai tenaiva vapuṣātha vām
BhP jāto bhūyas tayor eva satyaṃ me vyāhṛtaṃ sati
BhP etad vāṃ darśitaṃ rūpaṃ prāgjanmasmaraṇāya me
BhP nānyathā madbhavaṃ jñānaṃ martyaliṅgena jāyate
BhP yuvāṃ māṃ putrabhāvena brahmabhāvena cāsakṛt
BhP cintayantau kṛtasnehau yāsyethe madgatiṃ parām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity uktvāsīd dharis tūṣṇīṃ bhagavān ātmamāyayā
BhP pitroḥ sampaśyatoḥ sadyo babhūva prākṛtaḥ śiśuḥ
BhP tataś ca śaurir bhagavatpracoditaḥ
BhP sutaṃ samādāya sa sūtikāgṛhāt
BhP yadā bahir gantum iyeṣa tarhy ajā
BhP yā yogamāyājani nandajāyayā
BhP tayā hṛtapratyayasarvavṛttiṣu dvāḥstheṣu paureṣv api śāyiteṣv atha
BhP dvāraś ca sarvāḥ pihitā duratyayā bṛhatkapāṭāyasakīlaśṛṅkhalaiḥ
BhP tāḥ kṛṣṇavāhe vasudeva āgate svayaṃ vyavaryanta yathā tamo raveḥ
BhP vavarṣa parjanya upāṃśugarjitaḥ śeṣo 'nvagād vāri nivārayan phaṇaiḥ
BhP maghoni varṣaty asakṛd yamānujā gambhīratoyaughajavormiphenilā
BhP bhayānakāvartaśatākulā nadī mārgaṃ dadau sindhur iva śriyaḥ pateḥ
BhP nandavrajaṃ śaurir upetya tatra tān
BhP gopān prasuptān upalabhya nidrayā
BhP sutaṃ yaśodāśayane nidhāya tat
BhP sutām upādāya punar gṛhān agāt
BhP devakyāḥ śayane nyasya vasudevo 'tha dārikām
BhP pratimucya pador loham āste pūrvavad āvṛtaḥ
BhP yaśodā nandapatnī ca jātaṃ param abudhyata
BhP na talliṅgaṃ pariśrāntā nidrayāpagatasmṛtiḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP bahirantaḥpuradvāraḥ sarvāḥ pūrvavad āvṛtāḥ
BhP tato bāladhvaniṃ śrutvā gṛhapālāḥ samutthitāḥ
BhP te tu tūrṇam upavrajya devakyā garbhajanma tat
BhP ācakhyur bhojarājāya yad udvignaḥ pratīkṣate
BhP sa talpāt tūrṇam utthāya kālo 'yam iti vihvalaḥ
BhP sūtīgṛham agāt tūrṇaṃ praskhalan muktamūrdhajaḥ
BhP tam āha bhrātaraṃ devī kṛpaṇā karuṇaṃ satī
BhP snuṣeyaṃ tava kalyāṇa striyaṃ mā hantum arhasi
BhP bahavo hiṃsitā bhrātaḥ śiśavaḥ pāvakopamāḥ
BhP tvayā daivanisṛṣṭena putrikaikā pradīyatām
BhP nanv ahaṃ te hy avarajā dīnā hatasutā prabho
BhP dātum arhasi mandāyā aṅgemāṃ caramāṃ prajām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP upaguhyātmajām evaṃ rudatyā dīnadīnavat
BhP yācitas tāṃ vinirbhartsya hastād ācicchide khalaḥ
BhP tāṃ gṛhītvā caraṇayor jātamātrāṃ svasuḥ sutām
BhP apothayac chilāpṛṣṭhe svārthonmūlitasauhṛdaḥ
BhP sā taddhastāt samutpatya sadyo devy ambaraṃ gatā
BhP adṛśyatānujā viṣṇoḥ sāyudhāṣṭamahābhujā
BhP divyasragambarālepa ratnābharaṇabhūṣitā
BhP dhanuḥśūleṣucarmāsi śaṅkhacakragadādharā
BhP siddhacāraṇagandharvair apsaraḥkinnaroragaiḥ
BhP upāhṛtorubalibhiḥ stūyamānedam abravīt
BhP kiṃ mayā hatayā manda jātaḥ khalu tavāntakṛt

BhP iti prabhāṣya taṃ devī māyā bhagavatī bhuvi
BhP bahunāmaniketeṣu bahunāmā babhūva ha
BhP tayābhihitam ākarṇya kaṃsaḥ paramavismitaḥ
BhP devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca vimucya praśrito 'bravīt
BhP aho bhaginy aho bhāma mayā vāṃ bata pāpmanā
BhP puruṣāda ivāpatyaṃ bahavo hiṃsitāḥ sutāḥ
BhP sa tv ahaṃ tyaktakāruṇyas tyaktajñātisuhṛt khalaḥ
BhP kān lokān vai gamiṣyāmi brahmaheva mṛtaḥ śvasan
BhP daivam apy anṛtaṃ vakti na martyā eva kevalam
BhP yadviśrambhād ahaṃ pāpaḥ svasur nihatavāñ chiśūn
BhP mā śocataṃ mahābhāgāv ātmajān svakṛtaṃ bhujaḥ
BhP jāntavo na sadaikatra daivādhīnās tadāsate
BhP bhuvi bhaumāni bhūtāni yathā yānty apayānti ca
BhP nāyam ātmā tathaiteṣu viparyeti yathaiva bhūḥ
BhP yathānevaṃvido bhedo yata ātmaviparyayaḥ
BhP dehayogaviyogau ca saṃsṛtir na nivartate
BhP tasmād bhadre svatanayān mayā vyāpāditān api
BhP mānuśoca yataḥ sarvaḥ svakṛtaṃ vindate 'vaśaḥ
BhP yāvad dhato 'smi hantāsmī ty ātmānaṃ manyate 'svadṛk
BhP tāvat tadabhimāny ajño bādhyabādhakatām iyāt
BhP kṣamadhvaṃ mama daurātmyaṃ sādhavo dīnavatsalāḥ
BhP ity uktvāśrumukhaḥ pādau śyālaḥ svasror athāgrahīt
BhP mocayām āsa nigaḍād viśrabdhaḥ kanyakāgirā
BhP devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca darśayann ātmasauhṛdam
BhP bhrātuḥ samanutaptasya kṣāntaroṣā ca devakī
BhP vyasṛjad vasudevaś ca prahasya tam uvāca ha
BhP evam etan mahābhāga yathā vadasi dehinām
BhP ajñānaprabhavāhaṃdhīḥ svapareti bhidā yataḥ
BhP śokaharṣabhayadveṣa lobhamohamadānvitāḥ
BhP mitho ghnantaṃ na paśyanti bhāvair bhāvaṃ pṛthagdṛśaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP kaṃsa evaṃ prasannābhyāṃ viśuddhaṃ pratibhāṣitaḥ
BhP devakīvasudevābhyām anujñāto 'viśad gṛham
BhP tasyāṃ rātryāṃ vyatītāyāṃ kaṃsa āhūya mantriṇaḥ
BhP tebhya ācaṣṭa tat sarvaṃ yad uktaṃ yoganidrayā
BhP ākarṇya bhartur gaditaṃ tam ūcur devaśatravaḥ
BhP devān prati kṛtāmarṣā daiteyā nātikovidāḥ
BhP evaṃ cet tarhi bhojendra puragrāmavrajādiṣu
BhP anirdaśān nirdaśāṃś ca haniṣyāmo 'dya vai śiśūn
BhP kim udyamaiḥ kariṣyanti devāḥ samarabhīravaḥ
BhP nityam udvignamanaso jyāghoṣair dhanuṣas tava
BhP asyatas te śaravrātair hanyamānāḥ samantataḥ
BhP jijīviṣava utsṛjya palāyanaparā yayuḥ
BhP kecit prāñjalayo dīnā nyastaśastrā divaukasaḥ
BhP muktakacchaśikhāḥ kecid bhītāḥ sma iti vādinaḥ
BhP na tvaṃ vismṛtaśastrāstrān virathān bhayasaṃvṛtān
BhP haṃsy anyāsaktavimukhān bhagnacāpān ayudhyataḥ
BhP kiṃ kṣemaśūrair vibudhair asaṃyugavikatthanaiḥ
BhP rahojuṣā kiṃ hariṇā śambhunā vā vanaukasā

BhP tathāpi devāḥ sāpatnyān nopekṣyā iti manmahe

BhP yathendriyagrāma upekṣitas tathā ripur mahān baddhabalo na cālyate
BhP mūlaṃ hi viṣṇur devānāṃ yatra dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
BhP tasya ca brahmagoviprās tapo yajñāḥ sadakṣiṇāḥ
BhP tasmāt sarvātmanā rājan brāhmaṇān brahmavādinaḥ
BhP tapasvino yajñaśīlān gāś ca hanmo havirdughāḥ
BhP viprā gāvaś ca vedāś ca tapaḥ satyaṃ damaḥ śamaḥ
BhP śraddhā dayā titikṣā ca kratavaś ca hares tanūḥ
BhP sa hi sarvasurādhyakṣo hy asuradviḍ guhāśayaḥ
BhP tanmūlā devatāḥ sarvāḥ seśvarāḥ sacaturmukhāḥ
BhP ayaṃ vai tadvadhopāyo yad ṛṣīṇāṃ vihiṃsanam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ durmantribhiḥ kaṃsaḥ saha sammantrya durmatiḥ
BhP brahmahiṃsāṃ hitaṃ mene kālapāśāvṛto 'suraḥ
BhP sandiśya sādhulokasya kadane kadanapriyān
BhP kāmarūpadharān dikṣu dānavān gṛham āviśat
BhP te vai rajaḥprakṛtayas tamasā mūḍhacetasaḥ
BhP satāṃ vidveṣam ācerur ārād āgatamṛtyavaḥ
BhP āyuḥ śriyaṃ yaśo dharmaṃ lokān āśiṣa eva ca
BhP hanti śreyāṃsi sarvāṇi puṃso mahadatikramaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP nandas tv ātmaja utpanne jātāhlādo mahāmanāḥ
BhP āhūya viprān vedajñān snātaḥ śucir alaṅkṛtaḥ
BhP vācayitvā svastyayanaṃ jātakarmātmajasya vai
BhP kārayām āsa vidhivat pitṛdevārcanaṃ tathā
BhP dhenūnāṃ niyute prādād viprebhyaḥ samalaṅkṛte
BhP tilādrīn sapta ratnaugha śātakaumbhāmbarāvṛtān
BhP kālena snānaśaucābhyāṃ saṃskārais tapasejyayā
BhP śudhyanti dānaiḥ santuṣṭyā dravyāṇy ātmātmavidyayā
BhP saumaṅgalyagiro viprāḥ sūtamāgadhavandinaḥ
BhP gāyakāś ca jagur nedur bheryo dundubhayo muhuḥ
BhP vrajaḥ sammṛṣṭasaṃsikta dvārājiragṛhāntaraḥ
BhP citradhvajapatākāsrak cailapallavatoraṇaiḥ
BhP gāvo vṛṣā vatsatarā haridrātailarūṣitāḥ
BhP vicitradhātubarhasrag vastrakāñcanamālinaḥ
BhP mahārhavastrābharaṇa kañcukoṣṇīṣabhūṣitāḥ
BhP gopāḥ samāyayū rājan nānopāyanapāṇayaḥ
BhP gopyaś cākarṇya muditā yaśodāyāḥ sutodbhavam
BhP ātmānaṃ bhūṣayāṃ cakrur vastrākalpāñjanādibhiḥ
BhP navakuṅkumakiñjalka mukhapaṅkajabhūtayaḥ
BhP balibhis tvaritaṃ jagmuḥ pṛthuśroṇyaś calatkucāḥ
BhP gopyaḥ sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalaniṣkakaṇṭhyaś
BhP citrāmbarāḥ pathi śikhācyutamālyavarṣāḥ
BhP nandālayaṃ savalayā vrajatīr virejur
BhP vyālolakuṇḍalapayodharahāraśobhāḥ
BhP tā āśiṣaḥ prayuñjānāś ciraṃ pāhīti bālake
BhP haridrācūrṇatailādbhiḥ siñcantyo 'janam ujjaguḥ
BhP avādyanta vicitrāṇi vāditrāṇi mahotsave
BhP kṛṣṇe viśveśvare 'nante nandasya vrajam āgate
BhP gopāḥ parasparaṃ hṛṣṭā dadhikṣīraghṛtāmbubhiḥ
BhP āsiñcanto vilimpanto navanītaiś ca cikṣipuḥ
BhP nando mahāmanās tebhyo vāso 'laṅkāragodhanam
BhP sūtamāgadhavandibhyo ye 'nye vidyopajīvinaḥ
BhP tais taiḥ kāmair adīnātmā yathocitam apūjayat
BhP viṣṇor ārādhanārthāya svaputrasyodayāya ca
BhP rohiṇī ca mahābhāgā nandagopābhinanditā
BhP vyacarad divyavāsasrak kaṇṭhābharaṇabhūṣitā
BhP tata ārabhya nandasya vrajaḥ sarvasamṛddhimān
BhP harer nivāsātmaguṇai ramākrīḍam abhūn nṛpa
BhP gopān gokularakṣāyāṃ nirūpya mathurāṃ gataḥ
BhP nandaḥ kaṃsasya vārṣikyaṃ karaṃ dātuṃ kurūdvaha
BhP vasudeva upaśrutya bhrātaraṃ nandam āgatam
BhP jñātvā dattakaraṃ rājñe yayau tadavamocanam
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya dehaḥ prāṇam ivāgatam
BhP prītaḥ priyatamaṃ dorbhyāṃ sasvaje premavihvalaḥ
BhP pūjitaḥ sukham āsīnaḥ pṛṣṭvānāmayam ādṛtaḥ
BhP prasaktadhīḥ svātmajayor idam āha viśāmpate
BhP diṣṭyā bhrātaḥ pravayasa idānīm aprajasya te
BhP prajāśāyā nivṛttasya prajā yat samapadyata
BhP diṣṭyā saṃsāracakre 'smin vartamānaḥ punarbhavaḥ
BhP upalabdho bhavān adya durlabhaṃ priyadarśanam
BhP naikatra priyasaṃvāsaḥ suhṛdāṃ citrakarmaṇām
BhP oghena vyūhyamānānāṃ plavānāṃ srotaso yathā

BhP bṛhad vanaṃ tad adhunā yatrāsse tvaṃ suhṛdvṛtaḥ
BhP bhrātar mama sutaḥ kaccin mātrā saha bhavadvraje
BhP tātaṃ bhavantaṃ manvāno bhavadbhyām upalālitaḥ
BhP puṃsas trivargo vihitaḥ suhṛdo hy anubhāvitaḥ
BhP na teṣu kliśyamāneṣu trivargo 'rthāya kalpate
BhP śrīnanda uvāca
BhP aho te devakīputrāḥ kaṃsena bahavo hatāḥ

BhP adṛṣṭam ātmanas tattvaṃ yo veda na sa muhyati
BhP śrīvasudeva uvāca

BhP neha stheyaṃ bahutithaṃ santy utpātāś ca gokule
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti nandādayo gopāḥ proktās te śauriṇā yayuḥ
BhP anobhir anaḍudyuktais tam anujñāpya gokulam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP nandaḥ pathi vacaḥ śaurer na mṛṣeti vicintayan
BhP hariṃ jagāma śaraṇam utpātāgamaśaṅkitaḥ
BhP kaṃsena prahitā ghorā pūtanā bālaghātinī
BhP śiśūṃś cacāra nighnantī puragrāmavrajādiṣu
BhP na yatra śravaṇādīni rakṣoghnāni svakarmasu
BhP kurvanti sātvatāṃ bhartur yātudhānyaś ca tatra hi
BhP sā khecary ekadotpatya pūtanā nandagokulam
BhP yoṣitvā māyayātmānaṃ prāviśat kāmacāriṇī
BhP tāṃ keśabandhavyatiṣaktamallikāṃ

BhP tasmin stanaṃ durjaravīryam ulbaṇaṃ

BhP prāṇaiḥ samaṃ roṣasamanvito 'pibat

BhP rasā diśaś ca pratinedire janāḥ petuḥ kṣitau vajranipātaśaṅkayā
BhP niśācarītthaṃ vyathitastanā vyasur
BhP vyādāya keśāṃś caraṇau bhujāv api
BhP prasārya goṣṭhe nijarūpam āsthitā
BhP vajrāhato vṛtra ivāpatan nṛpa
BhP patamāno 'pi taddehas trigavyūtyantaradrumān

BhP andhakūpagabhīrākṣaṃ pulinārohabhīṣaṇam

BhP bālaṃ ca tasyā urasi krīḍantam akutobhayam

BhP yaśodārohiṇībhyāṃ tāḥ samaṃ bālasya sarvataḥ

BhP gopyaḥ saṃspṛṣṭasalilā aṅgeṣu karayoḥ pṛthak

BhP hṛt keśavas tvadura īśa inas tu kaṇṭhaṃ

BhP pṛśnigarbhas tu te buddhim ātmānaṃ bhagavān paraḥ
BhP krīḍantaṃ pātu govindaḥ śayānaṃ pātu mādhavaḥ
BhP vrajantam avyād vaikuṇṭha āsīnaṃ tvāṃ śriyaḥ patiḥ
BhP bhuñjānaṃ yajñabhuk pātu sarvagrahabhayaṅkaraḥ

BhP śrīśuka uvāca
