BhP śriyā kīrtyānubhāvena gopāyasva samāhitaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity ātmānaṃ samādiśya garge ca svagṛhaṃ gate
BhP nandaḥ pramudito mene ātmānaṃ pūrṇam āśiṣām
BhP kālena vrajatālpena gokule rāmakeśavau
BhP jānubhyāṃ saha pāṇibhyāṃ riṅgamāṇau vijahratuḥ
BhP tāv aṅghriyugmam anukṛṣya sarīsṛpantau
BhP ghoṣapraghoṣaruciraṃ vrajakardameṣu
BhP tannādahṛṣṭamanasāv anusṛtya lokaṃ
BhP mugdhaprabhītavad upeyatur anti mātroḥ
BhP tanmātarau nijasutau ghṛṇayā snuvantyau
BhP paṅkāṅgarāgarucirāv upagṛhya dorbhyām
BhP dattvā stanaṃ prapibatoḥ sma mukhaṃ nirīkṣya
BhP mugdhasmitālpadaśanaṃ yayatuḥ pramodam
BhP yarhy aṅganādarśanīyakumāralīlāv
BhP antarvraje tad abalāḥ pragṛhītapucchaiḥ
BhP vatsair itas tata ubhāv anukṛṣyamāṇau
BhP prekṣantya ujjhitagṛhā jahṛṣur hasantyaḥ
BhP śṛṅgyagnidaṃṣṭryasijaladvijakaṇṭakebhyaḥ
BhP krīḍāparāv aticalau svasutau niṣeddhum
BhP gṛhyāṇi kartum api yatra na tajjananyau
BhP śekāta āpatur alaṃ manaso 'navasthām
BhP kālenālpena rājarṣe rāmaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca gokule
BhP aghṛṣṭajānubhiḥ padbhir vicakramatur añjasā
BhP tatas tu bhagavān kṛṣṇo vayasyair vrajabālakaiḥ
BhP saharāmo vrajastrīṇāṃ cikrīḍe janayan mudam
BhP kṛṣṇasya gopyo ruciraṃ vīkṣya kaumāracāpalam
BhP śṛṇvantyāḥ kila tanmātur iti hocuḥ samāgatāḥ
BhP vatsān muñcan kvacid asamaye krośasañjātahāsaḥ
BhP steyaṃ svādv atty atha dadhipayaḥ kalpitaiḥ steyayogaiḥ
BhP markān bhokṣyan vibhajati sa cen nātti bhāṇḍaṃ bhinnatti
BhP dravyālābhe sagṛhakupito yāty upakrośya tokān
BhP hastāgrāhye racayati vidhiṃ pīṭhakolūkhalādyaiś
BhP chidraṃ hy antarnihitavayunaḥ śikyabhāṇḍeṣu tadvit
BhP dhvāntāgāre dhṛtamaṇigaṇaṃ svāṅgam arthapradīpaṃ
BhP kāle gopyo yarhi gṛhakṛtyeṣu suvyagracittāḥ
BhP evaṃ dhārṣṭyāny uśati kurute mehanādīni vāstau
BhP steyopāyair viracitakṛtiḥ supratīko yathāste
BhP itthaṃ strībhiḥ sabhayanayanaśrīmukhālokinībhir
BhP vyākhyātārthā prahasitamukhī na hy upālabdhum aicchat
BhP ekadā krīḍamānās te rāmādyā gopadārakāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇo mṛdaṃ bhakṣitavān iti mātre nyavedayan
BhP sā gṛhītvā kare kṛṣṇam upālabhya hitaiṣiṇī
BhP yaśodā bhayasambhrānta prekṣaṇākṣam abhāṣata
BhP kasmān mṛdam adāntātman bhavān bhakṣitavān rahaḥ
BhP vadanti tāvakā hy ete kumārās te 'grajo 'py ayam
BhP nāhaṃ bhakṣitavān amba sarve mithyābhiśaṃsinaḥ
BhP yadi satyagiras tarhi samakṣaṃ paśya me mukham
BhP yady evaṃ tarhi vyādehī ty uktaḥ sa bhagavān hariḥ
BhP vyādattāvyāhataiśvaryaḥ krīḍāmanujabālakaḥ
BhP sā tatra dadṛśe viśvaṃ jagat sthāsnu ca khaṃ diśaḥ
BhP sādridvīpābdhibhūgolaṃ savāyvagnīndutārakam
BhP jyotiścakraṃ jalaṃ tejo nabhasvān viyad eva ca
BhP vaikārikāṇīndriyāṇi mano mātrā guṇās trayaḥ
BhP etad vicitraṃ sahajīvakāla svabhāvakarmāśayaliṅgabhedam
BhP sūnos tanau vīkṣya vidāritāsye vrajaṃ sahātmānam avāpa śaṅkām
BhP kiṃ svapna etad uta devamāyā kiṃ vā madīyo bata buddhimohaḥ
BhP atho amuṣyaiva mamārbhakasya yaḥ kaścanautpattika ātmayogaḥ
BhP atho yathāvan na vitarkagocaraṃ cetomanaḥkarmavacobhir añjasā
BhP yadāśrayaṃ yena yataḥ pratīyate sudurvibhāvyaṃ praṇatāsmi tatpadam
BhP ahaṃ mamāsau patir eṣa me suto vrajeśvarasyākhilavittapā satī
BhP gopyaś ca gopāḥ sahagodhanāś ca me yanmāyayetthaṃ kumatiḥ sa me gatiḥ
BhP itthaṃ viditatattvāyāṃ gopikāyāṃ sa īśvaraḥ
BhP vaiṣṇavīṃ vyatanon māyāṃ putrasnehamayīṃ vibhuḥ
BhP sadyo naṣṭasmṛtir gopī sāropyāroham ātmajam
BhP pravṛddhasnehakalila hṛdayāsīd yathā purā
BhP trayyā copaniṣadbhiś ca sāṅkhyayogaiś ca sātvataiḥ
BhP upagīyamānamāhātmyaṃ hariṃ sāmanyatātmajam
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP nandaḥ kim akarod brahman śreya evaṃ mahodayam
BhP yaśodā ca mahābhāgā papau yasyāḥ stanaṃ hariḥ
BhP pitarau nānvavindetāṃ kṛṣṇodārārbhakehitam
BhP gāyanty adyāpi kavayo yal lokaśamalāpaham
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP droṇo vasūnāṃ pravaro dharayā bhāryayā saha
BhP kariṣyamāṇa ādeśān brahmaṇas tam uvāca ha
BhP jātayor nau mahādeve bhuvi viśveśvare harau
BhP bhaktiḥ syāt paramā loke yayāñjo durgatiṃ taret
BhP astv ity uktaḥ sa bhagavān vraje droṇo mahāyaśāḥ
BhP jajñe nanda iti khyāto yaśodā sā dharābhavat
BhP tato bhaktir bhagavati putrībhūte janārdane
BhP dampatyor nitarām āsīd gopagopīṣu bhārata
BhP kṛṣṇo brahmaṇa ādeśaṃ satyaṃ kartuṃ vraje vibhuḥ
BhP saharāmo vasaṃś cakre teṣāṃ prītiṃ svalīlayā
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ekadā gṛhadāsīṣu yaśodā nandagehinī
BhP karmāntaraniyuktāsu nirmamantha svayaṃ dadhi
BhP yāni yānīha gītāni tadbālacaritāni ca
BhP dadhinirmanthane kāle smarantī tāny agāyata
BhP kṣaumaṃ vāsaḥ pṛthukaṭitaṭe bibhratī sūtranaddhaṃ
BhP putrasnehasnutakucayugaṃ jātakampaṃ ca subhrūḥ
BhP rajjvākarṣaśramabhujacalatkaṅkaṇau kuṇḍale ca
BhP svinnaṃ vaktraṃ kabaravigalanmālatī nirmamantha
BhP tāṃ stanyakāma āsādya mathnantīṃ jananīṃ hariḥ
BhP gṛhītvā dadhimanthānaṃ nyaṣedhat prītim āvahan
BhP tam aṅkam ārūḍham apāyayat stanaṃ snehasnutaṃ sasmitam īkṣatī mukham
BhP atṛptam utsṛjya javena sā yayāv utsicyamāne payasi tv adhiśrite
BhP sañjātakopaḥ sphuritāruṇādharaṃ sandaśya dadbhir dadhimanthabhājanam
BhP bhittvā mṛṣāśrur dṛṣadaśmanā raho jaghāsa haiyaṅgavam antaraṃ gataḥ
BhP uttārya gopī suśṛtaṃ payaḥ punaḥ praviśya saṃdṛśya ca dadhyamatrakam
BhP bhagnaṃ vilokya svasutasya karma taj jahāsa taṃ cāpi na tatra paśyatī
BhP ulūkhalāṅghrer upari vyavasthitaṃ markāya kāmaṃ dadataṃ śici sthitam
BhP haiyaṅgavaṃ cauryaviśaṅkitekṣaṇaṃ nirīkṣya paścāt sutam āgamac chanaiḥ
BhP tām āttayaṣṭiṃ prasamīkṣya satvaras
BhP tato 'varuhyāpasasāra bhītavat
BhP gopy anvadhāvan na yam āpa yogināṃ
BhP kṣamaṃ praveṣṭuṃ tapaseritaṃ manaḥ
BhP anvañcamānā jananī bṛhaccalac chroṇībharākrāntagatiḥ sumadhyamā
BhP javena visraṃsitakeśabandhana cyutaprasūnānugatiḥ parāmṛśat
BhP kṛtāgasaṃ taṃ prarudantam akṣiṇī kaṣantam añjanmaṣiṇī svapāṇinā
BhP udvīkṣamāṇaṃ bhayavihvalekṣaṇaṃ haste gṛhītvā bhiṣayanty avāgurat
BhP tyaktvā yaṣṭiṃ sutaṃ bhītaṃ vijñāyārbhakavatsalā
BhP iyeṣa kila taṃ baddhuṃ dāmnātadvīryakovidā
BhP na cāntar na bahir yasya na pūrvaṃ nāpi cāparam
BhP pūrvāparaṃ bahiś cāntar jagato yo jagac ca yaḥ
BhP taṃ matvātmajam avyaktaṃ martyaliṅgam adhokṣajam
BhP gopikolūkhale dāmnā babandha prākṛtaṃ yathā
BhP tad dāma badhyamānasya svārbhakasya kṛtāgasaḥ
BhP dvyaṅgulonam abhūt tena sandadhe 'nyac ca gopikā
BhP yadāsīt tad api nyūnaṃ tenānyad api sandadhe
BhP tad api dvyaṅgulaṃ nyūnaṃ yad yad ādatta bandhanam
BhP evaṃ svagehadāmāni yaśodā sandadhaty api
BhP gopīnāṃ susmayantīnāṃ smayantī vismitābhavat
BhP svamātuḥ svinnagātrāyā visrastakabarasrajaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā pariśramaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛpayāsīt svabandhane
BhP evaṃ sandarśitā hy aṅga hariṇā bhṛtyavaśyatā
BhP svavaśenāpi kṛṣṇena yasyedaṃ seśvaraṃ vaśe
BhP nemaṃ viriñco na bhavo na śrīr apy aṅgasaṃśrayā
BhP prasādaṃ lebhire gopī yat tat prāpa vimuktidāt
BhP nāyaṃ sukhāpo bhagavān dehināṃ gopikāsutaḥ
BhP jñānināṃ cātmabhūtānāṃ yathā bhaktimatām iha
BhP kṛṣṇas tu gṛhakṛtyeṣu vyagrāyāṃ mātari prabhuḥ
BhP adrākṣīd arjunau pūrvaṃ guhyakau dhanadātmajau
BhP purā nāradaśāpena vṛkṣatāṃ prāpitau madāt
BhP nalakūvaramaṇigrīvāv iti khyātau śriyānvitau
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP kathyatāṃ bhagavann etat tayoḥ śāpasya kāraṇam
BhP yat tad vigarhitaṃ karma yena vā devarṣes tamaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP rudrasyānucarau bhūtvā sudṛptau dhanadātmajau
BhP kailāsopavane ramye mandākinyāṃ madotkaṭau
BhP vāruṇīṃ madirāṃ pītvā madāghūrṇitalocanau
BhP strījanair anugāyadbhiś ceratuḥ puṣpite vane
BhP antaḥ praviśya gaṅgāyām ambhojavanarājini
BhP cikrīḍatur yuvatibhir gajāv iva kareṇubhiḥ
BhP yadṛcchayā ca devarṣir bhagavāṃs tatra kaurava
BhP apaśyan nārado devau kṣībāṇau samabudhyata
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvā vrīḍitā devyo vivastrāḥ śāpaśaṅkitāḥ
BhP vāsāṃsi paryadhuḥ śīghraṃ vivastrau naiva guhyakau
BhP tau dṛṣṭvā madirāmattau śrīmadāndhau surātmajau
BhP tayor anugrahārthāya śāpaṃ dāsyann idaṃ jagau
BhP śrīnārada uvāca
BhP na hy anyo juṣato joṣyān buddhibhraṃśo rajoguṇaḥ
BhP śrīmadād ābhijātyādir yatra strī dyūtam āsavaḥ
BhP hanyante paśavo yatra nirdayair ajitātmabhiḥ
BhP manyamānair imaṃ deham ajarāmṛtyu naśvaram
BhP devasaṃjñitam apy ante kṛmiviḍbhasmasaṃjñitam
BhP bhūtadhruk tatkṛte svārthaṃ kiṃ veda nirayo yataḥ
BhP dehaḥ kim annadātuḥ svaṃ niṣektur mātur eva ca
BhP mātuḥ pitur vā balinaḥ kretur agneḥ śuno 'pi vā
BhP evaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ deham avyaktaprabhavāpyayam
BhP ko vidvān ātmasāt kṛtvā hanti jantūn ṛte 'sataḥ
BhP asataḥ śrīmadāndhasya dāridryaṃ param añjanam
BhP ātmaupamyena bhūtāni daridraḥ param īkṣate
BhP yathā kaṇṭakaviddhāṅgo jantor necchati tāṃ vyathām
BhP jīvasāmyaṃ gato liṅgair na tathāviddhakaṇṭakaḥ
BhP daridro nirahaṃstambho muktaḥ sarvamadair iha
BhP kṛcchraṃ yadṛcchayāpnoti tad dhi tasya paraṃ tapaḥ
BhP nityaṃ kṣutkṣāmadehasya daridrasyānnakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
BhP indriyāṇy anuśuṣyanti hiṃsāpi vinivartate
BhP daridrasyaiva yujyante sādhavaḥ samadarśinaḥ
BhP sadbhiḥ kṣiṇoti taṃ tarṣaṃ tata ārād viśuddhyati
BhP sādhūnāṃ samacittānāṃ mukundacaraṇaiṣiṇām
BhP upekṣyaiḥ kiṃ dhanastambhair asadbhir asadāśrayaiḥ
BhP tad ahaṃ mattayor mādhvyā vāruṇyā śrīmadāndhayoḥ
BhP tamomadaṃ hariṣyāmi straiṇayor ajitātmanoḥ
BhP yad imau lokapālasya putrau bhūtvā tamaḥplutau
BhP na vivāsasam ātmānaṃ vijānītaḥ sudurmadau
BhP ato 'rhataḥ sthāvaratāṃ syātāṃ naivaṃ yathā punaḥ
BhP smṛtiḥ syān matprasādena tatrāpi madanugrahāt
BhP vāsudevasya sānnidhyaṃ labdhvā divyaśaracchate
BhP vṛtte svarlokatāṃ bhūyo labdhabhaktī bhaviṣyataḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evam uktvā sa devarṣir gato nārāyaṇāśramam
BhP nalakūvaramaṇigrīvāv āsatur yamalārjunau
BhP ṛṣer bhāgavatamukhyasya satyaṃ kartuṃ vaco hariḥ
BhP jagāma śanakais tatra yatrāstāṃ yamalārjunau
BhP devarṣir me priyatamo yad imau dhanadātmajau
BhP tat tathā sādhayiṣyāmi yad gītaṃ tan mahātmanā
BhP ity antareṇārjunayoḥ kṛṣṇas tu yamayor yayau
BhP ātmanirveśamātreṇa tiryaggatam ulūkhalam
BhP bālena niṣkarṣayatānvag ulūkhalaṃ tad
BhP dāmodareṇa tarasotkalitāṅghribandhau
BhP niṣpetatuḥ paramavikramitātivepa
BhP skandhapravālaviṭapau kṛtacaṇḍaśabdau
BhP tatra śriyā paramayā kakubhaḥ sphurantau
BhP siddhāv upetya kujayor iva jātavedāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya śirasākhilalokanāthaṃ
BhP baddhāñjalī virajasāv idam ūcatuḥ sma
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahāyogiṃs tvam ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ paraḥ
BhP vyaktāvyaktam idaṃ viśvaṃ rūpaṃ te brāhmaṇā viduḥ
BhP tvam ekaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ dehāsvātmendriyeśvaraḥ
BhP tvam eva kālo bhagavān viṣṇur avyaya īśvaraḥ
BhP tvaṃ mahān prakṛtiḥ sūkṣmā rajaḥsattvatamomayī
BhP tvam eva puruṣo 'dhyakṣaḥ sarvakṣetravikāravit
BhP gṛhyamāṇais tvam agrāhyo vikāraiḥ prākṛtair guṇaiḥ
BhP ko nv ihārhati vijñātuṃ prāk siddhaṃ guṇasaṃvṛtaḥ
BhP tasmai tubhyaṃ bhagavate vāsudevāya vedhase
BhP ātmadyotaguṇaiś channa mahimne brahmaṇe namaḥ
BhP yasyāvatārā jñāyante śarīreṣv aśarīriṇaḥ
BhP tais tair atulyātiśayair vīryair dehiṣv asaṅgataiḥ
BhP sa bhavān sarvalokasya bhavāya vibhavāya ca
BhP avatīrṇo 'ṃśabhāgena sāmprataṃ patir āśiṣām
BhP namaḥ paramakalyāṇa namaḥ paramamaṅgala
BhP vāsudevāya śāntāya yadūnāṃ pataye namaḥ
BhP anujānīhi nau bhūmaṃs tavānucarakiṅkarau
BhP darśanaṃ nau bhagavata ṛṣer āsīd anugrahāt
BhP vāṇī guṇānukathane śravaṇau kathāyāṃ
BhP hastau ca karmasu manas tava pādayor naḥ
BhP smṛtyāṃ śiras tava nivāsajagatpraṇāme
BhP dṛṣṭiḥ satāṃ darśane 'stu bhavattanūnām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itthaṃ saṅkīrtitas tābhyāṃ bhagavān gokuleśvaraḥ
BhP dāmnā colūkhale baddhaḥ prahasann āha guhyakau
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP jñātaṃ mama puraivaitad ṛṣiṇā karuṇātmanā
BhP yac chrīmadāndhayor vāgbhir vibhraṃśo 'nugrahaḥ kṛtaḥ
BhP sādhūnāṃ samacittānāṃ sutarāṃ matkṛtātmanām
BhP darśanān no bhaved bandhaḥ puṃso 'kṣṇoḥ savitur yathā
BhP tad gacchataṃ matparamau nalakūvara sādanam
BhP sañjāto mayi bhāvo vām īpsitaḥ paramo 'bhavaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity uktau tau parikramya praṇamya ca punaḥ punaḥ
BhP baddholūkhalam āmantrya jagmatur diśam uttarām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP gopā nandādayaḥ śrutvā drumayoḥ patato ravam
BhP tatrājagmuḥ kuruśreṣṭha nirghātabhayaśaṅkitāḥ
BhP bhūmyāṃ nipatitau tatra dadṛśur yamalārjunau
BhP babhramus tad avijñāya lakṣyaṃ patanakāraṇam
BhP ulūkhalaṃ vikarṣantaṃ dāmnā baddhaṃ ca bālakam
BhP kasyedaṃ kuta āścaryam utpāta iti kātarāḥ
BhP bālā ūcur aneneti tiryaggatam ulūkhalam
BhP vikarṣatā madhyagena puruṣāv apy acakṣmahi
BhP na te taduktaṃ jagṛhur na ghaṭeteti tasya tat
BhP bālasyotpāṭanaṃ tarvoḥ kecit sandigdhacetasaḥ
BhP ulūkhalaṃ vikarṣantaṃ dāmnā baddhaṃ svam ātmajam
BhP vilokya nandaḥ prahasad vadano vimumoca ha
BhP gopībhiḥ stobhito 'nṛtyad bhagavān bālavat kvacit
BhP udgāyati kvacin mugdhas tadvaśo dāruyantravat
BhP bibharti kvacid ājñaptaḥ pīṭhakonmānapādukam
BhP bāhukṣepaṃ ca kurute svānāṃ ca prītim āvahan
BhP darśayaṃs tadvidāṃ loka ātmano bhṛtyavaśyatām
BhP vrajasyovāha vai harṣaṃ bhagavān bālaceṣṭitaiḥ
BhP krīṇīhi bhoḥ phalānīti śrutvā satvaram acyutaḥ
BhP phalārthī dhānyam ādāya yayau sarvaphalapradaḥ
BhP phalavikrayiṇī tasya cyutadhānyakaradvayam
BhP phalair apūrayad ratnaiḥ phalabhāṇḍam apūri ca
BhP sarittīragataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ bhagnārjunam athāhvayat
BhP rāmaṃ ca rohiṇī devī krīḍantaṃ bālakair bhṛśam
BhP nopeyātāṃ yadāhūtau krīḍāsaṅgena putrakau
BhP yaśodāṃ preṣayām āsa rohiṇī putravatsalām
BhP krīḍantaṃ sā sutaṃ bālair ativelaṃ sahāgrajam
BhP yaśodājohavīt kṛṣṇaṃ putrasnehasnutastanī
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇāravindākṣa tāta ehi stanaṃ piba
BhP alaṃ vihāraiḥ kṣutkṣāntaḥ krīḍāśrānto 'si putraka
BhP he rāmāgaccha tātāśu sānujaḥ kulanandana
BhP prātar eva kṛtāhāras tad bhavān bhoktum arhati
BhP pratīkṣate tvāṃ dāśārha bhokṣyamāṇo vrajādhipaḥ
BhP ehy āvayoḥ priyaṃ dhehi svagṛhān yāta bālakāḥ
BhP dhūlidhūsaritāṅgas tvaṃ putra majjanam āvaha
BhP janmarkṣaṃ te 'dya bhavati viprebhyo dehi gāḥ śuciḥ
BhP paśya paśya vayasyāṃs te mātṛmṛṣṭān svalaṅkṛtān
BhP tvaṃ ca snātaḥ kṛtāhāro viharasva svalaṅkṛtaḥ
BhP itthaṃ yaśodā tam aśeṣaśekharaṃ matvā sutaṃ snehanibaddhadhīr nṛpa
BhP haste gṛhītvā saharāmam acyutaṃ nītvā svavāṭaṃ kṛtavaty athodayam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP gopavṛddhā mahotpātān anubhūya bṛhadvane
BhP nandādayaḥ samāgamya vrajakāryam amantrayan
BhP tatropānandanāmāha gopo jñānavayo'dhikaḥ
BhP deśakālārthatattvajñaḥ priyakṛd rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP utthātavyam ito 'smābhir gokulasya hitaiṣibhiḥ
BhP āyānty atra mahotpātā bālānāṃ nāśahetavaḥ
BhP muktaḥ kathañcid rākṣasyā bālaghnyā bālako hy asau
BhP harer anugrahān nūnam anaś copari nāpatat
BhP cakravātena nīto 'yaṃ daityena vipadaṃ viyat
BhP śilāyāṃ patitas tatra paritrātaḥ sureśvaraiḥ
BhP yan na mriyeta drumayor antaraṃ prāpya bālakaḥ
BhP asāv anyatamo vāpi tad apy acyutarakṣaṇam
BhP yāvad autpātiko 'riṣṭo vrajaṃ nābhibhaved itaḥ
BhP tāvad bālān upādāya yāsyāmo 'nyatra sānugāḥ
BhP vanaṃ vṛndāvanaṃ nāma paśavyaṃ navakānanam
BhP gopagopīgavāṃ sevyaṃ puṇyādritṛṇavīrudham
BhP tat tatrādyaiva yāsyāmaḥ śakaṭān yuṅkta mā ciram
BhP godhanāny agrato yāntu bhavatāṃ yadi rocate
BhP tac chrutvaikadhiyo gopāḥ sādhu sādhv iti vādinaḥ
BhP vrajān svān svān samāyujya yayū rūḍhaparicchadāḥ
BhP vṛddhān bālān striyo rājan sarvopakaraṇāni ca
BhP anaḥsv āropya gopālā yattā āttaśarāsanāḥ
BhP godhanāni puraskṛtya śṛṅgāṇy āpūrya sarvataḥ
BhP tūryaghoṣeṇa mahatā yayuḥ sahapurohitāḥ
BhP gopyo rūḍharathā nūtna kucakuṅkumakāntayaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇalīlā jaguḥ prītyā niṣkakaṇṭhyaḥ suvāsasaḥ
BhP tathā yaśodārohiṇyāv ekaṃ śakaṭam āsthite
BhP rejatuḥ kṛṣṇarāmābhyāṃ tatkathāśravaṇotsuke
BhP vṛndāvanaṃ sampraviśya sarvakālasukhāvaham
BhP tatra cakrur vrajāvāsaṃ śakaṭair ardhacandravat
BhP vṛndāvanaṃ govardhanaṃ yamunāpulināni ca
BhP vīkṣyāsīd uttamā prītī rāmamādhavayor nṛpa
BhP evaṃ vrajaukasāṃ prītiṃ yacchantau bālaceṣṭitaiḥ
BhP kalavākyaiḥ svakālena vatsapālau babhūvatuḥ
BhP avidūre vrajabhuvaḥ saha gopāladārakaiḥ
BhP cārayām āsatur vatsān nānākrīḍāparicchadau
BhP kvacid vādayato veṇuṃ kṣepaṇaiḥ kṣipataḥ kvacit
BhP kvacit pādaiḥ kiṅkiṇībhiḥ kvacit kṛtrimagovṛṣaiḥ
BhP vṛṣāyamāṇau nardantau yuyudhāte parasparam
BhP anukṛtya rutair jantūṃś ceratuḥ prākṛtau yathā
BhP kadācid yamunātīre vatsāṃś cārayatoḥ svakaiḥ
BhP vayasyaiḥ kṛṣṇabalayor jighāṃsur daitya āgamat
BhP taṃ vatsarūpiṇaṃ vīkṣya vatsayūthagataṃ hariḥ
BhP darśayan baladevāya śanair mugdha ivāsadat
BhP gṛhītvāparapādābhyāṃ sahalāṅgūlam acyutaḥ
BhP bhrāmayitvā kapitthāgre prāhiṇod gatajīvitam
BhP sa kapitthair mahākāyaḥ pātyamānaiḥ papāta ha
BhP taṃ vīkṣya vismitā bālāḥ śaśaṃsuḥ sādhu sādhv iti
BhP devāś ca parisantuṣṭā babhūvuḥ puṣpavarṣiṇaḥ
BhP tau vatsapālakau bhūtvā sarvalokaikapālakau
BhP saprātarāśau govatsāṃś cārayantau viceratuḥ
BhP svaṃ svaṃ vatsakulaṃ sarve pāyayiṣyanta ekadā
BhP gatvā jalāśayābhyāśaṃ pāyayitvā papur jalam
BhP te tatra dadṛśur bālā mahāsattvam avasthitam
BhP tatrasur vajranirbhinnaṃ gireḥ śṛṅgam iva cyutam
BhP sa vai bako nāma mahān asuro bakarūpadhṛk
BhP āgatya sahasā kṛṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇatuṇḍo 'grasad balī
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ mahābakagrastaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmādayo 'rbhakāḥ
BhP babhūvur indriyāṇīva vinā prāṇaṃ vicetasaḥ
BhP taṃ tālumūlaṃ pradahantam agnivad gopālasūnuṃ pitaraṃ jagadguroḥ
BhP caccharda sadyo 'tiruṣākṣataṃ bakas tuṇḍena hantuṃ punar abhyapadyata
BhP tam āpatantaṃ sa nigṛhya tuṇḍayor dorbhyāṃ bakaṃ kaṃsasakhaṃ satāṃ patiḥ
BhP paśyatsu bāleṣu dadāra līlayā mudāvaho vīraṇavad divaukasām
BhP tadā bakāriṃ suralokavāsinaḥ samākiran nandanamallikādibhiḥ
BhP samīḍire cānakaśaṅkhasaṃstavais tad vīkṣya gopālasutā visismire
BhP muktaṃ bakāsyād upalabhya bālakā rāmādayaḥ prāṇam ivendriyo gaṇaḥ
BhP sthānāgataṃ taṃ parirabhya nirvṛtāḥ praṇīya vatsān vrajam etya taj jaguḥ
BhP śrutvā tad vismitā gopā gopyaś cātipriyādṛtāḥ
BhP pretyāgatam ivotsukyād aikṣanta tṛṣitekṣaṇāḥ
BhP aho batāsya bālasya bahavo mṛtyavo 'bhavan
BhP apy āsīd vipriyaṃ teṣāṃ kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ yato bhayam
BhP athāpy abhibhavanty enaṃ naiva te ghoradarśanāḥ
BhP jighāṃsayainam āsādya naśyanty agnau pataṅgavat
BhP aho brahmavidāṃ vāco nāsatyāḥ santi karhicit
BhP gargo yad āha bhagavān anvabhāvi tathaiva tat
BhP iti nandādayo gopāḥ kṛṣṇarāmakathāṃ mudā
BhP kurvanto ramamāṇāś ca nāvindan bhavavedanām
BhP evaṃ vihāraiḥ kaumāraiḥ kaumāraṃ jahatur vraje
BhP nilāyanaiḥ setubandhair markaṭotplavanādibhiḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP kvacid vanāśāya mano dadhad vrajāt prātaḥ samutthāya vayasyavatsapān
BhP prabodhayañ chṛṅgaraveṇa cāruṇā vinirgato vatsapuraḥsaro hariḥ
BhP tenaiva sākaṃ pṛthukāḥ sahasraśaḥ snigdhāḥ suśigvetraviṣāṇaveṇavaḥ
BhP svān svān sahasroparisaṅkhyayānvitān vatsān puraskṛtya viniryayur mudā
BhP kṛṣṇavatsair asaṅkhyātair yūthīkṛtya svavatsakān
BhP cārayanto 'rbhalīlābhir vijahrus tatra tatra ha
BhP phalaprabālastavaka sumanaḥpicchadhātubhiḥ
BhP kācaguñjāmaṇisvarṇa bhūṣitā apy abhūṣayan
BhP muṣṇanto 'nyonyaśikyādīn jñātān ārāc ca cikṣipuḥ
BhP tatratyāś ca punar dūrād dhasantaś ca punar daduḥ
BhP yadi dūraṃ gataḥ kṛṣṇo vanaśobhekṣaṇāya tam
BhP ahaṃ pūrvam ahaṃ pūrvam iti saṃspṛśya remire
BhP kecid veṇūn vādayanto dhmāntaḥ śṛṅgāṇi kecana
BhP kecid bhṛṅgaiḥ pragāyantaḥ kūjantaḥ kokilaiḥ pare
BhP vicchāyābhiḥ pradhāvanto gacchantaḥ sādhuhaṃsakaiḥ
BhP bakair upaviśantaś ca nṛtyantaś ca kalāpibhiḥ
BhP vikarṣantaḥ kīśabālān ārohantaś ca tair drumān
BhP vikurvantaś ca taiḥ sākaṃ plavantaś ca palāśiṣu
BhP sākaṃ bhekair vilaṅghantaḥ saritaḥ sravasamplutāḥ
BhP vihasantaḥ praticchāyāḥ śapantaś ca pratisvanān
BhP itthaṃ satāṃ brahmasukhānubhūtyā dāsyaṃ gatānāṃ paradaivatena
BhP māyāśritānāṃ naradārakeṇa sākaṃ vijahruḥ kṛtapuṇyapuñjāḥ
BhP yatpādapāṃsur bahujanmakṛcchrato
BhP dhṛtātmabhir yogibhir apy alabhyaḥ
BhP sa eva yaddṛgviṣayaḥ svayaṃ sthitaḥ
BhP kiṃ varṇyate diṣṭam ato vrajaukasām
BhP athāghanāmābhyapatan mahāsuras teṣāṃ sukhakrīḍanavīkṣaṇākṣamaḥ
BhP nityaṃ yadantar nijajīvitepsubhiḥ pītāmṛtair apy amaraiḥ pratīkṣyate
BhP dṛṣṭvārbhakān kṛṣṇamukhān aghāsuraḥ
BhP kaṃsānuśiṣṭaḥ sa bakībakānujaḥ
BhP ayaṃ tu me sodaranāśakṛt tayor
BhP dvayor mamainaṃ sabalaṃ haniṣye
BhP ete yadā matsuhṛdos tilāpaḥ kṛtās tadā naṣṭasamā vrajaukasaḥ
BhP prāṇe gate varṣmasu kā nu cintā prajāsavaḥ prāṇabhṛto hi ye te
BhP iti vyavasyājagaraṃ bṛhad vapuḥ sa yojanāyāmamahādripīvaram
BhP dhṛtvādbhutaṃ vyāttaguhānanaṃ tadā pathi vyaśeta grasanāśayā khalaḥ
BhP dharādharoṣṭho jaladottaroṣṭho daryānanānto giriśṛṅgadaṃṣṭraḥ
BhP dhvāntāntarāsyo vitatādhvajihvaḥ paruṣānilaśvāsadavekṣaṇoṣṇaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā taṃ tādṛśaṃ sarve matvā vṛndāvanaśriyam
BhP vyāttājagaratuṇḍena hy utprekṣante sma līlayā
BhP aho mitrāṇi gadata sattvakūṭaṃ puraḥ sthitam
BhP asmatsaṅgrasanavyātta vyālatuṇḍāyate na vā
BhP satyam arkakarāraktam uttarāhanuvad ghanam
BhP adharāhanuvad rodhas tatpraticchāyayāruṇam
BhP pratispardhete sṛkkabhyāṃ savyāsavye nagodare
BhP tuṅgaśṛṅgālayo 'py etās taddaṃṣṭrābhiś ca paśyata
BhP āstṛtāyāmamārgo 'yaṃ rasanāṃ pratigarjati
BhP eṣāṃ antargataṃ dhvāntam etad apy antarānanam
BhP dāvoṣṇakharavāto 'yaṃ śvāsavad bhāti paśyata
BhP taddagdhasattvadurgandho 'py antarāmiṣagandhavat
BhP asmān kim atra grasitā niviṣṭān ayaṃ tathā ced bakavad vinaṅkṣyati
BhP kṣaṇād aneneti bakāryuśanmukhaṃ vīkṣyoddhasantaḥ karatāḍanair yayuḥ
BhP itthaṃ mitho 'tathyam atajjñabhāṣitaṃ
BhP śrutvā vicintyety amṛṣā mṛṣāyate
BhP rakṣo viditvākhilabhūtahṛtsthitaḥ
BhP svānāṃ niroddhuṃ bhagavān mano dadhe
BhP tāvat praviṣṭās tv asurodarāntaraṃ paraṃ na gīrṇāḥ śiśavaḥ savatsāḥ
BhP pratīkṣamāṇena bakāriveśanaṃ hatasvakāntasmaraṇena rakṣasā
BhP tān vīkṣya kṛṣṇaḥ sakalābhayaprado
BhP hy ananyanāthān svakarād avacyutān
BhP dīnāṃś ca mṛtyor jaṭharāgnighāsān
BhP ghṛṇārdito diṣṭakṛtena vismitaḥ
BhP kṛtyaṃ kim atrāsya khalasya jīvanaṃ
BhP na vā amīṣāṃ ca satāṃ vihiṃsanam
BhP dvayaṃ kathaṃ syād iti saṃvicintya
BhP jñātvāviśat tuṇḍam aśeṣadṛg ghariḥ
BhP tadā ghanacchadā devā bhayād dhāheti cukruśuḥ
BhP jahṛṣur ye ca kaṃsādyāḥ kauṇapās tv aghabāndhavāḥ
BhP tac chrutvā bhagavān kṛṣṇas tv avyayaḥ sārbhavatsakam
BhP cūrṇīcikīrṣor ātmānaṃ tarasā vavṛdhe gale
BhP tato 'tikāyasya niruddhamārgiṇo hy udgīrṇadṛṣṭer bhramatas tv itas tataḥ
BhP pūrṇo 'ntaraṅge pavano niruddho mūrdhan vinirbhidya vinirgato bahiḥ
BhP tenaiva sarveṣu bahir gateṣu prāṇeṣu vatsān suhṛdaḥ paretān
BhP dṛṣṭyā svayotthāpya tadanvitaḥ punar vaktrān mukundo bhagavān viniryayau
BhP pīnāhibhogotthitam adbhutaṃ mahaj jyotiḥ svadhāmnā jvalayad diśo daśa
BhP pratīkṣya khe 'vasthitam īśanirgamaṃ viveśa tasmin miṣatāṃ divaukasām
BhP tato 'tihṛṣṭāḥ svakṛto 'kṛtārhaṇaṃ
BhP puṣpaiḥ sugā apsarasaś ca nartanaiḥ
BhP gītaiḥ surā vādyadharāś ca vādyakaiḥ
BhP stavaiś ca viprā jayaniḥsvanair gaṇāḥ
BhP tadadbhutastotrasuvādyagītikā jayādinaikotsavamaṅgalasvanān
BhP śrutvā svadhāmno 'nty aja āgato 'cirād dṛṣṭvā mahīśasya jagāma vismayam
BhP rājann ājagaraṃ carma śuṣkaṃ vṛndāvane 'dbhutam
BhP vrajaukasāṃ bahutithaṃ babhūvākrīḍagahvaram
BhP etat kaumārajaṃ karma harer ātmāhimokṣaṇam
BhP mṛtyoḥ paugaṇḍake bālā dṛṣṭvocur vismitā vraje
BhP naitad vicitraṃ manujārbhamāyinaḥ parāvarāṇāṃ paramasya vedhasaḥ
BhP agho 'pi yatsparśanadhautapātakaḥ prāpātmasāmyaṃ tv asatāṃ sudurlabham
BhP sakṛd yadaṅgapratimāntarāhitā manomayī bhāgavatīṃ dadau gatim
BhP sa eva nityātmasukhānubhūtyabhi vyudastamāyo 'ntargato hi kiṃ punaḥ
BhP śrīsūta uvāca
BhP itthaṃ dvijā yādavadevadattaḥ śrutvā svarātuś caritaṃ vicitram
BhP papraccha bhūyo 'pi tad eva puṇyaṃ vaiyāsakiṃ yan nigṛhītacetāḥ
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP brahman kālāntarakṛtaṃ tatkālīnaṃ kathaṃ bhavet
BhP yat kaumāre harikṛtaṃ jaguḥ paugaṇḍake 'rbhakāḥ
BhP tad brūhi me mahāyogin paraṃ kautūhalaṃ guro
BhP nūnam etad dharer eva māyā bhavati nānyathā
BhP vayaṃ dhanyatamā loke guro 'pi kṣatrabandhavaḥ
BhP vayaṃ pibāmo muhus tvattaḥ puṇyaṃ kṛṣṇakathāmṛtam
BhP śrīsūta uvāca
BhP itthaṃ sma pṛṣṭaḥ sa tu bādarāyaṇis
BhP tatsmāritānantahṛtākhilendriyaḥ
BhP kṛcchrāt punar labdhabahirdṛśiḥ śanaiḥ
BhP pratyāha taṃ bhāgavatottamottama
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ mahābhāga tvayā bhāgavatottama
BhP yan nūtanayasīśasya śṛṇvann api kathāṃ muhuḥ
BhP satām ayaṃ sārabhṛtāṃ nisargo yadarthavāṇīśruticetasām api
BhP pratikṣaṇaṃ navyavad acyutasya yat striyā viṭānām iva sādhu vārtā
BhP śṛṇuṣvāvahito rājann api guhyaṃ vadāmi te
BhP brūyuḥ snigdhasya śiṣyasya guravo guhyam apy uta
BhP tathāghavadanān mṛtyo rakṣitvā vatsapālakān
BhP saritpulinam ānīya bhagavān idam abravīt
BhP aho 'tiramyaṃ pulinaṃ vayasyāḥ svakelisampan mṛdulācchabālukam
BhP sphuṭatsarogandhahṛtālipatrika dhvanipratidhvānalasaddrumākulam
BhP atra bhoktavyam asmābhir divārūḍhaṃ kṣudhārditāḥ
BhP vatsāḥ samīpe 'paḥ pītvā carantu śanakais tṛṇam
BhP tatheti pāyayitvārbhā vatsān ārudhya śādvale
BhP muktvā śikyāni bubhujuḥ samaṃ bhagavatā mudā
BhP kṛṣṇasya viṣvak pururājimaṇḍalair
BhP abhyānanāḥ phulladṛśo vrajārbhakāḥ
BhP sahopaviṣṭā vipine virejuś
BhP chadā yathāmbhoruhakarṇikāyāḥ
BhP kecit puṣpair dalaiḥ kecit pallavair aṅkuraiḥ phalaiḥ
BhP śigbhis tvagbhir dṛṣadbhiś ca bubhujuḥ kṛtabhājanāḥ
BhP sarve mitho darśayantaḥ svasvabhojyaruciṃ pṛthak
BhP hasanto hāsayantaś cā bhyavajahruḥ saheśvarāḥ
BhP bibhrad veṇuṃ jaṭharapaṭayoḥ śṛṅgavetre ca kakṣe
BhP vāme pāṇau masṛṇakavalaṃ tatphalāny aṅgulīṣu
BhP tiṣṭhan madhye svaparisuhṛdo hāsayan narmabhiḥ svaiḥ
BhP svarge loke miṣati bubhuje yajñabhug bālakeliḥ
BhP bhārataivaṃ vatsapeṣu bhuñjāneṣv acyutātmasu
BhP vatsās tv antarvane dūraṃ viviśus tṛṇalobhitāḥ
BhP tān dṛṣṭvā bhayasantrastān ūce kṛṣṇo 'sya bhībhayam
BhP mitrāṇy āśān mā viramate hāneṣye vatsakān aham
BhP ity uktvādridarīkuñja gahvareṣv ātmavatsakān
BhP vicinvan bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ sapāṇikavalo yayau
BhP ambhojanmajanis tadantaragato māyārbhakasyeśitur
BhP draṣṭuṃ mañju mahitvam anyad api tadvatsān ito vatsapān
BhP nītvānyatra kurūdvahāntaradadhāt khe 'vasthito yaḥ purā
BhP dṛṣṭvāghāsuramokṣaṇaṃ prabhavataḥ prāptaḥ paraṃ vismayam
BhP tato vatsān adṛṣṭvaitya puline 'pi ca vatsapān
BhP ubhāv api vane kṛṣṇo vicikāya samantataḥ
BhP kvāpy adṛṣṭvāntarvipine vatsān pālāṃś ca viśvavit
BhP sarvaṃ vidhikṛtaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sahasāvajagāma ha
BhP tataḥ kṛṣṇo mudaṃ kartuṃ tanmātṝṇāṃ ca kasya ca
BhP ubhayāyitam ātmānaṃ cakre viśvakṛd īśvaraḥ
BhP yāvad vatsapavatsakālpakavapur yāvat karāṅghryādikaṃ
BhP yāvad yaṣṭiviṣāṇaveṇudalaśig yāvad vibhūṣāmbaram
BhP yāvac chīlaguṇābhidhākṛtivayo yāvad vihārādikaṃ
BhP sarvaṃ viṣṇumayaṃ giro 'ṅgavad ajaḥ sarvasvarūpo babhau
BhP svayam ātmātmagovatsān prativāryātmavatsapaiḥ
BhP krīḍann ātmavihāraiś ca sarvātmā prāviśad vrajam
BhP tattadvatsān pṛthaṅ nītvā tattadgoṣṭhe niveśya saḥ
BhP tattadātmābhavad rājaṃs tattatsadma praviṣṭavān
BhP tanmātaro veṇuravatvarotthitā utthāpya dorbhiḥ parirabhya nirbharam
BhP snehasnutastanyapayaḥsudhāsavaṃ matvā paraṃ brahma sutān apāyayan
BhP tato nṛponmardanamajjalepanā laṅkārarakṣātilakāśanādibhiḥ
BhP saṃlālitaḥ svācaritaiḥ praharṣayan sāyaṃ gato yāmayamena mādhavaḥ
BhP gāvas tato goṣṭham upetya satvaraṃ huṅkāraghoṣaiḥ parihūtasaṅgatān
BhP svakān svakān vatsatarān apāyayan muhur lihantyaḥ sravad audhasaṃ payaḥ
BhP gogopīnāṃ mātṛtāsminn āsīt snehardhikāṃ vinā
BhP purovad āsv api hares tokatā māyayā vinā
BhP vrajaukasāṃ svatokeṣu snehavally ābdam anvaham
BhP śanair niḥsīma vavṛdhe yathā kṛṣṇe tv apūrvavat
BhP ittham ātmātmanātmānaṃ vatsapālamiṣeṇa saḥ
BhP pālayan vatsapo varṣaṃ cikrīḍe vanagoṣṭhayoḥ
BhP ekadā cārayan vatsān sarāmo vanam āviśat
BhP pañcaṣāsu triyāmāsu hāyanāpūraṇīṣv ajaḥ
BhP tato vidūrāc carato gāvo vatsān upavrajam
BhP govardhanādriśirasi carantyo dadṛśus tṛṇam
BhP dṛṣṭvātha tatsnehavaśo 'smṛtātmā sa govrajo 'tyātmapadurgamārgaḥ
BhP dvipāt kakudgrīva udāsyapuccho 'gād dhuṅkṛtair āsrupayā javena
BhP sametya gāvo 'dho vatsān vatsavatyo 'py apāyayan
BhP gilantya iva cāṅgāni lihantyaḥ svaudhasaṃ payaḥ
BhP gopās tadrodhanāyāsa maughyalajjorumanyunā
BhP durgādhvakṛcchrato 'bhyetya govatsair dadṛśuḥ sutān
BhP tadīkṣaṇotpremarasāplutāśayā jātānurāgā gatamanyavo 'rbhakān
BhP uduhya dorbhiḥ parirabhya mūrdhani ghrāṇair avāpuḥ paramāṃ mudaṃ te
BhP tataḥ pravayaso gopās tokāśleṣasunirvṛtāḥ
BhP kṛcchrāc chanair apagatās tadanusmṛtyudaśravaḥ
BhP vrajasya rāmaḥ premardher vīkṣyautkaṇṭhyam anukṣaṇam
BhP muktastaneṣv apatyeṣv apy ahetuvid acintayat
BhP kim etad adbhutam iva vāsudeve 'khilātmani
BhP vrajasya sātmanas tokeṣv apūrvaṃ prema vardhate
BhP keyaṃ vā kuta āyātā daivī vā nāry utāsurī
BhP prāyo māyāstu me bhartur nānyā me 'pi vimohinī
BhP iti sañcintya dāśārho vatsān savayasān api
BhP sarvān ācaṣṭa vaikuṇṭhaṃ cakṣuṣā vayunena saḥ
BhP naite sureśā ṛṣayo na caite tvam eva bhāsīśa bhidāśraye 'pi
BhP sarvaṃ pṛthak tvaṃ nigamāt kathaṃ vadety uktena vṛttaṃ prabhuṇā balo 'vait
BhP tāvad etyātmabhūr ātma mānena truṭyanehasā
BhP purovad ābdaṃ krīḍantaṃ dadṛśe sakalaṃ harim
BhP yāvanto gokule bālāḥ savatsāḥ sarva eva hi
BhP māyāśaye śayānā me nādyāpi punar utthitāḥ
BhP ita ete 'tra kutratyā manmāyāmohitetare
BhP tāvanta eva tatrābdaṃ krīḍanto viṣṇunā samam
BhP evam eteṣu bhedeṣu ciraṃ dhyātvā sa ātmabhūḥ
BhP satyāḥ ke katare neti jñātuṃ neṣṭe kathañcana
BhP evaṃ sammohayan viṣṇuṃ vimohaṃ viśvamohanam
BhP svayaiva māyayājo 'pi svayam eva vimohitaḥ
BhP tamyāṃ tamovan naihāraṃ khadyotārcir ivāhani
BhP mahatītaramāyaiśyaṃ nihanty ātmani yuñjataḥ
BhP tāvat sarve vatsapālāḥ paśyato 'jasya tatkṣaṇāt
BhP vyadṛśyanta ghanaśyāmāḥ pītakauśeyavāsasaḥ
BhP caturbhujāḥ śaṅkhacakra gadārājīvapāṇayaḥ
BhP kirīṭinaḥ kuṇḍalino hāriṇo vanamālinaḥ
BhP śrīvatsāṅgadadoratna kambukaṅkaṇapāṇayaḥ
BhP nūpuraiḥ kaṭakair bhātāḥ kaṭisūtrāṅgulīyakaiḥ
BhP āṅghrimastakam āpūrṇās tulasīnavadāmabhiḥ
BhP komalaiḥ sarvagātreṣu bhūripuṇyavadarpitaiḥ
BhP candrikāviśadasmeraiḥ sāruṇāpāṅgavīkṣitaiḥ
BhP svakārthānām iva rajaḥ sattvābhyāṃ sraṣṭṛpālakāḥ
BhP ātmādistambaparyantair mūrtimadbhiś carācaraiḥ
BhP nṛtyagītādyanekārhaiḥ pṛthak pṛthag upāsitāḥ
BhP aṇimādyair mahimabhir ajādyābhir vibhūtibhiḥ
BhP caturviṃśatibhis tattvaiḥ parītā mahadādibhiḥ
BhP kālasvabhāvasaṃskāra kāmakarmaguṇādibhiḥ
BhP svamahidhvastamahibhir mūrtimadbhir upāsitāḥ
BhP satyajñānānantānanda mātraikarasamūrtayaḥ
BhP aspṛṣṭabhūrimāhātmyā api hy upaniṣaddṛśām
BhP evaṃ sakṛd dadarśājaḥ parabrahmātmano 'khilān
BhP yasya bhāsā sarvam idaṃ vibhāti sacarācaram
BhP tato 'tikutukodvṛtya stimitaikādaśendriyaḥ
BhP taddhāmnābhūd ajas tūṣṇīṃ pūrdevyantīva putrikā
BhP itīreśe 'tarkye nijamahimani svapramitike
BhP paratrājāto 'tannirasanamukhabrahmakamitau
BhP anīśe 'pi draṣṭuṃ kim idam iti vā muhyati sati
BhP cacchādājo jñātvā sapadi paramo 'jājavanikām
BhP tato 'rvāk pratilabdhākṣaḥ kaḥ paretavad utthitaḥ
BhP kṛcchrād unmīlya vai dṛṣṭīr ācaṣṭedaṃ sahātmanā
BhP sapady evābhitaḥ paśyan diśo 'paśyat puraḥsthitam
BhP vṛndāvanaṃ janājīvya drumākīrṇaṃ samāpriyam
BhP yatra naisargadurvairāḥ sahāsan nṛmṛgādayaḥ
BhP mitrāṇīvājitāvāsa drutaruṭtarṣakādikam
BhP tatrodvahat paśupavaṃśaśiśutvanāṭyaṃ
BhP brahmādvayaṃ param anantam agādhabodham
BhP vatsān sakhīn iva purā parito vicinvad
BhP ekaṃ sapāṇikavalaṃ parameṣṭhy acaṣṭa
BhP dṛṣṭvā tvareṇa nijadhoraṇato 'vatīrya
BhP pṛthvyāṃ vapuḥ kanakadaṇḍam ivābhipātya
BhP spṛṣṭvā caturmukuṭakoṭibhir aṅghriyugmaṃ
BhP natvā mudaśrusujalair akṛtābhiṣekam
BhP utthāyotthāya kṛṣṇasya cirasya pādayoḥ patan
BhP āste mahitvaṃ prāgdṛṣṭaṃ smṛtvā smṛtvā punaḥ punaḥ
BhP śanair athotthāya vimṛjya locane mukundam udvīkṣya vinamrakandharaḥ
BhP kṛtāñjaliḥ praśrayavān samāhitaḥ savepathur gadgadayailatelayā
BhP śrībrahmovāca
BhP naumīḍya te 'bhravapuṣe taḍidambarāya
BhP guñjāvataṃsaparipicchalasanmukhāya
BhP vanyasraje kavalavetraviṣāṇaveṇu
BhP lakṣmaśriye mṛdupade paśupāṅgajāya
BhP asyāpi deva vapuṣo madanugrahasya svecchāmayasya na tu bhūtamayasya ko 'pi
BhP neśe mahi tv avasituṃ manasāntareṇa sākṣāt tavaiva kim utātmasukhānubhūteḥ
BhP jñāne prayāsam udapāsya namanta eva
BhP jīvanti sanmukharitāṃ bhavadīyavārtām
BhP sthāne sthitāḥ śrutigatāṃ tanuvāṅmanobhir
BhP ye prāyaśo 'jita jito 'py asi tais trilokyām
BhP śreyaḥsṛtiṃ bhaktim udasya te vibho
BhP kliśyanti ye kevalabodhalabdhaye
BhP teṣām asau kleśala eva śiṣyate
BhP nānyad yathā sthūlatuṣāvaghātinām
BhP pureha bhūman bahavo 'pi yoginas tvadarpitehā nijakarmalabdhayā
BhP vibudhya bhaktyaiva kathopanītayā prapedire 'ñjo 'cyuta te gatiṃ parām
BhP tathāpi bhūman mahimāguṇasya te viboddhum arhaty amalāntarātmabhiḥ
BhP avikriyāt svānubhavād arūpato hy ananyabodhyātmatayā na cānyathā
BhP guṇātmanas te 'pi guṇān vimātuṃ hitāvatīṛnasya ka īśire 'sya
BhP kālena yair vā vimitāḥ sukalpair bhūpāṃśavaḥ khe mihikā dyubhāsaḥ
BhP tat te 'nukampāṃ susamīkṣamāṇo bhuñjāna evātmakṛtaṃ vipākam
BhP hṛdvāgvapurbhir vidadhan namas te jīveta yo muktipade sa dāyabhāk
BhP paśyeśa me 'nāryam ananta ādye parātmani tvayy api māyimāyini
BhP māyāṃ vitatyekṣitum ātmavaibhavaṃ hy ahaṃ kiyān aiccham ivārcir agnau
BhP ataḥ kṣamasvācyuta me rajobhuvo hy ajānatas tvatpṛthagīśamāninaḥ
BhP ajāvalepāndhatamo'ndhacakṣuṣa eṣo 'nukampyo mayi nāthavān iti
BhP kvāhaṃ tamomahadahaṃkhacarāgnivārbhū
BhP saṃveṣṭitāṇḍaghaṭasaptavitastikāyaḥ
BhP kvedṛgvidhāvigaṇitāṇḍaparāṇucaryā
BhP vātādhvaromavivarasya ca te mahitvam
BhP utkṣepaṇaṃ garbhagatasya pādayoḥ kiṃ kalpate mātur adhokṣajāgase
BhP kim astināstivyapadeśabhūṣitaṃ tavāsti kukṣeḥ kiyad apy anantaḥ
BhP jagattrayāntodadhisamplavode nārāyaṇasyodaranābhinālāt
BhP vinirgato 'jas tv iti vāṅ na vai mṛṣā kintv īśvara tvan na vinirgato 'smi
BhP nārāyaṇas tvaṃ na hi sarvadehinām ātmāsy adhīśākhilalokasākṣī
BhP nārāyaṇo 'ṅgaṃ narabhūjalāyanāt tac cāpi satyaṃ na tavaiva māyā
BhP tac cej jalasthaṃ tava saj jagadvapuḥ
BhP kiṃ me na dṛṣṭaṃ bhagavaṃs tadaiva
BhP kiṃ vā sudṛṣṭaṃ hṛdi me tadaiva
BhP kiṃ no sapady eva punar vyadarśi
BhP atraiva māyādhamanāvatāre hy asya prapañcasya bahiḥ sphuṭasya
BhP kṛtsnasya cāntar jaṭhare jananyā māyātvam eva prakaṭīkṛtaṃ te
BhP yasya kukṣāv idaṃ sarvaṃ sātmaṃ bhāti yathā tathā
BhP tat tvayy apīha tat sarvaṃ kim idaṃ māyayā vinā
BhP adyaiva tvad ṛte 'sya kiṃ mama na te māyātvam ādarśitam
BhP eko 'si prathamaṃ tato vrajasuhṛdvatsāḥ samastā api
BhP tāvanto 'si caturbhujās tad akhilaiḥ sākaṃ mayopāsitās
BhP tāvanty eva jaganty abhūs tad amitaṃ brahmādvayaṃ śiṣyate
BhP ajānatāṃ tvatpadavīm anātmany ātmātmanā bhāsi vitatya māyām
BhP sṛṣṭāv ivāhaṃ jagato vidhāna iva tvam eṣo 'nta iva trinetraḥ
BhP sureṣv ṛṣiṣv īśa tathaiva nṛṣv api tiryakṣu yādaḥsv api te 'janasya
BhP janmāsatāṃ durmadanigrahāya prabho vidhātaḥ sadanugrahāya ca
BhP ko vetti bhūman bhagavan parātman yogeśvarotīr bhavatas trilokyām
BhP kva vā kathaṃ vā kati vā kadeti vistārayan krīḍasi yogamāyām
BhP tasmād idaṃ jagad aśeṣam asatsvarūpaṃ
BhP svapnābham astadhiṣaṇaṃ puruduḥkhaduḥkham
BhP tvayy eva nityasukhabodhatanāv anante
BhP māyāta udyad api yat sad ivāvabhāti
BhP ekas tvam ātmā puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ satyaḥ svayaṃjyotir ananta ādyaḥ
BhP nityo 'kṣaro 'jasrasukho nirañjanaḥ pūrṇādvayo mukta upādhito 'mṛtaḥ
BhP evaṃvidhaṃ tvāṃ sakalātmanām api svātmānam ātmātmatayā vicakṣate
BhP gurvarkalabdhopaniṣatsucakṣuṣā ye te tarantīva bhavānṛtāmbudhim
BhP ātmānam evātmatayāvijānatāṃ tenaiva jātaṃ nikhilaṃ prapañcitam
BhP jñānena bhūyo 'pi ca tat pralīyate rajjvām aher bhogabhavābhavau yathā
BhP ajñānasaṃjñau bhavabandhamokṣau dvau nāma nānyau sta ṛtajñabhāvāt
BhP ajasracity ātmani kevale pare vicāryamāṇe taraṇāv ivāhanī
BhP tvām ātmānaṃ paraṃ matvā param ātmānam eva ca
BhP ātmā punar bahir mṛgya aho 'jñajanatājñatā
BhP antarbhave 'nanta bhavantam eva hy atat tyajanto mṛgayanti santaḥ
BhP asantam apy anty ahim antareṇa santaṃ guṇaṃ taṃ kim u yanti santaḥ
BhP athāpi te deva padāmbujadvaya prasādaleśānugṛhīta eva hi
BhP jānāti tattvaṃ bhagavanmahimno na cānya eko 'pi ciraṃ vicinvan
BhP tad astu me nātha sa bhūribhāgo bhave 'tra vānyatra tu vā tiraścām
BhP yenāham eko 'pi bhavajjanānāṃ bhūtvā niṣeve tava pādapallavam
BhP aho 'tidhanyā vrajagoramaṇyaḥ stanyāmṛtaṃ pītam atīva te mudā
BhP yāsāṃ vibho vatsatarātmajātmanā yattṛptaye 'dyāpi na cālam adhvarāḥ
BhP aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ nandagopavrajaukasām
BhP yanmitraṃ paramānandaṃ pūrṇaṃ brahma sanātanam
BhP eṣāṃ tu bhāgyamahimācyuta tāvad āstām
BhP ekādaśaiva hi vayaṃ bata bhūribhāgāḥ
BhP etaddhṛṣīkacaṣakair asakṛt pibāmaḥ
BhP śarvādayo 'ṅghryudajamadhvamṛtāsavaṃ te
BhP tad bhūribhāgyam iha janma kim apy aṭavyāṃ
BhP yad gokule 'pi katamāṅghrirajo'bhiṣekam
BhP yajjīvitaṃ tu nikhilaṃ bhagavān mukundas
BhP tv adyāpi yatpadarajaḥ śrutimṛgyam eva
BhP eṣāṃ ghoṣanivāsinām uta bhavān kiṃ deva rāteti naś
BhP ceto viśvaphalāt phalaṃ tvadaparaṃ kutrāpy ayan muhyati
BhP sadveṣād iva pūtanāpi sakulā tvām eva devāpitā
BhP yaddhāmārthasuhṛtpriyātmatanayaprāṇāśayās tvatkṛte
BhP tāvad rāgādayaḥ stenās tāvat kārāgṛhaṃ gṛham
BhP tāvan moho 'ṅghrinigaḍo yāvat kṛṣṇa na te janāḥ
BhP prapañcaṃ niṣprapañco 'pi viḍambayasi bhūtale
BhP prapannajanatānanda sandohaṃ prathituṃ prabho
BhP jānanta eva jānantu kiṃ bahūktyā na me prabho
BhP manaso vapuṣo vāco vaibhavaṃ tava gocaraḥ
BhP anujānīhi māṃ kṛṣṇa sarvaṃ tvaṃ vetsi sarvadṛk
BhP tvam eva jagatāṃ nātho jagad etat tavārpitam
BhP śrīkṛṣṇa vṛṣṇikulapuṣkarajoṣadāyin
BhP kṣmānirjaradvijapaśūdadhivṛddhikārin
BhP uddharmaśārvarahara kṣitirākṣasadhrug
BhP ākalpam ārkam arhan bhagavan namas te
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity abhiṣṭūya bhūmānaṃ triḥ parikramya pādayoḥ
BhP natvābhīṣṭaṃ jagaddhātā svadhāma pratyapadyata
BhP tato 'nujñāpya bhagavān svabhuvaṃ prāg avasthitān
BhP vatsān pulinam āninye yathāpūrvasakhaṃ svakam
BhP ekasminn api yāte 'bde prāṇeśaṃ cāntarātmanaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇamāyāhatā rājan kṣaṇārdhaṃ menire 'rbhakāḥ
BhP kiṃ kiṃ na vismarantīha māyāmohitacetasaḥ
BhP yanmohitaṃ jagat sarvam abhīkṣṇaṃ vismṛtātmakam
BhP ūcuś ca suhṛdaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ svāgataṃ te 'tiraṃhasā
BhP naiko 'py abhoji kavala ehītaḥ sādhu bhujyatām
BhP tato hasan hṛṣīkeśo 'bhyavahṛtya sahārbhakaiḥ
BhP darśayaṃś carmājagaraṃ nyavartata vanād vrajam
BhP barhaprasūnavanadhātuvicitritāṅgaḥ
BhP proddāmaveṇudalaśṛṅgaravotsavāḍhyaḥ
BhP vatsān gṛṇann anugagītapavitrakīrtir
BhP gopīdṛgutsavadṛśiḥ praviveśa goṣṭham
BhP adyānena mahāvyālo yaśodānandasūnunā
BhP hato 'vitā vayaṃ cāsmād iti bālā vraje jaguḥ
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP brahman parodbhave kṛṣṇe iyān premā kathaṃ bhavet
BhP yo 'bhūtapūrvas tokeṣu svodbhaveṣv api kathyatām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sarveṣām api bhūtānāṃ nṛpa svātmaiva vallabhaḥ
BhP itare 'patyavittādyās tadvallabhatayaiva hi
BhP tad rājendra yathā snehaḥ svasvakātmani dehinām
BhP na tathā mamatālambi putravittagṛhādiṣu
BhP dehātmavādināṃ puṃsām api rājanyasattama
BhP yathā dehaḥ priyatamas tathā na hy anu ye ca tam
BhP deho 'pi mamatābhāk cet tarhy asau nātmavat priyaḥ
BhP yaj jīryaty api dehe 'smin jīvitāśā balīyasī
BhP tasmāt priyatamaḥ svātmā sarveṣām api dehinām
BhP tadartham eva sakalaṃ jagad etac carācaram
BhP kṛṣṇam enam avehi tvam ātmānam akhilātmanām
BhP jagaddhitāya so 'py atra dehīvābhāti māyayā
BhP vastuto jānatām atra kṛṣṇaṃ sthāsnu cariṣṇu ca
BhP bhagavadrūpam akhilaṃ nānyad vastv iha kiñcana
BhP sarveṣām api vastūnāṃ bhāvārtho bhavati sthitaḥ
BhP tasyāpi bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ kim atad vastu rūpyatām
BhP samāśritā ye padapallavaplavaṃ mahatpadaṃ puṇyayaśo murāreḥ
BhP bhavāmbudhir vatsapadaṃ paraṃ padaṃ padaṃ padaṃ yad vipadāṃ na teṣām
BhP etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yat pṛṣṭo 'ham iha tvayā
BhP tat kaumāre harikṛtaṃ paugaṇḍe parikīrtitam
BhP etat suhṛdbhiś caritaṃ murārer aghārdanaṃ śādvalajemanaṃ ca
BhP vyaktetarad rūpam ajorvabhiṣṭavaṃ śṛṇvan gṛṇann eti naro 'khilārthān
BhP evaṃ vihāraiḥ kaumāraiḥ kaumāraṃ jahatur vraje
BhP nilāyanaiḥ setubandhair markaṭotplavanādibhiḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP tataś ca paugaṇḍavayaḥśrītau vraje
BhP babhūvatus tau paśupālasammatau
BhP gāś cārayantau sakhibhiḥ samaṃ padair
BhP vṛndāvanaṃ puṇyam atīva cakratuḥ
BhP tan mādhavo veṇum udīrayan vṛto gopair gṛṇadbhiḥ svayaśo balānvitaḥ
BhP paśūn puraskṛtya paśavyam āviśad vihartukāmaḥ kusumākaraṃ vanam
BhP tan mañjughoṣālimṛgadvijākulaṃ mahanmanaḥprakhyapayaḥsarasvatā
BhP vātena juṣṭaṃ śatapatragandhinā nirīkṣya rantuṃ bhagavān mano dadhe
BhP sa tatra tatrāruṇapallavaśriyā phalaprasūnorubhareṇa pādayoḥ
BhP spṛśac chikhān vīkṣya vanaspatīn mudā smayann ivāhāgrajam ādipūruṣaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP aho amī devavarāmarārcitaṃ pādāmbujaṃ te sumanaḥphalārhaṇam
BhP namanty upādāya śikhābhir ātmanas tamo'pahatyai tarujanma yatkṛtam
BhP ete 'linas tava yaśo 'khilalokatīrthaṃ
BhP gāyanta ādipuruṣānupathaṃ bhajante
BhP prāyo amī munigaṇā bhavadīyamukhyā
BhP gūḍhaṃ vane 'pi na jahaty anaghātmadaivam
BhP nṛtyanty amī śikhina īḍya mudā hariṇyaḥ
BhP kurvanti gopya iva te priyam īkṣaṇena
BhP sūktaiś ca kokilagaṇā gṛham āgatāya
BhP dhanyā vanaukasa iyān hi satāṃ nisargaḥ
BhP dhanyeyam adya dharaṇī tṛṇavīrudhas tvat
BhP pādaspṛśo drumalatāḥ karajābhimṛṣṭāḥ
BhP nadyo 'drayaḥ khagamṛgāḥ sadayāvalokair
BhP gopyo 'ntareṇa bhujayor api yatspṛhā śrīḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ vṛndāvanaṃ śrīmat kṛṣṇaḥ prītamanāḥ paśūn
BhP reme sañcārayann adreḥ saridrodhaḥsu sānugaḥ
BhP kvacid gāyati gāyatsu madāndhāliṣv anuvrataiḥ
BhP upagīyamānacaritaḥ pathi saṅkarṣaṇānvitaḥ
BhP anujalpati jalpantaṃ kalavākyaiḥ śukaṃ kvacit
BhP kvacit savalgu kūjantam anukūjati kokilam
BhP kvacic ca kālahaṃsānām anukūjati kūjitam
BhP abhinṛtyati nṛtyantaṃ barhiṇaṃ hāsayan kvacit
BhP meghagambhīrayā vācā nāmabhir dūragān paśūn
BhP kvacid āhvayati prītyā gogopālamanojñayā
BhP cakorakrauñcacakrāhva bhāradvājāṃś ca barhiṇaḥ
BhP anurauti sma sattvānāṃ bhītavad vyāghrasiṃhayoḥ
BhP kvacit krīḍāpariśrāntaṃ gopotsaṅgopabarhaṇam
BhP svayaṃ viśramayaty āryaṃ pādasaṃvāhanādibhiḥ
BhP nṛtyato gāyataḥ kvāpi valgato yudhyato mithaḥ
BhP gṛhītahastau gopālān hasantau praśaśaṃsatuḥ
BhP kvacit pallavatalpeṣu niyuddhaśramakarśitaḥ
BhP vṛkṣamūlāśrayaḥ śete gopotsaṅgopabarhaṇaḥ
BhP pādasaṃvāhanaṃ cakruḥ kecit tasya mahātmanaḥ
BhP apare hatapāpmāno vyajanaiḥ samavījayan
BhP anye tadanurūpāṇi manojñāni mahātmanaḥ
BhP gāyanti sma mahārāja snehaklinnadhiyaḥ śanaiḥ
BhP evaṃ nigūḍhātmagatiḥ svamāyayā gopātmajatvaṃ caritair viḍambayan
BhP reme ramālālitapādapallavo grāmyaiḥ samaṃ grāmyavad īśaceṣṭitaḥ
BhP śrīdāmā nāma gopālo rāmakeśavayoḥ sakhā
BhP subalastokakṛṣṇādyā gopāḥ premṇedam abruvan
BhP rāma rāma mahābāho kṛṣṇa duṣṭanibarhaṇa
BhP ito 'vidūre sumahad vanaṃ tālālisaṅkulam
BhP phalāni tatra bhūrīṇi patanti patitāni ca
BhP santi kintv avaruddhāni dhenukena durātmanā
BhP so 'tivīryo 'suro rāma he kṛṣṇa khararūpadhṛk
BhP ātmatulyabalair anyair jñātibhir bahubhir vṛtaḥ
BhP tasmāt kṛtanarāhārād bhītair nṛbhir amitrahan
BhP na sevyate paśugaṇaiḥ pakṣisaṅghair vivarjitam
BhP vidyante 'bhuktapūrvāṇi phalāni surabhīṇi ca
BhP eṣa vai surabhir gandho viṣūcīno 'vagṛhyate
BhP prayaccha tāni naḥ kṛṣṇa gandhalobhitacetasām
BhP vāñchāsti mahatī rāma gamyatāṃ yadi rocate
BhP evaṃ suhṛdvacaḥ śrutvā suhṛtpriyacikīrṣayā
BhP prahasya jagmatur gopair vṛtau tālavanaṃ prabhū
BhP balaḥ praviśya bāhubhyāṃ tālān samparikampayan
BhP phalāni pātayām āsa mataṅgaja ivaujasā
BhP phalānāṃ patatāṃ śabdaṃ niśamyāsurarāsabhaḥ
BhP abhyadhāvat kṣititalaṃ sanagaṃ parikampayan
BhP sametya tarasā pratyag dvābhyāṃ padbhyāṃ balaṃ balī
BhP nihatyorasi kāśabdaṃ muñcan paryasarat khalaḥ
BhP punar āsādya saṃrabdha upakroṣṭā parāk sthitaḥ
BhP caraṇāv aparau rājan balāya prākṣipad ruṣā
BhP sa taṃ gṛhītvā prapador bhrāmayitvaikapāṇinā
BhP cikṣepa tṛṇarājāgre bhrāmaṇatyaktajīvitam
BhP tenāhato mahātālo vepamāno bṛhacchirāḥ
BhP pārśvasthaṃ kampayan bhagnaḥ sa cānyaṃ so 'pi cāparam
BhP balasya līlayotsṛṣṭa kharadehahatāhatāḥ
BhP tālāś cakampire sarve mahāvāteritā iva
BhP naitac citraṃ bhagavati hy anante jagadīśvare
BhP otaprotam idaṃ yasmiṃs tantuṣv aṅga yathā paṭaḥ
BhP tataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ ca rāmaṃ ca jñātayo dhenukasya ye
BhP kroṣṭāro 'bhyadravan sarve saṃrabdhā hatabāndhavāḥ
BhP tāṃs tān āpatataḥ kṛṣṇo rāmaś ca nṛpa līlayā
BhP gṛhītapaścāccaraṇān prāhiṇot tṛṇarājasu
BhP phalaprakarasaṅkīrṇaṃ daityadehair gatāsubhiḥ
BhP rarāja bhūḥ satālāgrair ghanair iva nabhastalam
BhP tayos tat sumahat karma niśamya vibudhādayaḥ
BhP mumucuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi cakrur vādyāni tuṣṭuvuḥ
BhP atha tālaphalāny ādan manuṣyā gatasādhvasāḥ
BhP tṛṇaṃ ca paśavaś cerur hatadhenukakānane
BhP kṛṣṇaḥ kamalapatrākṣaḥ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanaḥ
BhP stūyamāno 'nugair gopaiḥ sāgrajo vrajam āvrajat
BhP taṃ gorajaśchuritakuntalabaddhabarha
BhP vanyaprasūnarucirekṣaṇacāruhāsam
BhP veṇum kvaṇantam anugair upagītakīrtiṃ
BhP gopyo didṛkṣitadṛśo 'bhyagaman sametāḥ
BhP pītvā mukundamukhasāragham akṣibhṛṅgais
BhP tāpaṃ jahur virahajaṃ vrajayoṣito 'hni
BhP tat satkṛtiṃ samadhigamya viveśa goṣṭhaṃ
BhP savrīḍahāsavinayaṃ yad apāṅgamokṣam
BhP tayor yaśodārohiṇyau putrayoḥ putravatsale
BhP yathākāmaṃ yathākālaṃ vyadhattāṃ paramāśiṣaḥ
BhP gatādhvānaśramau tatra majjanonmardanādibhiḥ
BhP nīvīṃ vasitvā rucirāṃ divyasraggandhamaṇḍitau
BhP jananyupahṛtaṃ prāśya svādy annam upalālitau
BhP saṃviśya varaśayyāyāṃ sukhaṃ suṣupatur vraje
BhP evaṃ sa bhagavān kṛṣṇo vṛndāvanacaraḥ kvacit
BhP yayau rāmam ṛte rājan kālindīṃ sakhibhir vṛtaḥ
BhP atha gāvaś ca gopāś ca nidāghātapapīḍitāḥ
BhP duṣṭaṃ jalaṃ papus tasyās tṛṣṇārtā viṣadūṣitam
BhP viṣāmbhas tad upaspṛśya daivopahatacetasaḥ
BhP nipetur vyasavaḥ sarve salilānte kurūdvaha
BhP vīkṣya tān vai tathābhūtān kṛṣṇo yogeśvareśvaraḥ
BhP īkṣayāmṛtavarṣiṇyā svanāthān samajīvayat
BhP te sampratītasmṛtayaḥ samutthāya jalāntikāt
BhP āsan suvismitāḥ sarve vīkṣamāṇāḥ parasparam
BhP anvamaṃsata tad rājan govindānugrahekṣitam
BhP pītvā viṣaṃ paretasya punar utthānam ātmanaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP vilokya dūṣitāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇāhinā vibhuḥ
BhP tasyā viśuddhim anvicchan sarpaṃ tam udavāsayat
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP katham antarjale 'gādhe nyagṛhṇād bhagavān ahim
BhP sa vai bahuyugāvāsaṃ yathāsīd vipra kathyatām
BhP brahman bhagavatas tasya bhūmnaḥ svacchandavartinaḥ
BhP gopālodāracaritaṃ kas tṛpyetāmṛtaṃ juṣan
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP kālindyāṃ kāliyasyāsīd hradaḥ kaścid viṣāgninā
BhP śrapyamāṇapayā yasmin patanty uparigāḥ khagāḥ
BhP vipruṣmatā viṣadormi mārutenābhimarśitāḥ
BhP mriyante tīragā yasya prāṇinaḥ sthirajaṅgamāḥ
BhP taṃ caṇḍavegaviṣavīryam avekṣya tena
BhP duṣṭāṃ nadīṃ ca khalasaṃyamanāvatāraḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaḥ kadambam adhiruhya tato 'tituṅgam
BhP āsphoṭya gāḍharaśano nyapatad viṣode
BhP sarpahradaḥ puruṣasāranipātavega
BhP saṅkṣobhitoragaviṣocchvasitāmburāśiḥ
BhP paryak pluto viṣakaṣāyabibhīṣaṇormir
BhP dhāvan dhanuḥśatam anantabalasya kiṃ tat
BhP tasya hrade viharato bhujadaṇḍaghūrṇa
BhP vārghoṣam aṅga varavāraṇavikramasya
BhP āśrutya tat svasadanābhibhavaṃ nirīkṣya
BhP cakṣuḥśravāḥ samasarat tad amṛṣyamāṇaḥ
BhP taṃ prekṣaṇīyasukumāraghanāvadātaṃ
BhP śrīvatsapītavasanaṃ smitasundarāsyam
BhP krīḍantam apratibhayaṃ kamalodarāṅghriṃ
BhP sandaśya marmasu ruṣā bhujayā cachāda
BhP taṃ nāgabhogaparivītam adṛṣṭaceṣṭam
BhP ālokya tatpriyasakhāḥ paśupā bhṛśārtāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇe 'rpitātmasuhṛdarthakalatrakāmā
BhP duḥkhānuśokabhayamūḍhadhiyo nipetuḥ
BhP gāvo vṛṣā vatsataryaḥ krandamānāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇe nyastekṣaṇā bhītā rudantya iva tasthire
BhP atha vraje mahotpātās trividhā hy atidāruṇāḥ
BhP utpetur bhuvi divy ātmany āsannabhayaśaṃsinaḥ
BhP tān ālakṣya bhayodvignā gopā nandapurogamāḥ
BhP vinā rāmeṇa gāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ jñātvā cārayituṃ gatam
BhP tair durnimittair nidhanaṃ matvā prāptam atadvidaḥ
BhP tatprāṇās tanmanaskās te duḥkhaśokabhayāturāḥ
BhP ābālavṛddhavanitāḥ sarve 'ṅga paśuvṛttayaḥ
BhP nirjagmur gokulād dīnāḥ kṛṣṇadarśanalālasāḥ
BhP tāṃs tathā kātarān vīkṣya bhagavān mādhavo balaḥ
BhP prahasya kiñcin novāca prabhāvajño 'nujasya saḥ
BhP te 'nveṣamāṇā dayitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sūcitayā padaiḥ
BhP bhagavallakṣaṇair jagmuḥ padavyā yamunātaṭam
BhP te tatra tatrābjayavāṅkuśāśani dhvajopapannāni padāni viśpateḥ
BhP mārge gavām anyapadāntarāntare nirīkṣamāṇā yayur aṅga satvarāḥ
BhP antar hrade bhujagabhogaparītam ārāt
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ nirīham upalabhya jalāśayānte
BhP gopāṃś ca mūḍhadhiṣaṇān paritaḥ paśūṃś ca
BhP saṅkrandataḥ paramakaśmalam āpur ārtāḥ
BhP gopyo 'nuraktamanaso bhagavaty anante
BhP tatsauhṛdasmitavilokagiraḥ smarantyaḥ
BhP graste 'hinā priyatame bhṛśaduḥkhataptāḥ
BhP śūnyaṃ priyavyatihṛtaṃ dadṛśus trilokam
BhP tāḥ kṛṣṇamātaram apatyam anupraviṣṭāṃ
BhP tulyavyathāḥ samanugṛhya śucaḥ sravantyaḥ
BhP tās tā vrajapriyakathāḥ kathayantya āsan
BhP kṛṣṇānane 'rpitadṛśo mṛtakapratīkāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaprāṇān nirviśato nandādīn vīkṣya taṃ hradam
BhP pratyaṣedhat sa bhagavān rāmaḥ kṛṣṇānubhāvavit
BhP ittham svagokulam ananyagatiṃ nirīkṣya
BhP sastrīkumāram atiduḥkhitam ātmahetoḥ
BhP ājñāya martyapadavīm anuvartamānaḥ
BhP sthitvā muhūrtam udatiṣṭhad uraṅgabandhāt
BhP tatprathyamānavapuṣā vyathitātmabhogas
BhP tyaktvonnamayya kupitaḥ svaphaṇān bhujaṅgaḥ
BhP tasthau śvasañ chvasanarandhraviṣāmbarīṣa
BhP stabdhekṣaṇolmukamukho harim īkṣamāṇaḥ
BhP taṃ jihvayā dviśikhayā parilelihānaṃ
BhP dve sṛkvaṇī hy atikarālaviṣāgnidṛṣṭim
BhP krīḍann amuṃ parisasāra yathā khagendro
BhP babhrāma so 'py avasaraṃ prasamīkṣamāṇaḥ
BhP evaṃ paribhramahataujasam unnatāṃsam
BhP ānamya tatpṛthuśiraḥsv adhirūḍha ādyaḥ
BhP tanmūrdharatnanikarasparśātitāmra
BhP pādāmbujo 'khilakalādigurur nanarta
BhP taṃ nartum udyatam avekṣya tadā tadīya
BhP gandharvasiddhamunicāraṇadevavadhvaḥ
BhP prītyā mṛdaṅgapaṇavānakavādyagīta
BhP puṣpopahāranutibhiḥ sahasopaseduḥ
BhP yad yac chiro na namate 'ṅga śataikaśīrṣṇas
BhP tat tan mamarda kharadaṇḍadharo 'ṅghripātaiḥ
BhP kṣīṇāyuṣo bhramata ulbaṇam āsyato 'sṛṅ
BhP nasto vaman paramakaśmalam āpa nāgaḥ
BhP tasyākṣibhir garalam udvamataḥ śiraḥsu
BhP yad yat samunnamati niḥśvasato ruṣoccaiḥ
BhP nṛtyan padānunamayan damayāṃ babhūva
BhP puṣpaiḥ prapūjita iveha pumān purāṇaḥ
BhP taccitratāṇḍavavirugnaphaṇāsahasro
BhP raktaṃ mukhair uru vaman nṛpa bhagnagātraḥ
BhP smṛtvā carācaraguruṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ
BhP nārāyaṇaṃ tam araṇaṃ manasā jagāma
BhP kṛṣṇasya garbhajagato 'tibharāvasannaṃ
BhP pārṣṇiprahāraparirugnaphaṇātapatram
BhP dṛṣṭvāhim ādyam upasedur amuṣya patnya
BhP ārtāḥ ślathadvasanabhūṣaṇakeśabandhāḥ
BhP tās taṃ suvignamanaso 'tha puraskṛtārbhāḥ
BhP kāyaṃ nidhāya bhuvi bhūtapatiṃ praṇemuḥ
BhP sādhvyaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ śamalasya bhartur
BhP mokṣepsavaḥ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannāḥ
BhP nāgapatnya ūcuḥ
BhP nyāyyo hi daṇḍaḥ kṛtakilbiṣe 'smiṃs
BhP tavāvatāraḥ khalanigrahāya
BhP ripoḥ sutānām api tulyadṛṣṭir
BhP dhatse damaṃ phalam evānuśaṃsan
BhP anugraho 'yaṃ bhavataḥ kṛto hi no daṇḍo 'satāṃ te khalu kalmaṣāpahaḥ
BhP yad dandaśūkatvam amuṣya dehinaḥ krodho 'pi te 'nugraha eva sammataḥ
BhP tapaḥ sutaptaṃ kim anena pūrvaṃ nirastamānena ca mānadena
BhP dharmo 'tha vā sarvajanānukampayā yato bhavāṃs tuṣyati sarvajīvaḥ
BhP kasyānubhāvo 'sya na deva vidmahe tavāṅghrireṇusparaśādhikāraḥ
BhP yadvāñchayā śrīr lalanācarat tapo vihāya kāmān suciraṃ dhṛtavratā
BhP na nākapṛṣṭhaṃ na ca sārvabhaumaṃ
BhP na pārameṣṭhyaṃ na rasādhipatyam
BhP na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vā
BhP vāñchanti yatpādarajaḥprapannāḥ
BhP tad eṣa nāthāpa durāpam anyais tamojaniḥ krodhavaśo 'py ahīśaḥ
BhP saṃsāracakre bhramataḥ śarīriṇo yadicchataḥ syād vibhavaḥ samakṣaḥ
BhP namas tubhyaṃ bhagavate puruṣāya mahātmane
BhP bhūtāvāsāya bhūtāya parāya paramātmane
BhP jñānavijñānanīdhaye brahmaṇe 'nantaśaktaye
BhP aguṇāyāvikārāya namas te prākṛtāya ca
BhP kālāya kālanābhāya kālāvayavasākṣiṇe
BhP viśvāya tadupadraṣṭre tatkartre viśvahetave
BhP bhūtamātrendriyaprāṇa manobuddhyāśayātmane
BhP triguṇenābhimānena gūḍhasvātmānubhūtaye
BhP namo 'nantāya sūkṣmāya kūṭasthāya vipaścite
BhP nānāvādānurodhāya vācyavācakaśaktaye
BhP namaḥ pramāṇamūlāya kavaye śāstrayonaye
BhP pravṛttāya nivṛttāya nigamāya namo namaḥ
BhP namaḥ kṛṣṇāya rāmāya vasudevasutāya ca
BhP pradyumnāyāniruddhāya sātvatāṃ pataye namaḥ
BhP namo guṇapradīpāya guṇātmacchādanāya ca
BhP guṇavṛttyupalakṣyāya guṇadraṣṭre svasaṃvide
BhP avyākṛtavihārāya sarvavyākṛtasiddhaye
BhP hṛṣīkeśa namas te 'stu munaye maunaśīline
BhP parāvaragatijñāya sarvādhyakṣāya te namaḥ
BhP aviśvāya ca viśvāya taddraṣṭre 'sya ca hetave
BhP tvaṃ hy asya janmasthitisaṃyamān vibho
BhP guṇair anīho 'kṛtakālaśaktidhṛk
BhP tattatsvabhāvān pratibodhayan sataḥ
BhP samīkṣayāmoghavihāra īhase
BhP tasyaiva te 'mūs tanavas trilokyāṃ
BhP śāntā aśāntā uta mūḍhayonayaḥ
BhP śāntāḥ priyās te hy adhunāvituṃ satāṃ
BhP sthātuś ca te dharmaparīpsayehataḥ
BhP aparādhaḥ sakṛd bhartrā soḍhavyaḥ svaprajākṛtaḥ
BhP kṣantum arhasi śāntātman mūḍhasya tvām ajānataḥ
BhP anugṛhṇīṣva bhagavan prāṇāṃs tyajati pannagaḥ
BhP strīṇāṃ naḥ sādhuśocyānāṃ patiḥ prāṇaḥ pradīyatām
BhP vidhehi te kiṅkarīṇām anuṣṭheyaṃ tavājñayā
BhP yacchraddhayānutiṣṭhan vai mucyate sarvato bhayāt
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itthaṃ sa nāgapatnībhir bhagavān samabhiṣṭutaḥ
BhP mūrcchitaṃ bhagnaśirasaṃ visasarjāṅghrikuṭṭanaiḥ
BhP pratilabdhendriyaprāṇaḥ kāliyaḥ śanakair harim
BhP kṛcchrāt samucchvasan dīnaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ prāha kṛtāñjaliḥ
BhP kāliya uvāca
BhP vayaṃ khalāḥ sahotpattyā tamasā dīrghamanyavaḥ
BhP svabhāvo dustyajo nātha lokānāṃ yad asadgrahaḥ
BhP tvayā sṛṣṭam idaṃ viśvaṃ dhātar guṇavisarjanam
BhP nānāsvabhāvavīryaujo yonibījāśayākṛti
BhP vayaṃ ca tatra bhagavan sarpā jātyurumanyavaḥ
BhP kathaṃ tyajāmas tvanmāyāṃ dustyajāṃ mohitāḥ svayam
BhP bhavān hi kāraṇaṃ tatra sarvajño jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP anugrahaṃ nigrahaṃ vā manyase tad vidhehi naḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity ākarṇya vacaḥ prāha bhagavān kāryamānuṣaḥ
BhP nātra stheyaṃ tvayā sarpa samudraṃ yāhi mā ciram
BhP svajñātyapatyadārāḍhyo gonṛbhir bhujyate nadī
BhP ya etat saṃsmaren martyas tubhyaṃ madanuśāsanam
BhP kīrtayann ubhayoḥ sandhyor na yuṣmad bhayam āpnuyāt
BhP yo 'smin snātvā madākrīḍe devādīṃs tarpayej jalaiḥ
BhP upoṣya māṃ smarann arcet sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
BhP dvīpaṃ ramaṇakaṃ hitvā hradam etam upāśritaḥ
BhP yadbhayāt sa suparṇas tvāṃ nādyān matpādalāñchitam
BhP śrīṛṣir uvāca
BhP mukto bhagavatā rājan kṛṣṇenādbhutakarmaṇā
BhP taṃ pūjayām āsa mudā nāgapatnyaś ca sādaram
BhP divyāmbarasraṅmaṇibhiḥ parārdhyair api bhūṣaṇaiḥ
BhP divyagandhānulepaiś ca mahatyotpalamālayā
BhP pūjayitvā jagannāthaṃ prasādya garuḍadhvajam
BhP tataḥ prīto 'bhyanujñātaḥ parikramyābhivandya tam
BhP sakalatrasuhṛtputro dvīpam abdher jagāma ha
BhP tadaiva sāmṛtajalā yamunā nirviṣābhavat
BhP anugrahād bhagavataḥ krīḍāmānuṣarūpiṇaḥ
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP nāgālayaṃ ramaṇakaṃ kathaṃ tatyāja kāliyaḥ
BhP kṛtaṃ kiṃ vā suparṇasya tenaikenāsamañjasam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP upahāryaiḥ sarpajanair māsi māsīha yo baliḥ
BhP vānaspatyo mahābāho nāgānāṃ prāṅnirūpitaḥ
BhP svaṃ svaṃ bhāgaṃ prayacchanti nāgāḥ parvaṇi parvaṇi
BhP gopīthāyātmanaḥ sarve suparṇāya mahātmane
BhP viṣavīryamadāviṣṭaḥ kādraveyas tu kāliyaḥ
BhP kadarthīkṛtya garuḍaṃ svayaṃ taṃ bubhuje balim
BhP tac chrutvā kupito rājan bhagavān bhagavatpriyaḥ
BhP vijighāṃsur mahāvegaḥ kāliyaṃ samapādravat
BhP tam āpatantaṃ tarasā viṣāyudhaḥ pratyabhyayād utthitanaikamastakaḥ
BhP dadbhiḥ suparṇaṃ vyadaśad dadāyudhaḥ karālajihrocchvasitogralocanaḥ
BhP taṃ tārkṣyaputraḥ sa nirasya manyumān
BhP pracaṇḍavego madhusūdanāsanaḥ
BhP pakṣeṇa savyena hiraṇyarociṣā
BhP jaghāna kadrusutam ugravikramaḥ
BhP suparṇapakṣābhihataḥ kāliyo 'tīva vihvalaḥ
BhP hradaṃ viveśa kālindyās tadagamyaṃ durāsadam
BhP tatraikadā jalacaraṃ garuḍo bhakṣyam īpsitam
BhP nivāritaḥ saubhariṇā prasahya kṣudhito 'harat
BhP mīnān suduḥkhitān dṛṣṭvā dīnān mīnapatau hate
BhP kṛpayā saubhariḥ prāha tatratyakṣemam ācaran
BhP atra praviśya garuḍo yadi matsyān sa khādati
BhP sadyaḥ prāṇair viyujyeta satyam etad bravīmy aham
BhP tat kāliyaḥ paraṃ veda nānyaḥ kaścana lelihaḥ
BhP avātsīd garuḍād bhītaḥ kṛṣṇena ca vivāsitaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ hradād viniṣkrāntaṃ divyasraggandhavāsasam
BhP mahāmaṇigaṇākīrṇaṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtam
BhP upalabhyotthitāḥ sarve labdhaprāṇā ivāsavaḥ
BhP pramodanibhṛtātmāno gopāḥ prītyābhirebhire
BhP yaśodā rohiṇī nando gopyo gopāś ca kaurava
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ sametya labdhehā āsan śuṣkā nagā api
BhP rāmaś cācyutam āliṅgya jahāsāsyānubhāvavit
BhP premṇā tam aṅkam āropya punaḥ punar udaikṣata
BhP gāvo vṛṣā vatsataryo lebhire paramāṃ mudam
BhP nandaṃ viprāḥ samāgatya guravaḥ sakalatrakāḥ
BhP ūcus te kāliyagrasto diṣṭyā muktas tavātmajaḥ
BhP dehi dānaṃ dvijātīnāṃ kṛṣṇanirmuktihetave
BhP nandaḥ prītamanā rājan gāḥ suvarṇaṃ tadādiśat
BhP yaśodāpi mahābhāgā naṣṭalabdhaprajā satī
BhP pariṣvajyāṅkam āropya mumocāśrukalāṃ muhuḥ
BhP tāṃ rātriṃ tatra rājendra kṣuttṛḍbhyāṃ śramakarṣitāḥ
BhP ūṣur vrayaukaso gāvaḥ kālindyā upakūlataḥ
BhP tadā śucivanodbhūto dāvāgniḥ sarvato vrajam
BhP suptaṃ niśītha āvṛtya pradagdhum upacakrame
BhP tata utthāya sambhrāntā dahyamānā vrajaukasaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ yayus te śaraṇaṃ māyāmanujam īśvaram
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahābhaga he rāmāmitavikrama
BhP eṣa ghoratamo vahnis tāvakān grasate hi naḥ
BhP sudustarān naḥ svān pāhi kālāgneḥ suhṛdaḥ prabho
BhP na śaknumas tvaccaraṇaṃ santyaktum akutobhayam
BhP itthaṃ svajanavaiklavyaṃ nirīkṣya jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP tam agnim apibat tīvram ananto 'nantaśaktidhṛk
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP atha kṛṣṇaḥ parivṛto jñātibhir muditātmabhiḥ
BhP anugīyamāno nyaviśad vrajaṃ gokulamaṇḍitam
BhP vraje vikrīḍator evaṃ gopālacchadmamāyayā
BhP grīṣmo nāmartur abhavan nātipreyāñ charīriṇām
BhP sa ca vṛndāvanaguṇair vasanta iva lakṣitaḥ
BhP yatrāste bhagavān sākṣād rāmeṇa saha keśavaḥ
BhP yatra nirjharanirhrāda nivṛttasvanajhillikam
BhP śaśvat tacchīkararjīṣa drumamaṇḍalamaṇḍitam
BhP saritsaraḥprasravaṇormivāyunā kahlārakañjotpalareṇuhāriṇā
BhP na vidyate yatra vanaukasāṃ davo nidāghavahnyarkabhavo 'tiśādvale
BhP agādhatoyahradinītaṭormibhir dravatpurīṣyāḥ pulinaiḥ samantataḥ
BhP na yatra caṇḍāṃśukarā viṣolbaṇā bhuvo rasaṃ śādvalitaṃ ca gṛhṇate
BhP vanaṃ kusumitaṃ śrīman nadaccitramṛgadvijam
BhP gāyan mayūrabhramaraṃ kūjatkokilasārasam
BhP krīḍiṣyamāṇas tat krṣṇo bhagavān balasaṃyutaḥ
BhP veṇuṃ viraṇayan gopair godhanaiḥ saṃvṛto 'viśat
BhP pravālabarhastabaka sragdhātukṛtabhūṣaṇāḥ
BhP rāmakṛṣṇādayo gopā nanṛtur yuyudhur jaguḥ
BhP kṛṣṇasya nṛtyataḥ kecij jaguḥ kecid avādayan
BhP veṇupāṇitalaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ praśaśaṃsur athāpare
BhP gopajātipraticchannā devā gopālarūpiṇau
BhP īḍire kṛṣṇarāmau ca naṭā iva naṭaṃ nṛpa
BhP bhramaṇair laṅghanaiḥ kṣepair āsphoṭanavikarṣaṇaiḥ
BhP cikrīḍatur niyuddhena kākapakṣadharau kvacit
BhP kvacin nṛtyatsu cānyeṣu gāyakau vādakau svayam
BhP śaśaṃsatur mahārāja sādhu sādhv iti vādinau
BhP kvacid bilvaiḥ kvacit kumbhaiḥ kvacāmalakamuṣṭibhiḥ
BhP aspṛśyanetrabandhādyaiḥ kvacin mṛgakhagehayā
BhP kvacic ca darduraplāvair vividhair upahāsakaiḥ
BhP kadācit syandolikayā karhicin nṛpaceṣṭayā
BhP evaṃ tau lokasiddhābhiḥ krīḍābhiś ceratur vane
BhP nadyadridroṇikuñjeṣu kānaneṣu saraḥsu ca
BhP paśūṃś cārayator gopais tadvane rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP goparūpī pralambo 'gād asuras tajjihīrṣayā
BhP taṃ vidvān api dāśārho bhagavān sarvadarśanaḥ
BhP anvamodata tatsakhyaṃ vadhaṃ tasya vicintayan
BhP tatropāhūya gopālān kṛṣṇaḥ prāha vihāravit
BhP he gopā vihariṣyāmo dvandvībhūya yathāyatham
BhP tatra cakruḥ parivṛḍhau gopā rāmajanārdanau
BhP kṛṣṇasaṅghaṭṭinaḥ kecid āsan rāmasya cāpare
BhP ācerur vividhāḥ krīḍā vāhyavāhakalakṣaṇāḥ
BhP yatrārohanti jetāro vahanti ca parājitāḥ
BhP vahanto vāhyamānāś ca cārayantaś ca godhanam
BhP bhāṇḍīrakaṃ nāma vaṭaṃ jagmuḥ kṛṣṇapurogamāḥ
BhP rāmasaṅghaṭṭino yarhi śrīdāmavṛṣabhādayaḥ
BhP krīḍāyāṃ jayinas tāṃs tān ūhuḥ kṛṣṇādayo nṛpa
BhP uvāha kṛṣṇo bhagavān śrīdāmānaṃ parājitaḥ
BhP vṛṣabhaṃ bhadrasenas tu pralambo rohiṇīsutam
BhP aviṣahyaṃ manyamānaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ dānavapuṅgavaḥ
BhP vahan drutataraṃ prāgād avarohaṇataḥ param
BhP tam udvahan dharaṇidharendragauravaṃ
BhP mahāsuro vigatarayo nijaṃ vapuḥ
BhP sa āsthitaḥ puraṭaparicchado babhau
BhP taḍiddyumān uḍupativāḍ ivāmbudaḥ
BhP nirīkṣya tadvapur alam ambare carat
BhP pradīptadṛg bhrukuṭitaṭogradaṃṣṭrakam
BhP jvalacchikhaṃ kaṭakakirīṭakuṇḍala
BhP tviṣādbhutaṃ haladhara īṣad atrasat
BhP athāgatasmṛtir abhayo ripuṃ balo vihāya sārtham iva harantam ātmanaḥ
BhP ruṣāhanac chirasi dṛḍhena muṣṭinā surādhipo girim iva vajraraṃhasā
BhP sa āhataḥ sapadi viśīrṇamastako mukhād vaman rudhiram apasmṛto 'suraḥ
BhP mahāravaṃ vyasur apatat samīrayan girir yathā maghavata āyudhāhataḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā pralambaṃ nihataṃ balena balaśālinā
BhP gopāḥ suvismitā āsan sādhu sādhv iti vādinaḥ
BhP āśiṣo 'bhigṛṇantas taṃ praśaśaṃsus tadarhaṇam
BhP pretyāgatam ivāliṅgya premavihvalacetasaḥ
BhP pāpe pralambe nihate devāḥ paramanirvṛtāḥ
BhP abhyavarṣan balaṃ mālyaiḥ śaśaṃsuḥ sādhu sādhv iti
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP krīḍāsakteṣu gopeṣu tadgāvo dūracāriṇīḥ
BhP svairaṃ carantyo viviśus tṛṇalobhena gahvaram
BhP ajā gāvo mahiṣyaś ca nirviśantyo vanād vanam
BhP īṣīkāṭavīṃ nirviviśuḥ krandantyo dāvatarṣitāḥ
BhP te 'paśyantaḥ paśūn gopāḥ kṛṣṇarāmādayas tadā
BhP jātānutāpā na vidur vicinvanto gavāṃ gatim
BhP tṛṇais tatkhuradacchinnair goṣpadair aṅkitair gavām
BhP mārgam anvagaman sarve naṣṭājīvyā vicetasaḥ
BhP muñjāṭavyāṃ bhraṣṭamārgaṃ krandamānaṃ svagodhanam
BhP samprāpya tṛṣitāḥ śrāntās tatas te sannyavartayan
BhP tā āhūtā bhagavatā meghagambhīrayā girā
BhP svanāmnāṃ ninadaṃ śrutvā pratineduḥ praharṣitāḥ
BhP tataḥ samantād davadhūmaketur yadṛcchayābhūt kṣayakṛd vanaukasām
BhP samīritaḥ sārathinolbaṇolmukair vilelihānaḥ sthirajaṅgamān mahān
BhP tam āpatantaṃ parito davāgniṃ gopāś ca gāvaḥ prasamīkṣya bhītāḥ
BhP ūcuś ca kṛṣṇaṃ sabalaṃ prapannā yathā hariṃ mṛtyubhayārditā janāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahāvīra he rāmāmogha vikrama
BhP dāvāgninā dahyamānān prapannāṃs trātum arhathaḥ
BhP nūnaṃ tvadbāndhavāḥ kṛṣṇa na cārhanty avasāditum
BhP vayaṃ hi sarvadharmajña tvannāthās tvatparāyaṇāḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP vaco niśamya kṛpaṇaṃ bandhūnāṃ bhagavān hariḥ
BhP nimīlayata mā bhaiṣṭa locanānīty abhāṣata
BhP tatheti mīlitākṣeṣu bhagavān agnim ulbaṇam
BhP pītvā mukhena tān kṛcchrād yogādhīśo vyamocayat
BhP tataś ca te 'kṣīṇy unmīlya punar bhāṇḍīram āpitāḥ
BhP niśamya vismitā āsann ātmānaṃ gāś ca mocitāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇasya yogavīryaṃ tad yogamāyānubhāvitam
BhP dāvāgner ātmanaḥ kṣemaṃ vīkṣya te menire 'maram
BhP gāḥ sannivartya sāyāhne saharāmo janārdanaḥ
BhP veṇuṃ viraṇayan goṣṭham agād gopair abhiṣṭutaḥ
BhP gopīnāṃ paramānanda āsīd govindadarśane

BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP tayos tad adbhutaṃ karma dāvāgner mokṣam ātmanaḥ
BhP gopāḥ strībhyaḥ samācakhyuḥ pralambavadham eva ca
BhP gopavṛddhāś ca gopyaś ca tad upākarṇya vismitāḥ
BhP menire devapravarau kṛṣṇarāmau vrajaṃ gatau
BhP tataḥ prāvartata prāvṛṭ sarvasattvasamudbhavā
BhP vidyotamānaparidhir visphūrjitanabhastalā
BhP sāndranīlāmbudair vyoma savidyutstanayitnubhiḥ
BhP aspaṣṭajyotir ācchannaṃ brahmeva saguṇaṃ babhau
BhP aṣṭau māsān nipītaṃ yad bhūmyāś codamayaṃ vasu
BhP svagobhir moktum ārebhe parjanyaḥ kāla āgate
BhP taḍidvanto mahāmeghāś caṇḍa śvasana vepitāḥ
BhP prīṇanaṃ jīvanaṃ hy asya mumucuḥ karuṇā iva
BhP tapaḥkṛśā devamīḍhā āsīd varṣīyasī mahī
BhP yathaiva kāmyatapasas tanuḥ samprāpya tatphalam
BhP niśāmukheṣu khadyotās tamasā bhānti na grahāḥ
BhP yathā pāpena pāṣaṇḍā na hi vedāḥ kalau yuge
BhP śrutvā parjanyaninadaṃ maṇḍukāḥ sasṛjur giraḥ
BhP tūṣṇīṃ śayānāḥ prāg yadvad brāhmaṇā niyamātyaye
BhP āsann utpathagāminyaḥ kṣudranadyo 'nuśuṣyatīḥ
BhP puṃso yathāsvatantrasya dehadraviṇa sampadaḥ
BhP haritā haribhiḥ śaṣpair indragopaiś ca lohitā

BhP māninām anutāpaṃ vai daivādhīnam ajānatām
BhP jalasthalaukasaḥ sarve navavāriniṣevayā

BhP abhibhūyamānā vyasanair yathādhokṣajacetasaḥ
BhP mārgā babhūvuḥ sandigdhās tṛṇaiś channā hy asaṃskṛtāḥ
BhP nābhyasyamānāḥ śrutayo dvijaiḥ kālena cāhatāḥ
BhP lokabandhuṣu megheṣu vidyutaś calasauhṛdāḥ
BhP sthairyaṃ na cakruḥ kāminyaḥ puruṣeṣu guṇiṣv iva
BhP dhanur viyati māhendraṃ nirguṇaṃ ca guṇiny abhāt
BhP vyakte guṇavyatikare 'guṇavān puruṣo yathā
BhP na rarājoḍupaś channaḥ svajyotsnārājitair ghanaiḥ
BhP ahaṃmatyā bhāsitayā svabhāsā puruṣo yathā
BhP meghāgamotsavā hṛṣṭāḥ pratyanandañ chikhaṇḍinaḥ
BhP gṛheṣu taptanirviṇṇā yathācyutajanāgame
BhP pītvāpaḥ pādapāḥ padbhir āsan nānātmamūrtayaḥ
BhP prāk kṣāmās tapasā śrāntā yathā kāmānusevayā
BhP saraḥsv aśāntarodhaḥsu nyūṣur aṅgāpi sārasāḥ
BhP gṛheṣv aśāntakṛtyeṣu grāmyā iva durāśayāḥ
BhP jalaughair nirabhidyanta setavo varṣatīśvare
BhP pāṣaṇḍinām asadvādair vedamārgāḥ kalau yathā
BhP vyamuñcan vāyubhir nunnā bhūtebhyaś cāmṛtaṃ ghanāḥ
BhP yathāśiṣo viśpatayaḥ kāle kāle dvijeritāḥ
BhP evaṃ vanaṃ tad varṣiṣṭhaṃ pakvakharjurajambumat
BhP gogopālair vṛto rantuṃ sabalaḥ prāviśad dhariḥ
BhP dhenavo mandagāminya ūdhobhāreṇa bhūyasā
BhP yayur bhagavatāhūtā drutaṃ prītyā snutastanāḥ
BhP vanaukasaḥ pramuditā vanarājīr madhucyutaḥ
BhP jaladhārā girer nādād āsannā dadṛśe guhāḥ
BhP kvacid vanaspatikroḍe guhāyāṃ cābhivarṣati
BhP nirviśya bhagavān reme kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ
BhP dadhyodanaṃ samānītaṃ śilāyāṃ salilāntike

BhP śādvalopari saṃviśya carvato mīlitekṣaṇān
BhP tṛptān vṛṣān vatsatarān gāś ca svodhobharaśramāḥ
BhP prāvṛṭśriyaṃ ca tāṃ vīkṣya sarvakālasukhāvahām
BhP bhagavān pūjayāṃ cakre ātmaśaktyupabṛṃhitām
BhP evaṃ nivasatos tasmin rāmakeśavayor vraje
BhP śarat samabhavad vyabhrā svacchāmbvaparuṣānilā
BhP śaradā nīrajotpattyā nīrāṇi prakṛtiṃ yayuḥ
BhP bhraṣṭānām iva cetāṃsi punar yoganiṣevayā
BhP vyomno 'bbhraṃ bhūtaśābalyaṃ bhuvaḥ paṅkam apāṃ malam
BhP śaraj jahārāśramiṇāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktir yathāśubham
BhP sarvasvaṃ jaladā hitvā virejuḥ śubhravarcasaḥ
BhP yathā tyaktaiṣaṇāḥ śāntā munayo muktakilbiṣāḥ
BhP girayo mumucus toyaṃ kvacin na mumucuḥ śivam
BhP yathā jñānāmṛtaṃ kāle jñānino dadate na vā
BhP naivāvidan kṣīyamāṇaṃ jalaṃ gādhajalecarāḥ
BhP yathāyur anvahaṃ kṣayyaṃ narā mūḍhāḥ kuṭumbinaḥ
BhP gādhavāricarās tāpam avindañ charadarkajam
BhP yathā daridraḥ kṛpaṇaḥ kuṭumby avijitendriyaḥ
BhP śanaiḥ śanair jahuḥ paṅkaṃ sthalāny āmaṃ ca vīrudhaḥ
BhP yathāhaṃmamatāṃ dhīrāḥ śarīrādiṣv anātmasu
BhP niścalāmbur abhūt tūṣṇīṃ samudraḥ śaradāgame
BhP ātmany uparate samyaṅ munir vyuparatāgamaḥ
BhP kedārebhyas tv apo 'gṛhṇan karṣakā dṛḍhasetubhiḥ
BhP yathā prāṇaiḥ sravaj jñānaṃ tannirodhena yoginaḥ
BhP śaradarkāṃśujāṃs tāpān bhūtānām uḍupo 'harat
BhP dehābhimānajaṃ bodho mukundo vrajayoṣitām
BhP kham aśobhata nirmeghaṃ śaradvimalatārakam
BhP sattvayuktaṃ yathā cittaṃ śabdabrahmārthadarśanam

BhP yathā yadupatiḥ kṛṣṇo vṛṣṇicakrāvṛto bhuvi
BhP āśliṣya samaśītoṣṇaṃ prasūnavanamārutam
BhP janās tāpaṃ jahur gopyo na kṛṣṇahṛtacetasaḥ
BhP gāvo mṛgāḥ khagā nāryaḥ puṣpiṇyaḥ śaradābhavan
BhP anvīyamānāḥ svavṛṣaiḥ phalair īśakriyā iva
BhP udahṛṣyan vārijāni sūryotthāne kumud vinā
BhP rājñā tu nirbhayā lokā yathā dasyūn vinā nṛpa

BhP babhau bhūḥ pakvaśaṣyāḍhyā kalābhyāṃ nitarāṃ hareḥ
BhP vaṇiṅmuninṛpasnātā nirgamyārthān prapedire

BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itthaṃ śaratsvacchajalaṃ padmākarasugandhinā

BhP kāścit parokṣaṃ kṛṣṇasya svasakhībhyo 'nvavarṇayan

BhP nāśakan smaravegena vikṣiptamanaso nṛpa
BhP barhāpīḍaṃ naṭavaravapuḥ karṇayoḥ karṇikāraṃ
BhP bibhrad vāsaḥ kanakakapiśaṃ vaijayantīṃ ca mālām

BhP śrīgopya ūcuḥ
BhP akṣaṇvatāṃ phalam idaṃ na paraṃ vidāmaḥ
BhP sakhyaḥ paśūn anaviveśayator vayasyaiḥ
BhP vaktraṃ vrajeśasutayor anaveṇujuṣṭaṃ

BhP gopyaḥ kim ācarad ayaṃ kuśalaṃ sma veṇur

BhP bhuṅkte svayaṃ yad avaśiṣṭarasaṃ hradinyo

BhP vṛndāvanaṃ sakhi bhuvo vitanoti kīṛtiṃ
BhP yad devakīsutapadāmbujalabdhalakṣmi
BhP govindaveṇum anu mattamayūranṛtyaṃ
BhP prekṣyādrisānvavaratānyasamastasattvam
BhP dhanyāḥ sma mūḍhagatayo 'pi hariṇya etā
BhP yā nandanandanam upāttavicitraveśam
BhP ākarṇya veṇuraṇitaṃ sahakṛṣṇasārāḥ
BhP pūjāṃ dadhur viracitāṃ praṇayāvalokaiḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ nirīkṣya vanitotsavarūpaśīlaṃ
BhP śrutvā ca tatkvaṇitaveṇuviviktagītam
BhP devyo vimānagatayaḥ smaranunnasārā
BhP bhraśyatprasūnakabarā mumuhur vinīvyaḥ
BhP gāvaś ca kṛṣṇamukhanirgataveṇugīta
BhP pīyūṣam uttabhitakarṇapuṭaiḥ pibantyaḥ
BhP śāvāḥ snutastanapayaḥkavalāḥ sma tasthur
BhP govindam ātmani dṛśāśrukalāḥ spṛśantyaḥ
BhP prāyo batāmba vihagā munayo vane 'smin
BhP kṛṣṇekṣitaṃ taduditaṃ kalaveṇugītam
BhP āruhya ye drumabhujān rucirapravālān
BhP śṛṇvanti mīlitadṛśo vigatānyavācaḥ
BhP nadyas tadā tad upadhārya mukundagītam

BhP dṛṣṭvātape vrajapaśūn saha rāmagopaiḥ
BhP sañcārayantam anu veṇum udīrayantam

BhP sakhyur vyadhāt svavapuṣāmbuda ātapatram
BhP pūrṇāḥ pulindya urugāyapadābjarāga
BhP śrīkuṅkumena dayitāstanamaṇḍitena

BhP hantāyam adrir abalā haridāsavaryo

BhP mānaṃ tanoti sahagogaṇayos tayor yat

BhP gā gopakair anuvanaṃ nayator udāra
BhP veṇusvanaiḥ kalapadais tanubhṛtsu sakhyaḥ
BhP aspandanaṃ gatimatāṃ pulakas taruṇāṃ

BhP varṇayantyo mitho gopyaḥ krīḍās tanmayatāṃ yayuḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca

BhP cerur haviṣyaṃ bhuñjānāḥ kātyāyanyarcanavratam
BhP āplutyāmbhasi kālindyā jalānte codite 'ruṇe
BhP kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ devīm ānarcur nṛpa saikatīm
BhP gandhair mālyaiḥ surabhibhir balibhir dhūpadīpakaiḥ
BhP uccāvacaiś copahāraiḥ pravālaphalataṇḍulaiḥ
BhP kātyāyani mahāmāye mahāyoginy adhīśvari
BhP nandagopasutaṃ devi patiṃ me kuru te namaḥ
BhP iti mantraṃ japantyas tāḥ pūjāṃ cakruḥ kamārikāḥ
BhP evaṃ māsaṃ vrataṃ ceruḥ kumāryaḥ kṛṣṇacetasaḥ
BhP bhadrakālīṃ samānarcur bhūyān nandasutaḥ patiḥ
BhP ūṣasy utthāya gotraiḥ svair anyonyābaddhabāhavaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇam uccair jagur yāntyaḥ kālindyāṃ snātum anvaham
BhP nadyāḥ kadācid āgatya tīre nikṣipya pūrvavat
BhP vāsāṃsi kṛṣṇaṃ gāyantyo vijahruḥ salile mudā
BhP bhagavāṃs tad abhipretya kṛṣno yogeśvareśvaraḥ
BhP vayasyair āvṛtas tatra gatas tatkarmasiddhaye

BhP hasadbhiḥ prahasan bālaiḥ parihāsam uvāca ha
BhP atrāgatyābalāḥ kāmaṃ svaṃ svaṃ vāsaḥ pragṛhyatām
BhP satyaṃ bravāṇi no narma yad yūyaṃ vratakarśitāḥ
BhP na mayoditapūrvaṃ vā anṛtaṃ tad ime viduḥ
BhP ekaikaśaḥ pratīcchadhvaṃ sahaiveti sumadhyamāḥ
BhP tasya tat kṣvelitaṃ dṛṣṭvā gopyaḥ premapariplutāḥ
BhP vrīḍitāḥ prekṣya cānyonyaṃ jātahāsā na niryayuḥ
BhP evaṃ bruvati govinde narmaṇākṣiptacetasaḥ
BhP ākaṇṭhamagnāḥ śītode vepamānās tam abruvan
BhP mānayaṃ bhoḥ kṛthās tvāṃ tu nandagopasutaṃ priyam
BhP jānīmo 'ṅga vrajaślāghyaṃ dehi vāsāṃsi vepitāḥ
BhP śyāmasundara te dāsyaḥ karavāma tavoditam
BhP dehi vāsāṃsi dharmajña no ced rājñe bruvāma he
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP bhavatyo yadi me dāsyo mayoktaṃ vā kariṣyatha
BhP atrāgatya svavāsāṃsi pratīcchata śucismitāḥ
BhP no cen nāhaṃ pradāsye kiṃ kruddho rājā kariṣyati
BhP tato jalāśayāt sarvā dārikāḥ śītavepitāḥ
BhP pāṇibhyāṃ yonim ācchādya protteruḥ śītakarśitāḥ
BhP bhagavān āhatā vīkṣya śuddha bhāvaprasāditaḥ
BhP skandhe nidhāya vāsāṃsi prītaḥ provāca sasmitam
BhP yūyaṃ vivastrā yad apo dhṛtavratā vyagāhataitat tad u devahelanam
BhP baddhvāñjaliṃ mūrdhny apanuttaye 'ṃhasaḥ kṛtvā namo 'dhovasanaṃ pragṛhyatām
BhP ity acyutenābhihitaṃ vrajābalā matvā vivastrāplavanaṃ vratacyutim
BhP tatpūrtikāmās tadaśeṣakarmaṇāṃ sākṣātkṛtaṃ nemur avadyamṛg yataḥ
BhP tās tathāvanatā dṛṣṭvā bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP vāsāṃsi tābhyaḥ prāyacchat karuṇas tena toṣitaḥ
BhP dṛḍhaṃ pralabdhās trapayā ca hāpitāḥ
BhP prastobhitāḥ krīḍanavac ca kāritāḥ
BhP vastrāṇi caivāpahṛtāny athāpy amuṃ
BhP tā nābhyasūyan priyasaṅganirvṛtāḥ
BhP paridhāya svavāsāṃsi preṣṭhasaṅgamasajjitāḥ

BhP tāsāṃ vijñāya bhagavān svapādasparśakāmyayā

BhP saṅkalpo viditaḥ sādhvyo bhavatīnāṃ madarcanam
BhP mayānumoditaḥ so 'sau satyo bhavitum arhati
BhP na mayy āveśitadhiyāṃ kāmaḥ kāmāya kalpate

BhP yātābalā vrajaṃ siddhā mayemā raṃsyathā kṣapāḥ
BhP yad uddiśya vratam idaṃ cerur āryārcanaṃ satīḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity ādiṣṭā bhagavatā labdhakāmāḥ kumārikāḥ
BhP dhyāyantyas tatpadāmbhojam kṛcchrān nirviviśur vrajam
BhP atha gopaiḥ parivṛto bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP vṛndāvanād gato dūraṃ cārayan gāḥ sahāgrajaḥ
BhP nidaghārkātape tigme chāyābhiḥ svābhir ātmanaḥ
BhP ātapatrāyitān vīkṣya drumān āha vrajaukasaḥ
BhP he stokakṛṣṇa he aṃśo śrīdāman subalārjuna
BhP viśāla vṛṣabhaujasvin devaprastha varūthapa

BhP aho eṣāṃ varaṃ janma sarva prāṇyupajīvanam
BhP sujanasyeva yeṣāṃ vai vimukhā yānti nārthinaḥ

BhP śrīśuka uvāca

BhP prāptāñ jānīta bhadraṃ vo gopān no rāmacoditān

BhP dīkṣāyāḥ paśusaṃsthāyāḥ sautrāmaṇyāś ca sattamāḥ
BhP anyatra dīkṣitasyāpi nānnam aśnan hi duṣyati
BhP iti te bhagavadyācñāṃ śṛṇvanto 'pi na śuśruvuḥ
BhP kṣudrāśā bhūrikarmāṇo bāliśā vṛddhamāninaḥ
BhP deśaḥ kālaḥ pṛthag dravyaṃ mantratantrartvijo 'gnayaḥ
BhP devatā yajamānaś ca kratur dharmaś ca yanmayaḥ
BhP taṃ brahma paramaṃ sākṣād bhagavantam adhokṣajam

BhP na te yad om iti procur na neti ca parantapa
BhP gopā nirāśāḥ pratyetya tathocuḥ kṛṣṇarāmayoḥ
BhP tad upākarṇya bhagavān prahasya jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP vyājahāra punar gopān darśayan laukikīṃ gatim
BhP māṃ jñāpayata patnībhyaḥ sasaṅkarṣaṇam āgatam
