BhP tās tathā tyaktasarvāśāḥ prāptā ātmadidṛkṣayā
BhP vijñāyākhiladṛgdraṣṭā prāha prahasitānanaḥ
BhP svāgataṃ vo mahābhāgā āsyatāṃ karavāma kim
BhP yan no didṛkṣayā prāptā upapannam idaṃ hi vaḥ
BhP nanv addhā mayi kurvanti kuśalāḥ svārthadarśinaḥ
BhP ahaituky avyavahitāṃ bhaktim ātmapriye yathā
BhP prāṇabuddhimanaḥsvātma dārāpatyadhanādayaḥ
BhP yatsamparkāt priyā āsaṃs tataḥ ko nv aparaḥ priyaḥ
BhP tad yāta devayajanaṃ patayo vo dvijātayaḥ
BhP svasatraṃ pārayiṣyanti yuṣmābhir gṛhamedhinaḥ
BhP śrīpatnya ūcuḥ
BhP maivaṃ vibho 'rhati bhavān gadituṃ nrśaṃsaṃ
BhP satyaṃ kuruṣva nigamaṃ tava padamūlam
BhP prāptā vayaṃ tulasidāma padāvasṛṣṭaṃ
BhP keśair nivoḍhum atilaṅghya samastabandhūn
BhP gṛhṇanti no na patayaḥ pitarau sutā vā
BhP na bhrātṛbandhusuhṛdaḥ kuta eva cānye
BhP tasmād bhavatprapadayoḥ patitātmanāṃ no
BhP nānyā bhaved gatir arindama tad vidhehi
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP patayo nābhyasūyeran pitṛbhrātṛsutādayaḥ
BhP lokāś ca vo mayopetā devā apy anumanvate
BhP na prītaye 'nurāgāya hy aṅgasaṅgo nṛṇām iha
BhP tan mano mayi yuñjānā acirān mām avāpsyatha
BhP śravaṇād darśanād dhyānān mayi bhāvo 'nukīrtanāt
BhP na tathā sannikarṣeṇa pratiyāta tato gṛhān
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity uktā dvijapatnyas tā yajñavāṭaṃ punar gatāḥ
BhP te cānasūyavas tābhiḥ strībhiḥ satram apārayan
BhP tatraikā vidhṛtā bhartrā bhagavantaṃ yathāśrutam
BhP hṛḍopaguhya vijahau dehaṃ karmānubandhanam
BhP bhagavān api govindas tenaivānnena gopakān
BhP caturvidhenāśayitvā svayaṃ ca bubhuje prabhuḥ
BhP evaṃ līlānaravapur nrlokam anuśīlayan
BhP reme gogopagopīnāṃ ramayan rūpavākkṛtaiḥ
BhP athānusmṛtya viprās te anvatapyan kṛtāgasaḥ
BhP yad viśveśvarayor yācñām ahanma nṛviḍambayoḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā strīṇāṃ bhagavati kṛṣṇe bhaktim alaukikīm
BhP ātmānaṃ ca tayā hīnam anutaptā vyagarhayan
BhP dhig janma nas trivṛd yat tad dhig vrataṃ dhig bahujñatām
BhP dhik kulaṃ dhik kriyādākṣyaṃ vimukhā ye tv adhokṣaje
BhP nūnaṃ bhagavato māyā yoginām api mohinī
BhP yad vayaṃ guravo nṛṇāṃ svārthe muhyāmahe dvijāḥ
BhP aho paśyata nārīṇām api kṛṣṇe jagadgurau
BhP durantabhāvaṃ yo 'vidhyan mṛtyupāśān gṛhābhidhān
BhP nāsāṃ dvijātisaṃskāro na nivāso gurāv api
BhP na tapo nātmamīmāṃsā na śaucaṃ na kriyāḥ śubhāḥ
BhP tathāpi hy uttamaḥśloke kṛṣṇe yogeśvareśvare
BhP bhaktir dṛḍhā na cāsmākaṃ saṃskārādimatām api
BhP nanu svārthavimūḍhānāṃ pramattānāṃ gṛhehayā
BhP aho naḥ smārayām āsa gopavākyaiḥ satāṃ gatiḥ
BhP anyathā pūrṇakāmasya kaivalyādyaśiṣāṃ pateḥ
BhP īśitavyaiḥ kim asmābhir īśasyaitad viḍambanam
BhP hitvānyān bhajate yaṃ śrīḥ pādasparśāśayāsakṛt
BhP svātmadoṣāpavargeṇa tadyācñā janamohinī
BhP deśaḥ kālaḥ pṛthag dravyaṃ mantratantrartvijo 'gnayaḥ
BhP devatā yajamānaś ca kratur dharmaś ca yanmayaḥ
BhP sa eva bhagavān sākṣād viṣṇur yogeśvareśvaraḥ
BhP jāto yaduṣv ity āśṛṇma hy api mūḍhā na vidmahe
BhP tasmai namo bhagavate kṛṣṇāyākuṇṭhamedhase
BhP yanmāyāmohitadhiyo bhramāmaḥ karmavartmasu
BhP sa vai na ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ svamāyāmohitātmanām
BhP avijñatānubhāvānāṃ kṣantum arhaty atikramam
BhP iti svāgham anusmṛtya kṛṣṇe te kṛtahelanāḥ
BhP didṛkṣavo vrajam atha kaṃsād bhītā na cācalan
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP bhagavān api tatraiva baladevena saṃyutaḥ
BhP apaśyan nivasan gopān indrayāgakṛtodyamān
BhP tadabhijño 'pi bhagavān sarvātmā sarvadarśanaḥ
BhP praśrayāvanato 'pṛcchad vṛddhān nandapurogamān
BhP kathyatāṃ me pitaḥ ko 'yaṃ sambhramo va upāgataḥ
BhP kiṃ phalaṃ kasya voddeśaḥ kena vā sādhyate makhaḥ
BhP etad brūhi mahān kāmo mahyaṃ śuśrūṣave pitaḥ
BhP na hi gopyaṃ hi sadhūnāṃ kṛtyaṃ sarvātmanām iha
BhP asty asvaparadṛṣṭīnām amitrodāstavidviṣām
BhP udāsīno 'rivad varjya
BhP ātmavat suhṛd ucyate
BhP jñatvājñātvā ca karmāṇi jano 'yam anutiṣṭhati
BhP viduṣaḥ karmasiddhiḥ syād yathā nāviduṣo bhavet
BhP tatra tāvat kriyāyogo bhavatāṃ kiṃ vicāritaḥ
BhP atha vā laukikas tan me pṛcchataḥ sādhu bhaṇyatām
BhP śrīnanda uvāca
BhP parjanyo bhagavān indro meghās tasyātmamūrtayaḥ
BhP te 'bhivarṣanti bhūtānāṃ prīṇanaṃ jīvanaṃ payaḥ
BhP taṃ tāta vayam anye ca vārmucāṃ patim īśvaram
BhP dravyais tadretasā siddhair yajante kratubhir narāḥ
BhP taccheṣeṇopajīvanti trivargaphalahetave
BhP puṃsāṃ puruṣakārāṇāṃ parjanyaḥ phalabhāvanaḥ
BhP ya enaṃ visṛjed dharmaṃ paramparyāgataṃ naraḥ
BhP kāmād dveṣād bhayāl lobhāt sa vai nāpnoti śobhanam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP vaco niśamya nandasya tathānyeṣāṃ vrajaukasām
BhP indrāya manyuṃ janayan pitaraṃ prāha keśavaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP karmaṇā jāyate jantuḥ karmaṇaiva pralīyate
BhP sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhayaṃ kṣemaṃ karmaṇaivābhipadyate
BhP asti ced īśvaraḥ kaścit phalarūpy anyakarmaṇām
BhP kartāraṃ bhajate so 'pi na hy akartuḥ prabhur hi saḥ
BhP kim indreṇeha bhūtānāṃ svasvakarmānuvartinām
BhP anīśenānyathā kartuṃ svabhāvavihitaṃ nṛṇām
BhP svabhāvatantro hi janaḥ svabhāvam anuvartate
BhP svabhāvastham idaṃ sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam
BhP dehān uccāvacāñ jantuḥ prāpyotsṛjati karmaṇā
BhP śatrur mitram udāsīnaḥ karmaiva gurur īśvaraḥ
BhP tasmāt sampūjayet karma svabhāvasthaḥ svakarmakṛt
BhP anjasā yena varteta tad evāsya hi daivatam
BhP ājīvyaikataraṃ bhāvaṃ yas tv anyam upajīvati
BhP na tasmād vindate kṣemaṃ jārān nāry asatī yathā
BhP varteta brahmaṇā vipro rājanyo rakṣayā bhuvaḥ
BhP vaiśyas tu vārtayā jīvec chūdras tu dvijasevayā
BhP kṛṣivāṇijyagorakṣā kusīdaṃ tūryam ucyate
BhP vārtā caturvidhā tatra vayaṃ govṛttayo 'niśam
BhP sattvaṃ rajas tama iti sthityutpattyantahetavaḥ
BhP rajasotpadyate viśvam anyonyaṃ vividhaṃ jagat
BhP rajasā coditā meghā varṣanty ambūni sarvataḥ
BhP prajās tair eva sidhyanti mahendraḥ kiṃ kariṣyati
BhP na naḥ purojanapadā na grāmā na gṛhā vayam
BhP vanaukasas tāta nityaṃ vanaśailanivāsinaḥ
BhP tasmād gavāṃ brāhmaṇānām adreś cārabhyatāṃ makhaḥ
BhP ya indrayāgasambhārās tair ayaṃ sādhyatāṃ makhaḥ
BhP pacyantāṃ vividhāḥ pākāḥ sūpāntāḥ pāyasādayaḥ
BhP saṃyāvāpūpaśaṣkulyaḥ sarvadohaś ca gṛhyatām
BhP hūyantām agnayaḥ samyag brāhmaṇair brahmavādibhiḥ
BhP annaṃ bahuguṇaṃ tebhyo deyaṃ vo dhenudakṣiṇāḥ
BhP anyebhyaś cāśvacāṇḍāla patitebhyo yathārhataḥ
BhP yavasaṃ ca gavāṃ dattvā giraye dīyatāṃ baliḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtā bhuktavantaḥ svanuliptāḥ suvāsasaḥ
BhP pradakṣiṇāṃ ca kuruta goviprānalaparvatān
BhP etan mama mataṃ tāta kriyatāṃ yadi rocate
BhP ayaṃ gobrāhmaṇādrīṇāṃ mahyaṃ ca dayito makhaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP kālātmanā bhagavatā śakradarpajighāṃsayā
BhP proktaṃ niśamya nandādyāḥ sādhv agṛhṇanta tadvacaḥ
BhP tathā ca vyadadhuḥ sarvaṃ yathāha madhusūdanaḥ
BhP vācayitvā svastyayanaṃ taddravyeṇa giridvijān
BhP upahṛtya balīn samyag ādṛtā yavasaṃ gavām
BhP godhanāni puraskṛtya giriṃ cakruḥ pradakṣiṇam
BhP anāṃsy anaḍudyuktāni te cāruhya svalaṅkṛtāḥ
BhP gopyaś ca kṛṣṇavīryāṇi gāyantyaḥ sadvijāśiṣaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇas tv anyatamaṃ rūpaṃ gopaviśrambhaṇaṃ gataḥ
BhP śailo 'smīti bruvan bhūri balim ādad bṛhadvapuḥ
BhP tasmai namo vrajajanaiḥ saha cakra ātmanātmane
BhP aho paśyata śailo 'sau rūpī no 'nugrahaṃ vyadhāt
BhP eṣo 'vajānato martyān kāmarūpī vanaukasaḥ
BhP hanti hy asmai namasyāmaḥ śarmaṇe ātmano gavām
BhP ity adrigodvijamakhaṃ vāsudevapracoditāḥ
BhP yathā vidhāya te gopā sahakṛṣṇā vrajaṃ yayuḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP indras tadātmanaḥ pūjāṃ vijñāya vihatāṃ nṛpa
BhP gopebhyaḥ kṛṣṇanāthebhyo nandādibhyaś cukopa ha
BhP gaṇaṃ sāṃvartakaṃ nāma meghānāṃ cāntakārīṇām
BhP indraḥ pracodayat kruddho vākyaṃ cāheśamāny uta
BhP aho śrīmadamāhātmyaṃ gopānāṃ kānanaukasām
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ martyam upāśritya ye cakrur devahelanam
BhP yathādṛḍhaiḥ karmamayaiḥ kratubhir nāmanaunibhaiḥ
BhP vidyām ānvīkṣikīṃ hitvā titīrṣanti bhavārṇavam
BhP vācālaṃ bāliśaṃ stabdham ajñaṃ paṇḍitamāninam
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ martyam upāśritya gopā me cakrur apriyam
BhP eṣāṃ śriyāvaliptānāṃ kṛṣṇenādhmāpitātmanām
BhP dhunuta śrīmadastambhaṃ paśūn nayata saṅkṣayam
BhP ahaṃ cairāvataṃ nāgam āruhyānuvraje vrajam
BhP marudgaṇair mahāvegair nandagoṣṭhajighāṃsayā
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itthaṃ maghavatājñaptā meghā nirmuktabandhanāḥ
BhP nandagokulam āsāraiḥ pīḍayām āsur ojasā
BhP vidyotamānā vidyudbhiḥ stanantaḥ stanayitnubhiḥ
BhP tīvrair marudgaṇair nunnā vavṛṣur jalaśarkarāḥ
BhP sthūṇāsthūlā varṣadhārā muñcatsv abhreṣv abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
BhP jalaughaiḥ plāvyamānā bhūr nādṛśyata natonnatam
BhP atyāsārātivātena paśavo jātavepanāḥ
BhP gopā gopyaś ca śītārtā govindaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ
BhP śiraḥ sutāṃś ca kāyena pracchādyāsārapīḍitāḥ
BhP vepamānā bhagavataḥ pādamūlam upāyayuḥ
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahābhāga tvannāthaṃ gokulaṃ prabho
BhP trātum arhasi devān naḥ kupitād bhaktavatsala
BhP śilāvarṣātivātena hanyamānam acetanam
BhP nirīkṣya bhagavān mene kupitendrakṛtaṃ hariḥ
BhP apartv atyulbaṇaṃ varṣam ativātaṃ śilāmayam
BhP svayāge vihate 'smābhir indro nāśāya varṣati
BhP tatra pratividhiṃ samyag ātmayogena sādhaye
BhP lokeśamānināṃ mauḍhyād dhaniṣye śrīmadaṃ tamaḥ
BhP na hi sadbhāvayuktānāṃ surāṇām īśavismayaḥ
BhP matto 'satāṃ mānabhaṅgaḥ praśamāyopakalpate
BhP tasmān maccharaṇaṃ goṣṭhaṃ mannāthaṃ matparigraham
BhP gopāye svātmayogena so 'yaṃ me vrata āhitaḥ
BhP ity uktvaikena hastena kṛtvā govardhanācalam
BhP dadhāra līlayā viṣṇuś chatrākam iva bālakaḥ
BhP athāha bhagavān gopān he 'mba tāta vrajaukasaḥ
BhP yathopajoṣaṃ viśata girigartaṃ sagodhanāḥ
BhP na trāsa iha vaḥ kāryo maddhastādrinipātanāt
BhP vātavarṣabhayenālaṃ tattrāṇaṃ vihitaṃ hi vaḥ
BhP tathā nirviviśur gartaṃ kṛṣṇāśvāsitamānasaḥ
BhP yathāvakāśaṃ sadhanāḥ savrajāḥ sopajīvinaḥ
BhP kṣuttṛḍvyathāṃ sukhāpekṣāṃ hitvā tair vrajavāsibhiḥ
BhP vīkṣyamāṇo dadhārādriṃ saptāhaṃ nācalat padāt
BhP kṛṣṇayogānubhāvaṃ taṃ niśamyendro 'tivismitaḥ
BhP nistambho bhraṣṭasaṅkalpaḥ svān meghān sannyavārayat
BhP khaṃ vyabhram uditādityaṃ vātavarṣaṃ ca dāruṇam
BhP niśamyoparataṃ gopān govardhanadharo 'bravīt
BhP niryāta tyajata trāsaṃ gopāḥ sastrīdhanārbhakāḥ
BhP upārataṃ vātavarṣaṃ vyudaprāyāś ca nimnagāḥ
BhP tatas te niryayur gopāḥ svaṃ svam ādāya godhanam
BhP śakaṭoḍhopakaraṇaṃ strībālasthavirāḥ śanaiḥ
BhP bhagavān api taṃ śailaṃ svasthāne pūrvavat prabhuḥ
BhP paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sthāpayām āsa līlayā
BhP taṃ premavegān nirbhṛtā vrajaukaso
BhP yathā samīyuḥ parirambhaṇādibhiḥ
BhP gopyaś ca sasneham apūjayan mudā
BhP dadhyakṣatādbhir yuyujuḥ sadāśiṣaḥ
BhP yaśodā rohiṇī nando rāmaś ca balināṃ varaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇam āliṅgya yuyujur āśiṣaḥ snehakātarāḥ
BhP divi devagaṇāḥ siddhāḥ sādhyā gandharvacāraṇāḥ
BhP tuṣṭuvur mumucus tuṣṭāḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi pārthiva
BhP śaṅkhadundubhayo nedur divi devapracoditāḥ
BhP jagur gandharvapatayas tumburupramukhā nṛpa
BhP tato 'nuraktaiḥ paśupaiḥ pariśrito rājan svagoṣṭhaṃ sabalo 'vrajad dhariḥ
BhP tathāvidhāny asya kṛtāni gopikā gāyantya īyur muditā hṛdispṛśaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃvidhāni karmāṇi gopāḥ kṛṣṇasya vīkṣya te
BhP atadvīryavidaḥ procuḥ samabhyetya suvismitāḥ
BhP bālakasya yad etāni karmāṇy atyadbhutāni vai
BhP katham arhaty asau janma grāmyeṣv ātmajugupsitam
BhP yaḥ saptahāyano bālaḥ kareṇaikena līlayā
BhP kathaṃ bibhrad girivaraṃ puṣkaraṃ gajarāḍ iva
BhP tokenāmīlitākṣeṇa pūtanāyā mahaujasaḥ
BhP pītaḥ stanaḥ saha prāṇaiḥ kāleneva vayas tanoḥ
BhP hinvato 'dhaḥ śayānasya māsyasya caraṇāv udak
BhP ano 'patad viparyastaṃ rudataḥ prapadāhatam
BhP ekahāyana āsīno hriyamāṇo vihāyasā
BhP daityena yas tṛṇāvartam ahan kaṇṭhagrahāturam
BhP kvacid dhaiyaṅgavastainye mātrā baddha udūkhale
BhP gacchann arjunayor madhye bāhubhyāṃ tāv apātayat
BhP vane sañcārayan vatsān sarāmo bālakair vṛtaḥ
BhP hantukāmaṃ bakaṃ dorbhyāṃ mukhato 'rim apāṭayat
BhP vatseṣu vatsarūpeṇa praviśantaṃ jighāṃsayā
BhP hatvā nyapātayat tena kapitthāni ca līlayā
BhP hatvā rāsabhadaiteyaṃ tadbandhūṃś ca balānvitaḥ
BhP cakre tālavanaṃ kṣemaṃ paripakvaphalānvitam
BhP pralambaṃ ghātayitvograṃ balena balaśālinā
BhP amocayad vrajapaśūn gopāṃś cāraṇyavahnitaḥ
BhP āśīviṣatamāhīndraṃ damitvā vimadaṃ hradāt
BhP prasahyodvāsya yamunāṃ cakre 'sau nirviṣodakām
BhP dustyajaś cānurāgo 'smin sarveṣāṃ no vrajaukasām
BhP nanda te tanaye 'smāsu tasyāpy autpattikaḥ katham
BhP kva saptahāyano bālaḥ kva mahādrividhāraṇam
BhP tato no jāyate śaṅkā vrajanātha tavātmaje
BhP śrīnanda uvāca
BhP śrūyatāṃ me vaco gopā vyetu śaṅkā ca vo 'rbhake
BhP enam kumāram uddiśya gargo me yad uvāca ha
BhP varṇās trayaḥ kilāsyāsan gṛhṇato 'nuyugaṃ tanūḥ
BhP śuklo raktas tathā pīta idānīṃ kṛṣṇatāṃ gataḥ
BhP prāgayaṃ vasudevasya kvacij jātas tavātmajaḥ
BhP vāsudeva iti śrīmān abhijñāḥ sampracakṣate
BhP bahūni santi nāmāni rūpāṇi ca sutasya te
BhP guṇa karmānurūpāṇi tāny ahaṃ veda no janāḥ
BhP eṣa vaḥ śreya ādhāsyad gopagokulanandanaḥ
BhP anena sarvadurgāṇi yūyam añjas tariṣyatha
BhP purānena vrajapate sādhavo dasyupīḍitāḥ
BhP arājake rakṣyamāṇā jigyur dasyūn samedhitāḥ
BhP ya etasmin mahābhāge prītiṃ kurvanti mānavāḥ
BhP nārayo 'bhibhavanty etān viṣṇupakṣān ivāsurāḥ
BhP tasmān nanda kumāro 'yaṃ nārāyaṇasamo guṇaiḥ
BhP śriyā kīrtyānubhāvena tatkarmasu na vismayaḥ
BhP ity addhā māṃ samādiśya garge ca svagṛhaṃ gate
BhP manye nārāyaṇasyāṃśaṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam
BhP iti nandavacaḥ śrutvā gargagītaṃ taṃ vrajaukasaḥ
BhP muditā nandam ānarcuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ ca gatavismayāḥ
BhP deve varṣati yajñaviplavaruṣā vajrāsmavarṣānilaiḥ
BhP sīdatpālapaśustriy ātmaśaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭvānukampy utsmayan
BhP utpāṭyaikakareṇa śailam abalo līlocchilīndhraṃ yathā
BhP bibhrad goṣṭham apān mahendramadabhit prīyān na indro gavām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP govardhane dhṛte śaile āsārād rakṣite vraje
BhP golokād āvrajat kṛṣṇaṃ surabhiḥ śakra eva ca
BhP vivikta upasaṅgamya vrīḍītaḥ kṛtahelanaḥ
BhP pasparśa pādayor enaṃ kirīṭenārkavarcasā
BhP dṛṣṭaśrutānubhāvo 'sya kṛṣṇasyāmitatejasaḥ
BhP naṣṭatrilokeśamada idam āha kṛtāñjaliḥ
BhP indra uvāca
BhP viśuddhasattvaṃ tava dhāma śāntaṃ tapomayaṃ dhvastarajastamaskam
BhP māyāmayo 'yaṃ guṇasampravāho na vidyate te grahaṇānubandhaḥ
BhP kuto nu taddhetava īśa tatkṛtā lobhādayo ye 'budhalingabhāvāḥ
BhP tathāpi daṇḍaṃ bhagavān bibharti dharmasya guptyai khalanigrahāya
BhP pitā gurus tvaṃ jagatām adhīśo duratyayaḥ kāla upāttadaṇḍaḥ
BhP hitāya cecchātanubhiḥ samīhase mānaṃ vidhunvan jagadīśamāninām
BhP ye madvidhājñā jagadīśamāninas tvāṃ vīkṣya kāle 'bhayam āśu tanmadam

BhP kṣantuṃ prabho 'thārhasi mūḍhacetaso maivaṃ punar bhūn matir īśa me 'satī
BhP tavāvatāro 'yam adhokṣajeha bhuvo bharāṇām urubhārajanmanām
BhP camūpatīnām abhavāya deva bhavāya yuṣmaccaraṇānuvartinām
BhP namas tubhyaṃ bhagavate puruṣāya mahātmane
BhP vāsudevāya kṛṣṇāya sātvatāṃ pataye namaḥ
BhP svacchandopāttadehāya viśuddhajñānamūrtaye
BhP sarvasmai sarvabījāya sarvabhūtātmane namaḥ
BhP mayedaṃ bhagavan goṣṭha nāśāyāsāravāyubhiḥ
BhP ceṣṭitaṃ vihate yajñe māninā tīvramanyunā
BhP tvayeśānugṛhīto 'smi dhvastastambho vṛthodyamaḥ
BhP īśvaraṃ gurum ātmānaṃ tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca

BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP mayā te 'kāri maghavan makhabhaṅgo 'nugṛhṇatā
BhP madanusmṛtaye nityaṃ mattasyendraśriyā bhṛśam
BhP mām aiśvaryaśrīmadāndho daṇḍa pāṇiṃ na paśyati
BhP taṃ bhraṃśayāmi sampadbhyo yasya cecchāmy anugraham
BhP gamyatāṃ śakra bhadraṃ vaḥ kriyatāṃ me 'nuśāsanam
BhP sthīyatāṃ svādhikāreṣu yuktair vaḥ stambhavarjitaiḥ
BhP athāha surabhiḥ kṛṣṇam abhivandya manasvinī

BhP tvaṃ naḥ paramakaṃ daivaṃ tvaṃ na indro jagatpate
BhP bhavāya bhava govipra devānāṃ ye ca sādhavaḥ
BhP indraṃ nas tvābhiṣekṣyāmo brahmaṇā coditā vayam
BhP avatīrṇo 'si viśvātman bhūmer bhārāpanuttaye
BhP śṛīśuka uvāca

BhP abhyasiñcata dāśārhaṃ govinda iti cābhyadhāt

BhP taṃ tuṣṭuvur devanikāyaketavo hy avākiraṃś cādbhutapuṣpavṛṣṭibhiḥ
BhP lokāḥ parāṃ nirvṛtim āpnuvaṃs trayo gāvas tadā gām anayan payodrutām
BhP nānārasaughāḥ sarito vṛkṣā āsan madhusravāḥ
BhP akṛṣṭapacyauṣadhayo girayo 'bibhran un maṇīn

BhP iti gogokulapatiṃ govindam abhiṣicya saḥ

BhP bhagavāṃs tad upaśrutya pitaraṃ varuṇāhṛtam
BhP tadantikaṃ gato rājan svānām abhayado vibhuḥ
BhP prāptaṃ vīkṣya hṛṣīkeśaṃ lokapālaḥ saparyayā
BhP mahatyā pūjayitvāha taddarśanamahotsavaḥ
BhP śrīvaruṇa uvāca

BhP tvatpādabhājo bhagavann avāpuḥ pāram adhvanaḥ
BhP namas tubhyaṃ bhagavate brahmaṇe paramātmane
BhP na yatra śrūyate māyā lokasṛṣṭivikalpanā

BhP govinda nīyatām eṣa pitā te pitṛvatsala
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ prasāditaḥ kṛṣṇo bhagavān īśvareśvaraḥ
BhP ādāyāgāt svapitaraṃ bandhūnāṃ cāvahan mudam
BhP nandas tv atīndriyaṃ dṛṣṭvā lokapālamahodayam
BhP kṛṣṇe ca sannatiṃ teṣāṃ jñātibhyo vismito 'bravīt
BhP te cautsukyadhiyo rājan matvā gopās tam īśvaram
BhP api naḥ svagatiṃ sūkṣmām upādhāsyad adhīśvaraḥ
BhP iti svānāṃ sa bhagavān vijñāyākhiladṛk svayam
BhP saṅkalpasiddhaye teṣāṃ kṛpayaitad acintayat
BhP jano vai loka etasminn avidyākāmakarmabhiḥ
BhP uccāvacāsu gatiṣu na veda svāṃ gatiṃ bhraman
BhP iti sañcintya bhagavān mahākāruṇiko hariḥ
BhP darśayām āsa lokaṃ svaṃ gopānāṃ tamasaḥ param
BhP satyaṃ jñānam anantaṃ yad brahmajyotiḥ sanātanam
BhP yad dhi paśyanti munayo guṇāpāye samāhitāḥ
BhP te tu brahmahradam nītā magnāḥ kṛṣṇena coddhṛtāḥ
BhP dadṛśur brahmaṇo lokaṃ yatrākrūro 'dhyagāt purā
BhP nandādayas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā paramānandanivṛtāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ ca tatra cchandobhiḥ stūyamānaṃ suvismitāḥ
BhP śrībādarāyaṇir uvāca
BhP bhagavān api tā rātṛīḥ śāradotphullamallikāḥ
BhP vīkṣya rantuṃ manaś cakre yogamāyām upāśritaḥ
BhP tadoḍurājaḥ kakubhaḥ karair mukhaṃ prācyā vilimpann aruṇena śantamaiḥ
BhP sa carṣaṇīnām udagāc chuco mṛjan priyaḥ priyāyā iva dīrghadarśanaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā kumudvantam akhaṇḍamaṇḍalaṃ
BhP ramānanābhaṃ navakuṅkumāruṇam
BhP vanaṃ ca tatkomalagobhī rañjitaṃ
BhP jagau kalaṃ vāmadṛśāṃ manoharam

BhP ājagmur anyonyam alakṣitodyamāḥ sa yatra kānto javalolakuṇḍalāḥ
BhP duhantyo 'bhiyayuḥ kāścid dohaṃ hitvā samutsukāḥ

BhP pariveṣayantyas tad dhitvā pāyayantyaḥ śiśūn payaḥ
BhP śuśrūṣantyaḥ patīn kāścid aśnantyo 'pāsya bhojanam
BhP limpantyaḥ pramṛjantyo 'nyā añjantyaḥ kāśca locane
BhP vyatyastavastrābharaṇāḥ kāścit kṛṣṇāntikaṃ yayuḥ
BhP tā vāryamāṇāḥ patibhiḥ pitṛbhir bhrātṛbandhubhiḥ
BhP govindāpahṛtātmāno na nyavartanta mohitāḥ
BhP antargṛhagatāḥ kāścid gopyo 'labdhavinirgamāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ tadbhāvanāyuktā dadhyur mīlitalocanāḥ
BhP duḥsahapreṣṭhaviraha tīvratāpadhutāśubhāḥ
BhP dhyānaprāptācyutāśleṣa nirvṛtyā kṣīṇamaṅgalāḥ
BhP tam eva paramātmānaṃ jārabuddhyāpi saṅgatāḥ
BhP jahur guṇamayaṃ dehaṃ sadyaḥ prakṣīṇabandhanāḥ
BhP śrīparīkṣid uvāca

BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP uktaṃ purastād etat te caidyaḥ siddhiṃ yathā gataḥ
BhP dviṣann api hṛṣīkeśaṃ kim utādhokṣajapriyāḥ
BhP nṛṇāṃ niḥśreyasārthāya vyaktir bhagavato nṛpa

BhP kāmaṃ krodhaṃ bhayaṃ sneham aikyaṃ sauhṛdam eva ca
BhP nityaṃ harau vidadhato yānti tanmayatāṃ hi te
BhP na caivaṃ vismayaḥ kāryo bhavatā bhagavaty aje
BhP yogeśvareśvare kṛṣṇe yata etad vimucyate
BhP tā dṛṣṭvāntikam āyātā bhagavān vrajayoṣitaḥ
BhP avadad vadatāṃ śreṣṭho vācaḥ peśair vimohayan
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP svāgataṃ vo mahābhāgāḥ priyaṃ kiṃ karavāṇi vaḥ

BhP rajany eṣā ghorarūpā ghorasattvaniṣevitā
BhP pratiyāta vrajaṃ neha stheyaṃ strībhiḥ sumadhyamāḥ
BhP mātaraḥ pitaraḥ putrā bhrātaraḥ patayaś ca vaḥ
BhP vicinvanti hy apaśyanto mā kṛḍhvaṃ bandhusādhvasam

BhP āgatā hy upapannaṃ vaḥ prīyante mayi jantavaḥ

BhP patiḥ strībhir na hātavyo lokepsubhir apātakī

BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti vipriyam ākarṇya gopyo govindabhāṣitam
BhP viṣaṇṇā bhagnasaṅkalpāś cintām āpur duratyayām
BhP kṛtvā mukhāny ava śucaḥ śvasanena śuṣyad
BhP bimbādharāṇi caraṇena bhuvaḥ likhantyaḥ
BhP asrair upāttamasibhiḥ kucakuṅkumāni

BhP śrīgopya ūcuḥ

BhP preṣṭho bhavāṃs tanubhṛtāṃ kila bandhur ātmā

BhP nityapriye patisutādibhir ārtidaiḥ kim

BhP cittaṃ sukhena bhavatāpahṛtaṃ gṛheṣu

BhP bāhuṃ priyāṃsa upadhāya gṛhītapadmo

BhP anvīyamāna iha vas taravaḥ praṇāmaṃ

BhP nūnaṃ tatkarajaspṛṣṭā bibhraty utpulakāny aho
BhP ity unmattavaco gopyaḥ kṛṣṇānveṣaṇakātarāḥ
BhP līlā bhagavatas tās tā hy anucakrus tadātmikāḥ
BhP kasyācit pūtanāyantyāḥ kṛṣṇāyanty apibat stanam
BhP tokayitvā rudaty anyā padāhan śakaṭāyatīm
BhP daityāyitvā jahārānyām eko kṛṣṇārbhabhāvanām
BhP riṅgayām āsa kāpy aṅghrī karṣantī ghoṣaniḥsvanaiḥ
BhP kṛṣṇarāmāyite dve tu gopāyantyaś ca kāścana
BhP vatsāyatīṃ hanti cānyā tatraikā tu bakāyatīm
BhP āhūya dūragā yadvat kṛṣṇas tam anuvartatīm
BhP veṇuṃ kvaṇantīṃ krīḍantīm anyāḥ śaṃsanti sādhv iti
BhP kasyāñcit svabhujaṃ nyasya calanty āhāparā nanu
BhP kṛṣṇo 'haṃ paśyata gatiṃ lalitām iti tanmanāḥ
BhP mā bhaiṣṭa vātavarṣābhyāṃ tattrāṇaṃ vihitaṃ maya
BhP ity uktvaikena hastena yatanty unnidadhe 'mbaram
BhP āruhyaikā padākramya śirasy āhāparāṃ nṛpa
BhP duṣṭāhe gaccha jāto 'haṃ khalānām nanu daṇḍakṛt
BhP tatraikovāca he gopā dāvāgniṃ paśyatolbaṇam
BhP cakṣūṃṣy āśv apidadhvaṃ vo vidhāsye kṣemam añjasā
BhP baddhānyayā srajā kācit tanvī tatra ulūkhale
BhP badhnāmi bhāṇḍabhettāraṃ haiyaṅgavamuṣaṃ tv iti
BhP bhītā sudṛk pidhāyāsyaṃ bheje bhītiviḍambanam
BhP evaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ pṛcchamānā vrṇdāvanalatās tarūn
BhP vyacakṣata vanoddeśe padāni paramātmanaḥ
BhP padāni vyaktam etāni nandasūnor mahātmanaḥ
BhP lakṣyante hi dhvajāmbhoja vajrāṅkuśayavādibhiḥ
BhP tais taiḥ padais tatpadavīm anvicchantyo 'grato'balāḥ
BhP vadhvāḥ padaiḥ supṛktāni vilokyārtāḥ samabruvan
BhP kasyāḥ padāni caitāni yātāyā nandasūnunā
BhP aṃsanyastaprakoṣṭhāyāḥ kareṇoḥ kariṇā yathā
BhP anayārādhito nūnaṃ bhagavān harir īśvaraḥ
BhP yan no vihāya govindaḥ prīto yām anayad rahaḥ
BhP dhanyā aho amī ālyo govindāṅghryabjareṇavaḥ
BhP yān brahmeśau ramā devī dadhur mūrdhny aghanuttaye
BhP tasyā amūni naḥ kṣobhaṃ kurvanty uccaiḥ padāni yat
BhP yaikāpahṛtya gopīnām raho bhunkte 'cyutādharam
BhP na lakṣyante padāny atra tasyā nūnaṃ tṛṇāṅkuraiḥ
BhP khidyatsujātāṅghritalām unninye preyasīṃ priyaḥ
BhP imāny adhikamagnāni padāni vahato vadhūm
BhP gopyaḥ paśyata kṛṣṇasya bhārākrāntasya kāminaḥ
BhP atrāvaropitā kāntā puṣpahetor mahātmanā
BhP atra prasūnāvacayaḥ priyārthe preyasā kṛtaḥ
BhP prapadākramaṇa ete paśyatāsakale pade
BhP keśaprasādhanaṃ tv atra kāminyāḥ kāminā kṛtam
BhP tāni cūḍayatā kāntām upaviṣṭam iha dhruvam
BhP reme tayā cātmarata ātmārāmo 'py akhaṇḍitaḥ
BhP kāmināṃ darśayan dainyaṃ strīṇāṃ caiva durātmatām
BhP ity evaṃ darśayantyas tāś cerur gopyo vicetasaḥ
BhP yāṃ gopīm anayat kṛṣṇo vihāyānyāḥ striyo vane
BhP sā ca mene tadātmānaṃ variṣṭhaṃ sarvayoṣitām
BhP hitvā gopīḥ kāmayānā mām asau bhajate priyaḥ
BhP tato gatvā vanoddeśaṃ dṛptā keśavam abravīt
BhP na pāraye 'haṃ calituṃ naya māṃ yatra te manaḥ
BhP evam uktaḥ priyām āha skandha āruhyatām iti
BhP tataś cāntardadhe kṛṣṇaḥ sā vadhūr anvatapyata
BhP hā nātha ramaṇa preṣṭha kvāsi kvāsi mahābhuja
BhP dāsyās te kṛpaṇāyā me sakhe darśaya sannidhim
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP anvicchantyo bhagavato mārgaṃ gopyo 'vidūritaḥ
BhP dadṛśuḥ priyaviśleṣān mohitāṃ duḥkhitāṃ sakhīm
BhP tayā kathitam ākarṇya mānaprāptiṃ ca mādhavāt
BhP avamānaṃ ca daurātmyād vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ
BhP tato 'viśan vanaṃ candra jyotsnā yāvad vibhāvyate
BhP tamaḥ praviṣṭam ālakṣya tato nivavṛtuḥ striyaḥ
BhP tanmanaskās tadalāpās tadviceṣṭās tadātmikāḥ
BhP tadguṇān eva gāyantyo nātmagārāṇi sasmaruḥ
BhP punaḥ pulinam āgatya kālindyāḥ kṛṣṇabhāvanāḥ
BhP samavetā jaguḥ kṛṣṇaṃ tadāgamanakāṅkṣitāḥ
BhP gopya ūcuḥ
BhP jayati te 'dhikaṃ janmanā vrajaḥ śrayata indirā śaśvad atra hi
BhP dayita dṛśyatāṃ dikṣu tāvakās tvayi dhṛtāsavas tvāṃ vicinvate
BhP śaradudāśaye sādhujātasat sarasijodaraśrīmuṣā dṛśā
BhP suratanātha te 'śulkadāsikā varada nighnato neha kiṃ vadhaḥ
BhP viṣajalāpyayād vyālarākṣasād varṣamārutād vaidyutānalāt
BhP vṛṣamayātmajād viśvato bhayād ṛṣabha te vayaṃ rakṣitā muhuḥ
BhP na khalu gopīkānandano bhavān akhiladehinām antarātmadṛk
BhP vikhanasārthito viśvaguptaye sakha udeyivān sātvatāṃ kule
BhP viracitābhayaṃ vṛṣṇidhūrya te caraṇam īyuṣāṃ saṃsṛter bhayāt
BhP karasaroruhaṃ kānta kāmadaṃ śirasi dhehi naḥ śrīkaragraham
BhP vrajajanārtihan vīra yoṣitāṃ nijajanasmayadhvaṃsanasmita
BhP bhaja sakhe bhavatkiṅkarīḥ sma no jalaruhānanaṃ cāru darśaya
BhP praṇatadehināṃ pāpakarṣaṇaṃ tṛṇacarānugaṃ śrīniketanam
BhP phaṇiphaṇārpitaṃ te padāmbujaṃ kṛṇu kuceṣu naḥ kṛndhi hṛcchayam
BhP madhurayā girā valguvākyayā budhamanojñayā puṣkarekṣaṇa
BhP vidhikarīr imā vīra muhyatīr adharasīdhunāpyāyayasva naḥ
BhP tava kathāmṛtaṃ taptajīvanaṃ kavibhir īḍitaṃ kalmaṣāpaham
BhP śravaṇamaṅgalaṃ śrīmad ātataṃ bhuvi gṛṇanti ye bhūridā janāḥ
BhP prahasitaṃ priyapremavīkṣaṇaṃ viharaṇaṃ ca te dhyānamaṅgalam
BhP rahasi saṃvido yā hṛdi spṛśaḥ kuhaka no manaḥ kṣobhayanti hi
BhP calasi yad vrajāc cārayan paśūn nalinasundaraṃ nātha te padam
BhP śilatṛṇāṅkuraiḥ sīdatīti naḥ kalilatāṃ manaḥ kānta gacchati
BhP dinaparikṣaye nīlakuntalair vanaruhānanaṃ bibhrad āvṛtam
BhP ghanarajasvalaṃ darśayan muhur manasi naḥ smaraṃ vīra yacchasi
BhP praṇatakāmadaṃ padmajārcitaṃ dharaṇimaṇḍanaṃ dhyeyam āpadi
BhP caraṇapaṅkajaṃ śantamaṃ ca te ramaṇa naḥ staneṣv arpayādhihan
BhP suratavardhanaṃ śokanāśanaṃ svaritaveṇunā suṣṭhu cumbitam
BhP itararāgavismāraṇaṃ nṛṇāṃ vitara vīra nas te 'dharāmṛtam
BhP aṭati yad bhavān ahni kānanaṃ truṭi yugāyate tvām apaśyatām
BhP kuṭilakuntalaṃ śrīmukhaṃ ca te jaḍa udīkṣatāṃ pakṣmakṛd dṛśām
BhP patisutānvayabhrātṛbāndhavān ativilaṅghya te 'nty acyutāgatāḥ
BhP gatividas tavodgītamohitāḥ kitava yoṣitaḥ kas tyajen niśi
BhP rahasi saṃvidaṃ hṛcchayodayaṃ prahasitānanaṃ premavīkṣaṇam
BhP bṛhaduraḥ śriyo vīkṣya dhāma te muhur atispṛhā muhyate manaḥ
BhP vrajavanaukasāṃ vyaktir aṅga te vṛjinahantry alaṃ viśvamaṅgalam
BhP tyaja manāk ca nas tvatspṛhātmanāṃ svajanahṛdrujāṃ yan niṣūdanam
BhP yat te sujātacaraṇāmburuhaṃ staneṣu
BhP bhītāḥ śanaiḥ priya dadhīmahi karkaśeṣu
BhP tenāṭavīm aṭasi tad vyathate na kiṃ svit
BhP kūrpādibhir bhramati dhīr bhavadāyuṣāṃ naḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti gopyaḥ pragāyantyaḥ pralapantyaś ca citradhā
BhP ruruduḥ susvaraṃ rājan kṛṣṇadarśanalālasāḥ
BhP tāsām āvirabhūc chauriḥ smayamānamukhāmbujaḥ
BhP pītāmbaradharaḥ sragvī sākṣān manmathamanmathaḥ
BhP taṃ vilokyāgataṃ preṣṭhaṃ prītyutphulladṛśo 'balāḥ
BhP uttasthur yugapat sarvās tanvaḥ prāṇam ivāgatam
BhP kācit karāmbujaṃ śaurer jagṛhe 'ñjalinā mudā
BhP kācid dadhāra tadbāhum aṃse candanabhūṣitam
BhP kācid añjalināgṛhṇāt tanvī tāmbūlacarvitam
BhP ekā tadaṅghrikamalaṃ santaptā stanayor adhāt
BhP ekā bhrukuṭim ābadhya premasaṃrambhavihvalā
BhP ghnantīvaikṣat kaṭākṣepaiḥ sandaṣṭadaśanacchadā
BhP aparānimiṣaddṛgbhyāṃ juṣāṇā tanmukhāmbujam
BhP āpītam api nātṛpyat santas taccaraṇaṃ yathā
BhP taṃ kācin netrarandhreṇa hṛdi kṛtvā nimīlya ca
BhP pulakāṅgy upaguhyāste yogīvānandasamplutā
BhP sarvās tāḥ keśavāloka paramotsavanirvṛtāḥ
BhP jahur virahajaṃ tāpaṃ prājñaṃ prāpya yathā janāḥ
BhP tābhir vidhūtaśokābhir bhagavān acyuto vṛtaḥ
BhP vyarocatādhikaṃ tāta puruṣaḥ śaktibhir yathā
BhP tāḥ samādāya kālindyā nirviśya pulinaṃ vibhuḥ
BhP vikasatkundamandāra surabhyanilaṣaṭpadam
BhP śaraccandrāṃśusandoha dhvastadoṣātamaḥ śivam
BhP kṛṣṇāyā hastataralā citakomalavālukam
BhP taddarśanāhlādavidhūtahṛdrujo manorathāntaṃ śrutayo yathā yayuḥ
BhP svair uttarīyaiḥ kucakuṅkumāṅkitair acīkḷpann āsanam ātmabandhave
BhP tatropaviṣṭo bhagavān sa īśvaro yogeśvarāntarhṛdi kalpitāsanaḥ
BhP cakāsa gopīpariṣadgato 'rcitas trailokyalakṣmyekapadaṃ vapur dadhat
BhP sabhājayitvā tam anaṅgadīpanaṃ sahāsalīlekṣaṇavibhramabhruvā
BhP saṃsparśanenāṅkakṛtāṅghrihastayoḥ saṃstutya īṣat kupitā babhāṣire
BhP śrīgopya ūcuḥ
BhP bhajato 'nubhajanty eka eka etadviparyayam
BhP nobhayāṃś ca bhajanty eka etan no brūhi sādhu bhoḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP mitho bhajanti ye sakhyaḥ svārthaikāntodyamā hi te
BhP na tatra sauhṛdaṃ dharmaḥ svārthārthaṃ tad dhi nānyathā
BhP bhajanty abhajato ye vai karuṇāḥ pitarau yathā
BhP dharmo nirapavādo 'tra sauhṛdaṃ ca sumadhyamāḥ
BhP bhajato 'pi na vai kecid bhajanty abhajataḥ kutaḥ
BhP ātmārāmā hy āptakāmā akṛtajñā gurudruhaḥ
BhP nāhaṃ tu sakhyo bhajato 'pi jantūn bhajāmy amīṣām anuvṛttivṛttaye
BhP yathādhano labdhadhane vinaṣṭe taccintayānyan nibhṛto na veda
BhP evaṃ madarthojjhitalokaveda svānām hi vo mayy anuvṛttaye 'balāḥ
BhP mayāparokṣaṃ bhajatā tirohitaṃ māsūyituṃ mārhatha tat priyaṃ priyāḥ
BhP na pāraye 'haṃ niravadyasaṃyujāṃ svasādhukṛtyaṃ vibudhāyuṣāpi vaḥ
BhP yā mābhajan durjaragehaśṛṅkhalāḥ saṃvṛścya tad vaḥ pratiyātu sādhunā
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itthaṃ bhagavato gopyaḥ śrutvā vācaḥ supeśalāḥ
BhP jahur virahajaṃ tāpaṃ tadaṅgopacitāśiṣaḥ
BhP tatrārabhata govindo rāsakrīḍām anuvrataiḥ
BhP strīratnair anvitaḥ prītair anyonyābaddhabāhubhiḥ
BhP rāsotsavaḥ sampravṛtto gopīmaṇḍalamaṇḍitaḥ
BhP yogeśvareṇa kṛṣṇena tāsāṃ madhye dvayor dvayoḥ
BhP praviṣṭena gṛhītānāṃ kaṇṭhe svanikaṭaṃ striyaḥ
BhP yaṃ manyeran nabhas tāvad vimānaśatasaṅkulam
BhP divaukasāṃ sadārāṇām autsukyāpahṛtātmanām
BhP tato dundubhayo nedur nipetuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭayaḥ
BhP jagur gandharvapatayaḥ sastrīkās tadyaśo 'malam
BhP valayānāṃ nūpurāṇāṃ kiṅkiṇīnāṃ ca yoṣitām
BhP sapriyāṇām abhūc chabdas tumulo rāsamaṇḍale
BhP tatrātiśuśubhe tābhir bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP madhye maṇīnāṃ haimānāṃ mahāmarakato yathā
BhP pādanyāsair bhujavidhutibhiḥ sasmitair bhrūvilāsair
BhP bhajyan madhyaiś calakucapaṭaiḥ kuṇḍalair gaṇḍalolaiḥ
BhP svidyanmukhyaḥ kavararasanāgranthayaḥ kṛṣṇavadhvo
BhP gāyantyas taṃ taḍita iva tā meghacakre virejuḥ
BhP uccair jagur nṛtyamānā raktakaṇṭhyo ratipriyāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇābhimarśamuditā yadgītenedam āvṛtam
BhP kācit samaṃ mukundena svarajātīr amiśritāḥ
BhP unninye pūjitā tena prīyatā sādhu sādhv iti
BhP tad eva dhruvam unninye tasyai mānaṃ ca bahv adāt
BhP kācid rāsapariśrāntā pārśvasthasya gadābhṛtaḥ
BhP jagrāha bāhunā skandhaṃ ślathadvalayamallikā
BhP tatraikāṃsagataṃ bāhuṃ kṛṣṇasyotpalasaurabham
BhP candanāliptam āghrāya hṛṣṭaromā cucumba ha
BhP kasyāścin nāṭyavikṣipta kuṇḍalatviṣamaṇḍitam
BhP gaṇḍaṃ gaṇḍe sandadhatyāḥ prādāt tāmbūlacarvitam
BhP nṛtyatī gāyatī kācit kūjan nūpuramekhalā
BhP pārśvasthācyutahastābjaṃ śrāntādhāt stanayoḥ śivam
BhP gopyo labdhvācyutaṃ kāntaṃ śriya ekāntavallabham
BhP gṛhītakaṇṭhyas taddorbhyāṃ gāyantyas tam vijahrire
BhP karṇotpalālakaviṭaṅkakapolagharma
BhP vaktraśriyo valayanūpuraghoṣavādyaiḥ
BhP gopyaḥ samaṃ bhagavatā nanṛtuḥ svakeśa
BhP srastasrajo bhramaragāyakarāsagoṣṭhyām
BhP evaṃ pariṣvaṅgakarābhimarśa snigdhekṣaṇoddāmavilāsahāsaiḥ
BhP reme rameśo vrajasundarībhir yathārbhakaḥ svapratibimbavibhramaḥ
BhP tadaṅgasaṅgapramudākulendriyāḥ keśān dukūlaṃ kucapaṭṭikāṃ vā
BhP nāñjaḥ prativyoḍhum alaṃ vrajastriyo visrastamālābharaṇāḥ kurūdvaha
BhP kṛṣṇavikrīḍitaṃ vīkṣya mumuhuḥ khecarastriyaḥ
BhP kāmārditāḥ śaśāṅkaś ca sagaṇo vismito 'bhavat
BhP kṛtvā tāvantam ātmānaṃ yāvatīr gopayoṣitaḥ
BhP reme sa bhagavāṃs tābhir ātmārāmo 'pi līlayā
BhP tāsāṃ rativihāreṇa śrāntānāṃ vadanāni saḥ
BhP prāmṛjat karuṇaḥ premṇā śantamenāṅga pāṇinā
BhP gopyaḥ sphuratpuraṭakuṇḍalakuntalatviḍ
BhP gaṇḍaśriyā sudhitahāsanirīkṣaṇena
BhP mānaṃ dadhatya ṛṣabhasya jaguḥ kṛtāni
BhP puṇyāni tatkararuhasparśapramodāḥ
BhP tābhir yutaḥ śramam apohitum aṅgasaṅga
BhP ghṛṣṭasrajaḥ sa kucakuṅkumarañjitāyāḥ
BhP gandharvapālibhir anudruta āviśad vāḥ
BhP śrānto gajībhir ibharāḍ iva bhinnasetuḥ
BhP so 'mbhasy alaṃ yuvatibhiḥ pariṣicyamānaḥ
BhP premṇekṣitaḥ prahasatībhir itas tato 'ṅga
BhP vaimānikaiḥ kusumavarṣibhir īdyamāno
BhP reme svayaṃ svaratir atra gajendralīlaḥ
BhP tataś ca kṛṣṇopavane jalasthala prasūnagandhānilajuṣṭadiktaṭe
BhP cacāra bhṛṅgapramadāgaṇāvṛto yathā madacyud dviradaḥ kareṇubhiḥ
BhP evaṃ śaśāṅkāṃśuvirājitā niśāḥ sa satyakāmo 'nuratābalāgaṇaḥ
BhP siṣeva ātmany avaruddhasaurataḥ sarvāḥ śaratkāvyakathārasāśrayāḥ
BhP śrīparīkṣid uvāca
BhP saṃsthāpanāya dharmasya praśamāyetarasya ca
BhP avatīrṇo hi bhagavān aṃśena jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP sa kathaṃ dharmasetūnāṃ vaktā kartābhirakṣitā
BhP pratīpam ācarad brahman paradārābhimarśanam
BhP āptakāmo yadupatiḥ kṛtavān vai jugupsitam
BhP kimabhiprāya etan naḥ śaṃśayaṃ chindhi suvrata
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP dharmavyatikramo dṛṣṭa īśvarāṇāṃ ca sāhasam
BhP tejīyasāṃ na doṣāya vahneḥ sarvabhujo yathā
BhP naitat samācarej jātu manasāpi hy anīśvaraḥ
BhP vinaśyaty ācaran mauḍhyād yathārudro 'bdhijaṃ viṣam
BhP īśvarāṇāṃ vacaḥ satyaṃ tathaivācaritaṃ kvacit
BhP teṣāṃ yat svavacoyuktaṃ buddhimāṃs tat samācaret
BhP kuśalācaritenaiṣām iha svārtho na vidyate
BhP viparyayeṇa vānartho nirahaṅkāriṇāṃ prabho
BhP kim utākhilasattvānāṃ tiryaṅmartyadivaukasām
BhP īśituś ceśitavyānāṃ kuśalākuśalānvayaḥ
BhP yatpādapaṅkajaparāganiṣevatṛptā
BhP yogaprabhāvavidhutākhilakarmabandhāḥ
BhP svairaṃ caranti munayo 'pi na nahyamānās
BhP tasyecchayāttavapuṣaḥ kuta eva bandhaḥ
BhP gopīnāṃ tatpatīnāṃ ca sarveṣām eva dehinām
BhP yo 'ntaś carati so 'dhyakṣaḥ krīḍaneneha dehabhāk

BhP tvam ātmā sarvabhūtānām eko jyotir ivaidhasām
BhP gūḍho guhāśayaḥ sākṣī mahāpuruṣa īśvaraḥ
BhP ātmanātmāśrayaḥ pūrvaṃ māyayā sasṛje guṇān
BhP tair idaṃ satyasaṅkalpaḥ sṛjasy atsy avasīśvaraḥ
BhP sa tvaṃ bhūdharabhūtānāṃ daityapramatharakṣasām
BhP avatīrṇo vināśāya sādhunāṃ rakṣaṇāya ca
BhP diṣṭyā te nihato daityo līlayāyaṃ hayākṛtiḥ
BhP yasya heṣitasantrastās tyajanty animiṣā divam
BhP cāṇūraṃ muṣṭikaṃ caiva mallān anyāṃś ca hastinam
BhP kaṃsaṃ ca nihataṃ drakṣye paraśvo 'hani te vibho
BhP tasyānu śaṅkhayavana murāṇāṃ narakasya ca
BhP pārijātāpaharaṇam indrasya ca parājayam
BhP udvāhaṃ vīrakanyānāṃ vīryaśulkādilakṣaṇam
BhP nṛgasya mokṣaṇaṃ śāpād dvārakāyāṃ jagatpate
BhP syamantakasya ca maṇer ādānaṃ saha bhāryayā
BhP mṛtaputrapradānaṃ ca brāhmaṇasya svadhāmataḥ
BhP pauṇḍrakasya vadhaṃ paścāt kāśipuryāś ca dīpanam
BhP dantavakrasya nidhanaṃ caidyasya ca mahākratau
BhP yāni cānyāni vīryāṇi dvārakām āvasan bhavān
BhP kartā drakṣyāmy ahaṃ tāni geyāni kavibhir bhuvi
BhP atha te kālarūpasya kṣapayiṣṇor amuṣya vai
BhP akṣauhiṇīnāṃ nidhanaṃ drakṣyāmy arjunasāratheḥ
BhP viśuddhavijñānaghanaṃ svasaṃsthayā
BhP samāptasarvārtham amoghavāñchitam
BhP svatejasā nityanivṛttamāyā
BhP guṇapravāhaṃ bhagavantam īmahi
BhP tvām īśvaraṃ svāśrayam ātmamāyayā vinirmitāśeṣaviśeṣakalpanam
BhP krīḍārtham adyāttamanuṣyavigrahaṃ nato 'smi dhuryaṃ yaduvṛṣṇisātvatām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ yadupatiṃ kṛṣṇaṃ bhāgavatapravaro muniḥ
BhP praṇipatyābhyanujñāto yayau taddarśanotsavaḥ
BhP bhagavān api govindo hatvā keśinam āhave
BhP paśūn apālayat pālaiḥ prītair vrajasukhāvahaḥ
BhP ekadā te paśūn pālāś cārayanto 'drisānuṣu
BhP cakrur nilāyanakrīḍāś corapālāpadeśataḥ
BhP tatrāsan katicic corāḥ pālāś ca katicin nṛpa
BhP meṣāyitāś ca tatraike vijahrur akutobhayāḥ
BhP mayaputro mahāmāyo vyomo gopālaveṣadhṛk
BhP meṣāyitān apovāha prāyaś corāyito bahūn
BhP giridaryāṃ vinikṣipya nītaṃ nītaṃ mahāsuraḥ
BhP śilayā pidadhe dvāraṃ catuḥpañcāvaśeṣitāḥ
BhP tasya tat karma vijñāya kṛṣṇaḥ śaraṇadaḥ satām
BhP gopān nayantaṃ jagrāha vṛkaṃ harir ivaujasā
BhP sa nijaṃ rūpam āsthāya girīndrasadṛśaṃ balī
BhP icchan vimoktum ātmānaṃ nāśaknod grahaṇāturaḥ
BhP taṃ nigṛhyācyuto dorbhyāṃ pātayitvā mahītale
BhP paśyatāṃ divi devānāṃ paśumāram amārayat
BhP guhāpidhānaṃ nirbhidya gopān niḥsārya kṛcchrataḥ
BhP stūyamānaḥ surair gopaiḥ praviveśa svagokulam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP akrūro 'pi ca tāṃ rātriṃ madhupuryāṃ mahāmatiḥ
BhP uṣitvā ratham āsthāya prayayau nandagokulam
BhP gacchan pathi mahābhāgo bhagavaty ambujekṣaṇe
BhP bhaktiṃ parām upagata evam etad acintayat
BhP kiṃ mayācaritaṃ bhadraṃ kiṃ taptaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ
BhP kiṃ vāthāpy arhate dattaṃ yad drakṣyāmy adya keśavam
BhP mamaitad durlabhaṃ manya uttamaḥślokadarśanam
BhP viṣayātmano yathā brahma kīrtanaṃ śūdrajanmanaḥ
BhP maivaṃ mamādhamasyāpi syād evācyutadarśanam
BhP hriyamāṇaḥ kalanadyā kvacit tarati kaścana
BhP mamādyāmaṅgalaṃ naṣṭaṃ phalavāṃś caiva me bhavaḥ
BhP yan namasye bhagavato yogidhyeyānghripaṅkajam
BhP kaṃso batādyākṛta me 'tyanugrahaṃ drakṣye 'ṅghripadmaṃ prahito 'munā hareḥ
BhP kṛtāvatārasya duratyayaṃ tamaḥ pūrve 'taran yannakhamaṇḍalatviṣā
BhP yad arcitaṃ brahmabhavādibhiḥ suraiḥ
BhP śriyā ca devyā munibhiḥ sasātvataiḥ
BhP gocāraṇāyānucaraiś carad vane
BhP yad gopikānāṃ kucakuṅkumāṅkitam
BhP drakṣyāmi nūnaṃ sukapolanāsikaṃ smitāvalokāruṇakañjalocanam
BhP mukhaṃ mukundasya guḍālakāvṛtaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ me pracaranti vai mṛgāḥ
BhP apy adya viṣṇor manujatvam īyuṣo bhārāvatārāya bhuvo nijecchayā
BhP lāvaṇyadhāmno bhavitopalambhanaṃ mahyaṃ na na syāt phalam añjasā dṛśaḥ
BhP ya īkṣitāhaṃrahito 'py asatsatoḥ svatejasāpāstatamobhidābhramaḥ
BhP svamāyayātman racitais tadīkṣayā prāṇākṣadhībhiḥ sadaneṣv abhīyate
BhP yasyākhilāmīvahabhiḥ sumaṅgalaiḥ vāco vimiśrā guṇakarmajanmabhiḥ
BhP prāṇanti śumbhanti punanti vai jagat yās tadviraktāḥ śavaśobhanā matāḥ
BhP sa cāvatīrṇaḥ kila satvatānvaye svasetupālāmaravaryaśarmakṛt
BhP yaśo vitanvan vraja āsta īśvaro gāyanti devā yad aśeṣamaṅgalam
BhP taṃ tv adya nūnaṃ mahatāṃ gatiṃ guruṃ
BhP trailokyakāntaṃ dṛśimanmahotsavam
BhP rūpaṃ dadhānaṃ śriya īpsitāspadaṃ
BhP drakṣye mamāsann uṣasaḥ sudarśanāḥ
BhP athāvarūḍhaḥ sapadīśayo rathāt pradhānapuṃsoś caraṇaṃ svalabdhaye
BhP dhiyā dhṛtaṃ yogibhir apy ahaṃ dhruvaṃ namasya ābhyāṃ ca sakhīn vanaukasaḥ
BhP apy aṅghrimūle patitasya me vibhuḥ
BhP śirasy adhāsyan nijahastapaṅkajam
BhP dattābhayaṃ kālabhujāṅgaraṃhasā
BhP prodvejitānāṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇāṃ ṇṛnām
BhP samarhaṇaṃ yatra nidhāya kauśikas tathā baliś cāpa jagattrayendratām
BhP yad vā vihāre vrajayoṣitāṃ śramaṃ sparśena saugandhikagandhy apānudat
BhP na mayy upaiṣyaty aribuddhim acyutaḥ
BhP kaṃsasya dūtaḥ prahito 'pi viśvadṛk
BhP yo 'ntar bahiś cetasa etad īhitaṃ
BhP kṣetrajña īkṣaty amalena cakṣuṣā
BhP apy aṅghrimūle 'vahitaṃ kṛtāñjaliṃ
BhP mām īkṣitā sasmitam ārdrayā dṛśā
BhP sapady apadhvastasamastakilbiṣo
BhP voḍhā mudaṃ vītaviśaṅka ūrjitām
BhP suhṛttamaṃ jñātim ananyadaivataṃ dorbhyāṃ bṛhadbhyāṃ parirapsyate 'tha mām
BhP ātmā hi tīrthīkriyate tadaiva me bandhaś ca karmātmaka ucchvasity ataḥ
BhP labdhvāṅgasaṅgam praṇatam kṛtāñjaliṃ
BhP māṃ vakṣyate 'krūra tatety uruśravāḥ
BhP tadā vayaṃ janmabhṛto mahīyasā
BhP naivādṛto yo dhig amuṣya janma tat
BhP na tasya kaścid dayitaḥ suhṛttamo na cāpriyo dveṣya upekṣya eva vā
BhP tathāpi bhaktān bhajate yathā tathā suradrumo yadvad upāśrito 'rthadaḥ
BhP kiṃ cāgrajo māvanataṃ yadūttamaḥ smayan pariṣvajya gṛhītam añjalau
BhP gṛhaṃ praveṣyāptasamastasatkṛtaṃ samprakṣyate kaṃsakṛtaṃ svabandhuṣu
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti sañcintayan kṛṣṇaṃ śvaphalkatanayo 'dhvani
BhP rathena gokulaṃ prāptaḥ sūryaś cāstagiriṃ nṛpa
BhP padāni tasyākhilalokapāla kirīṭajuṣṭāmalapādareṇoḥ
BhP dadarśa goṣṭhe kṣitikautukāni vilakṣitāny abjayavāṅkuśādyaiḥ
BhP taddarśanāhlādavivṛddhasambhramaḥ
BhP premṇordhvaromāśrukalākulekṣaṇaḥ
BhP rathād avaskandya sa teṣv aceṣṭata
BhP prabhor amūny aṅghrirajāṃsy aho iti
BhP dehaṃbhṛtām iyān artho hitvā dambhaṃ bhiyaṃ śucam
BhP sandeśād yo harer liṅga darśanaśravaṇādibhiḥ
BhP dadarśa kṛṣṇaṃ rāmaṃ ca vraje godohanaṃ gatau
BhP pītanīlāmbaradharau śaradamburahekṣaṇau
BhP kiśorau śyāmalaśvetau śrīniketau bṛhadbhujau
BhP sumukhau sundaravarau baladviradavikramau
BhP dhvajavajrāṅkuśāmbhojaiś cihnitair aṅghribhir vrajam
BhP śobhayantau mahātmānau sānukrośasmitekṣaṇau
BhP udārarucirakrīḍau sragviṇau vanamālinau
BhP puṇyagandhānuliptāṅgau snātau virajavāsasau
BhP pradhānapuruṣāv ādyau jagaddhetū jagatpatī
BhP avatīrṇau jagatyarthe svāṃśena balakeśavau
BhP diśo vitimirā rājan kurvāṇau prabhayā svayā
BhP yathā mārakataḥ śailo raupyaś ca kanakācitau
BhP rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya so 'krūraḥ snehavihvalaḥ
BhP papāta caraṇopānte daṇḍavad rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP bhagavaddarśanāhlāda bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ
BhP pulakacitāṅga autkaṇṭhyāt svākhyāne nāśakan nṛpa
BhP bhagavāṃs tam abhipretya rathāṅgāṅkitapāṇinā
BhP parirebhe 'bhyupākṛṣya prītaḥ praṇatavatsalaḥ
BhP saṅkarṣaṇaś ca praṇatam upaguhya mahāmanāḥ
BhP gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇī anayat sānujo gṛham
BhP pṛṣṭvātha svāgataṃ tasmai nivedya ca varāsanam
BhP prakṣālya vidhivat pādau madhuparkārhaṇam āharat
BhP nivedya gāṃ cātithaye saṃvāhya śrāntam āḍṛtaḥ
BhP annaṃ bahuguṇaṃ medhyaṃ śraddhayopāharad vibhuḥ
BhP tasmai bhuktavate prītyā rāmaḥ paramadharmavit
BhP makhavāsair gandhamālyaiḥ parāṃ prītiṃ vyadhāt punaḥ
BhP papraccha satkṛtaṃ nandaḥ kathaṃ stha niranugrahe
BhP kaṃse jīvati dāśārha saunapālā ivāvayaḥ
BhP yo 'vadhīt svasvasus tokān krośantyā asutṛp khalaḥ
BhP kiṃ nu svit tatprajānāṃ vaḥ kuśalaṃ vimṛśāmahe
BhP itthaṃ sūnṛtayā vācā nandena susabhājitaḥ
BhP akrūraḥ paripṛṣṭena jahāv adhvapariśramam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sukhopaviṣṭaḥ paryaṅke ramakṛṣṇorumānitaḥ
BhP lebhe manorathān sarvān pathi yān sa cakāra ha
BhP kim alabhyaṃ bhagavati prasanne śrīniketane
BhP tathāpi tatparā rājan na hi vāñchanti kiñcana
BhP sāyantanāśanaṃ kṛtvā bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP suhṛtsu vṛttaṃ kaṃsasya papracchānyac cikīrṣitam
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP tāta saumyāgataḥ kaccit svāgataṃ bhadram astu vaḥ
BhP api svajñātibandhūnām anamīvam anāmayam
BhP kiṃ nu naḥ kuśalaṃ pṛcche edhamāne kulāmaye
BhP kaṃse mātulanāmnāṅga svānāṃ nas tatprajāsu ca
BhP aho asmad abhūd bhūri pitror vṛjinam āryayoḥ
BhP yaddhetoḥ putramaraṇaṃ yaddhetor bandhanaṃ tayoḥ
BhP diṣṭyādya darśanaṃ svānāṃ mahyaṃ vaḥ saumya kāṅkṣitam
BhP sañjātaṃ varṇyatāṃ tāta tavāgamanakāraṇam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP pṛṣṭo bhagavatā sarvaṃ varṇayām āsa mādhavaḥ
BhP vairānubandhaṃ yaduṣu vasudevavadhodyamam
BhP yatsandeśo yadarthaṃ vā dūtaḥ sampreṣitaḥ svayam
BhP yad uktaṃ nāradenāsya svajanmānakadundubheḥ
BhP śrutvākrūravacaḥ kṛṣṇo balaś ca paravīrahā
BhP prahasya nandaṃ pitaraṃ rājñā diṣṭaṃ vijajñatuḥ
BhP gopān samādiśat so 'pi gṛhyatāṃ sarvagorasaḥ
BhP upāyanāni gṛhṇīdhvaṃ yujyantāṃ śakaṭāni ca
BhP yāsyāmaḥ śvo madhupurīṃ dāsyāmo nṛpate rasān
BhP drakṣyāmaḥ sumahat parva yānti jānapadāḥ kila
BhP evam āghoṣayat kṣatrā nandagopaḥ svagokule
BhP gopyas tās tad upaśrutya babhūvur vyathitā bhṛśam
BhP rāmakṛṣṇau purīṃ netum akrūraṃ vrajam āgatam
BhP kāścit tatkṛtahṛttāpa śvāsamlānamukhaśriyaḥ
BhP sraṃsaddukūlavalaya keśagranthyaś ca kāścana
BhP anyāś ca tadanudhyāna nivṛttāśeṣavṛttayaḥ
BhP nābhyajānann imaṃ lokam ātmalokaṃ gatā iva
BhP smarantyaś cāparāḥ śaurer anurāgasmiteritāḥ
BhP hṛdispṛśaś citrapadā giraḥ sammumuhuḥ striyaḥ
BhP gatiṃ sulalitāṃ ceṣṭāṃ snigdhahāsāvalokanam
BhP śokāpahāni narmāṇi proddāmacaritāni ca
BhP cintayantyo mukundasya bhītā virahakātarāḥ
BhP sametāḥ saṅghaśaḥ procur aśrumukhyo 'cyutāśayāḥ
BhP śrīgopya ūcuḥ
BhP aho vidhātas tava na kvacid dayā saṃyojya maitryā praṇayena dehinaḥ
BhP tāṃś cākṛtārthān viyunaṅkṣy apārthakaṃ vikrīḍitaṃ te 'rbhakaceṣṭitaṃ yathā
BhP yas tvaṃ pradarśyāsitakuntalāvṛtaṃ
BhP mukundavaktraṃ sukapolam unnasam
BhP śokāpanodasmitaleśasundaraṃ
BhP karoṣi pārokṣyam asādhu te kṛtam
BhP krūras tvam akrūrasamākhyayā sma naś
BhP cakṣur hi dattaṃ harase batājñavat
BhP yenaikadeśe 'khilasargasauṣṭhavaṃ
BhP tvadīyam adrākṣma vayaṃ madhudviṣaḥ
BhP na nandasūnuḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasauhṛdaḥ
BhP samīkṣate naḥ svakṛtāturā bata
BhP vihāya gehān svajanān sutān patīṃs
BhP taddāsyam addhopagatā navapriyaḥ
BhP sukhaṃ prabhātā rajanīyam āśiṣaḥ satyā babhūvuḥ purayoṣitāṃ dhruvam
BhP yāḥ saṃpraviṣṭasya mukhaṃ vrajaspateḥ pāsyanty apāṅgotkalitasmitāsavam
BhP tāsāṃ mukundo madhumañjubhāṣitair
BhP gṛhītacittaḥ paravān manasvy api
BhP kathaṃ punar naḥ pratiyāsyate 'balā
BhP grāmyāḥ salajjasmitavibhramair bhraman
BhP adya dhruvaṃ tatra dṛśo bhaviṣyate dāśārhabhojāndhakavṛṣṇisātvatām
BhP mahotsavaḥ śrīramaṇaṃ guṇāspadaṃ drakṣyanti ye cādhvani devakīsutam
BhP maitadvidhasyākaruṇasya nāma bhūd akrūra ity etad atīva dāruṇaḥ
BhP yo 'sāv anāśvāsya suduḥkhitam janaṃ priyāt priyaṃ neṣyati pāram adhvanaḥ
BhP anārdradhīr eṣa samāsthito rathaṃ tam anv amī ca tvarayanti durmadāḥ
BhP gopā anobhiḥ sthavirair upekṣitaṃ daivaṃ ca no 'dya pratikūlam īhate
BhP nivārayāmaḥ samupetya mādhavaṃ kiṃ no 'kariṣyan kulavṛddhabāndhavāḥ
BhP mukundasaṅgān nimiṣārdhadustyajād daivena vidhvaṃsitadīnacetasām
BhP yasyānurāgalalitasmitavalgumantra
BhP līlāvalokaparirambhaṇarāsagoṣṭhām
BhP nītāḥ sma naḥ kṣaṇam iva kṣaṇadā vinā taṃ
BhP gopyaḥ kathaṃ nv atitarema tamo durantam
BhP yo 'hnaḥ kṣaye vrajam anantasakhaḥ parīto
BhP gopair viśan khurarajaśchuritālakasrak
BhP veṇuṃ kvaṇan smitakatākṣanirīkṣaṇena
BhP cittaṃ kṣiṇoty amum ṛte nu kathaṃ bhavema
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ bruvāṇā virahāturā bhṛśaṃ vrajastriyaḥ kṛṣṇaviṣaktamānasāḥ
BhP visṛjya lajjāṃ ruruduḥ sma susvaraṃ govinda dāmodara mādhaveti
BhP strīṇām evaṃ rudantīnām udite savitary atha
BhP akrūraś codayām āsa kṛtamaitrādiko ratham
BhP gopās tam anvasajjanta nandādyāḥ śakaṭais tataḥ
BhP ādāyopāyanaṃ bhūri kumbhān gorasasambhṛtān
BhP gopyaś ca dayitaṃ kṛṣṇam anuvrajyānurañjitāḥ
BhP pratyādeśaṃ bhagavataḥ kāṅkṣantyaś cāvatasthire
BhP tās tathā tapyatīr vīkṣya svaprasthāṇe yadūttamaḥ
BhP sāntvayām asa sapremair āyāsya iti dautyakaiḥ
BhP yāvad ālakṣyate ketur yāvad reṇū rathasya ca
BhP anuprasthāpitātmāno lekhyānīvopalakṣitāḥ
BhP tā nirāśā nivavṛtur govindavinivartane
BhP viśokā ahanī ninyur gāyantyaḥ priyaceṣṭitam
BhP bhagavān api samprāpto rāmākrūrayuto nṛpa
BhP rathena vāyuvegena kālindīm aghanāśinīm
BhP tatropaspṛśya pānīyaṃ pītvā mṛṣṭaṃ maṇiprabham
BhP vṛkṣaṣaṇḍam upavrajya sarāmo ratham āviśat
BhP akrūras tāv upāmantrya niveśya ca rathopari
BhP kālindyā hradam āgatya snānaṃ vidhivad ācarat
BhP nimajjya tasmin salile japan brahma sanātanam
BhP tāv eva dadṛśe 'krūro rāmakṛṣṇau samanvitau
BhP tau rathasthau katham iha sutāv ānakadundubheḥ
BhP tarhi svit syandane na sta ity unmajjya vyacaṣṭa saḥ
BhP tatrāpi ca yathāpūrvam āsīnau punar eva saḥ
BhP nyamajjad darśanaṃ yan me mṛṣā kiṃ salile tayoḥ
BhP bhūyas tatrāpi so 'drākṣīt stūyamānam ahīśvaram
BhP siddhacāraṇagandharvair asurair natakandharaiḥ
BhP sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ sahasraphaṇamaulinam

BhP kaṭisūtrabrahmasūtra hāranūpurakuṇḍalaiḥ

BhP sunandanandapramukhaiḥ parṣadaiḥ sanakādibhiḥ
BhP sureśair brahmarudrādyair navabhiś ca dvijottamaiḥ
BhP prahrādanāradavasu pramukhair bhāgavatottamaiḥ
BhP stūyamānaṃ pṛthagbhāvair vacobhir amalātmabhiḥ
BhP śriyā puṣṭyā girā kāntyā kīrtyā tuṣṭyelayorjayā
BhP vidyayāvidyayā śaktyā māyayā ca niṣevitam

BhP praṇamya mūrdhnāvahitaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ śanaiḥ
BhP śrīakrūra uvāca
BhP nato 'smy ahaṃ tvākhilahetuhetuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ pūruṣam ādyam avyayam
BhP yannābhijātād aravindakoṣād brahmāvirāsīd yata eṣa lokaḥ
BhP bhūs toyam agniḥ pavanaṃ kham ādir mahān ajādir mana indriyāṇi
BhP sarvendriyārthā vibudhāś ca sarve ye hetavas te jagato 'ṅgabhūtāḥ
BhP naite svarūpaṃ vidur ātmanas te hy ajādayo 'nātmatayā gṛhītaḥ
BhP ajo 'nubaddhaḥ sa guṇair ajāyā guṇāt paraṃ veda na te svarūpam
BhP tvāṃ yogino yajanty addhā mahāpuruṣam īśvaram
BhP sādhyātmaṃ sādhibhūtaṃ ca sādhidaivaṃ ca sādhavaḥ
BhP trayyā ca vidyayā kecit tvāṃ vai vaitānikā dvijāḥ
BhP yajante vitatair yajñair nānārūpāmarākhyayā
BhP eke tvākhilakarmāṇi sannyasyopaśamaṃ gatāḥ
BhP jñānino jñānayajñena yajanti jñānavigraham
BhP anye ca saṃskṛtātmāno vidhinābhihitena te
BhP yajanti tvanmayās tvāṃ vai bahumūrtyekamūrtikam
BhP tvām evānye śivoktena mārgeṇa śivarūpiṇam
BhP bahvācāryavibhedena bhagavantarn upāsate
BhP sarva eva yajanti tvāṃ sarvadevamayeśvaram
BhP ye 'py anyadevatābhaktā yady apy anyadhiyaḥ prabho
BhP yathādriprabhavā nadyaḥ parjanyāpūritāḥ prabho
BhP viśanti sarvataḥ sindhuṃ tadvat tvāṃ gatayo 'ntataḥ
BhP sattvaṃ rajas tama iti bhavataḥ prakṛter guṇāḥ
BhP teṣu hi prākṛtāḥ protā ābrahmasthāvarādayaḥ
BhP tubhyaṃ namas te tv aviṣaktadṛṣṭaye

BhP pravartate devanṛtiryagātmasu

BhP dyauḥ kaṃ surendrās tava bāhavo 'rṇavāḥ
BhP kukṣir marut prāṇabalaṃ prakalpitam

BhP nimeṣaṇaṃ rātryahanī prajāpatir

BhP yathā jale sañjihate jalaukaso 'py udumbare vā maśakā manomaye
BhP yāni yānīha rūpāṇi krīḍanārthaṃ bibharṣi hi
BhP tair āmṛṣṭaśuco lokā mudā gāyanti te yaśaḥ
BhP namaḥ kāraṇamatsyāya pralayābdhicarāya ca
BhP hayaśīrṣṇe namas tubhyaṃ madhukaiṭabhamṛtyave
BhP akūpārāya bṛhate namo mandaradhāriṇe
BhP kṣityuddhāravihārāya namaḥ śūkaramūrtaye
BhP namas te 'dbhutasiṃhāya sādhulokabhayāpaha
BhP vāmanāya namas tubhyaṃ krāntatribhuvanāya ca
BhP namo bhṛguṇāṃ pataye dṛptakṣatravanacchide
BhP namas te raghuvaryāya rāvaṇāntakarāya ca
BhP namas te vāsudevāya namaḥ saṅkarṣaṇāya ca
BhP pradyumnāyaniruddhāya sātvatāṃ pataye namaḥ
BhP namo buddhāya śuddhāya daityadānavamohine
BhP mlecchaprāyakṣatrahantre namas te kalkirūpiṇe
BhP bhagavan jīvaloko 'yaṃ mohitas tava māyayā
BhP ahaṃ mamety asadgrāho bhrāmyate karmavartmasu
BhP ahaṃ cātmātmajāgāra dārārthasvajanādiṣu
BhP bhramāmi svapnakalpeṣu mūḍhaḥ satyadhiyā vibho
BhP anityānātmaduḥkheṣu viparyayamatir hy aham
BhP dvandvārāmas tamoviṣṭo na jāne tvātmanaḥ priyam
BhP yathābudho jalaṃ hitvā praticchannaṃ tadudbhavaiḥ
BhP abhyeti mṛgatṛṣṇāṃ vai tadvat tvāhaṃ parāṅmukhaḥ
BhP notsahe 'haṃ kṛpaṇadhīḥ kāmakarmahataṃ manaḥ
BhP roddhuṃ pramāthibhiś cākṣair hriyamāṇam itas tataḥ
BhP so 'haṃ tavāṅghryupagato 'smy asatāṃ durāpaṃ
BhP tac cāpy ahaṃ bhavadanugraha īśa manye
BhP puṃso bhaved yarhi saṃsaraṇāpavargas
BhP tvayy abjanābha sadupāsanayā matiḥ syāt
BhP namo vijñānamātrāya sarvapratyayahetave

BhP namas te vāsudevāya sarvabhūtakṣayāya ca
BhP hṛṣīkeśa namas tubhyaṃ prapannaṃ pāhi māṃ prabho
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP stuvatas tasya bhagavān darśayitvā jale vapuḥ
BhP bhūyaḥ samāharat kṛṣṇo naṭo nāṭyam ivātmanaḥ
BhP so 'pi cāntarhitaṃ vīkṣya jalād unmajya satvaraḥ
BhP kṛtvā cāvaśyakaṃ sarvaṃ vismito ratham āgamat
BhP tam apṛcchad dhṛṣīkeśaḥ kiṃ te dṛṣṭam ivādbhutam
BhP bhūmau viyati toye vā tathā tvāṃ lakṣayāmahe
BhP śrīakrūra uvāca
BhP adbhutānīha yāvanti bhūmau viyati vā jale
BhP tvayi viśvātmake tāni kiṃ me 'dṛṣṭaṃ vipaśyataḥ
BhP yatrādbhutāni sarvāṇi bhūmau viyati vā jale
BhP taṃ tvānupaśyato brahman kiṃ me dṛṣṭam ihādbhutam
BhP ity uktvā codayām āsa syandanaṃ gāndinīsutaḥ
BhP mathurām anayad rāmaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ caiva dinātyaye
BhP mārge grāmajanā rājaṃs tatra tatropasaṅgatāḥ
BhP vasudevasutau vīkṣya prītā dṛṣṭiṃ na cādaduḥ
BhP tāvad vrajaukasas tatra nandagopādayo 'grataḥ
BhP puropavanam āsādya pratīkṣanto 'vatasthire

BhP gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇiṃ praśritaṃ prahasann iva
BhP bhavān praviśatām agre sahayānaḥ purīṃ gṛham
BhP vayaṃ tv ihāvamucyātha tato drakṣyāmahe purīm
BhP śrīakrūra uvāca
BhP nāhaṃ bhavadbhyāṃ rahitaḥ pravekṣye mathurāṃ prabho
BhP tyaktuṃ nārhasi māṃ nātha bhaktaṃ te bhaktavatsala
BhP āgaccha yāma gehān naḥ sanāthān kurv adhokṣaja
BhP sahāgrajaḥ sagopālaiḥ suhṛdbhiś ca suhṛttama
BhP punīhi pādarajasā gṛhān no gṛhamedhinām
BhP yacchaucenānutṛpyanti pitaraḥ sāgnayaḥ surāḥ
BhP avanijyāṅghriyugalam āsīt ślokyo balir mahān

BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evam ukto bhagavatā so 'krūro vimanā iva

BhP athāparāhne bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ saṅkarṣaṇānvitaḥ
BhP mathurāṃ prāviśad gopair didṛkṣuḥ parivāritaḥ
BhP dadarśa tāṃ sphāṭikatuṇgagopura dvārāṃ bṛhaddhemakapāṭatoraṇām

BhP manāṃsi tāsām aravindalocanaḥ pragalbhalīlāhasitāvalokaiḥ

BhP tāv ānarcuḥ pramuditās tatra tatra dvijātayaḥ
BhP ūcuḥ paurā aho gopyas tapaḥ kim acaran mahat

BhP rajakaṃ kañcid āyāntaṃ raṅgakāraṃ gadāgrajaḥ

BhP bhaviṣyati paraṃ śreyo dātus te nātra saṃśayaḥ
BhP sa yācito bhagavatā paripūrṇena sarvataḥ
BhP sākṣepaṃ ruṣitaḥ prāha bhṛtyo rājñaḥ sudurmadaḥ
BhP īdṛśāny eva vāsāṃsī nityaṃ girivanecaraḥ
BhP paridhatta kim udvṛttā rājadravyāṇy abhīpsatha

BhP rajakasya karāgreṇa śiraḥ kāyād apātayat

BhP vicitravarṇaiś caileyair ākalpair anurūpataḥ

BhP śriyaṃ ca paramāṃ loke balaiśvaryasmṛtīndriyam
BhP tataḥ sudāmno bhavanaṃ mālākārasya jagmatuḥ
BhP tau dṛṣṭvā sa samutthāya nanāma śirasā bhuvi

BhP pūjāṃ sānugayoś cakre sraktāmbūlānulepanaiḥ
BhP prāha naḥ sārthakaṃ janma pāvitaṃ ca kulaṃ prabho

BhP samayoḥ sarvabhūteṣu bhajantaṃ bhajator api

BhP tayos tad adbhutaṃ vīryaṃ niśāmya puravāsinaḥ
BhP tejaḥ prāgalbhyaṃ rūpaṃ ca menire vibudhottamau
BhP tayor vicaratoḥ svairam ādityo 'stam upeyivān
BhP kṛṣṇarāmau vṛtau gopaiḥ purāc chakaṭam īyatuḥ
BhP gopyo mukundavigame virahāturā yā āśāsatāśiṣa ṛtā madhupury abhūvan
BhP sampaśyatāṃ puruṣabhūṣaṇagātralakṣmīṃ hitvetarān nu bhajataś cakame 'yanaṃ śrīḥ
BhP avaniktāṅghriyugalau bhuktvā kṣīropasecanam
BhP ūṣatus tāṃ sukhaṃ rātriṃ jñātvā kaṃsacikīrṣitam
BhP kaṃsas tu dhanuṣo bhaṅgaṃ rakṣiṇāṃ svabalasya ca
BhP vadhaṃ niśamya govinda rāmavikrīḍitaṃ param
BhP dīrghaprajāgaro bhīto durnimittāni durmatiḥ
BhP bahūny acaṣṭobhayathā mṛtyor dautyakarāṇi ca
BhP adarśanaṃ svaśirasaḥ pratirūpe ca saty api
BhP asaty api dvitīye ca dvairūpyaṃ jyotiṣāṃ tathā
BhP chidrapratītiś chāyāyāṃ prāṇaghoṣānupaśrutiḥ
BhP svarṇapratītir vṛkṣeṣu svapadānām adarśanam
BhP svapne pretapariṣvaṅgaḥ kharayānaṃ viṣādanam
BhP yāyān naladamāly ekas tailābhyakto digambaraḥ
BhP anyāni cetthaṃbhūtāni svapnajāgaritāni ca
BhP paśyan maraṇasantrasto nidrāṃ lebhe na cintayā
BhP vyuṣṭāyāṃ niśi kauravya sūrye cādbhyaḥ samutthite
BhP kārayām āsa vai kaṃso mallakrīḍāmahotsavam
BhP ānarcuḥ puruṣā raṅgaṃ tūryabheryaś ca jaghnire
BhP mañcāś cālaṅkṛtāḥ sragbhiḥ patākācailatoraṇaiḥ
BhP teṣu paurā jānapadā brahmakṣatrapurogamāḥ
BhP yathopajoṣaṃ viviśū rājānaś ca kṛtāsanāḥ
BhP kaṃsaḥ parivṛto 'mātyai rājamañca upāviśat
BhP maṇḍaleśvaramadhyastho hṛdayena vidūyatā
BhP vādyamānesu tūryeṣu mallatālottareṣu ca
BhP mallāḥ svalaṅkṛtāḥ dṛptāḥ sopādhyāyāḥ samāsata
BhP cāṇūro muṣṭikaḥ kūtaḥ śalas tośala eva ca
BhP ta āsedur upasthānaṃ valguvādyapraharṣitāḥ
BhP nandagopādayo gopā bhojarājasamāhutāḥ
BhP niveditopāyanās ta ekasmin mañca āviśan
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP atha kṛṣṇaś ca rāmaś ca kṛtaśaucau parantapa
BhP malladundubhinirghoṣaṃ śrutvā draṣṭum upeyatuḥ
BhP raṅgadvāraṃ samāsādya tasmin nāgam avasthitam
BhP apaśyat kuvalayāpīḍaṃ kṛṣṇo 'mbaṣṭhapracoditam
BhP baddhvā parikaraṃ śauriḥ samuhya kuṭilālakān
BhP uvāca hastipaṃ vācā meghanādagabhīrayā
BhP ambaṣṭhāmbaṣṭha mārgaṃ nau dehy apakrama mā ciram
BhP no cet sakuñjaraṃ tvādya nayāmi yamasādanam
BhP evaṃ nirbhartsito 'mbaṣṭhaḥ kupitaḥ kopitaṃ gajam
BhP codayām āsa kṛṣṇāya kālāntakayamopamam
BhP karīndras tam abhidrutya kareṇa tarasāgrahīt
BhP karād vigalitaḥ so 'muṃ nihatyāṅghriṣv alīyata
BhP saṅkruddhas tam acakṣāṇo ghrāṇadṛṣṭiḥ sa keśavam
BhP parāmṛśat puṣkareṇa sa prasahya vinirgataḥ
BhP pucche pragṛhyātibalaṃ dhanuṣaḥ pañcaviṃśatim
BhP vicakarṣa yathā nāgaṃ suparṇa iva līlayā
BhP sa paryāvartamānena savyadakṣiṇato 'cyutaḥ
BhP babhrāma bhrāmyamāṇena govatseneva bālakaḥ
BhP tato 'bhimakham abhyetya pāṇināhatya vāraṇam
BhP prādravan pātayām āsa spṛśyamānaḥ pade pade
BhP sa dhāvan kṛīdayā bhūmau patitvā sahasotthitaḥ
BhP tam matvā patitaṃ kruddho dantābhyāṃ so 'hanat kṣitim
BhP svavikrame pratihate kuñjarendro 'tyamarṣitaḥ
BhP codyamāno mahāmātraiḥ kṛṣṇam abhyadravad ruṣā
BhP tam āpatantam āsādya bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ
BhP nigṛhya pāṇinā hastaṃ pātayām āsa bhūtale
BhP patitasya padākramya mṛgendra iva līlayā
BhP dantam utpāṭya tenebhaṃ hastipāṃś cāhanad dhariḥ
BhP mṛtakaṃ dvipam utsṛjya dantapāṇiḥ samāviśat
BhP aṃsanyastaviṣāṇo 'sṛṅ madabindubhir aṅkitaḥ
BhP virūḍhasvedakaṇikā vadanāmburuho babhau
BhP vṛtau gopaiḥ katipayair baladevajanārdanau
BhP raṅgaṃ viviśatū rājan gajadantavarāyudhau
BhP mallānām aśanir nṛṇāṃ naravaraḥ strīṇāṃ smaro mūrtimān
BhP gopānāṃ svajano 'satāṃ kṣitibhujāṃ śāstā svapitroḥ śiśuḥ
BhP mṛtyur bhojapater virāḍ aviduṣāṃ tattvaṃ paraṃ yogināṃ
BhP vṛṣṇīnāṃ paradevateti vidito raṅgaṃ gataḥ sāgrajaḥ
BhP hataṃ kuvalayāpīḍaṃ dṛṣṭvā tāv api durjayau
BhP kaṃso manasy api tadā bhṛśam udvivije nṛpa
BhP tau rejatū raṅgagatau mahābhujau vicitraveṣābharaṇasragambarau
BhP yathā naṭāv uttamaveṣadhāriṇau manaḥ kṣipantau prabhayā nirīkṣatām
BhP nirīkṣya tāv uttamapūruṣau janā mañcasthitā nāgararāṣṭrakā nṛpa
BhP praharṣavegotkalitekṣaṇānanāḥ papur na tṛptā nayanais tadānanam
BhP pibanta iva cakṣurbhyāṃ lihanta iva jihvayā
BhP jighranta iva nāsābhyāṃ śliṣyanta iva bāhubhiḥ
BhP ūcuḥ parasparaṃ te vai yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam
BhP tadrūpaguṇamādhurya prāgalbhyasmāritā iva
BhP etau bhagavataḥ sākṣād dharer nārāyaṇasya hi
BhP avatīrṇāv ihāṃśena vasudevasya veśmani
BhP eṣa vai kila devakyāṃ jāto nītaś ca gokulam
BhP kālam etaṃ vasan gūḍho vavṛdhe nandaveśmani
BhP pūtanānena nītāntaṃ cakravātaś ca dānavaḥ
BhP arjunau guhyakaḥ keśī dhenuko 'nye ca tadvidhāḥ
BhP gāvaḥ sapālā etena dāvāgneḥ parimocitāḥ
BhP kāliyo damitaḥ sarpa indraś ca vimadaḥ kṛtaḥ
BhP saptāham ekahastena dhṛto 'dripravaro 'munā
BhP varṣavātāśanibhyaś ca paritrātaṃ ca gokulam
BhP gopyo 'sya nityamudita hasitaprekṣaṇaṃ mukham
BhP paśyantyo vividhāṃs tāpāṃs taranti smāśramaṃ mudā
BhP vadanty anena vaṃśo 'yaṃ yadoḥ subahuviśrutaḥ
BhP śriyaṃ yaśo mahatvaṃ ca lapsyate parirakṣitaḥ
BhP ayaṃ cāsyāgrajaḥ śrīmān rāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ
BhP pralambo nihato yena vatsako ye bakādayaḥ
BhP janeṣv evaṃ bruvāṇeṣu tūryeṣu ninadatsu ca
BhP kṛṣṇarāmau samābhāṣya cāṇūro vākyam abravīt
BhP he nandasūno he rāma bhavantau vīrasammatau
BhP niyuddhakuśalau śrutvā rājñāhūtau didṛkṣuṇā
BhP priyaṃ rājñaḥ prakurvatyaḥ śreyo vindanti vai prajāḥ
BhP manasā karmaṇā vācā viparītam ato 'nyathā
BhP nityaṃ pramuditā gopā vatsapālā yathāsphuṭam
BhP vaneṣu mallayuddhena krīḍantaś cārayanti gāḥ
BhP tasmād rājñaḥ priyaṃ yūyaṃ vayaṃ ca karavāma he
BhP bhūtāni naḥ prasīdanti sarvabhūtamayo nṛpaḥ
BhP tan niśamyābravīt kṛṣṇo deśakālocitaṃ vacaḥ
BhP niyuddham ātmano 'bhīṣṭaṃ manyamāno 'bhinandya ca
BhP prajā bhojapater asya vayaṃ cāpi vanecarāḥ
BhP karavāma priyaṃ nityaṃ tan naḥ param anugrahaḥ
BhP bālā vayaṃ tulyabalaiḥ krīḍiṣyāmo yathocitam
BhP bhaven niyuddhaṃ mādharmaḥ spṛśen mallasabhāsadaḥ
BhP cāṇūra uvāca
BhP na bālo na kiśoras tvaṃ balaś ca balināṃ varaḥ
BhP līlayebho hato yena sahasradvipasattvabhṛt
BhP tasmād bhavadbhyāṃ balibhir yoddhavyaṃ nānayo 'tra vai
BhP mayi vikrama vārṣṇeya balena saha muṣṭikaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ carcitasaṅkalpo bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ
BhP āsasādātha caṇūraṃ muṣṭtikaṃ rohiṇīsutaḥ
BhP hastābhyāṃ hastayor baddhvā padbhyām eva ca pādayoḥ
BhP vicakarṣatur anyonyaṃ prasahya vijigīṣayā
BhP aratnī dve aratnibhyāṃ jānubhyāṃ caiva jānunī
BhP śiraḥ śīrṣṇorasoras tāv anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
BhP paribhrāmaṇavikṣepa parirambhāvapātanaiḥ
BhP utsarpaṇāpasarpaṇaiś cānyonyaṃ pratyarundhatām
BhP utthāpanair unnayanaiś cālanaiḥ sthāpanair api
BhP parasparaṃ jigīṣantāv apacakratur ātmanaḥ
BhP tad balābalavad yuddhaṃ sametāḥ sarvayoṣitaḥ
BhP ūcuḥ parasparaṃ rājan sānukampā varūthaśaḥ
BhP mahān ayaṃ batādharma eṣāṃ rājasabhāsadām
BhP ye balābalavad yuddhaṃ rājño 'nvicchanti paśyataḥ
BhP kva vajrasārasarvāṅgau mallau śailendrasannibhau
BhP kva cātisukumārāṅgau kiśorau nāptayauvanau
BhP dharmavyatikramo hy asya samājasya dhruvaṃ bhavet
BhP yatrādharmaḥ samuttiṣṭhen na stheyaṃ tatra karhicit
BhP na sabhāṃ praviśet prājñaḥ sabhyadoṣān anusmaran
BhP abruvan vibruvann ajño naraḥ kilbiṣam aśnute
BhP valgataḥ śatrum abhitaḥ kṛṣṇasya vadanāmbujam
BhP vīkṣyatāṃ śramavāryuptaṃ padmakośam ivāmbubhiḥ
BhP kiṃ na paśyata rāmasya mukham ātāmralocanam
BhP muṣṭikaṃ prati sāmarṣaṃ hāsasaṃrambhaśobhitam
BhP puṇyā bata vrajabhuvo yad ayaṃ nṛliṅga
BhP gūḍhaḥ purāṇapuruṣo vanacitramālyaḥ
BhP gāḥ pālayan sahabalaḥ kvaṇayaṃś ca veṇuṃ
BhP vikrīdayāñcati giritraramārcitāṅghriḥ
BhP gopyas tapaḥ kim acaran yad amuṣya rūpaṃ
BhP lāvaṇyasāram asamordhvam ananyasiddham
BhP dṛgbhiḥ pibanty anusavābhinavaṃ durāpam
BhP ekāntadhāma yaśasaḥ śrīya aiśvarasya
BhP yā dohane 'vahanane mathanopalepa preṅkheṅkhanārbharuditokṣaṇamārjanādau
BhP gāyanti cainam anuraktadhiyo 'śrukaṇṭhyo dhanyā vrajastriya urukramacittayānāḥ
BhP prātar vrajād vrajata āviśataś ca sāyaṃ
BhP gobhiḥ samaṃ kvaṇayato 'sya niśamya veṇum
BhP nirgamya tūrṇam abalāḥ pathi bhūripuṇyāḥ
BhP paśyanti sasmitamukhaṃ sadayāvalokam
BhP evaṃ prabhāṣamāṇāsu strīṣu yogeśvaro hariḥ
BhP śatruṃ hantuṃ manaś cakre bhagavān bharatarṣabha
BhP sabhayāḥ strīgiraḥ śrutvā putrasnehaśucāturau
BhP pitarāv anvatapyetāṃ putrayor abudhau balam
BhP tais tair niyuddhavidhibhir vividhair acyutetarau
BhP yuyudhāte yathānyonyaṃ tathaiva balamuṣṭikau
BhP bhagavadgātraniṣpātair vajranīṣpeṣaniṣṭhuraiḥ
BhP cāṇūro bhajyamānāṅgo muhur glānim avāpa ha
BhP sa śyenavega utpatya muṣṭīkṛtya karāv ubhau
BhP bhagavantaṃ vāsudevaṃ kruddho vakṣasy abādhata
BhP nācalat tatprahāreṇa mālāhata iva dvipaḥ
BhP bāhvor nigṛhya cāṇūraṃ bahuśo bhrāmayan hariḥ
BhP bhūpṛṣṭhe pothayām āsa tarasā kṣīṇa jīvitam
BhP visrastākalpakeśasrag indradhvaja ivāpatat
BhP tathaiva muṣṭikaḥ pūrvaṃ svamuṣṭyābhihatena vai
BhP balabhadreṇa balinā talenābhihato bhṛśam
BhP pravepitaḥ sa rudhiram udvaman mukhato 'rditaḥ
BhP vyasuḥ papātorvyupasthe vātāhata ivāṅghripaḥ
BhP tataḥ kūṭam anuprāptaṃ rāmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
BhP avadhīl līlayā rājan sāvajñaṃ vāmamuṣṭinā
BhP tarhy eva hi śalaḥ kṛṣṇa prapadāhataśīrṣakaḥ
BhP dvidhā vidīrṇas tośalaka ubhāv api nipetatuḥ
BhP cāṇūre muṣṭike kūṭe śale tośalake hate
BhP śeṣāḥ pradudruvur mallāḥ sarve prāṇaparīpsavaḥ
BhP gopān vayasyān ākṛṣya taiḥ saṃsṛjya vijahratuḥ
BhP vādyamāneṣu tūryeṣu valgantau rutanūpurau
BhP janāḥ prajahṛṣuḥ sarve karmaṇā rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP ṛte kaṃsaṃ vipramukhyāḥ sādhavaḥ sādhu sādhv iti
BhP hateṣu mallavaryeṣu vidruteṣu ca bhojarāṭ
BhP nyavārayat svatūryāṇi vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha
BhP niḥsārayata durvṛttau vasudevātmajau purāt
BhP dhanaṃ harata gopānāṃ nandaṃ badhnīta durmatim
BhP vasudevas tu durmedhā hanyatām āśv asattamaḥ
BhP ugrasenaḥ pitā cāpi sānugaḥ parapakṣagaḥ
BhP evaṃ vikatthamāne vai kaṃse prakupito 'vyayaḥ
BhP laghimnotpatya tarasā mañcam uttuṅgam āruhat
BhP tam āviśantam ālokya mṛtyum ātmana āsanāt
BhP manasvī sahasotthāya jagṛhe so 'sicarmaṇī
BhP taṃ khaḍgapāṇiṃ vicarantam āśu śyenaṃ yathā dakṣiṇasavyam ambare
BhP samagrahīd durviṣahogratejā yathoragaṃ tārkṣyasutaḥ prasahya
BhP pragṛhya keśeṣu calatkirītaṃ nipātya raṅgopari tuṅgamañcāt

BhP abhyadhāvann atikruddhā bhrātur nirveśakāriṇaḥ

BhP ahan parigham udyamya paśūn iva mṛgādhipaḥ
BhP nedur dundubhayo vyomni brahmeśādyā vibhūtayaḥ
BhP puṣpaiḥ kirantas taṃ prītāḥ śaśaṃsur nanṛtuḥ striyaḥ
BhP teṣāṃ striyo mahārāja suhṛnmaraṇaduḥkhitāḥ
BhP tatrābhīyur vinighnantyaḥ śīrṣāṇy aśruvilocanāḥ
BhP śayānān vīraśayāyāṃ patīn āliṅgya śocatīḥ
BhP vilepuḥ susvaraṃ nāryo visṛjantyo muhuḥ śucaḥ
BhP hā nātha priya dharmajña karuṇānāthavatsala

BhP tvayā virahitā patyā purīyaṃ puruṣarṣabha

BhP goptā ca tadavadhyāyī na kvacit sukham edhate

BhP yām āhur laukikīṃ saṃsthāṃ hatānāṃ samakārayat
BhP mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva mocayitvātha bandhanāt

BhP devakī vasudevaś ca vijñāya jagadīśvarau

BhP śrīśuka uvāca

BhP mā bhūd iti nijāṃ māyāṃ tatāna janamohinīm
BhP uvāca pitarāv etya sāgrajaḥ sātvanarṣabhaḥ
BhP praśrayāvanataḥ prīṇann amba tāteti sādaram
BhP nāsmatto yuvayos tāta nityotkaṇṭhitayor api

BhP na tayor yāti nirveśaṃ pitror martyaḥ śatāyuṣā
BhP yas tayor ātmajaḥ kalpa ātmanā ca dhanena ca
BhP vṛttiṃ na dadyāt taṃ pretya svamāṃsaṃ khādayanti hi
BhP mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vṛddhaṃ bhāryāṃ sādhvīṃ sutam śiśum
BhP guruṃ vipraṃ prapannaṃ ca kalpo 'bibhrac chvasanmṛtaḥ
BhP tan nāv akalpayoḥ kaṃsān nityam udvignacetasoḥ
BhP mogham ete vyatikrāntā divasā vām anarcatoḥ
BhP tat kṣantum arhathas tāta mātar nau paratantrayoḥ
BhP akurvator vāṃ śuśrūṣāṃ kliṣṭayor durhṛdā bhṛśam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti māyāmanuṣyasya harer viśvātmano girā
BhP mohitāv aṅkam āropya pariṣvajyāpatur mudam
BhP siñcantāv aśrudhārābhiḥ snehapāśena cāvṛtau
BhP na kiñcid ūcatū rājan bāṣpakaṇṭhau vimohitau
BhP evam āśvāsya pitarau bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP mātāmahaṃ tūgrasenaṃ yadūnām akaron ṇṛpam
