BhP yayātiśāpād yadubhir nāsitavyaṃ nṛpāsane
BhP mayi bhṛtya upāsīne bhavato vibudhādayaḥ
BhP baliṃ haranty avanatāḥ kim utānye narādhipāḥ
BhP sarvān svān jñatisambandhān digbhyaḥ kaṃsabhayākulān
BhP yaduvṛṣṇyandhakamadhu dāśārhakukurādikān
BhP sabhājitān samāśvāsya videśāvāsakarśitān
BhP nyavāsayat svageheṣu vittaiḥ santarpya viśvakṛt
BhP kṛṣṇasaṅkarṣaṇabhujair guptā labdhamanorathāḥ
BhP gṛheṣu remire siddhāḥ kṛṣṇarāmagatajvarāḥ
BhP vīkṣanto 'har ahaḥ prītā mukundavadanāmbujam
BhP nityaṃ pramuditaṃ śrīmat sadayasmitavīkṣaṇam
BhP tatra pravayaso 'py āsan yuvāno 'tibalaujasaḥ
BhP pibanto 'kṣair mukundasya mukhāmbujasudhāṃ muhuḥ
BhP atha nandaṃ samasādya bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP saṅkarṣaṇaś ca rājendra pariṣvajyedam ūcatuḥ
BhP pitar yuvābhyāṃ snigdhābhyāṃ poṣitau lālitau bhṛśam
BhP pitror abhyadhikā prītir ātmajeṣv ātmano 'pi hi
BhP sa pitā sā ca jananī yau puṣṇītāṃ svaputravat
BhP śiśūn bandhubhir utsṛṣṭān akalpaiḥ poṣarakṣaṇe
BhP yāta yūyaṃ vrajaṃn tāta vayaṃ ca snehaduḥkhitān
BhP jñātīn vo draṣṭum eṣyāmo vidhāya suhṛdāṃ sukham
BhP evaṃ sāntvayya bhagavān nandaṃ savrajam acyutaḥ
BhP vāso'laṅkārakupyādyair arhayām āsa sādaram
BhP ity uktas tau pariṣvajya nandaḥ praṇayavihvalaḥ
BhP pūrayann aśrubhir netre saha gopair vrajaṃ yayau
BhP atha śūrasuto rājan putrayoḥ samakārayat
BhP purodhasā brāhmaṇaiś ca yathāvad dvijasaṃskṛtim
BhP tebhyo 'dād dakṣiṇā gāvo rukmamālāḥ svalaṅkṛtāḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtebhyaḥ sampūjya savatsāḥ kṣaumamālinīḥ
BhP yāḥ kṛṣṇarāmajanmarkṣe manodattā mahāmatiḥ
BhP tāś cādadād anusmṛtya kaṃsenādharmato hṛtāḥ
BhP tataś ca labdhasaṃskārau dvijatvaṃ prāpya suvratau
BhP gargād yadukulācāryād gāyatraṃ vratam āsthitau
BhP prabhavau sarvavidyānāṃ sarvajñau jagadīśvarau
BhP nānyasiddhāmalaṃ jñānaṃ gūhamānau narehitaiḥ
BhP atho gurukule vāsam icchantāv upajagmatuḥ
BhP kāśyaṃ sāndīpaniṃ nāma hy avantipuravāsinam
BhP yathopasādya tau dāntau gurau vṛttim aninditām
BhP grāhayantāv upetau sma bhaktyā devam ivādṛtau
BhP tayor dvijavaras tuṣṭaḥ śuddhabhāvānuvṛttibhiḥ
BhP provāca vedān akhilān saṅgopaniṣado guruḥ
BhP sarahasyaṃ dhanurvedaṃ dharmān nyāyapathāṃs tathā
BhP tathā cānvīkṣikīṃ vidyāṃ rājanītiṃ ca ṣaḍvidhām
BhP sarvaṃ naravaraśreṣṭhau sarvavidyāpravartakau
BhP sakṛn nigadamātreṇa tau sañjagṛhatur nṛpa
BhP ahorātraiś catuḥṣaṣṭyā saṃyattau tāvatīḥ kalāḥ
BhP gurudakṣiṇayācāryaṃ chandayām āsatur nṛpa
BhP dvijas tayos taṃ mahimānam adbhutaṃ
BhP saṃlokṣya rājann atimānusīṃ matim
BhP sammantrya patnyā sa mahārṇave mṛtaṃ
BhP bālaṃ prabhāse varayāṃ babhūva ha
BhP tethety athāruhya mahārathau rathaṃ
BhP prabhāsam āsādya durantavikramau
BhP velām upavrajya niṣīdatuḥ kṣanaṃ
BhP sindhur viditvārhanam āharat tayoḥ
BhP tam āha bhagavān āśu guruputraḥ pradīyatām
BhP yo 'sāv iha tvayā grasto bālako mahatormiṇā
BhP śrīsamudra uvāca
BhP na cāhārṣam ahaṃ deva daityaḥ pañcajano mahān
BhP antarjalacaraḥ kṛṣṇa śaṅkharūpadharo 'suraḥ
BhP āste tenāhṛto nūnaṃ tac chrutvā satvaraṃ prabhuḥ
BhP jalam āviśya taṃ hatvā nāpaśyad udare 'rbhakam
BhP tadaṅgaprabhavaṃ śaṅkham ādāya ratham āgamat
BhP tataḥ saṃyamanīṃ nāma yamasya dayitāṃ purīm
BhP gatvā janārdanaḥ śaṅkhaṃ pradadhmau sahalāyudhaḥ
BhP śaṅkhanirhrādam ākarṇya prajāsaṃyamano yamaḥ
BhP tayoḥ saparyāṃ mahatīṃ cakre bhaktyupabṛṃhitām
BhP uvācāvanataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ sarvabhūtāśayālayam
BhP līlāmanuṣyayor viṣṇo yuvayoḥ karavāma kim
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP guruputram ihānītaṃ nijakarmanibandhanam
BhP ānayasva mahārāja macchāsanapuraskṛtaḥ
BhP tatheti tenopānītaṃ guruputraṃ yadūttamau
BhP dattvā svagurave bhūyo vṛṇīṣveti tam ūcatuḥ
BhP śrīgurur uvāca
BhP samyak sampādito vatsa bhavadbhyāṃ guruniṣkrayaḥ
BhP ko nu yuṣmadvidhaguroḥ kāmānām avaśiṣyate
BhP gacchataṃ svagṛhaṃ vīrau kīrtir vām astu pāvanī
BhP chandāṃsy ayātayāmāni bhavantv iha paratra ca
BhP guruṇaivam anujñātau rathenānilaraṃhasā
BhP āyātau svapuraṃ tāta parjanyaninadena vai
BhP samanandan prajāḥ sarvā dṛṣṭvā rāmajanārdanau
BhP apaśyantyo bahv ahāni naṣṭalabdhadhanā iva
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP vṛṣṇīnāṃ pravaro mantrī kṛṣṇasya dayitaḥ sakhā
BhP śiṣyo bṛhaspateḥ sākṣād uddhavo buddhisattamaḥ
BhP tam āha bhagavān preṣṭhaṃ bhaktam ekāntinaṃ kvacit
BhP gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇiṃ prapannārtiharo hariḥ
BhP gacchoddhava vrajaṃ saumya pitror nau prītim āvaha
BhP gopīnāṃ madviyogādhiṃ matsandeśair vimocaya
BhP tā manmanaskā tṛṣṭprāṇā madarthe tyaktadaihikāḥ
BhP mām eva dayitaṃ preṣṭham ātmānaṃ manasā gatāḥ
BhP ye tyaktalokadharmāś ca madarthe tān bibharmy aham
BhP mayi tāḥ preyasāṃ preṣṭhe dūrasthe gokulastriyaḥ
BhP smarantyo 'ṅga vimuhyanti virahautkaṇṭhyavihvalāḥ
BhP dhārayanty atikṛcchreṇa prāyaḥ prāṇān kathañcana
BhP pratyāgamanasandeśair ballavyo me madātmikāḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity ukta uddhavo rājan sandeśaṃ bhartur ādṛtaḥ
BhP ādāya ratham āruhya prayayau nandagokulam
BhP prāpto nandavrajaṃ śrīmān nimlocati vibhāvasau
BhP channayānaḥ praviśatāṃ paśūnāṃ khurareṇubhiḥ
BhP vāsitārthe 'bhiyudhyadbhir nāditaṃ śuśmibhir vṛṣaiḥ
BhP dhāvantībhiś ca vāsrābhir udhobhāraiḥ svavatsakān
BhP itas tato vilaṅghadbhir govatsair maṇḍitaṃ sitaiḥ
BhP godohaśabdābhiravaṃ veṇūnāṃ niḥsvanena ca
BhP gāyantībhiś ca karmāṇi śubhāni balakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtābhir gopībhir gopaiś ca suvirājitam
BhP agnyarkātithigovipra pitṛdevārcanānvitaiḥ
BhP dhūpadīpaiś ca mālyaiś ca gopāvāsair manoramam
BhP sarvataḥ puṣpitavanaṃ dvijālikulanāditam
BhP haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇaiḥ padmaṣaṇḍaiś ca maṇḍitam
BhP tam āgataṃ samāgamya kṛṣṇasyānucaraṃ priyam
BhP nandaḥ prītaḥ pariṣvajya vāsudevadhiyārcayat
BhP bhojitaṃ paramānnena saṃviṣṭaṃ kaśipau sukham
BhP gataśramaṃ paryapṛcchat pādasaṃvāhanādibhiḥ
BhP kaccid aṅga mahābhāga sakhā naḥ śūranandanaḥ
BhP āste kuśaly apatyādyair yukto muktaḥ suhṛdvrataḥ
BhP diṣṭyā kaṃso hataḥ pāpaḥ sānugaḥ svena pāpmanā
BhP sādhūnāṃ dharmaśīlānāṃ yadūnāṃ dveṣṭi yaḥ sadā
BhP api smarati naḥ kṛṣṇo mātaraṃ suhṛdaḥ sakhīn
BhP gopān vrajaṃ cātmanāthaṃ gāvo vṛndāvanaṃ girim
BhP apy āyāsyati govindaḥ svajanān sakṛd īkṣitum
BhP tarhi drakṣyāma tadvaktraṃ sunasaṃ susmitekṣaṇam
BhP dāvāgner vātavarṣāc ca vṛṣasarpāc ca rakṣitāḥ
BhP duratyayebhyo mṛtyubhyaḥ kṛṣṇena sumahātmanā
BhP smaratāṃ kṛṣṇavīryāṇi līlāpāṅganirīkṣitam
BhP hasitaṃ bhāṣitaṃ cāṅga sarvā naḥ śithilāḥ kriyāḥ
BhP saricchailavanoddeśān mukundapadabhūṣitān
BhP ākrīḍān īkṣyamāṇānāṃ mano yāti tadātmatām
BhP manye kṛṣṇaṃ ca rāmaṃ ca prāptāv iha surottamau
BhP surāṇāṃ mahadarthāya gargasya vacanaṃ yathā
BhP kaṃsaṃ nāgāyutaprāṇaṃ mallau gajapatiṃ yathā
BhP avadhiṣṭāṃ līlayaiva paśūn iva mṛgādhipaḥ
BhP tālatrayaṃ mahāsāraṃ dhanur yaṣṭim ivebharāṭ
BhP babhañjaikena hastena saptāham adadhād girim
BhP pralambo dhenuko 'riṣṭas tṛṇāvarto bakādayaḥ
BhP daityāḥ surāsurajito hatā yeneha līlayā
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya nandaḥ kṛṣṇānuraktadhīḥ
BhP atyutkaṇṭho 'bhavat tūṣṇīṃ premaprasaravihvalaḥ
BhP yaśodā varṇyamānāni putrasya caritāni ca
BhP śṛṇvanty aśrūṇy avāsrākṣīt snehasnutapayodharā
BhP tayor itthaṃ bhagavati kṛṣṇe nandayaśodayoḥ
BhP vīkṣyānurāgaṃ paramaṃ nandam āhoddhavo mudā
BhP śrīuddhava uvāca
BhP yuvāṃ ślāghyatamau nūnaṃ dehinām iha mānada
BhP nārāyaṇe 'khilagurau yat kṛtā matir īdṛśī
BhP etau hi viśvasya ca bījayonī rāmo mukundaḥ puruṣaḥ pradhānam
BhP anvīya bhūteṣu vilakṣaṇasya jñānasya ceśāta imau purāṇau
BhP yasmin janaḥ prāṇaviyogakāle kṣanaṃ samāveśya mano 'viśuddham
BhP nirhṛtya karmāśayam āśu yāti parāṃ gatiṃ brahmamayo 'rkavarṇaḥ
BhP tasmin bhavantāv akhilātmahetau nārāyaṇe kāraṇamartyamūrtau
BhP bhāvaṃ vidhattāṃ nitarāṃ mahātman kiṃ vāvaśiṣṭaṃ yuvayoḥ sukṛtyam
BhP āgamiṣyaty adīrgheṇa kālena vrajam acyutaḥ
BhP priyaṃ vidhāsyate pitror bhagavān sātvatāṃ patiḥ
BhP hatvā kaṃsaṃ raṅgamadhye pratīpaṃ sarvasātvatām
BhP yad āha vaḥ samāgatya kṛṣṇaḥ satyaṃ karoti tat
BhP mā khidyataṃ mahābhāgau drakṣyathaḥ kṛṣṇam antike
BhP antar hṛdi sa bhūtānām āste jyotir ivaidhasi
BhP na hy asyāsti priyaḥ kaścin nāpriyo vāsty amāninaḥ
BhP nottamo nādhamo vāpi samānasyāsamo 'pi vā
BhP na mātā na pitā tasya na bhāryā na sutādayaḥ
BhP nātmīyo na paraś cāpi na deho janma eva ca
BhP na cāsya karma vā loke sadasanmiśrayoniṣu
BhP krīḍārthaṃ so 'pi sādhūnāṃ paritrāṇāya kalpate
BhP sattvaṃ rajas tama iti bhajate nirguṇo guṇān
BhP krīḍann atīto 'pi guṇaiḥ sṛjaty avan hanty ajaḥ
BhP yathā bhramarikādṛṣṭyā bhrāmyatīva mahīyate
BhP citte kartari tatrātmā kartevāhaṃdhiyā smṛtaḥ
BhP yuvayor eva naivāyam ātmajo bhagavān hariḥ
BhP sarveṣām ātmajo hy ātmā pitā mātā sa īśvaraḥ
BhP dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ bhūtabhavadbhaviṣyat
BhP sthāsnuś cariṣṇur mahad alpakaṃ ca
BhP vinācyutād vastu tarāṃ na vācyaṃ
BhP sa eva sarvaṃ paramātmabhūtaḥ
BhP evaṃ niśā sā bruvator vyatītā nandasya kṛṣṇānucarasya rājan
BhP gopyaḥ samutthāya nirūpya dīpān vāstūn samabhyarcya daudhīny amanthun
BhP tā dīpadīptair maṇibhir virejū rajjūr vikarṣadbhujakaṅkaṇasrajaḥ
BhP calannitambastanahārakuṇḍala tviṣatkapolāruṇakuṅkumānanāḥ
BhP udgāyatīnām aravindalocanaṃ vrajāṅganānāṃ divam aspṛśad dhvaniḥ
BhP dadhnaś ca nirmanthanaśabdamiśrito nirasyate yena diśām amaṅgalam
BhP bhagavaty udite sūrye nandadvāri vrajaukasaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā rathaṃ śātakaumbhaṃ kasyāyam iti cābruvan
BhP akrūra āgataḥ kiṃ vā yaḥ kaṃsasyārthasādhakaḥ
BhP yena nīto madhupurīṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kamalalocanaḥ
BhP kiṃ sādhayiṣyaty asmābhir bhartuḥ prītasya niṣkṛtim
BhP tataḥ strīṇāṃ vadantīnām uddhavo 'gāt kṛtāhnikaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP taṃ vīkṣya kṛṣānucaraṃ vrajastriyaḥ
BhP pralambabāhuṃ navakañjalocanam
BhP pītāmbaraṃ puṣkaramālinaṃ lasan
BhP mukhāravindaṃ parimṛṣṭakuṇḍalam
BhP suvismitāḥ ko 'yam apīvyadarśanaḥ
BhP kutaś ca kasyācyutaveṣabhūṣaṇaḥ
BhP iti sma sarvāḥ parivavrur utsukās
BhP tam uttamaḥślokapadāmbujāśrayam
BhP taṃ praśrayeṇāvanatāḥ susatkṛtaṃ savrīḍahāsekṣaṇasūnṛtādibhiḥ
BhP rahasy apṛcchann upaviṣṭam āsane vijñāya sandeśaharaṃ ramāpateḥ
BhP jānīmas tvāṃ yadupateḥ pārṣadaṃ samupāgatam
BhP bhartreha preṣitaḥ pitror bhavān priyacikīrṣayā
BhP anyathā govraje tasya smaraṇīyaṃ na cakṣmahe
BhP snehānubandho bandhūnāṃ muner api sudustyajaḥ
BhP anyeṣv arthakṛtā maitrī yāvadarthaviḍambanam
BhP pumbhiḥ strīṣu kṛtā yadvat sumanaḥsv iva ṣaṭpadaiḥ
BhP niḥsvaṃ tyajanti gaṇikā akalpaṃ nṛpatiṃ prajāḥ
BhP adhītavidyā ācāryam ṛtvijo dattadakṣiṇam
BhP khagā vītaphalaṃ vṛkṣaṃ bhuktvā cātithayo gṛham
BhP dagdhaṃ mṛgās tathāraṇyaṃ jārā bhuktvā ratāṃ striyam
BhP iti gopyo hi govinde gatavākkāyamānasāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇadūte samāyāte uddhave tyaktalaukikāḥ
BhP gāyantyaḥ prīyakarmāṇi rudantyaś ca gatahriyaḥ
BhP tasya saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya yāni kaiśorabālyayoḥ
BhP kācin madhukaraṃ dṛṣṭvā dhyāyantī kṛṣṇasaṅgamam
BhP priyaprasthāpitaṃ dūtaṃ kalpayitvedam abravīt
BhP gopy uvāca
BhP madhupa kitavabandho mā spṛśaṅghriṃ sapatnyāḥ
BhP kucavilulitamālākuṅkumaśmaśrubhir naḥ
BhP vahatu madhupatis tanmāninīnāṃ prasādaṃ
BhP yadusadasi viḍambyaṃ yasya dūtas tvam īdṛk
BhP sakṛd adharasudhāṃ svāṃ mohinīṃ pāyayitvā
BhP sumanasa iva sadyas tatyaje 'smān bhavādṛk
BhP paricarati kathaṃ tatpādapadmaṃ nu padmā
BhP hy api bata hṛtacetā hy uttamaḥślokajalpaiḥ
BhP kim iha bahu ṣaḍaṅghre gāyasi tvaṃ yadūnām
BhP adhipatim agṛhāṇām agrato naḥ purāṇam
BhP vijayasakhasakhīnāṃ gīyatāṃ tatprasaṅgaḥ
BhP kṣapitakucarujas te kalpayantīṣṭam iṣṭāḥ
BhP divi bhuvi ca rasāyāṃ kāḥ striyas taddurāpāḥ
BhP kapaṭarucirahāsabhrūvijṛmbhasya yāḥ syuḥ
BhP caraṇaraja upāste yasya bhūtir vayaṃ kā
BhP api ca kṛpaṇapakṣe hy uttamaḥślokaśabdaḥ
BhP visṛja śirasi pādaṃ vedmy ahaṃ cātukārair
BhP anunayaviduṣas te 'bhyetya dautyair mukundāt
BhP svakṛta iha viṣṛṣṭāpatyapatyanyalokā
BhP vyasṛjad akṛtacetāḥ kiṃ nu sandheyam asmin
BhP mṛgayur iva kapīndraṃ vivyadhe lubdhadharmā
BhP striyam akṛta virūpāṃ strījitaḥ kāmayānām
BhP balim api balim attvāveṣṭayad dhvāṅkṣavad yas
BhP tad alam asitasakhyair dustyajas tatkathārthaḥ
BhP yadanucaritalīlākarṇapīyūṣavipruṭ
BhP sakṛdadanavidhūtadvandvadharmā vinaṣṭāḥ
BhP sapadi gṛhakuṭumbaṃ dīnam utsṛjya dīnā
BhP bahava iha vihaṅgā bhikṣucaryāṃ caranti
BhP vayam ṛtam iva jihmavyāhṛtaṃ śraddadhānāḥ
BhP kulikarutam ivājñāḥ kṛṣṇavadhvo hariṇyaḥ
BhP dadṛśur asakṛd etat tannakhasparśatīvra
BhP smararuja upamantrin bhaṇyatām anyavārtā
BhP priyasakha punar āgāḥ preyasā preṣitaḥ kiṃ
BhP varaya kim anurundhe mānanīyo 'si me 'ṅga
BhP nayasi katham ihāsmān dustyajadvandvapārśvaṃ
BhP satatam urasi saumya śrīr vadhūḥ sākam āste
BhP api bata madhupuryām āryaputro 'dhunāste
BhP smarati sa pitṛgehān saumya bandhūṃś ca gopān
BhP kvacid api sa kathā naḥ kiṅkarīṇāṃ gṛṇīte
BhP bhujam agurusugandhaṃ mūrdhny adhāsyat kadā nu
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP athoddhavo niśamyaivaṃ kṛṣṇadarśanalālasāḥ
BhP sāntvayan priyasandeśair gopīr idam abhāṣata
BhP śrīuddhava uvāca
BhP aho yūyaṃ sma pūrṇārthā bhavatyo lokapūjitāḥ
BhP vāsudeve bhagavati yāsām ity arpitaṃ manaḥ
BhP dānavratatapohoma japasvādhyāyasaṃyamaiḥ
BhP śreyobhir vividhaiś cānyaiḥ kṛṣṇe bhaktir hi sādhyate
BhP bhagavaty uttamaḥśloke bhavatībhir anuttamā
BhP bhaktiḥ pravartitā diṣṭyā munīnām api durlabhā
BhP diṣṭyā putrān patīn dehān svajanān bhavanāni ca
BhP hitvāvṛnīta yūyaṃ yat kṛṣṇākhyaṃ puruṣaṃ param
BhP sarvātmabhāvo 'dhikṛto bhavatīnām adhokṣaje
BhP viraheṇa mahābhāgā mahān me 'nugrahaḥ kṛtaḥ
BhP śrūyatāṃ priyasandeśo bhavatīnāṃ sukhāvahaḥ
BhP yam ādāyāgato bhadrā ahaṃ bhartū rahaskaraḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP bhavatīnāṃ viyogo me na hi sarvātmanā kvacit
BhP yathā bhūtāni bhūteṣu khaṃ vāyvagnir jalaṃ mahī
BhP tathāhaṃ ca manaḥprāṇa bhūtendriyaguṇāśrayaḥ
BhP ātmany evātmanātmānaṃ sṛje hanmy anupālaye
BhP ātmamāyānubhāvena bhūtendriyaguṇātmanā
BhP ātmā jñānamayaḥ śuddho vyatirikto 'guṇānvayaḥ
BhP suṣuptisvapnajāgradbhir māyāvṛttibhir īyate
BhP yenendriyārthān dhyāyeta mṛṣā svapnavad utthitaḥ
BhP tan nirundhyād indriyāṇi vinidraḥ pratyapadyata
BhP etadantaḥ samāmnāyo yogaḥ sāṅkhyaṃ manīṣiṇām
BhP tyāgas tapo damaḥ satyaṃ samudrāntā ivāpagāḥ
BhP yat tv ahaṃ bhavatīnāṃ vai dūre varte priyo dṛśām
BhP manasaḥ sannikarṣārthaṃ madanudhyānakāmyayā
BhP yathā dūracare preṣṭhe mana āviśya vartate
BhP strīṇāṃ ca na tathā cetaḥ sannikṛṣṭe 'kṣigocare
BhP mayy āveśya manaḥ kṛtsnaṃ vimuktāśeṣavṛtti yat
BhP anusmarantyo māṃ nityam acirān mām upaiṣyatha
BhP yā mayā krīḍatā rātryāṃ vane 'smin vraja āsthitāḥ
BhP alabdharāsāḥ kalyāṇyo māpur madvīryacintayā
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ priyatamādiṣṭam ākarṇya vrajayoṣitaḥ
BhP tā ūcur uddhavaṃ prītās tatsandeśāgatasmṛtīḥ
BhP gopya ūcuḥ
BhP diṣṭyāhito hataḥ kaṃso yadūnāṃ sānugo 'ghakṛt
BhP diṣṭyāptair labdhasarvārthaiḥ kuśaly āste 'cyuto 'dhunā
BhP kaccid gadāgrajaḥ saumya karoti purayoṣitām
BhP prītiṃ naḥ snigdhasavrīḍa hāsodārekṣaṇārcitaḥ
BhP kathaṃ rativiśeṣajñaḥ priyaś ca purayoṣitām
BhP nānubadhyeta tadvākyair vibhramaiś cānubhājitaḥ
BhP api smarati naḥ sādho govindaḥ prastute kvacit
BhP goṣṭhimadhye purastrīṇām grāmyāḥ svairakathāntare
BhP tāḥ kiṃ niśāḥ smarati yāsu tadā priyābhir
BhP vṛndāvane kumudakundaśaśāṅkaramye
BhP reme kvaṇaccaraṇanūpurarāsagoṣṭhyām
BhP asmābhir īḍitamanojñakathaḥ kadācit
BhP apy eṣyatīha dāśārhas taptāḥ svakṛtayā śucā
BhP sañjīvayan nu no gātrair yathendro vanam ambudaiḥ
BhP kasmāt kṛṣṇa ihāyāti prāptarājyo hatāhitaḥ
BhP narendrakanyā udvāhya prītaḥ sarvasuhṛdvṛtaḥ
BhP kim asmābhir vanaukobhir anyābhir vā mahātmanaḥ
BhP śrīpater āptakāmasya kriyetārthaḥ kṛtātmanaḥ
BhP paraṃ saukhyaṃ hi nairāśyaṃ svairiṇy apy āha piṅgalā
BhP taj jānatīnāṃ naḥ kṛṣṇe tathāpy āśā duratyayā
BhP ka utsaheta santyaktum uttamaḥślokasaṃvidam
BhP anicchato 'pi yasya śrīr aṅgān na cyavate kvacit
BhP saricchailavanoddeśā gāvo veṇuravā ime
BhP saṅkarṣaṇasahāyena kṛṣṇenācaritāḥ prabho
BhP punaḥ punaḥ smārayanti nandagopasutaṃ bata
BhP śrīniketais tatpadakair vismartuṃ naiva śaknumaḥ
BhP gatyā lalitayodāra hāsalīlāvalokanaiḥ
BhP mādhvyā girā hṛtadhiyaḥ kathaṃ taṃ vismarāma he
BhP he nātha he ramānātha vrajanāthārtināśana
BhP magnam uddhara govinda gokulaṃ vṛjinārṇavāt
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP tatas tāḥ kṛṣṇasandeśair vyapetavirahajvarāḥ
BhP uddhavaṃ pūjayāṃ cakrur jñātvātmānam adhokṣajam
BhP uvāsa katicin māsān gopīnāṃ vinudan śucaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇalīlākathāṃ gāyan ramayām āsa gokulam
BhP yāvanty ahāni nandasya vraje 'vātsīt sa uddhavaḥ
BhP vrajaukasāṃ kṣaṇaprāyāṇy āsan kṛṣṇasya vārtayā
BhP saridvanagiridroṇīr vīkṣan kusumitān drumān
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ saṃsmārayan reme haridāso vrajaukasām
BhP dṛṣṭvaivamādi gopīnāṃ kṛṣṇāveśātmaviklavam
BhP uddhavaḥ paramaprītas tā namasyann idaṃ jagau
BhP etāḥ paraṃ tanubhṛto bhuvi gopavadhvo
BhP govinda eva nikhilātmani rūḍhabhāvāḥ
BhP vāñchanti yad bhavabhiyo munayo vayaṃ ca
BhP kiṃ brahmajanmabhir anantakathārasasya
BhP kvemāḥ striyo vanacarīr vyabhicāraduṣṭāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇe kva caiṣa paramātmani rūḍhabhāvaḥ
BhP nanv īśvaro 'nubhajato 'viduṣo 'pi sākṣāc
BhP chreyas tanoty agadarāja ivopayuktaḥ
BhP nāyaṃ śriyo 'ṅga u nitāntarateḥ prasādaḥ
BhP svaryoṣitāṃ nalinagandharucāṃ kuto 'nyāḥ
BhP rāsotsave 'sya bhujadaṇḍagṛhītakaṇṭha
BhP labdhāśiṣāṃ ya udagād vrajavallabhīnām
BhP āsām aho caraṇareṇujuṣām ahaṃ syāṃ
BhP vṛndāvane kim api gulmalatauṣadhīnām
BhP yā dustyajaṃ svajanam āryapathaṃ ca hitvā
BhP bhejur mukundapadavīṃ śrutibhir vimṛgyām
BhP yā vai śriyārcitam ajādibhir āptakāmair
BhP yogeśvarair api yad ātmani rāsagoṣṭhyām
BhP kṛṣṇasya tad bhagavataḥ caraṇāravindaṃ
BhP nyastaṃ staneṣu vijahuḥ parirabhya tāpam
BhP vande nandavrajastrīṇāṃ pādareṇum abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
BhP yāsāṃ harikathodgītaṃ punāti bhuvanatrayam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP atha gopīr anujñāpya yaśodāṃ nandam eva ca
BhP gopān āmantrya dāśārho yāsyann āruruhe ratham
BhP taṃ nirgataṃ samāsādya nānopāyanapāṇayaḥ
BhP nandādayo 'nurāgeṇa prāvocann aśrulocanāḥ
BhP manaso vṛttayo naḥ syuḥ kṛṣṇa pādāmbujāśrayāḥ
BhP vāco 'bhidhāyinīr nāmnāṃ kāyas tatprahvaṇādiṣu
BhP karmabhir bhrāmyamāṇānāṃ yatra kvāpīśvarecchayā
BhP maṅgalācaritair dānai ratir naḥ kṛṣṇa īśvare
BhP evaṃ sabhājito gopaiḥ kṛṣṇabhaktyā narādhipa
BhP uddhavaḥ punar āgacchan mathurāṃ kṛṣṇapālitām
BhP kṛṣṇāya praṇipatyāha bhaktyudrekaṃ vrajaukasām
BhP vasudevāya rāmāya rājñe copāyanāny adāt
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP atha vijñāya bhagavān sarvātmā sarvadarśanaḥ
BhP sairandhryāḥ kāmataptāyāḥ priyam icchan gṛhaṃ yayau
BhP mahārhopaskarair āḍhyaṃ kāmopāyopabṛṃhitam
BhP muktādāmapatākābhir vitānaśayanāsanaiḥ
BhP dhūpaiḥ surabhibhir dīpaiḥ sraggandhair api maṇḍitam
BhP gṛhaṃ tam āyāntam avekṣya sāsanāt sadyaḥ samutthāya hi jātasambhramā
BhP yathopasaṅgamya sakhībhir acyutaṃ sabhājayām āsa sadāsanādibhiḥ
BhP tathoddhavaḥ sādhutayābhipūjito nyaṣīdad urvyām abhimṛśya cāsanam
BhP kṛṣṇo 'pi tūrṇaṃ śayanaṃ mahādhanaṃ viveśa lokācaritāny anuvrataḥ
BhP sā majjanālepadukūlabhūṣaṇa sraggandhatāmbūlasudhāsavādibhiḥ
BhP prasādhitātmopasasāra mādhavaṃ savrīḍalīlotsmitavibhramekṣitaiḥ
BhP āhūya kāntāṃ navasaṅgamahriyā viśaṅkitāṃ kaṅkaṇabhūṣite kare
BhP pragṛhya śayyām adhiveśya rāmayā reme 'nulepārpaṇapuṇyaleśayā
BhP sānaṅgataptakucayor urasas tathākṣṇor
BhP jighranty anantacaraṇena rujo mṛjantī
BhP dorbhyāṃ stanāntaragataṃ parirabhya kāntam
BhP ānandamūrtim ajahād atidīrghatāpam
BhP saivaṃ kaivalyanāthaṃ taṃ prāpya duṣprāpyam īśvaram
BhP aṅgarāgārpaṇenāho durbhagedam ayācata
BhP sahoṣyatām iha preṣṭha dināni katicin mayā
BhP ramasva notsahe tyaktuṃ saṅgaṃ te 'mburuhekṣaṇa
BhP tasyai kāmavaraṃ dattvā mānayitvā ca mānadaḥ
BhP sahoddhavena sarveśaḥ svadhāmāgamad ṛddhimat
BhP durārdhyaṃ samārādhya viṣṇuṃ sarveśvareśvaram
BhP yo vṛṇīte manogrāhyam asattvāt kumanīṣy asau
BhP akrūrabhavanaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ saharāmoddhavaḥ prabhuḥ
BhP kiñcic cikīrṣayan prāgād akrūraprīyakāmyayā
BhP sa tān naravaraśreṣṭhān ārād vīkṣya svabāndhavān
BhP pratyutthāya pramuditaḥ pariṣvajyābhinandya ca
BhP nanāma kṛṣṇaṃ rāmaṃ ca sa tair apy abhivāditaḥ
BhP pūjayām āsa vidhivat kṛtāsanaparigrahān
BhP pādāvanejanīr āpo dhārayan śirasā nṛpa
BhP arhaṇenāmbarair divyair gandhasragbhūṣaṇottamaiḥ
BhP arcitvā śirasānamya pādāv aṅkagatau mṛjan
BhP praśrayāvanato 'krūraḥ kṛṣṇarāmāv abhāṣata
BhP diṣṭyā pāpo hataḥ kaṃsaḥ sānugo vām idaṃ kulam
BhP bhavadbhyām uddhṛtaṃ kṛcchrād durantāc ca samedhitam
BhP yuvāṃ pradhānapuruṣau jagaddhetū jaganmayau
BhP bhavadbhyāṃ na vinā kiñcit param asti na cāparam
BhP ātmasṛṣṭam idaṃ viśvam anvāviśya svaśaktibhiḥ
BhP īyate bahudhā brahman śru tapratyakṣagocaram
BhP yathā hi bhūteṣu carācareṣu mahyādayo yoniṣu bhānti nānā
BhP evaṃ bhavān kevala ātmayoniṣv ātmātmatantro bahudhā vibhāti
BhP sṛjasy atho lumpasi pāsi viśvaṃ rajastamaḥsattvaguṇaiḥ svaśaktibhiḥ
BhP na badhyase tadguṇakarmabhir vā jñānātmanas te kva ca bandhahetuḥ
BhP dehādyupādher anirūpitatvād bhavo na sākṣān na bhidātmanaḥ syāt
BhP ato na bandhas tava naiva mokṣaḥ syātām nikāmas tvayi no 'vivekaḥ
BhP tvayodito 'yaṃ jagato hitāya yadā yadā vedapathaḥ purāṇaḥ
BhP bādhyeta pāṣaṇḍapathair asadbhis tadā bhavān sattvaguṇaṃ bibharti
BhP sa tvam prabho 'dya vasudevagṛhe 'vatīrṇaḥ
BhP svāṃśena bhāram apanetum ihāsi bhūmeḥ
BhP akṣauhiṇīśatavadhena suretarāṃśa
BhP rājñām amuṣya ca kulasya yaśo vitanvan
BhP adyeśa no vasatayaḥ khalu bhūribhāgā
BhP yaḥ sarvadevapitṛbhūtanṛdevamūrtiḥ
BhP yatpādaśaucasalilaṃ trijagat punāti
BhP sa tvaṃ jagadgurur adhokṣaja yāḥ praviṣṭaḥ
BhP kaḥ paṇḍitas tvad aparaṃ śaraṇaṃ samīyād
BhP bhaktapriyād ṛtagiraḥ suhṛdaḥ kṛtajñāt
BhP sarvān dadāti suhṛdo bhajato 'bhikāmān
BhP ātmānam apy upacayāpacayau na yasya
BhP diṣṭyā janārdana bhavān iha naḥ pratīto
BhP yogeśvarair api durāpagatiḥ sureśaiḥ
BhP chindhy āśu naḥ sutakalatradhanāptageha
BhP dehādimoharaśanāṃ bhavadīyamāyām
BhP ity arcitaḥ saṃstutaś ca bhaktena bhagavān hariḥ
BhP akrūraṃ sasmitaṃ prāha gīrbhiḥ sammohayann iva
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP tvaṃ no guruḥ pitṛvyaś ca ślāghyo bandhuś ca nityadā
BhP vayaṃ tu rakṣyāḥ poṣyāś ca anukampyāḥ prajā hi vaḥ
BhP bhavadvidhā mahābhāgā niṣevyā arhasattamāḥ
BhP śreyaskāmair nṛbhir nityaṃ devāḥ svārthā na sādhavaḥ
BhP na hy ammayāni tīrthāni na devā mṛcchilāmayāḥ
BhP te punanty urukālena darśanād eva sādhavaḥ
BhP sa bhavān suhṛdāṃ vai naḥ śreyān śreyaścikīrṣayā
BhP jijñāsārthaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ gacchasva tvaṃ gajāhvayam
BhP pitary uparate bālāḥ saha mātrā suduḥkhitāḥ
BhP ānītāḥ svapuraṃ rājñā vasanta iti śuśruma
BhP teṣu rājāmbikāputro bhrātṛputreṣu dīnadhīḥ
BhP samo na vartate nūnaṃ duṣputravaśago 'ndhadṛk
BhP gaccha jānīhi tadvṛttam adhunā sādhv asādhu vā
BhP vijñāya tad vidhāsyāmo yathā śaṃ suhṛdāṃ bhavet
BhP ity akrūraṃ samādiśya bhagavān harir īśvaraḥ
BhP saṅkarṣaṇoddhavābhyāṃ vai tataḥ svabhavanaṃ yayau
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa gatvā hāstinapuraṃ pauravendrayaśo'ṅkitam
BhP dadarśa tatrāmbikeyaṃ sabhīṣmaṃ viduraṃ pṛthām
BhP sahaputraṃ ca bāhlīkaṃ bhāradvājaṃ sagautamam
BhP karnaṃ suyodhanaṃ drauṇiṃ pāṇḍavān suhṛdo 'parān
BhP yathāvad upasaṅgamya bandhubhir gāndinīsutaḥ
BhP sampṛṣṭas taiḥ suhṛdvārtāṃ svayaṃ cāpṛcchad avyayam
BhP uvāsa katicin māsān rājño vṛttavivitsayā
BhP duṣprajasyālpasārasya khalacchandānuvartinaḥ
BhP teja ojo balaṃ vīryaṃ praśrayādīṃś ca sadguṇān
BhP prajānurāgaṃ pārtheṣu na sahadbhiś cikīṛṣitam
BhP kṛtaṃ ca dhārtarāṣṭrair yad garadānādy apeśalam
BhP ācakhyau sarvam evāsmai pṛthā vidura eva ca
BhP pṛthā tu bhrātaraṃ prāptam akrūram upasṛtya tam
BhP uvāca janmanilayaṃ smaranty aśrukalekṣaṇā
BhP api smaranti naḥ saumya pitarau bhrātaraś ca me
BhP bhaginyau bhrātṛputrāś ca jāmayaḥ sakhya eva ca
BhP bhrātreyo bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ śaraṇyo bhaktavatsalaḥ
BhP paitṛṣvasreyān smarati rāmaś cāmburuhekṣaṇaḥ
BhP sapatnamadhye śocantīṃ vṛkānāṃ hariṇīm iva
BhP sāntvayiṣyati māṃ vākyaiḥ pitṛhīnāṃś ca bālakān
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahāyogin viśvātman viśvabhāvana
BhP prapannāṃ pāhi govinda śiśubhiś cāvasīdatīm
BhP nānyat tava padāmbhojāt paśyāmi śaraṇaṃ nṛṇām
BhP bibhyatāṃ mṛtyusaṃsārād īsvarasyāpavargikāt
BhP namaḥ kṛṣṇāya śuddhāya brahmaṇe paramātmane
BhP yogeśvarāya yogāya tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity anusmṛtya svajanaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca jagadīśvaram
BhP prārudad duḥkhitā rājan bhavatāṃ prapitāmahī
BhP samaduḥkhasukho 'krūro viduraś ca mahāyaśāḥ
BhP sāntvayām āsatuḥ kuntīṃ tatputrotpattihetubhiḥ
BhP yāsyan rājānam abhyetya viṣamaṃ putralālasam
BhP avadat suhṛdāṃ madhye bandhubhiḥ sauhṛdoditam
BhP akrūra uvāca
BhP bho bho vaicitravīrya tvaṃ kurūṇāṃ kīrtivardhana
BhP bhrātary uparate pāṇḍāv adhunāsanam āsthitaḥ
BhP dharmeṇa pālayann urvīṃ prajāḥ śīlena rañjayan
BhP vartamānaḥ samaḥ sveṣu śreyaḥ kīrtim avāpsyasi
BhP anyathā tv ācaraṃl loke garhito yāsyase tamaḥ
BhP tasmāt samatve vartasva pāṇḍaveṣv ātmajeṣu ca
BhP neha cātyantasaṃvāsaḥ kasyacit kenacit saha
BhP rājan svenāpi dehena kim u jāyātmajādibhiḥ
BhP ekaḥ prasūyate jantur eka eva pralīyate
BhP eko 'nubhuṅkte sukṛtam eka eva ca duṣkṛtam
BhP adharmopacitaṃ vittaṃ haranty anye 'lpamedhasaḥ
BhP sambhojanīyāpadeśair jalānīva jalaukasaḥ
BhP puṣṇāti yān adharmeṇa svabuddhyā tam apaṇḍitam
BhP te 'kṛtārthaṃ prahiṇvanti prāṇā rāyaḥ sutādayaḥ
BhP svayaṃ kilbiṣam ādāya tais tyakto nārthakovidaḥ
BhP asiddhārtho viśaty andhaṃ svadharmavimukhas tamaḥ
BhP tasmāl lokam imaṃ rājan svapnamāyāmanoratham
BhP vīkṣyāyamyātmanātmānaṃ samaḥ śānto bhava prabho
BhP dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
BhP yathā vadati kalyāṇīṃ vācaṃ dānapate bhavān
BhP tathānayā na tṛpyāmi martyaḥ prāpya yathāmṛtam
BhP tathāpi sūnṛtā saumya hṛdi na sthīyate cale
BhP putrānurāgaviṣame vidyut saudāmanī yathā
BhP īśvarasya vidhiṃ ko nu vidhunoty anyathā pumān
BhP bhūmer bhārāvatārāya yo 'vatīrṇo yadoḥ kule
BhP yo durvimarśapathayā nijamāyayedaṃ
BhP sṛṣṭvā guṇān vibhajate tadanupraviṣṭaḥ
BhP tasmai namo duravabodhavihāratantra
BhP saṃsāracakragataye parameśvarāya
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity abhipretya nṛpater abhiprāyaṃ sa yādavaḥ
BhP suhṛdbhiḥ samanujñātaḥ punar yadupurīm agāt
BhP śaśaṃsa rāmakṛṣṇābhyāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraviceṣṭitam
BhP pāṇdavān prati kauravya yadarthaṃ preṣitaḥ svayam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP astiḥ prāptiś ca kaṃsasya mahiṣyau bharatarṣabha
BhP mṛte bhartari duḥkhārte īyatuḥ sma pitur gṛhān
BhP pitre magadharājāya jarāsandhāya duḥkhite
BhP vedayāṃ cakratuḥ sarvam ātmavaidhavyakāraṇam
BhP sa tad apriyam ākarṇya śokāmarṣayuto nṛpa
BhP ayādavīṃ mahīṃ kartuṃ cakre paramam udyamam
BhP akṣauhiṇībhir viṃśatyā tisṛbhiś cāpi saṃvṛtaḥ
BhP yadurājadhānīṃ mathurāṃ nyarudhat sarvato diśam
BhP nirīkṣya tadbalaṃ kṛṣṇa udvelam iva sāgaram
BhP svapuraṃ tena saṃruddhaṃ svajanaṃ ca bhayākulam
BhP cintayām āsa bhagavān hariḥ kāraṇamānuṣaḥ
BhP taddeśakālānuguṇaṃ svāvatāraprayojanam
BhP haniṣyāmi balaṃ hy etad bhuvi bhāraṃ samāhitam
BhP māgadhena samānītaṃ vaśyānāṃ sarvabhūbhujām
BhP akṣauhiṇībhiḥ saṅkhyātaṃ bhaṭāśvarathakuñjaraiḥ
BhP māgadhas tu na hantavyo bhūyaḥ kartā balodyamam
BhP etadartho 'vatāro 'yaṃ bhūbhāraharaṇāya me
BhP saṃrakṣaṇāya sādhūnāṃ kṛto 'nyeṣāṃ vadhāya ca
BhP anyo 'pi dharmarakṣāyai dehaḥ saṃbhriyate mayā
BhP virāmāyāpy adharmasya kāle prabhavataḥ kvacit
BhP evaṃ dhyāyati govinda ākāśāt sūryavarcasau
BhP rathāv upasthitau sadyaḥ sasūtau saparicchadau
BhP āyudhāni ca divyāni purāṇāni yadṛcchayā
BhP dṛṣṭvā tāni hṛṣīkeśaḥ saṅkarṣaṇam athābravīt
BhP paśyārya vyasanaṃ prāptaṃ yadūnāṃ tvāvatāṃ prabho
BhP eṣa te ratha āyāto dayitāny āyudhāni ca
BhP etadarthaṃ hi nau janma sādhūnām īśa śarmakṛt
BhP trayoviṃśatyanīkākhyaṃ bhūmer bhāram apākuru
BhP evaṃ sammantrya dāśārhau daṃśitau rathinau purāt
BhP nirjagmatuḥ svāyudhāḍhyau balenālpīyasā vṛtau
BhP śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau vinirgatya harir dārukasārathiḥ
BhP tato 'bhūt parasainyānāṃ hṛdi vitrāsavepathuḥ
BhP tāv āha māgadho vīkṣya he kṛṣṇa puruṣādhama
BhP na tvayā yoddhum icchāmi bālenaikena lajjayā
BhP guptena hi tvayā manda na yotsye yāhi bandhuhan
BhP tava rāma yadi śraddhā yudhyasva dhairyam udvaha
BhP hitvā vā maccharaiś chinnaṃ dehaṃ svar yāhi māṃ jahi
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP na vai śūrā vikatthante darśayanty eva pauruṣam
BhP na gṛhṇīmo vaco rājann āturasya mumūrṣataḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP jarāsutas tāv abhisṛtya mādhavau mahābalaughena balīyasāvṛnot
BhP sasainyayānadhvajavājisārathī sūryānalau vāyur ivābhrareṇubhiḥ
BhP suparṇatāladhvajacihitnau rathāv
BhP alakṣayantyo harirāmayor mṛdhe
BhP striyaḥ purāṭṭālakaharmyagopuraṃ
BhP samāśritāḥ sammumuhuḥ śucārditaḥ
BhP hariḥ parānīkapayomucāṃ muhuḥ śilīmukhātyulbaṇavarṣapīḍitam
BhP svasainyam ālokya surāsurārcitaṃ vyasphūrjayac chārṅgaśarāsanottamam
BhP gṛhṇan niśaṅgād atha sandadhac charān
BhP vikṛṣya muñcan śitabāṇapūgān
BhP nighnan rathān kuñjaravājipattīn
BhP nirantaraṃ yadvad alātacakram
BhP nirbhinnakumbhāḥ kariṇo nipetur anekaśo 'śvāḥ śaravṛkṇakandharāḥ
BhP rathā hatāśvadhvajasūtanāyakāḥ padāyataś chinnabhujorukandharāḥ
BhP sañchidyamānadvipadebhavājinām aṅgaprasūtāḥ śataśo 'sṛgāpagāḥ
BhP bhujāhayaḥ pūruṣaśīrṣakacchapā hatadvipadvīpahaya grahākulāḥ
BhP karorumīnā narakeśaśaivalā dhanustaraṅgāyudhagulmasaṅkulāḥ
BhP acchūrikāvartabhayānakā mahā maṇipravekābharaṇāśmaśarkarāḥ
BhP pravartitā bhīrubhayāvahā mṛdhe manasvināṃ harṣakarīḥ parasparam
BhP vinighnatārīn muṣalena durmadān saṅkarṣaṇenāparīmeyatejasā
BhP balaṃ tad aṅgārṇavadurgabhairavaṃ durantapāraṃ magadhendrapālitam
BhP kṣayaṃ praṇītaṃ vasudevaputrayor vikrīḍitaṃ taj jagadīśayoḥ param
BhP sthityudbhavāntaṃ bhuvanatrayasya yaḥ
BhP samīhite 'nantaguṇaḥ svalīlayā
BhP na tasya citraṃ parapakṣanigrahas
BhP tathāpi martyānuvidhasya varṇyate
BhP jagrāha virathaṃ rāmo jarāsandhaṃ mahābalam
BhP hatānīkāvaśiṣṭāsuṃ siṃhaḥ siṃham ivaujasā
BhP badhyamānaṃ hatārātiṃ pāśair vāruṇamānuṣaiḥ
BhP vārayām āsa govindas tena kāryacikīrṣayā
BhP sā mukto lokanāthābhyāṃ vrīḍito vīrasammataḥ
BhP tapase kṛtasaṅkalpo vāritaḥ pathi rājabhiḥ
BhP vākyaiḥ pavitrārthapadair nayanaiḥ prākṛtair api
BhP svakarmabandhaprāpto 'yaṃ yadubhis te parābhavaḥ
BhP hateṣu sarvānīkeṣu nṛpo bārhadrathas tadā
BhP upekṣito bhagavatā magadhān durmanā yayau
BhP mukundo 'py akṣatabalo nistīrṇāribalārṇavaḥ
BhP vikīryamāṇaḥ kusumais trīdaśair anumoditaḥ
BhP māthurair upasaṅgamya vijvarair muditātmabhiḥ
BhP upagīyamānavijayaḥ sūtamāgadhavandibhiḥ
BhP śaṅkhadundubhayo nedur bherītūryāṇy anekaśaḥ
BhP vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgāni puraṃ praviśati prabhau
BhP siktamārgāṃ hṛṣṭajanāṃ patākābhir abhyalaṅkṛtām
BhP nirghuṣṭāṃ brahmaghoṣeṇa kautukābaddhatoraṇām
BhP nicīyamāno nārībhir mālyadadhyakṣatāṅkuraiḥ
BhP nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ sasnehaṃ prītyutkalitalocanaiḥ
BhP āyodhanagataṃ vittam anantaṃ vīrabhūṣaṇam
BhP yadurājāya tat sarvam āhṛtaṃ prādiśat prabhuḥ
BhP evaṃ saptadaśakṛtvas tāvaty akṣauhiṇībalaḥ
BhP yuyudhe māgadho rājā yadubhiḥ kṛṣṇapālitaiḥ
BhP akṣiṇvaṃs tadbalaṃ sarvaṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇatejasā
BhP hateṣu sveṣv anīkeṣu tyakto 'gād aribhir nṛpaḥ
BhP aṣṭādaśama saṅgrāma āgāmini tadantarā
BhP nāradapreṣito vīro yavanaḥ pratyadṛśyata
BhP rurodha mathurām etya tisṛbhir mlecchakoṭibhiḥ
BhP nṛloke cāpratidvandvo vṛṣṇīn śrutvātmasammitān
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvācintayat kṛṣṇaḥ saṅkarṣaṇa sahāyavān
BhP aho yadūnāṃ vṛjinaṃ prāptaṃ hy ubhayato mahat
BhP yavano 'yaṃ nirundhe 'smān adya tāvan mahābalaḥ
BhP māgadho 'py adya vā śvo vā paraśvo vāgamiṣyati
BhP āvayoḥ yudhyator asya yady āgantā jarāsutaḥ
BhP bandhūn haniṣyaty atha vā neṣyate svapuraṃ balī
BhP tasmād adya vidhāsyāmo durgaṃ dvipadadurgamam
BhP tatra jñātīn samādhāya yavanaṃ ghātayāmahe
BhP iti sammantrya bhagavān durgaṃ dvādaśayojanam
BhP antaḥsamudre nagaraṃ kṛtsnādbhutam acīkarat
BhP dṛśyate yatra hi tvāṣṭraṃ vijñānaṃ śilpanaipuṇam
BhP rathyācatvaravīthībhir yathāvāstu vinirmitam
BhP suradrumalatodyāna vicitropavanānvitam
BhP hemaśṛṅgair divispṛgbhiḥ sphaṭikāṭṭālagopuraiḥ
BhP rājatārakuṭaiḥ koṣṭhair hemakumbhair alaṅkṛtaiḥ
BhP ratnakūtair gṛhair hemair mahāmārakatasthalaiḥ
BhP vāstoṣpatīnāṃ ca gṛhair vallabhībhiś ca nirmitam
BhP cāturvarṇyajanākīrṇaṃ yadudevagṛhollasat
BhP sudharmāṃ pārijātaṃ ca mahendraḥ prāhiṇod dhareḥ
BhP yatra cāvasthito martyo martyadharmair na yujyate
BhP śyāmaikavarṇān varuṇo hayān śuklān manojavān
BhP aṣṭau nidhipatiḥ kośān lokapālo nijodayān
BhP yad yad bhagavatā dattam ādhipatyaṃ svasiddhaye
BhP sarvaṃ pratyarpayām āsur harau bhūmigate nṛpa
BhP tatra yogaprabhāvena nītvā sarvajanaṃ hariḥ
BhP prajāpālena rāmeṇa kṛṣṇaḥ samanumantritaḥ
BhP nirjagāma puradvārāt padmamālī nirāyudhaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP taṃ vilokya viniṣkrāntam ujjihānam ivoḍupam
BhP darśanīyatamaṃ śyāmaṃ pītakauśeyavāsasam
BhP śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ bhrājat kaustubhāmuktakandharam
BhP pṛthudīrghacaturbāhuṃ navakañjāruṇekṣaṇam
BhP nityapramuditaṃ śrīmat sukapolaṃ śucismitam
BhP mukhāravindaṃ bibhrāṇaṃ sphuranmakarakuṇḍalam
BhP vāsudevo hy ayam iti pumān śrīvatsalāñchanaḥ
BhP caturbhujo 'ravindākṣo vanamāly atisundaraḥ
BhP lakṣaṇair nāradaproktair nānyo bhavitum arhati
BhP nirāyudhaś calan padbhyāṃ yotsye 'nena nirāyudhaḥ
BhP iti niścitya yavanaḥ prādravad taṃ parāṅmukham
BhP anvadhāvaj jighṛkṣus taṃ durāpam api yoginām
BhP hastaprāptam ivātmānaṃ harīṇā sa pade pade
BhP nīto darśayatā dūraṃ yavaneśo 'drikandaram
BhP palāyanaṃ yadukule jātasya tava nocitam
BhP iti kṣipann anugato nainaṃ prāpāhatāśubhaḥ
BhP evaṃ kṣipto 'pi bhagavān prāviśad girikandaram
BhP so 'pi praviṣṭas tatrānyaṃ śayānaṃ dadṛśe naram
BhP nanv asau dūram ānīya śete mām iha sādhuvat
BhP iti matvācyutaṃ mūḍhas taṃ padā samatāḍayat
BhP sa utthāya ciraṃ suptaḥ śanair unmīlya locane
BhP diśo vilokayan pārśve tam adrākṣīd avasthitam
BhP sa tāvat tasya ruṣṭasya dṛṣṭipātena bhārata
BhP dehajenāgninā dagdho bhasmasād abhavat kṣaṇāt
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP ko nāma sa pumān brahman kasya kiṃvīrya eva ca
BhP kasmād guhāṃ gataḥ śiṣye kiṃtejo yavanārdanaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa ikṣvākukule jāto māndhātṛtanayo mahān
BhP mucukunda iti khyāto brahmaṇyaḥ satyasaṅgaraḥ
BhP sa yācitaḥ suragaṇair indrādyair ātmarakṣaṇe
BhP asurebhyaḥ paritrastais tadrakṣāṃ so 'karoc ciram
BhP labdhvā guhaṃ te svaḥpālaṃ mucukundam athābruvan
BhP rājan viramatāṃ kṛcchrād bhavān naḥ paripālanāt
BhP naralokaṃ parityajya rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam
BhP asmān pālayato vīra kāmās te sarva ujjhitāḥ
BhP sutā mahiṣyo bhavato jñātayo 'mātyamantrinaḥ
BhP prajāś ca tulyakālīnā nādhunā santi kālitāḥ
BhP kālo balīyān balināṃ bhagavān īśvaro 'vyayaḥ
BhP prajāḥ kālayate krīḍan paśupālo yathā paśūn
BhP varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te ṛte kaivalyam adya naḥ
BhP eka eveśvaras tasya bhagavān viṣṇur avyayaḥ
BhP evam uktaḥ sa vai devān abhivandya mahāyaśāḥ
BhP aśayiṣṭa guhāviṣṭo nidrayā devadattayā
BhP yavane bhasmasān nīte bhagavān sātvatarṣabhaḥ
BhP ātmānaṃ darśayām āsa mucukundāya dhīmate
BhP tam ālokya ghanaśyāmaṃ pītakauśeyavāsasam
BhP śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ bhrājat kaustubhena virājitam
BhP caturbhujaṃ rocamānaṃ vaijayantyā ca mālayā
BhP cāruprasannavadanaṃ sphuranmakarakuṇḍalam
BhP prekṣaṇīyaṃ nṛlokasya sānurāgasmitekṣaṇam
BhP apīvyavayasaṃ matta mṛgendrodāravikramam
BhP paryapṛcchan mahābuddhis tejasā tasya dharṣitaḥ
BhP śaṅkitaḥ śanakai rājā durdharṣam iva tejasā
BhP śrīmucukunda uvāca
BhP ko bhavān iha samprāpto vipine girigahvare
BhP padbhyāṃ padmapalāśābhyāṃ vicarasy urukaṇṭake
BhP kiṃ svit tejasvināṃ tejo bhagavān vā vibhāvasuḥ
BhP sūryaḥ somo mahendro vā lokapālo paro 'pi vā
BhP manye tvāṃ devadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ puruṣarṣabham
BhP yad bādhase guhādhvāntaṃ pradīpaḥ prabhayā yathā
BhP śuśrūṣatām avyalīkam asmākaṃ narapuṅgava
BhP svajanma karma gotraṃ vā kathyatāṃ yadi rocate
BhP vayaṃ tu puruṣavyāghra aikṣvākāḥ kṣatrabandhavaḥ
BhP mucukunda iti prokto yauvanāśvātmajaḥ prabho
BhP ciraprajāgaraśrānto nidrayāpahatendriyaḥ
BhP śaye 'smin vijane kāmaṃ kenāpy utthāpito 'dhunā
BhP so 'pi bhasmīkṛto nūnam ātmīyenaiva pāpmanā
BhP anantaraṃ bhavān śrīmāṃl lakṣito 'mitraśāsanaḥ
BhP tejasā te 'viṣahyeṇa bhūri draṣṭuṃ na śaknumaḥ
BhP hataujasā mahābhāga mānanīyo 'si dehinām
BhP evaṃ sambhāṣito rājñā bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ
BhP pratyāha prahasan vāṇyā meghanādagabhīrayā
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP janmakarmābhidhānāni santi me 'ṅga sahasraśaḥ
BhP na śakyante 'nusaṅkhyātum anantatvān mayāpi hi
BhP kvacid rajāṃsi vimame pārthivāny urujanmabhiḥ
BhP guṇakarmābhidhānāni na me janmāni karhicit
BhP kālatrayopapannāni janmakarmāṇi me nṛpa
BhP anukramanto naivāntaṃ gacchanti paramarṣayaḥ
BhP tathāpy adyatanāny aṅga śṛnuṣva gadato mama
BhP vijñāpito viriñcena purāhaṃ dharmaguptaye
BhP bhūmer bhārāyamāṇānām asurāṇāṃ kṣayāya ca
BhP avatīrṇo yadukule gṛha ānakadundubheḥ
BhP vadanti vāsudeveti vasudevasutaṃ hi mām
BhP kālanemir hataḥ kaṃsaḥ pralambādyāś ca saddviṣaḥ
BhP ayaṃ ca yavano dagdho rājaṃs te tigmacakṣuṣā
BhP so 'haṃ tavānugrahārthaṃ guhām etām upāgataḥ
BhP prārthitaḥ pracuraṃ pūrvaṃ tvayāhaṃ bhaktavatsalaḥ
BhP varān vṛṇīṣva rājarṣe sarvān kāmān dadāmi te
BhP māṃ prasanno janaḥ kaścin na bhūyo 'rhati śocitum
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity uktas taṃ praṇamyāha mucukundo mudānvitaḥ
BhP jñātvā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ gargavākyam anusmaran
BhP śrīmucukunda uvāca
BhP vimohito 'yaṃ jana īśa māyayā tvadīyayā tvāṃ na bhajaty anarthadṛk
BhP sukhāya duḥkhaprabhaveṣu sajjate gṛheṣu yoṣit puruṣaś ca vañcitaḥ
BhP labdhvā jano durlabham atra mānuṣaṃ
BhP kathañcid avyaṅgam ayatnato 'nagha
BhP pādāravindaṃ na bhajaty asanmatir
BhP gṛhāndhakūpe patito yathā paśuḥ
BhP mamaiṣa kālo 'jita niṣphalo gato rājyaśriyonnaddhamadasya bhūpateḥ
BhP martyātmabuddheḥ sutadārakośabhūṣv āsajjamānasya durantacintayā
BhP kalevare 'smin ghaṭakuḍyasannibhe
BhP nirūḍhamāno naradeva ity aham
BhP vṛto rathebhāśvapadātyanīkapair
BhP gāṃ paryaṭaṃs tvāgaṇayan sudurmadaḥ
BhP pramattam uccair itikṛtyacintayā pravṛddhalobhaṃ viṣayeṣu lālasam
BhP tvam apramattaḥ sahasābhipadyase kṣullelihāno 'hir ivākhum antakaḥ
BhP purā rathair hemapariṣkṛtaiś caran
BhP mataṃgajair vā naradevasaṃjñitaḥ
BhP sa eva kālena duratyayena te
BhP kalevaro viṭkṛmibhasmasaṃjñitaḥ
BhP nirjitya dikcakram abhūtavigraho varāsanasthaḥ samarājavanditaḥ
BhP gṛheṣu maithunyasukheṣu yoṣitāṃ krīḍāmṛgaḥ pūruṣa īśa nīyate
BhP karoti karmāṇi tapaḥsuniṣṭhito nivṛttabhogas tadapekṣayādadat
BhP punaś ca bhūyāsam ahaṃ svarāḍ iti pravṛddhatarṣo na sukhāya kalpate
BhP bhavāpavargo bhramato yadā bhavej janasya tarhy acyuta satsamāgamaḥ
BhP satsaṅgamo yarhi tadaiva sadgatau parāvareśe tvayi jāyate matiḥ
BhP manye mamānugraha īśa te kṛto rājyānubandhāpagamo yadṛcchayā
BhP yaḥ prārthyate sādhubhir ekacaryayā vanaṃ vivikṣadbhir akhaṇḍabhūmipaiḥ
BhP na kāmaye 'nyaṃ tava pādasevanād akiñcanaprārthyatamād varaṃ vibho
BhP ārādhya kas tvāṃ hy apavargadaṃ hare vṛṇīta āryo varam ātmabandhanam
BhP tasmād visṛjyāśiṣa īśa sarvato rajastamaḥsattvaguṇānubandhanāḥ
BhP nirañjanaṃ nirguṇam advayaṃ paraṃ tvāṃ jñāptimātraṃ puruṣaṃ vrajāmy aham
BhP ciram iha vṛjinārtas tapyamāno 'nutāpair
BhP avitṛṣaṣaḍamitro 'labdhaśāntiḥ kathañcit
BhP śaraṇada samupetas tvatpadābjaṃ parātman
BhP abhayam ṛtam aśokaṃ pāhi māpannam īśa
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP sārvabhauma mahārāja matis te vimalorjitā
BhP varaiḥ pralobhitasyāpi na kāmair vihatā yataḥ
BhP pralobhito varair yat tvam apramādāya viddhi tat
BhP na dhīr ekāntabhaktānām āśīrbhir bhidyate kvacit
BhP yuñjānānām abhaktānāṃ prāṇāyāmādibhir manaḥ
BhP akṣīṇavāsanaṃ rājan dṛśyate punar utthitam
BhP vicarasva mahīṃ kāmaṃ mayy āveśitamānasaḥ
BhP astv evaṃ nityadā tubhyaṃ bhaktir mayy anapāyinī
BhP kṣātradharmasthito jantūn nyavadhīr mṛgayādibhiḥ
BhP samāhitas tat tapasā jahy aghaṃ madupāśritaḥ
BhP janmany anantare rājan sarvabhūtasuhṛttamaḥ
BhP bhūtvā dvijavaras tvaṃ vai mām upaiṣyasi kevalam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itthaṃ so 'nagrahīto 'nga kṛṣṇenekṣvāku nandanaḥ
BhP taṃ parikramya sannamya niścakrāma guhāmukhāt
BhP saṃvīkṣya kṣullakān martyān paśūn vīrudvanaspatīn
BhP matvā kaliyugaṃ prāptaṃ jagāma diśam uttarām
BhP tapaḥśraddhāyuto dhīro niḥsaṅgo muktasaṃśayaḥ
BhP samādhāya manaḥ kṛṣṇe prāviśad gandhamādanam
BhP badaryāśramam āsādya naranārāyaṇālayam

BhP bhagavān punar āvrajya purīṃ yavanaveṣṭitām
BhP hatvā mlecchabalaṃ ninye tadīyaṃ dvārakāṃ dhanam
BhP nīyamāne dhane gobhir nṛbhiś cācyutacoditaiḥ

BhP palāyamānau tau dṛṣṭvā māgadhaḥ prahasan balī
BhP anvadhāvad rathānīkair īśayor apramāṇavit
BhP pradrutya dūraṃ saṃśrāntau tuṅgam āruhatāṃ girim

BhP girau nilīnāv ājñāya nādhigamya padaṃ nṛpa
BhP dadāha girim edhobhiḥ samantād agnim utsṛjan
BhP tata utpatya tarasā dahyamānataṭād ubhau
BhP daśaikayojanāt tuṅgān nipetatur adho bhuvi

BhP brahmaṇā coditaḥ prādād balāyeti puroditam
BhP bhagavān api govinda upayeme kurūdvaha
BhP vaidarbhīṃ bhīṣmakasutāṃ śriyo mātrāṃ svayaṃvare
BhP pramathya tarasā rājñaḥ śālvādīṃś caidyapakṣagān
BhP paśyatāṃ sarvalokānāṃ tārkṣyaputraḥ sudhām iva
BhP śrīrājovāca

BhP rākṣasena vidhānena upayema iti śrutam
BhP bhagavan śrotum icchāmi kṛṣṇasyāmitatejasaḥ
BhP yathā māgadhaśālvādīn jitvā kanyām upāharat
BhP brahman kṛṣṇakathāḥ puṇyā mādhvīr lokamalāpahāḥ
BhP ko nu tṛpyeta śṛṇvānaḥ śrutajño nityanūtanāḥ
BhP śrībādarāyaṇir uvāca
BhP rājāsīd bhīṣmako nāma vidarbhādhipatir mahān
BhP tasya pancābhavan putrāḥ kanyaikā ca varānanā
BhP rukmy agrajo rukmaratho rukmabāhur anantaraḥ
BhP rukmakeśo rukmamālī rukmiṇy eṣā svasā satī
BhP sopaśrutya mukundasya rūpavīryaguṇaśriyaḥ
BhP gṛhāgatair gīyamānās taṃ mene sadṛśaṃ patim
BhP tāṃ buddhilakṣaṇaudārya rūpaśīlaguṇāśrayām
BhP kṛṣṇaś ca sadṛśīṃ bhāryāṃ samudvoḍhuṃ mano dadhe
BhP bandhūnām icchatāṃ dātuṃ kṛṣṇāya bhaginīṃ nṛpa
BhP tato nivārya kṛṣṇadviḍ rukmī caidyam amanyata
BhP tad avetyāsitāpāṅgī vaidarbhī durmanā bhṛśam
BhP vicintyāptaṃ dvijaṃ kañcit kṛṣṇāya prāhiṇod drutam
BhP dvārakāṃ sa samabhyetya pratīhāraiḥ praveśitaḥ
BhP apaśyad ādyaṃ puruṣam āsīnaṃ kāñcanāsane
BhP dṛṣṭvā brahmaṇyadevas tam avaruhya nijāsanāt
BhP upaveśyārhayāṃ cakre yathātmānaṃ divaukasaḥ
BhP taṃ bhuktavantaṃ viśrāntam upagamya satāṃ gatiḥ
BhP pāṇinābhimṛśan pādāv avyagras tam apṛcchata
BhP kaccid dvijavaraśreṣṭha dharmas te vṛddhasammataḥ
BhP vartate nātikṛcchreṇa santuṣṭamanasaḥ sadā
BhP santuṣṭo yarhi varteta brāhmaṇo yena kenacit
BhP ahīyamānaḥ svad dharmāt sa hy asyākhilakāmadhuk
BhP asantuṣṭo 'sakṛl lokān āpnoty api sureśvaraḥ
BhP akiñcano 'pi santuṣṭaḥ śete sarvāṅgavijvaraḥ
BhP viprān svalābhasantuṣṭān sādhūn bhūtasuhṛttamān
BhP nirahaṅkāriṇaḥ śāntān namasye śirasāsakṛt
BhP kaccid vaḥ kuśalaṃ brahman rājato yasya hi prajāḥ
BhP sukhaṃ vasanti viṣaye pālyamānāḥ sa me priyaḥ
BhP yatas tvam āgato durgaṃ nistīryeha yadicchayā
BhP sarvaṃ no brūhy aguhyaṃ cet kiṃ kāryaṃ karavāma te
BhP evaṃ sampṛṣṭasampraśno brāhmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinā
BhP līlāgṛhītadehena tasmai sarvam avarṇayat
BhP śrīrukmiṇy uvāca
BhP śrutvā guṇān bhuvanasundara śṛṇvatāṃ te
BhP nirviśya karṇavivarair harato 'ṅgatāpam
BhP rūpaṃ dṛśāṃ dṛśimatām akhilārthalābhaṃ
BhP tvayy acyutāviśati cittam apatrapaṃ me
BhP kā tvā mukunda mahatī kulaśīlarūpa
BhP vidyāvayodraviṇadhāmabhir ātmatulyam
BhP dhīrā patiṃ kulavatī na vṛṇīta kanyā
BhP kāle nṛsiṃha naralokamano'bhirāmam
BhP tan me bhavān khalu vṛtaḥ patir aṅga jāyām
BhP ātmārpitaś ca bhavato 'tra vibho vidhehi
BhP mā vīrabhāgam abhimarśatu caidya ārād
BhP gomāyuvan mṛgapater balim ambujākṣa
BhP pūrteṣṭadattaniyamavratadevavipra

BhP ārādhito yadi gadāgraja etya pāṇiṃ

BhP śvo bhāvini tvam ajitodvahane vidarbhān
BhP guptaḥ sametya pṛtanāpatibhiḥ parītaḥ
BhP nirmathya caidyamagadhendrabalaṃ prasahya
BhP māṃ rākṣasena vidhinodvaha vīryaśulkām
BhP antaḥpurāntaracarīm anihatya bandhūn
BhP tvām udvahe katham iti pravadāmy upāyam
BhP pūrvedyur asti mahatī kuladevayātrā
BhP yasyāṃ bahir navavadhūr girijām upeyāt

BhP yarhy ambujākṣa na labheya bhavatprasādaṃ
BhP jahyām asūn vratakṛśān śatajanmabhiḥ syāt
BhP brāhmaṇa uvāca

BhP vimṛśya kartuṃ yac cātra kriyatāṃ tad anantaram
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP vaidarbhyāḥ sa tu sandeśaṃ niśamya yadunandanaḥ
BhP pragṛhya pāṇinā pāṇiṃ prahasann idam abravīt
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP tathāham api taccitto nidrāṃ ca na labhe niśi
BhP vedāham rukmiṇā dveṣān mamodvāho nivāritaḥ
BhP tām ānayiṣya unmathya rājanyāpasadān mṛdhe
BhP matparām anavadyāṅgīm edhaso 'gniśikhām iva
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP udvāharkṣaṃ ca vijñāya rukmiṇyā madhusūdanaḥ
BhP rathaḥ saṃyujyatām āśu dārukety āha sārathim
BhP sa cāśvaiḥ śaibyasugrīva meghapuṣpabalāhakaiḥ
BhP yuktaṃ ratham upānīya tasthau prāñjalir agrataḥ
BhP āruhya syandanaṃ śaurir dvijam āropya tūrṇagaiḥ
BhP ānartād ekarātreṇa vidarbhān agamad dhayaiḥ
BhP rājā sa kuṇḍinapatiḥ putrasnehavaśānugaḥ
BhP śiśupālāya svāṃ kanyāṃ dāsyan karmāṇy akārayat

BhP pitṝn devān samabhyarcya viprāṃś ca vidhivan nṛpa
BhP bhojayitvā yathānyāyaṃ vācayām āsa maṅgalam
BhP susnātāṃ sudatīṃ kanyāṃ kṛtakautukamaṅgalām

BhP cakruḥ sāmargyajurmantrair vadhvā rakṣāṃ dvijottamāḥ
BhP purohito 'tharvavid vai juhāva grahaśāntaye
BhP hiraṇyarūpya vāsāṃsi tilāṃś ca guḍamiśritān
BhP prādād dhenūś ca viprebhyo rājā vidhividāṃ varaḥ
BhP evaṃ cedipatī rājā damaghoṣaḥ sutāya vai
BhP kārayām āsa mantrajñaiḥ sarvam abhyudayocitam
BhP madacyudbhir gajānīkaiḥ syandanair hemamālibhiḥ

BhP niveśayām āsa mudā kalpitānyaniveśane

BhP yotsyāmaḥ saṃhatās tena iti niścitamānasāḥ
BhP ājagmur bhūbhujaḥ sarve samagrabalavāhanāḥ

BhP balena mahatā sārdhaṃ bhrātṛsnehapariplutaḥ
BhP tvaritaḥ kuṇḍinaṃ prāgād gajāśvarathapattibhiḥ
BhP bhīṣmakanyā varārohā kāṅkṣanty āgamanaṃ hareḥ
BhP pratyāpattim apaśyantī dvijasyācintayat tadā

BhP nāgacchaty aravindākṣo nāhaṃ vedmy atra kāraṇam
BhP so 'pi nāvartate 'dyāpi matsandeśaharo dvijaḥ
BhP api mayy anavadyātmā dṛṣṭvā kiñcij jugupsitam
BhP matpāṇigrahaṇe nūnaṃ nāyāti hi kṛtodyamaḥ
BhP durbhagāyā na me dhātā nānukūlo maheśvaraḥ
BhP devī vā vimukhī gaurī rudrāṇī girijā satī
BhP evaṃ cintayatī bālā govindahṛtamānasā

BhP atha kṛṣṇavinirdiṣṭaḥ sa eva dvijasattamaḥ
BhP antaḥpuracarīṃ devīṃ rājaputrīm dadarśa ha

BhP ālakṣya lakṣaṇābhijñā samapṛcchac chucismitā
BhP tasyā āvedayat prāptaṃ śaśaṃsa yadunandanam
BhP uktaṃ ca satyavacanam ātmopanayanaṃ prati
BhP tam āgataṃ samājñāya vaidarbhī hṛṣṭamānasā
BhP na paśyantī brāhmaṇāya priyam anyan nanāma sā
BhP prāptau śrutvā svaduhitur udvāhaprekṣaṇotsukau
BhP abhyayāt tūryaghoṣeṇa rāmakṛṣṇau samarhaṇaiḥ
BhP madhuparkam upānīya vāsāṃsi virajāṃsi saḥ
BhP upāyanāny abhīṣṭāni vidhivat samapūjayat

BhP sasainyayoḥ sānugayor ātithyaṃ vidadhe yathā

BhP yathābalaṃ yathāvittaṃ sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ samarhayat

BhP āgatya netrāñjalibhiḥ papus tanmukhapaṅkajam

BhP kiñcit sucaritaṃ yan nas tena tuṣṭas trilokakṛt

BhP na priyāpriyayo rājan niṣṭhā dehiṣu dṛśyate

BhP yasyeṣadutkalitaroṣakaṭākṣamokṣair
BhP vartmādiśat kṣubhitanakratimiṅgalo 'bdhiḥ
BhP setuḥ kṛtaḥ svayaśa ujjvalitā ca laṅkā
BhP rakṣaḥśirāṃsi bhuvi petur iṣukṣatāni
BhP iti vijñātaviijñānam ṛkṣarājānam acyutaḥ
BhP vyājahāra mahārāja bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP abhimṛśyāravindākṣaḥ pāṇinā śaṃkareṇa tam
BhP kṛpayā parayā bhaktaṃ meghagambhīrayā girā
BhP maṇihetor iha prāptā vayam ṛkṣapate bilam
BhP mithyābhiśāpaṃ pramṛjann ātmano maṇināmunā
BhP ity uktaḥ svāṃ duhitaraṃ kanyāṃ jāmbavatīṃ mudā
BhP arhaṇārtham sa maṇinā kṛṣṇāyopajahāra ha
BhP adṛṣṭvā nirgamaṃ śaureḥ praviṣṭasya bilaṃ janāḥ
BhP pratīkṣya dvādaśāhāni duḥkhitāḥ svapuraṃ yayuḥ
BhP niśamya devakī devī rakmiṇy ānakadundubhiḥ
BhP suhṛdo jñātayo 'śocan bilāt kṛṣṇam anirgatam
BhP satrājitaṃ śapantas te duḥkhitā dvārakaukasaḥ
BhP upatasthuś candrabhāgāṃ durgāṃ kṛṣṇopalabdhaye
BhP teṣāṃ tu devyupasthānāt pratyādiṣṭāśiṣā sa ca
BhP prādurbabhūva siddhārthaḥ sadāro harṣayan hariḥ
BhP upalabhya hṛṣīkeśaṃ mṛtaṃ punar ivāgatam
BhP saha patnyā maṇigrīvaṃ sarve jātamahotsavāḥ
BhP satrājitaṃ samāhūya sabhāyāṃ rājasannidhau
BhP prāptiṃ cākhyāya bhagavān maṇiṃ tasmai nyavedayat
BhP sa cātivrīḍito ratnaṃ gṛhītvāvāṅmukhas tataḥ
BhP anutapyamāno bhavanam agamat svena pāpmanā
BhP so 'nudhyāyaṃs tad evāghaṃ balavadvigrahākulaḥ
BhP kathaṃ mṛjāmy ātmarajaḥ prasīded vācyutaḥ katham
BhP kim kṛtvā sādhu mahyaṃ syān na śaped vā jano yathā
BhP adīrghadarśanaṃ kṣudraṃ mūḍhaṃ draviṇalolupam
BhP dāsye duhitaraṃ tasmai strīratnaṃ ratnam eva ca
BhP upāyo 'yaṃ samīcīnas tasya śāntir na cānyathā
BhP evaṃ vyavasito buddhyā satrājit svasutāṃ śubhām
BhP maṇiṃ ca svayam udyamya kṛṣṇāyopajahāra ha
BhP tāṃ satyabhāmāṃ bhagavān upayeme yathāvidhi
BhP bahubhir yācitāṃ śīla rūpaudāryaguṇānvitām
BhP bhagavān āha na maṇiṃ pratīcchāmo vayaṃ nṛpa
BhP tavāstāṃ devabhaktasya vayaṃ ca phalabhāginaḥ
BhP śrībādarāyaṇir uvāca
BhP vijñātārtho 'pi govindo dagdhān ākarṇya pāṇḍavān
BhP kuntīṃ ca kulyakaraṇe saharāmo yayau kurūn
BhP bhīṣmaṃ kṛpaṃ sa viduraṃ gāndhārīṃ droṇam eva ca
BhP tulyaduḥkhau ca saṅgamya hā kaṣṭam iti hocatuḥ
BhP labdhvaitad antaraṃ rājan śatadhanvānam ūcatuḥ
BhP akrūrakṛtavarmāṇau maniḥ kasmān na gṛhyate
BhP yo 'smabhyaṃ sampratiśrutya kanyāratnaṃ vigarhya naḥ
BhP kṛṣṇāyādān na satrājit kasmād bhrātaram anviyāt
BhP evaṃ bhinnamatis tābhyāṃ satrājitam asattamaḥ
BhP śayānam avadhīl lobhāt sa pāpaḥ kṣīṇa jīvitaḥ
BhP strīṇāṃ vikrośamānānāṃ krandantīnām anāthavat
BhP hatvā paśūn saunikavan maṇim ādāya jagmivān
BhP satyabhāmā ca pitaraṃ hataṃ vīkṣya śucārpitā
BhP vyalapat tāta tāteti hā hatāsmīti muhyatī
BhP tailadroṇyāṃ mṛtaṃ prāsya jagāma gajasāhvayam
BhP kṛṣṇāya viditārthāya taptācakhyau pitur vadham
BhP tad ākarṇyeśvarau rājann anusṛtya nṛlokatām
BhP aho naḥ paramaṃ kaṣṭam ity asrākṣau vilepatuḥ
BhP āgatya bhagavāṃs tasmāt sabhāryaḥ sāgrajaḥ puram
BhP śatadhanvānam ārebhe hantuṃ hartuṃ maṇiṃ tataḥ
BhP so 'pi kṛtodyamaṃ jñātvā bhītaḥ prāṇaparīpsayā
BhP sāhāyye kṛtavarmāṇam ayācata sa cābravīt
BhP nāham īsvarayoḥ kuryāṃ helanaṃ rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP ko nu kṣemāya kalpeta tayor vṛjinam ācaran
BhP kaṃsaḥ sahānugo 'pīto yaddveṣāt tyājitaḥ śriyā
BhP jarāsandhaḥ saptadaśa saṃyugād viratho gataḥ
BhP pratyākhyātaḥ sa cākrūraṃ pārṣṇigrāham ayācata
BhP so 'py āha ko virudhyeta vidvān īśvarayor balam
BhP ya idaṃ līlayā viśvaṃ sṛjaty avati hanti ca
BhP ceṣṭāṃ viśvasṛjo yasya na vidur mohitājayā
BhP yaḥ saptahāyanaḥ śailam utpāṭyaikena pāṇinā
BhP dadhāra līlayā bāla ucchilīndhram ivārbhakaḥ
BhP namas tasmai bhagavate kṛṣṇāyādbhutakarmaṇe
BhP anantāyādibhūtāya kūṭasthāyātmane namaḥ
BhP pratyākhyātaḥ sa tenāpi śatadhanvā mahāmaṇim
BhP tasmin nyasyāśvam āruhya śatayojanagaṃ yayau
BhP garuḍadhvajam āruhya rathaṃ rāmajanārdanau
BhP anvayātāṃ mahāvegair aśvai rājan gurudruham
BhP mithilāyām upavane visṛjya patitaṃ hayam
BhP padbhyām adhāvat santrastaḥ kṛṣṇo 'py anvadravad ruṣā
BhP padāter bhagavāṃs tasya padātis tigmaneminā
BhP cakreṇa śira utkṛtya vāsasor vyacinon maṇim
BhP alabdhamaṇir āgatya kṛṣṇa āhāgrajāntikam
BhP vṛthā hataḥ śatadhanur maṇis tatra na vidyate
BhP tata āha balo nūnaṃ sa maṇiḥ śatadhanvanā
BhP kasmiṃścit puruṣe nyastas tam anveṣa puraṃ vraja
BhP ahaṃ vaideham icchāmi draṣṭuṃ priyatamaṃ mama
BhP ity uktvā mithilāṃ rājan viveśa yadanandanaḥ
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya maithilaḥ prītamānasaḥ
BhP arhayāṃ āsa vidhivad arhaṇīyaṃ samarhaṇaiḥ
BhP uvāsa tasyāṃ katicin mithilāyāṃ samā vibhuḥ
BhP mānitaḥ prītiyuktena janakena mahātmanā
BhP tato 'śikṣad gadāṃ kāle dhārtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhanaḥ
BhP keśavo dvārakām etya nidhanaṃ śatadhanvanaḥ
BhP aprāptiṃ ca maṇeḥ prāha priyāyāḥ priyakṛd vibhuḥ
BhP tataḥ sa kārayām āsa kriyā bandhor hatasya vai
BhP sākaṃ suhṛdbhir bhagavān yā yāḥ syuḥ sāmparāyikīḥ
BhP akrūraḥ kṛtavarmā ca śrutvā śatadhanor vadham
BhP vyūṣatur bhayavitrastau dvārakāyāḥ prayojakau
BhP akrūre proṣite 'riṣṭāny āsan vai dvārakaukasām
BhP śārīrā mānasās tāpā muhur daivikabhautikāḥ
BhP ity aṅgopadiśanty eke vismṛtya prāg udāhṛtam
BhP munivāsanivāse kiṃ ghaṭetāriṣṭadarśanam
BhP deve 'varṣati kāśīśaḥ śvaphalkāyāgatāya vai
BhP svasutāṃ gāṇdinīṃ prādāt tato 'varṣat sma kāśiṣu
BhP tatsutas tatprabhāvo 'sāv akrūro yatra yatra ha
BhP devo 'bhivarṣate tatra nopatāpā na mārīkāḥ
BhP iti vṛddhavacaḥ śrutvā naitāvad iha kāraṇam
BhP iti matvā samānāyya prāhākrūraṃ janārdanaḥ
BhP pūjayitvābhibhāṣyainaṃ kathayitvā priyāḥ kathāḥ
BhP vijñatākhilacitta jñaḥ smayamāna uvāca ha
BhP nanu dānapate nyastas tvayy āste śatadhanvanā
BhP syamantako maniḥ śrīmān viditaḥ pūrvam eva naḥ
BhP satrājito 'napatyatvād gṛhṇīyur duhituḥ sutāḥ
BhP dāyaṃ ninīyāpaḥ piṇḍān vimucyarṇaṃ ca śeṣitam
BhP tathāpi durdharas tv anyais tvayy āstāṃ suvrate maṇiḥ
BhP kintu mām agrajaḥ samyaṅ na pratyeti maṇiṃ prati
BhP darśayasva mahābhāga bandhūnāṃ śāntim āvaha
BhP avyucchinnā makhās te 'dya vartante rukmavedayaḥ
BhP evaṃ sāmabhir ālabdhaḥ śvaphalkatanayo maṇim
BhP ādāya vāsasācchannaḥ dadau sūryasamaprabham
BhP syamantakaṃ darśayitvā jñātibhyo raja ātmanaḥ
BhP vimṛjya maṇinā bhūyas tasmai pratyarpayat prabhuḥ
BhP yas tv etad bhagavata īśvarasya viṣṇor
BhP vīryāḍhyaṃ vṛjinaharaṃ sumaṅgalaṃ ca
BhP ākhyānaṃ paṭhati śṛṇoty anusmared vā
BhP duṣkīrtiṃ duritam apohya yāti śāntim
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ekadā pāṇḍavān draṣṭuṃ pratītān puruṣottamaḥ
BhP indraprasthaṃ gataḥ śṛīmān yuyudhānādibhir vṛtaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā tam āgataṃ pārthā mukundam akhileśvaram
BhP uttasthur yugapad vīrāḥ prāṇā mukhyam ivāgatam
BhP pariṣvajyācyutaṃ vīrā aṅgasaṅgahatainasaḥ
BhP sānurāgasmitaṃ vaktraṃ vīkṣya tasya mudaṃ yayuḥ
BhP yudhiṣṭhirasya bhīmasya kṛtvā pādābhivandanam
BhP phālgunaṃ parirabhyātha yamābhyāṃ cābhivanditaḥ
BhP paramāsana āsīnaṃ kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇam aninditā
BhP navoḍhā vrīḍitā kiñcic chanair etyābhyavandata
BhP tathaiva sātyakiḥ pārthaiḥ pūjitaś cābhivanditaḥ
BhP niṣasādāsane 'nye ca pūjitāḥ paryupāsata
BhP pṛthām samāgatya kṛtābhivādanas tayātihārdārdradṛśābhirambhitaḥ
BhP āpṛṣṭavāṃs tāṃ kuśalaṃ sahasnuṣāṃ pitṛṣvasāram paripṛṣṭabāndhavaḥ
BhP tam āha premavaiklavya ruddhakaṇṭhāśrulocanā
BhP smarantī tān bahūn kleśān kleśāpāyātmadarśanam
BhP tadaiva kuśalaṃ no 'bhūt sanāthās te kṛtā vayam
BhP jñatīn naḥ smaratā kṛṣṇa bhrātā me preṣitas tvayā
BhP na te 'sti svaparabhrāntir viśvasya suhṛdātmanaḥ
BhP tathāpi smaratāṃ śaśvat kleśān haṃsi hṛdi sthitaḥ
BhP yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
BhP kiṃ na ācaritaṃ śreyo na vedāham adhīśvara
BhP yogeśvarāṇāṃ durdarśo yan no dṛṣṭaḥ kumedhasām
BhP iti vai vārṣikān māsān rājñā so 'bhyarthitaḥ sukham
BhP janayan nayanānandam indraprasthaukasāṃ vibhuḥ
BhP ekadā ratham āruhya vijayo vānaradhvajam
BhP gāṇḍīvaṃ dhanur ādāya tūṇau cākṣayasāyakau
BhP sākaṃ kṛṣṇena sannaddho vihartuṃ vipinaṃ mahat
BhP bahuvyālamṛgākīrṇaṃ prāviśat paravīrahā
BhP tatrāvidhyac charair vyāghrān śūkarān mahiṣān rurūn
BhP śarabhān gavayān khaḍgān hariṇān śaśaśallakān
BhP tān ninyuḥ kiṅkarā rājñe medhyān parvaṇy upāgate
BhP tṛṭparītaḥ pariśrānto bibhatsur yamunām agāt
BhP tatropaspṛśya viśadaṃ pītvā vāri mahārathau
BhP kṛṣṇau dadṛśatuḥ kanyāṃ carantīṃ cārudarśanām
BhP tām āsādya varārohāṃ sudvijāṃ rucirānanām
BhP papraccha preṣitaḥ sakhyā phālgunaḥ pramadottamām
BhP kā tvaṃ kasyāsi suśroṇi kuto vā kiṃ cikīrṣasi
BhP manye tvāṃ patim icchantīṃ sarvaṃ kathaya śobhane
BhP śrīkālindy uvāca
BhP ahaṃ devasya savitur duhitā patim icchatī
BhP viṣṇuṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ tapaḥ paramam āsthitaḥ
BhP nānyaṃ patiṃ vṛṇe vīra tam ṛte śrīniketanam
BhP tuṣyatāṃ me sa bhagavān mukundo 'nāthasaṃśrayaḥ
BhP kālindīti samākhyātā vasāmi yamunājale
BhP nirmite bhavane pitrā yāvad acyutadarśanam
BhP tathāvadad guḍākeśo vāsudevāya so 'pi tām
BhP ratham āropya tadvidvān dharmarājam upāgamat
BhP yadaiva kṛṣṇaḥ sandiṣṭaḥ pārthānāṃ paramādbutam
BhP kārayām āsa nagaraṃ vicitraṃ viśvakarmaṇā
BhP bhagavāṃs tatra nivasan svānāṃ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP agnaye khāṇḍavaṃ dātum arjunasyāsa sārathiḥ
BhP so 'gnis tuṣṭo dhanur adād dhayān śvetān rathaṃ nṛpa
BhP arjunāyākṣayau tūṇau varma cābhedyam astribhiḥ
BhP mayaś ca mocito vahneḥ sabhāṃ sakhya upāharat
BhP yasmin duryodhanasyāsīj jalasthaladṛśibhramaḥ
BhP sa tena samanujñātaḥ suhṛdbhiś cānumoditaḥ
BhP āyayau dvārakāṃ bhūyaḥ sātyakipramakhair vṛtaḥ
BhP athopayeme kālindīṃ supuṇyartvṛkṣa ūrjite
BhP vitanvan paramānandaṃ svānāṃ paramamaṅgalaḥ
BhP vindyānuvindyāv āvantyau duryodhanavaśānugau
BhP svayaṃvare svabhaginīṃ kṛṣṇe saktāṃ nyaṣedhatām
BhP rājādhidevyās tanayāṃ mitravindāṃ pitṛṣvasuḥ
BhP prasahya hṛtavān kṛṣṇo rājan rājñāṃ prapaśyatām
BhP nagnajin nāma kauśalya āsīd rājātidhārmikaḥ
BhP tasya satyābhavat kanyā devī nāgnajitī nṛpa
BhP na tāṃ śekur nṛpā voḍhum ajitvā saptagovṛṣān
BhP tīkṣṇaśṛṅgān sudurdharṣān vīryagandhāsahān khalān
BhP tāṃ śrutvā vṛṣajillabhyāṃ bhagavān sātvatāṃ patiḥ
BhP jagāma kauśalyapuraṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
BhP sa kośalapatiḥ prītaḥ pratyutthānāsanādibhiḥ
BhP arhaṇenāpi guruṇā pūjayan pratinanditaḥ
BhP varaṃ vilokyābhimataṃ samāgataṃ narendrakanyā cakame ramāpatim
BhP bhūyād ayaṃ me patir āśiṣo 'nalaḥ karotu satyā yadi me dhṛto vrataḥ
BhP yatpādapaṅkajarajaḥ śirasā bibharti
BhP śṛīr abyajaḥ sagiriśaḥ saha lokapālaiḥ
BhP līlātanuḥ svakṛtasetuparīpsayā yaḥ
BhP kāle 'dadhat sa bhagavān mama kena tuṣyet
BhP arcitaṃ punar ity āha nārāyaṇa jagatpate
BhP ātmānandena pūrṇasya karavāṇi kim alpakaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP tam āha bhagavān hṛṣṭaḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ
BhP meghagambhīrayā vācā sasmitaṃ kurunandana
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP narendra yācñā kavibhir vigarhitā rājanyabandhor nijadharmavartinaḥ
BhP tathāpi yāce tava sauhṛdecchayā kanyāṃ tvadīyāṃ na hi śulkadā vayam
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP ko 'nyas te 'bhyadhiko nātha kanyāvara ihepsitaḥ
BhP guṇaikadhāmno yasyāṅge śrīr vasaty anapāyinī
BhP kintv asmābhiḥ kṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ samayaḥ sātvatarṣabha
BhP puṃsāṃ vīryaparīkṣārthaṃ kanyāvaraparīpsayā
BhP saptaite govṛṣā vīra durdāntā duravagrahāḥ
BhP etair bhagnāḥ subahavo bhinnagātrā nṛpātmajāḥ
BhP yad ime nigṛhītāḥ syus tvayaiva yadunandana
BhP varo bhavān abhimato duhitur me śriyaḥpate
BhP evaṃ samayam ākarṇya baddhvā parikaraṃ prabhuḥ
BhP ātmānaṃ saptadhā kṛtvā nyagṛhṇāl līlayaiva tān
BhP baddhvā tān dāmabhiḥ śaurir bhagnadarpān hataujasaḥ
BhP vyakarsal līlayā baddhān bālo dārumayān yathā
BhP tataḥ prītaḥ sutāṃ rājā dadau kṛṣṇāya vismitaḥ
BhP tāṃ pratyagṛhṇād bhagavān vidhivat sadṛśīṃ prabhuḥ
BhP rājapatnyaś ca duhituḥ kṛṣṇaṃ labdhvā priyaṃ patim
BhP lebhire paramānandaṃ jātaś ca paramotsavaḥ
BhP śaṅkhabheryānakā nedur gītavādyadvijāśiṣaḥ
BhP narā nāryaḥ pramuditāḥ suvāsaḥsragalaṅkṛtāḥ
BhP daśadhenusahasrāṇi pāribarham adād vibhuḥ
BhP yuvatīnāṃ trisāhasraṃ niṣkagrīvasuvāsasam
BhP navanāgasahasrāṇi nāgāc chataguṇān rathān
BhP rathāc chataguṇān aśvān aśvāc chataguṇān narān
BhP dampatī ratham āropya mahatyā senayā vṛtau
BhP snehapraklinnahṛdayo yāpayām āsa kośalaḥ
BhP śrutvaitad rurudhur bhūpā nayantaṃ pathi kanyakām
BhP bhagnavīryāḥ sudurmarṣā yadubhir govṛṣaiḥ purā
BhP tān asyataḥ śaravrātān bandhupriyakṛd arjunaḥ
BhP gāṇḍīvī kālayām āsa siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgān iva
BhP pāribarham upāgṛhya dvārakām etya satyayā
BhP reme yadūnām ṛṣabho bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP śrutakīrteḥ sutāṃ bhadrāṃ upayeme pitṛṣvasuḥ
BhP kaikeyīṃ bhrātṛbhir dattāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ santardanādibhiḥ
BhP sutāṃ ca madrādhipater lakṣmaṇāṃ lakṣaṇair yatām
BhP svayaṃvare jahāraikaḥ sa suparṇaḥ sudhām iva
BhP anyāś caivaṃvidhā bhāryāḥ kṛṣṇasyāsan sahasraśaḥ
BhP bhaumaṃ hatvā tannirodhād āhṛtāś cārudarśanāḥ
BhP śrīrājovāca yathā hato bhagavatā bhaumo yene ca tāḥ striyaḥ
BhP niruddhā etad ācakṣva vikramaṃ śārṅgadhanvanaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP indreṇa hṛtachatreṇa hṛtakuṇḍalabandhunā
BhP hṛtāmarādristhānena jñāpito bhaumaceṣṭitam
BhP sabhāryo garuḍārūḍhaḥ prāgjyotiṣapuraṃ yayau
