BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ sauratasaṃlāpair bhagavān jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP svarato ramayā reme naralokaṃ viḍambayan
BhP tathānyāsām api vibhur gṛhesu gṛhavān iva
BhP āsthito gṛhamedhīyān dharmān lokagurur hariḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ekaikaśas tāḥ kṛṣṇasya putrān daśadaśābaāḥ
BhP ajījanann anavamān pituḥ sarvātmasampadā
BhP gṛhād anapagaṃ vīkṣya rājaputryo 'cyutaṃ sthitam
BhP preṣṭhaṃ nyamaṃsata svaṃ svaṃ na tattattvavidaḥ striyaḥ
BhP cārvabjakośavadanāyatabāhunetra
BhP sapremahāsarasavīkṣitavalgujalpaiḥ
BhP sammohitā bhagavato na mano vijetuṃ
BhP svair vibhramaiḥ samaśakan vanitā vibhūmnaḥ
BhP smāyāvalokalavadarśitabhāvahāri
BhP bhrūmaṇḍalaprahitasauratamantraśauṇḍaiḥ
BhP patnyas tu śoḍaśasahasram anaṅgabāṇair
BhP yasyendriyaṃ vimathitum karaṇair na śekuḥ
BhP itthaṃ ramāpatim avāpya patiṃ striyas tā
BhP brahmādayo 'pi na viduḥ padavīṃ yadīyām
BhP bhejur mudāviratam edhitayānurāga
BhP hāsāvalokanavasaṅgamalālasādyam
BhP pratyudgamāsanavarārhaṇapādaśauca
BhP tāmbūlaviśramaṇavījanagandhamālyaiḥ
BhP keśaprasāraśayanasnapanopahāryaiḥ
BhP dāsīśatā api vibhor vidadhuḥ sma dāsyam
BhP tāsāṃ yā daśaputrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇastrīṇāṃ puroditāḥ
BhP aṣṭau mahiṣyas tatputrān pradyumnādīn gṛṇāmi te
BhP cārudeṣṇaḥ sudeṣṇaś ca cārudehaś ca vīryavān
BhP sucāruś cāruguptaś ca bhadracārus tathāparaḥ
BhP cārucandro vicāruś ca cāruś ca daśamo hareḥ
BhP pradyumnapramukhā jātā rukmiṇyāṃ nāvamāḥ pituḥ
BhP bhānuḥ subhānuḥ svarbhānuḥ prabhānur bhānumāṃs tathā
BhP candrabhānur bṛhadbhānur atibhānus tathāṣṭamaḥ
BhP śrībhānuḥ pratibhānuś ca satyabhāmātmajā daśa
BhP sāmbaḥ sumitraḥ purujic chatajic ca sahasrajit
BhP viyayaś citraketuś ca vasumān draviḍaḥ kratuḥ
BhP jāmbavatyāḥ sutā hy ete sāmbādyāḥ pitṛsammatāḥ
BhP vīraś candro 'śvasenaś ca citragur vegavān vṛṣaḥ
BhP āmaḥ śaṅkur vasuḥ śrīmān kuntir nāgnajiteḥ sutāḥ
BhP śrutaḥ kavir vṛṣo vīraḥ subāhur bhadra ekalaḥ
BhP śāntir darśaḥ pūrṇamāsaḥ kālindyāḥ somako 'varaḥ
BhP praghoṣo gātravān siṃho balaḥ prabala ūrdhagaḥ
BhP mādryāḥ putrā mahāśaktiḥ saha ojo 'parājitaḥ
BhP vṛko harṣo 'nilo gṛdhro vardhanonnāda eva ca
BhP mahāṃsaḥ pāvano vahnir mitravindātmajāḥ kṣudhiḥ
BhP saṅgrāmajid bṛhatsenaḥ śūraḥ praharaṇo 'rijit
BhP jayaḥ subhadro bhadrāyā vāma āyuś ca satyakaḥ
BhP dīptimāṃs tāmrataptādyā rohiṇyās tanayā hareḥ
BhP pradyamnāc cāniruddho 'bhūd rukmavatyāṃ mahābalaḥ
BhP putryāṃ tu rukmiṇo rājan nāmnā bhojakaṭe pure
BhP eteṣāṃ putrapautrāś ca babhūvuḥ koṭiśo nṛpa
BhP mātaraḥ kṛṣṇajātīnāṃ sahasrāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP kathaṃ rukmy arīputrāya prādād duhitaraṃ yudhi
BhP kṛṣṇena paribhūtas taṃ hantuṃ randhraṃ pratīkṣate
BhP etad ākhyāhi me vidvan dviṣor vaivāhikaṃ mithaḥ
BhP anāgatam atītaṃ ca vartamānam atīndriyam
BhP viprakṛṣṭaṃ vyavahitaṃ samyak paśyanti yoginaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP vṛtaḥ svayaṃvare sākṣād anaṇgo 'ṇgayutas tayā
BhP rājñaḥ sametān nirjitya jahāraikaratho yudhi
BhP yady apy anusmaran vairaṃ rukmī kṛṣṇāvamānitaḥ
BhP vyatarad bhāgineyāya sutāṃ kurvan svasuḥ priyam
BhP rukmiṇyās tanayāṃ rājan kṛtavarmasuto balī
BhP upayeme viśālākṣīṃ kanyāṃ cārumatīṃ kila
BhP dauhitrāyāniruddhāya pautrīṃ rukmy ādadād dhareḥ
BhP rocanāṃ baddhavairo 'pi svasuḥ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP jānann adharmaṃ tad yaunaṃ snehapāśānubandhanaḥ
BhP tasminn abhyudaye rājan rukmiṇī rāmakeśavau
BhP puraṃ bhojakaṭaṃ jagmuḥ sāmbapradyumnakādayaḥ
BhP tasmin nivṛtta udvāhe kāliṅgapramukhā nṛpāḥ
BhP dṛptās te rukmiṇaṃ procur balam akṣair vinirjaya
BhP anakṣajño hy ayaṃ rājann api tadvyasanaṃ mahat
BhP ity ukto balam āhūya tenākṣair rukmy adīvyata
BhP śataṃ sahasram ayutaṃ rāmas tatrādade paṇam
BhP taṃ tu rukmy ajayat tatra kāliṅgaḥ prāhasad balam
BhP dantān sandarśayann uccair nāmṛṣyat tad dhalāyudhaḥ
BhP tato lakṣaṃ rukmy agṛhṇād glahaṃ tatrājayad balaḥ
BhP jitavān aham ity āha rukmī kaitavam āśritaḥ
BhP manyunā kṣubhitaḥ śrīmān samudra iva parvaṇi
BhP jātyāruṇākṣo 'tiruṣā nyarbudaṃ glaham ādade
BhP taṃ cāpi jitavān rāmo dharmeṇa chalam āśritaḥ
BhP rukmī jitaṃ mayātreme vadantu prāśnikā iti
BhP tadābravīn nabhovāṇī balenaiva jito glahaḥ
BhP dharmato vacanenaiva rukmī vadati vai mṛṣā
BhP tām anādṛtya vaidarbho duṣṭarājanyacoditaḥ
BhP saṅkarṣaṇaṃ parihasan babhāṣe kālacoditaḥ
BhP naivākṣakovidā yūyaṃ gopālā vanagocarāḥ
BhP akṣair dīvyanti rājāno bāṇaiś ca na bhavādṛśāḥ
BhP rukmiṇaivam adhikṣipto rājabhiś copahāsitaḥ
BhP kruddhaḥ parigham udyamya jaghne taṃ nṛmṇasaṃsadi
BhP kaliṅgarājaṃ tarasā gṛhītvā daśame pade
BhP dantān apātayat kruddho yo 'hasad vivṛtair dvijaiḥ
BhP anye nirbhinnabāhūru śiraso rudhirokṣitāḥ
BhP rājāno dudravar bhītā balena paṅghārditāḥ
BhP nihate rukmiṇi śyāle nābravīt sādhv asādhu vā
BhP rakmiṇībalayo rājan snehabhaṅgabhayād dhariḥ
BhP tato 'niruddhaṃ saha sūryayā varaṃ rathaṃ samāropya yayuḥ kuśasthalīm
BhP rāmādayo bhojakaṭād daśārhāḥ siddhākhilārthā madhusūdanāśrayāḥ
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP bāṇasya tanayām ūṣām upayeme yadūttamaḥ
BhP tatra yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ hariśaṅkarayor mahat
BhP etat sarvaṃ mahāyogin samākhyātuṃ tvam arhasi
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP bāṇaḥ putraśatajyeṣṭho baler āsīn mahātmanaḥ
BhP yena vāmanarūpāya haraye 'dāyi medinī
BhP tasyaurasaḥ suto bānaḥ śivabhaktirataḥ sadā
BhP mānyo vadānyo dhīmāṃś ca satyasandho dṛḍhavrataḥ
BhP śoṇitākhye pure ramye sa rājyam akarot purā
BhP tasya śambhoḥ prasādena kiṅkarā iva te 'marāḥ
BhP sahasrabāhur vādyena tāṇdave 'toṣayan mṛḍam
BhP bhagavān sarvabhūteśaḥ śaraṇyo bhaktavatsalaḥ
BhP vareṇa chandayām āsa sa taṃ vavre purādhipam
BhP sa ekadāha giriśaṃ pārśvasthaṃ vīryadurmadaḥ
BhP kirīṭenārkavarṇena saṃspṛśaṃs tatpadāmbujam
BhP namasye tvāṃ mahādeva lokānāṃ gurum īśvaram
BhP puṃsām apūrṇakāmānāṃ kāmapūrāmarāṅghripam
BhP doḥsahasraṃ tvayā dattaṃ paraṃ bhārāya me 'bhavat
BhP trilokyāṃ pratiyoddhāraṃ na labhe tvad ṛte samam
BhP kaṇḍūtyā nibhṛtair dorbhir yuyutsur diggajān aham
BhP ādyāyāṃ cūrṇayann adrīn bhītās te 'pi pradudruvuḥ
BhP tac chrutvā bhagavān kruddhaḥ ketus te bhajyate yadā
BhP tvaddarpaghnaṃ bhaven mūḍha saṃyugaṃ matsamena te
BhP ity uktaḥ kumatir hṛṣṭaḥ svagṛhaṃ prāviśan nṛpa
BhP pratīkṣan giriśādeśaṃ svavīryanaśanam kudhīḥ
BhP tasyoṣā nāma duhitā svapne prādyumninā ratim
BhP kanyālabhata kāntena prāg adṛṣṭaśrutena sā
BhP sā tatra tam apaśyantī kvāsi kānteti vādinī
BhP sakhīnāṃ madhya uttasthau vihvalā vrīḍitā bhṛśam
BhP bāṇasya mantrī kumbhāṇḍaś citralekhā ca tatsutā
BhP sakhy apṛcchat sakhīm ūṣāṃ kautūhalasamanvitā
BhP kaṃ tvaṃ mṛgayase subhru kīdṛśas te manorathaḥ
BhP hastagrāhaṃ na te 'dyāpi rājaputry upalakṣaye
BhP dṛṣṭaḥ kaścin naraḥ svapne śyāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ
BhP pītavāsā bṛhadbāhur yoṣitāṃ hṛdayaṃgamaḥ
BhP tam ahaṃ mṛgaye kāntaṃ pāyayitvādharaṃ madhu
BhP kvāpi yātaḥ spṛhayatīṃ kṣiptvā māṃ vṛjinārṇave
BhP citralekhovāca
BhP vyasanaṃ te 'pakarṣāmi trilokyāṃ yadi bhāvyate
BhP tam āneṣye varaṃ yas te manohartā tam ādiśa
BhP ity uktvā devagandharva siddhacāraṇapannagān
BhP daityavidyādharān yakṣān manujāṃś ca yathālikhat
BhP manujeṣu ca sā vṛṣnīn śūram ānakadundubhim
BhP vyalikhad rāmakṛṣṇau ca pradyumnaṃ vīkṣya lajjitā
BhP aniruddhaṃ vilikhitaṃ vīkṣyoṣāvāṅmukhī hriyā
BhP so 'sāv asāv iti prāha smayamānā mahīpate
BhP citralekhā tam ājñāya pautraṃ kṛṣṇasya yoginī
BhP yayau vihāyasā rājan dvārakāṃ kṛṣṇapālitām
BhP tatra suptaṃ suparyaṅke prādyumniṃ yogam āsthitā
BhP gṛhītvā śoṇitapuraṃ sakhyai priyam adarśayat
BhP sā ca taṃ sundaravaraṃ vilokya muditānanā
BhP duṣprekṣye svagṛhe pumbhī reme prādyumninā samam
BhP parārdhyavāsaḥsraggandha dhūpadīpāsanādibhiḥ
BhP pānabhojanabhakṣyaiś ca vākyaiḥ śuśrūṣaṇārcitaḥ
BhP gūḍhaḥ kanyāpure śaśvat pravṛddhasnehayā tayā
BhP nāhargaṇān sa bubudhe ūṣayāpahṛtendriyaḥ
BhP tāṃ tathā yaduvīreṇa bhujyamānāṃ hatavratām
BhP hetubhir lakṣayāṃ cakrur āpṛītāṃ duravacchadaiḥ
BhP bhaṭā āvedayāṃ cakrū rājaṃs te duhitur vayam
BhP viceṣṭitaṃ lakṣayāma kanyāyāḥ kuladūṣaṇam
BhP anapāyibhir asmābhir guptāyāś ca gṛhe prabho
BhP kanyāyā dūṣaṇaṃ pumbhir duṣprekṣyāyā na vidmahe
BhP tataḥ pravyathito bāṇo duhituḥ śrutadūṣaṇaḥ
BhP tvaritaḥ kanyakāgāraṃ prāpto 'drākṣīd yadūdvaham
BhP kāmātmajaṃ taṃ bhuvanaikasundaraṃ śyāmaṃ piśaṅgāmbaram ambujekṣaṇam
BhP bṛhadbhujaṃ kuṇḍalakuntalatviṣā smitāvalokena ca maṇḍitānanam
BhP dīvyantam akṣaiḥ priyayābhinṛmṇayā tadaṅgasaṅgastanakuṅkumasrajam
BhP bāhvor dadhānaṃ madhumallikāśritāṃ tasyāgra āsīnam avekṣya vismitaḥ
BhP sa taṃ praviṣṭaṃ vṛtam ātatāyibhir bhaṭair anīkair avalokya mādhavaḥ
BhP udyamya maurvaṃ parighaṃ vyavasthito yathāntako daṇḍadharo jighāṃsayā
BhP jighṛkṣayā tān paritaḥ prasarpataḥ śuno yathā śūkarayūthapo 'hanat
BhP te hanyamānā bhavanād vinirgatā nirbhinnamūrdhorubhujāḥ pradudruvuḥ
BhP taṃ nāgapāśair balinandano balī ghnantaṃ svasainyaṃ kupito babandha ha
BhP ūṣā bhṛśaṃ śokaviṣādavihvalā baddhaṃ niśamyāśrukalākṣy arautsīt
BhP śṛīśuka uvāca
BhP apaśyatāṃ cāniruddhaṃ tadbandhūnāṃ ca bhārata
BhP catvāro vārṣikā māsā vyatīyur anuśocatām
BhP nāradāt tad upākarṇya vārtāṃ baddhasya karma ca
BhP prayayuḥ śoṇitapuraṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇadaivatāḥ
BhP pradyumno yuyudhānaś ca gadaḥ sāmbo 'tha sāraṇaḥ
BhP nandopanandabhadrādyā rāmakṛṣṇānuvartinaḥ
BhP akṣauhiṇībhir dvādaśabhiḥ sametāḥ sarvato diśam
BhP rurudhur bāṇanagaraṃ samantāt sātvatarṣabhāḥ
BhP bhajyamānapurodyāna prākārāṭṭālagopuram
BhP prekṣamāṇo ruṣāviṣṭas tulyasainyo 'bhiniryayau
BhP bāṇārthe bhagavān rudraḥ sasutaḥ pramathair vṛtaḥ
BhP āruhya nandivṛṣabhaṃ yuyudhe rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP āsīt sutumulaṃ yuddham adbhutaṃ romaharṣaṇam
BhP kṛṣṇaśaṅkarayo rājan pradyumnaguhayor api
BhP kumbhāṇḍakūpakarṇābhyāṃ balena saha saṃyugaḥ
BhP sāmbasya bāṇaputreṇa bāṇena saha sātyakeḥ
BhP brahmādayaḥ surādhīśā munayaḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
BhP gandharvāpsaraso yakṣā vimānair draṣṭum āgaman
BhP śaṅkarānucarān śaurir bhūtapramathaguhyakān
BhP ḍākinīr yātudhānāṃś ca vetālān savināyakān
BhP pretamātṛpiśācāṃś ca kuṣmāṇḍān brahmarākṣasān
BhP drāvayām āsa tīkṣṇāgraiḥ śaraiḥ śārṅgadhanuścyutaiḥ
BhP pṛthagvidhāni prāyuṅkta piṇāky astrāṇi śārṅgiṇe
BhP pratyastraiḥ śamayām āsa śārṅgapāṇir avismitaḥ
BhP brahmāstrasya ca brahmāstraṃ vāyavyasya ca pārvatam
BhP āgneyasya ca pārjanyaṃ naijaṃ pāśupatasya ca
BhP mohayitvā tu giriśaṃ jṛmbhaṇāstreṇa jṛmbhitam
BhP bāṇasya pṛtanāṃ śaurir jaghānāsigadeṣubhiḥ
BhP skandaḥ pradyumnabāṇaughair ardyamānaḥ samantataḥ
BhP asṛg vimuñcan gātrebhyaḥ śikhināpakramad raṇāt
BhP kumbhāṇḍakūpakarṇaś ca petatur muṣalārditau
BhP dudruvus tadanīkani hatanāthāni sarvataḥ
BhP viśīryamāṇam svabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā bāṇo 'tyamarṣitaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇam abhyadravat saṅkhye rathī hitvaiva sātyakim
BhP dhanūṃṣy ākṛṣya yugapad bāṇaḥ pañcaśatāni vai
BhP ekaikasmin śarau dvau dvau sandadhe raṇadurmadaḥ
BhP tāni ciccheda bhagavān dhanūṃsi yugapad dhariḥ
BhP sārathiṃ ratham aśvāṃś ca hatvā śaṅkham apūrayat
BhP tanmātā koṭarā nāma nagnā maktaśiroruhā
BhP puro 'vatasthe kṛṣṇasya putraprāṇarirakṣayā
BhP tatas tiryaṅmukho nagnām anirīkṣan gadāgrajaḥ
BhP bāṇaś ca tāvad virathaś chinnadhanvāviśat puram
BhP vidrāvite bhūtagaṇe jvaras tu trīśirās trīpāt
BhP abhyadhāvata dāśārhaṃ dahann iva diśo daśa
BhP atha nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ taṃ dṛṣṭvā vyasṛjaj jvaram
BhP māheśvaro vaiṣṇavaś ca yuyudhāte jvarāv ubhau
BhP māheśvaraḥ samākrandan vaiṣṇavena balārditaḥ
BhP alabdhvābhayam anyatra bhīto māheśvaro jvaraḥ
BhP śaraṇārthī hṛṣīkeśaṃ tuṣṭāva prayatāñjaliḥ
BhP jvara uvāca
BhP namāmi tvānantaśaktiṃ pareśam sarvātmānaṃ kevalaṃ jñaptimātram
BhP viśvotpattisthānasaṃrodhahetuṃ yat tad brahma brahmaliṅgam praśāntam
BhP kālo daivaṃ karma jīvaḥ svabhāvo dravyaṃ kṣetraṃ prāṇa ātmā vikāraḥ
BhP tatsaṅghāto bījarohapravāhas tvanmāyaiṣā tanniṣedhaṃ prapadye
BhP nānābhāvair līlayaivopapannair devān sādhūn lokasetūn bibharṣi
BhP haṃsy unmārgān hiṃsayā vartamānān janmaitat te bhārahārāya bhūmeḥ
BhP tapto 'ham te tejasā duḥsahena śāntogreṇātyulbaṇena jvareṇa
BhP tāvat tāpo dehināṃ te 'nghrimūlaṃ no severan yāvad āśānubaddhāḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP triśiras te prasanno 'smi vyetu te majjvarād bhayam
BhP yo nau smarati saṃvādaṃ tasya tvan na bhaved bhayam
BhP ity ukto 'cyutam ānamya gato māheśvaro jvaraḥ
BhP bāṇas tu ratham ārūḍhaḥ prāgād yotsyan janārdanam
BhP tato bāhusahasreṇa nānāyudhadharo 'suraḥ
BhP mumoca paramakruddho bāṇāṃś cakrāyudhe nṛpa
BhP tasyāsyato 'strāṇy asakṛc cakreṇa kṣuraneminā
BhP ciccheda bhagavān bāhūn śākhā iva vanaspateḥ
BhP bāhuṣu chidyamāneṣu bāṇasya bhagavān bhavaḥ
BhP bhaktānakampy upavrajya cakrāyudham abhāṣata
BhP śrīrudra uvāca
BhP tvaṃ hi brahma paraṃ jyotir gūḍhaṃ brahmaṇi vāṅmaye
BhP yaṃ paśyanty amalātmāna ākāśam iva kevalam
BhP nābhir nabho 'gnir mukham ambu reto
BhP dyauḥ śīrṣam āśāḥ śrutir aṅghrir urvī
BhP candro mano yasya dṛg arka ātmā
BhP ahaṃ samudro jaṭharaṃ bhujendraḥ
BhP romāṇi yasyauṣadhayo 'mbuvāhāḥ
BhP keśā viriñco dhiṣaṇā visargaḥ
BhP prajāpatir hṛdayaṃ yasya dharmaḥ
BhP sa vai bhavān puruṣo lokakalpaḥ
BhP tavāvatāro 'yam akuṇṭhadhāman dharmasya guptyai jagato hitāya
BhP vayaṃ ca sarve bhavatānubhāvitā vibhāvayāmo bhuvanāni sapta
BhP tvam eka ādyaḥ puruṣo 'dvitīyas turyaḥ svadṛg dhetur ahetur īśaḥ
BhP pratīyase 'thāpi yathāvikāraṃ svamāyayā sarvaguṇaprasiddhyai
BhP yathaiva sūryaḥ pihitaś chāyayā svayā
BhP chāyāṃ ca rūpāṇi ca sañcakāsti
BhP evaṃ guṇenāpihito guṇāṃs tvam
BhP ātmapradīpo guṇinaś ca bhūman
BhP yanmāyāmohitadhiyaḥ putradāragṛhādiṣu
BhP unmajjanti nimajjanti prasaktā vṛjinārṇave
BhP devadattam imaṃ labdhvā nṛlokam ajitendriyaḥ
BhP yo nādriyeta tvatpādau sa śocyo hy ātmavañcakaḥ
BhP yas tvāṃ visṛjate martya ātmānaṃ priyam īśvaram
BhP viparyayendriyārthārthaṃ viṣam atty amṛtaṃ tyajan
BhP ahaṃ brahmātha vibudhā munayaś cāmalāśayāḥ
BhP sarvātmanā prapannās tvām ātmānaṃ preṣṭham īśvaram
BhP taṃ tvā jagatsthityudayāntahetuṃ
BhP samaṃ prasāntaṃ suhṛdātmadaivam
BhP ananyam ekaṃ jagadātmaketaṃ
BhP bhavāpavargāya bhajāma devam
BhP ayaṃ mameṣṭo dayito 'nuvartī mayābhayaṃ dattam amuṣya deva
BhP sampādyatāṃ tad bhavataḥ prasādo yathā hi te daityapatau prasādaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP yad āttha bhagavaṃs tvaṃ naḥ karavāma priyaṃ tava
BhP bhavato yad vyavasitaṃ tan me sādhv anumoditam
BhP avadhyo 'yaṃ mamāpy eṣa vairocanisuto 'suraḥ
BhP prahrādāya varo datto na vadhyo me tavānvayaḥ
BhP darpopaśamanāyāsya pravṛkṇā bāhavo mayā
BhP sūditaṃ ca balaṃ bhūri yac ca bhārāyitaṃ bhuvaḥ
BhP catvāro 'sya bhujāḥ śiṣṭā bhaviṣyaty ajarāmaraḥ
BhP pārṣadamukhyo bhavato na kutaścidbhayo 'suraḥ
BhP iti labdhvābhayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya śirasāsuraḥ
BhP prādyumniṃ ratham āropya savadhvo samupānayat
BhP akṣauhiṇyā parivṛtaṃ suvāsaḥsamalaṅkṛtam
BhP sapatnīkaṃ puraskṛtya yayau rudrānumoditaḥ
BhP svarājadhānīṃ samalaṅkṛtāṃ dhvajaiḥ
BhP satoraṇair ukṣitamārgacatvarām
BhP viveśa śaṅkhānakadundubhisvanair
BhP abhyudyataḥ paurasuhṛddvijātibhiḥ
BhP ya evaṃ kṛṣṇavijayaṃ śaṅkareṇa ca saṃyugam
BhP saṃsmaret prātar utthāya na tasya syāt parājayaḥ
BhP śrībādarāyaṇir uvāca
BhP ekadopavanaṃ rājan jagmur yadukumārakāḥ
BhP vihartuṃ sāmbapradyumna cārubhānugadādayaḥ
BhP krīḍitvā suciraṃ tatra vicinvantaḥ pipāsitāḥ
BhP jalaṃ nirudake kūpe dadṛśuḥ sattvam adbhutam
BhP kṛkalāsaṃ girinibhaṃ vīkṣya vismitamānasāḥ
BhP tasya coddharaṇe yatnaṃ cakrus te kṛpayānvitāḥ
BhP carmajais tāntavaiḥ pāśair baddhvā patitam arbhakāḥ
BhP nāśaknuran samuddhartuṃ kṛṣṇāyācakhyur utsukāḥ
BhP tatrāgatyāravindākṣo bhagavān viśvabhāvanaḥ
BhP vīkṣyojjahāra vāmena taṃ kareṇa sa līlayā
BhP sa uttamaḥślokakarābhimṛṣṭo vihāya sadyaḥ kṛkalāsarūpam
BhP santaptacāmīkaracāruvarṇaḥ svargy adbhutālaṅkaraṇāmbarasrak
BhP papraccha vidvān api tannidānaṃ janeṣu vikhyāpayituṃ mukundaḥ
BhP kas tvaṃ mahābhāga vareṇyarūpo devottamaṃ tvāṃ gaṇayāmi nūnam
BhP daśām imāṃ vā katamena karmaṇā samprāpito 'sy atadarhaḥ subhadra
BhP ātmānam ākhyāhi vivitsatāṃ no yan manyase naḥ kṣamam atra vaktum
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti sma rājā sampṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇenānantamūrtinā
BhP mādhavaṃ praṇipatyāha kirīṭenārkavarcasā
BhP nṛga uvāca
BhP nṛgo nāma narendro 'ham ikṣvākutanayaḥ prabho
BhP dāniṣv ākhyāyamāneṣu yadi te karṇam aspṛśam
BhP kiṃ nu te 'viditaṃ nātha sarvabhūtātmasākṣiṇaḥ
BhP kālenāvyāhatadṛśo vakṣye 'thāpi tavājñayā
BhP yāvatyaḥ sikatā bhūmer yāvatyo divi tārakāḥ
BhP yāvatyo varṣadhārāś ca tāvatīr adadaṃ sma gāḥ
BhP payasvinīs taruṇīḥ śīlarūpa guṇopapannāḥ kapilā hemasṛṅgīḥ
BhP nyāyārjitā rūpyakhurāḥ savatsā dukūlamālābharaṇā dadāv aham
BhP svalaṅkṛtebhyo guṇaśīlavadbhyaḥ sīdatkuṭumbebhya ṛtavratebhyaḥ
BhP tapaḥśrutabrahmavadānyasadbhyaḥ prādāṃ yuvabhyo dvijapuṅgavebhyaḥ
BhP gobhūhiraṇyāyatanāśvahastinaḥ kanyāḥ sadāsīs tilarūpyaśayyāḥ
BhP vāsāṃsi ratnāni paricchadān rathān iṣṭaṃ ca yajñaiś caritaṃ ca pūrtam
BhP kasyacid dvijamukhyasya bhraṣṭā gaur mama godhane
BhP sampṛktāviduṣā sā ca mayā dattā dvijātaye
BhP tāṃ nīyamānāṃ tatsvāmī dṛṣṭrovāca mameti tam
BhP mameti parigrāhy āha nṛgo me dattavān iti
BhP viprau vivadamānau mām ūcatuḥ svārthasādhakau
BhP bhavān dātāpaharteti tac chrutvā me 'bhavad bhramaḥ
BhP anunītāv ubhau viprau dharmakṛcchragatena vai
BhP gavāṃ lakṣaṃ prakṛṣṭānāṃ dāsyāmy eṣā pradīyatām
BhP bhavantāv anugṛhṇītāṃ kiṅkarasyāvijānataḥ
BhP samuddharataṃ māṃ kṛcchrāt patantaṃ niraye 'śucau
BhP nāhaṃ pratīcche vai rājann ity uktvā svāmy apākramat
BhP nānyad gavām apy ayutam icchāmīty aparo yayau
BhP etasminn antare yāmair dūtair nīto yamakṣayam
BhP yamena pṛṣṭas tatrāhaṃ devadeva jagatpate
BhP pūrvaṃ tvam aśubhaṃ bhuṅkṣa utāho nṛpate śubham
BhP nāntaṃ dānasya dharmasya paśye lokasya bhāsvataḥ
BhP pūrvaṃ devāśubhaṃ bhuñja iti prāha pateti saḥ
BhP tāvad adrākṣam ātmānaṃ kṛkalāsaṃ patan prabho
BhP brahmaṇyasya vadānyasya tava dāsasya keśava
BhP smṛtir nādyāpi vidhvastā bhavatsandarśanārthinaḥ
BhP sa tvaṃ kathaṃ mama vibho 'kṣipathaḥ parātmā
BhP yogeśvaraḥ śrutidṛśāmalahṛdvibhāvyaḥ
BhP sākṣād adhokṣaja uruvyasanāndhabuddheḥ
BhP syān me 'nudṛśya iha yasya bhavāpavargaḥ
BhP devadeva jagannātha govinda puruṣottama
BhP nārāyaṇa hṛṣīkeśa puṇyaślokācyutāvyaya
BhP anujānīhi māṃ kṛṣṇa yāntaṃ devagatiṃ prabho
BhP yatra kvāpi sataś ceto bhūyān me tvatpadāspadam
BhP namas te sarvabhāvāya brahmaṇe 'nantaśaktaye
BhP kṛṣṇāya vāsudevāya yogānāṃ pataye namaḥ
BhP ity uktvā taṃ parikramya pādau spṛṣṭvā svamaulinā
BhP anujñāto vimānāgryam āruhat paśyatāṃ nṛṇām
BhP kṛṣṇaḥ parijanaṃ prāha bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP brahmaṇyadevo dharmātmā rājanyān anuśikṣayan
BhP durjaraṃ bata brahmasvaṃ bhuktam agner manāg api
BhP tejīyaso 'pi kim uta rājñāṃ īśvaramāninām
BhP nāhaṃ hālāhalaṃ manye viṣaṃ yasya pratikriyā
BhP brahmasvaṃ hi viṣaṃ proktaṃ nāsya pratividhir bhuvi
BhP hinasti viṣam attāraṃ vahnir adbhiḥ praśāmyati
BhP kulaṃ samūlaṃ dahati brahmasvāraṇipāvakaḥ
BhP brahmasvaṃ duranujñātaṃ bhuktaṃ hanti tripūruṣam
BhP prasahya tu balād bhuktaṃ daśa pūrvān daśāparān
BhP rājāno rājalakṣmyāndhā nātmapātaṃ vicakṣate
BhP nirayaṃ ye 'bhimanyante brahmasvaṃ sādhu bāliśāḥ
BhP gṛhṇanti yāvataḥ pāṃśūn krandatām aśrubindavaḥ
BhP viprāṇāṃ hṛtavṛttīnām vadānyānāṃ kuṭumbinām
BhP rājāno rājakulyāś ca tāvato 'bdān niraṅkuśāḥ
BhP kumbhīpākeṣu pacyante brahmadāyāpahāriṇaḥ
BhP svadattāṃ paradattāṃ vā brahmavṛttiṃ harec ca yaḥ
BhP ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ
BhP na me brahmadhanaṃ bhūyād yad gṛdhvālpāyuṣo narāḥ
BhP parājitāś cyutā rājyād bhavanty udvejino 'hayaḥ
BhP vipraṃ kṛtāgasam api naiva druhyata māmakāḥ
BhP ghnantaṃ bahu śapantaṃ vā namaskuruta nityaśaḥ
BhP yathāhaṃ praṇame viprān anukālaṃ samāhitaḥ
BhP tathā namata yūyaṃ ca yo 'nyathā me sa daṇḍabhāk
BhP brāhmaṇārtho hy apahṛto hartāraṃ pātayaty adhaḥ
BhP ajānantam api hy enaṃ nṛgaṃ brāhmaṇagaur iva
BhP evaṃ viśrāvya bhagavān mukundo dvārakaukasaḥ
BhP pāvanaḥ sarvalokānāṃ viveśa nijamandiram
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP balabhadraḥ kuruśreṣṭha bhagavān ratham āsthitaḥ
BhP suhṛddidṛkṣur utkaṇṭhaḥ prayayau nandagokulam
BhP pariṣvaktaś cirotkaṇṭhair gopair gopībhir eva ca
BhP rāmo 'bhivādya pitarāv āśīrbhir abhinanditaḥ
BhP ciraṃ naḥ pāhi dāśārha sānujo jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP ity āropyāṅkam āliṅgya netraiḥ siṣicatur jalaiḥ
BhP gopavṛddhāṃś ca vidhivad yaviṣṭhair abhivanditaḥ
BhP yathāvayo yathāsakhyaṃ yathāsambandham ātmanaḥ
BhP samupetyātha gopālān hāsyahastagrahādibhiḥ
BhP viśrāntam sukham āsīnaṃ papracchuḥ paryupāgatāḥ
BhP pṛṣṭāś cānāmayaṃ sveṣu premagadgadayā girā
BhP kṛṣṇe kamalapatrākṣe sannyastākhilarādhasaḥ
BhP kaccin no bāndhavā rāma sarve kuśalam āsate
BhP kaccit smaratha no rāma yūyaṃ dārasutānvitāḥ
BhP diṣṭyā kaṃso hataḥ pāpo diṣṭyā muktāḥ suhṛjjanāḥ
BhP nihatya nirjitya ripūn diṣṭyā durgaṃ samāśrītāḥ
BhP gopyo hasantyaḥ papracchū rāmasandarśanādṛtāḥ
BhP kaccid āste sukhaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ purastrījanavallabhaḥ
BhP kaccit smarati vā bandhūn pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca saḥ
BhP apy asau mātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ sakṛd apy āgamiṣyati
BhP api vā smarate 'smākam anusevāṃ mahābhujaḥ
BhP mātaraṃ pitaraṃ bhrātṝn patīn putrān svasṝn api
BhP yadarthe jahima dāśārha dustyajān svajanān prabho
BhP tā naḥ sadyaḥ parityajya gataḥ sañchinnasauhṛdaḥ
BhP kathaṃ nu tādṛśaṃ strībhir na śraddhīyeta bhāṣitam
BhP kathaṃ nu gṛhṇanty anavasthitātmano
BhP vacaḥ kṛtaghnasya budhāḥ purastriyaḥ
BhP gṛhṇanti vai citrakathasya sundara
BhP smitāvalokocchvasitasmarāturāḥ
BhP kiṃ nas tatkathayā gopyaḥ kathāḥ kathayatāparāḥ
BhP yāty asmābhir vinā kālo yadi tasya tathaiva naḥ
BhP iti prahasitaṃ śaurer jalpitaṃ cāruvīkṣitam
BhP gatiṃ premapariṣvaṅgaṃ smarantyo ruruduḥ striyaḥ
BhP saṅkarṣaṇas tāḥ kṛṣṇasya sandeśair hṛdayaṃgamaiḥ
BhP sāntvayām āsa bhagavān nānānunayakovidaḥ
BhP dvau māsau tatra cāvātsīn madhuṃ mādhavaṃ eva ca
BhP rāmaḥ kṣapāsu bhagavān gopīnāṃ ratim āvahan
BhP pūrṇacandrakalāmṛṣṭe kaumudīgandhavāyunā
BhP yamunopavane reme sevite strīgaṇair vṛtaḥ
BhP varuṇapreṣitā devī vāruṇī vṛkṣakoṭarāt
BhP patantī tad vanaṃ sarvaṃ svagandhenādhyavāsayat
BhP taṃ gandhaṃ madhudhārāyā vāyunopahṛtaṃ balaḥ
BhP āghrāyopagatas tatra lalanābhiḥ samaṃ papau
BhP upagīyamāno gandharvair vanitāśobhimaṇḍale
BhP reme kareṇuyūtheśo māhendra iva vāraṇaḥ
BhP nedur dundubhayo vyomni vavṛṣuḥ kusumair mudā
BhP gandharvā munayo rāmaṃ tadvīryair īḍire tadā
BhP upagīyamānacarito vanitābhir halāyudha
BhP vaneṣu vyacarat kṣīvo madavihvalalocanaḥ
BhP sragvy ekakuṇḍalo matto vaijayantyā ca mālayā
BhP bibhrat smitamukhāmbhojaṃ svedaprāleyabhūṣitam
BhP sa ājuhāva yamunāṃ jalakrīḍārtham īśvaraḥ
BhP nijaṃ vākyam anādṛtya matta ity āpagāṃ balaḥ
BhP anāgatāṃ halāgreṇa kupito vicakarṣa ha
BhP pāpe tvaṃ mām avajñāya yan nāyāsi mayāhutā
BhP neṣye tvāṃ lāṅgalāgreṇa śatadhā kāmacāriṇīm
BhP evaṃ nirbhartsitā bhītā yamunā yadunandanam
BhP uvāca cakitā vācaṃ patitā pādayor nṛpa
BhP rāma rāma mahābāho na jāne tava vikramam
BhP yasyaikāṃśena vidhṛtā jagatī jagataḥ pate
BhP paraṃ bhāvaṃ bhagavato bhagavan mām ajānatīm
BhP moktum arhasi viśvātman prapannāṃ bhaktavatsala
BhP tato vyamuñcad yamunāṃ yācito bhagavān balaḥ
BhP vijagāha jalaṃ strībhiḥ kareṇubhir ivebharāṭ
BhP kāmaṃ vihṛtya salilād uttīrṇāyāsītāmbare
BhP bhūṣaṇāni mahārhāṇi dadau kāntiḥ śubhāṃ srajam
BhP vasitvā vāsasī nīle mālāṃ āmucya kāñcanīm
BhP reye svalaṅkṛto lipto māhendra iva vāraṇaḥ
BhP adyāpi dṛśyate rājan yamunākṛṣṭavartmanā
BhP balasyānantavīryasya vīryaṃ sūcayatīva hi
BhP evaṃ sarvā niśā yātā ekeva ramato vraje
BhP rāmasyākṣiptacittasya mādhuryair vrajayoṣitām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP nandavrajaṃ gate rāme karūṣādhipatir nṛpa
BhP vāsudevo 'ham ity ajño dūtaṃ kṛṣṇāya prāhiṇot
BhP tvaṃ vāsudevo bhagavān avatīṛno jagatpatiḥ
BhP iti prastobhito bālair mena ātmānam acyutam
BhP dūtaṃ ca prāhiṇon mandaḥ kṛṣṇāyāvyaktavartmane
BhP dvārakāyāṃ yathā bālo nṛpo bālakṛto 'budhaḥ
BhP dūtas tu dvārakām etya sabhāyām āsthitaṃ prabhum
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ kamalapatrākṣaṃ rājasandeśam abravīt
BhP vāsudevo 'vatīrno 'ham eka eva na cāparaḥ
BhP bhūtānām anukampārthaṃ tvaṃ tu mithyābhidhāṃ tyaja
BhP yāni tvam asmaccihnāni mauḍhyād bibharṣi sātvata
BhP tyaktvaihi māṃ tvaṃ śaraṇaṃ no ced dehi mamāhavam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP katthanaṃ tad upākarṇya pauṇḍrakasyālpamedhasaḥ
BhP ugrasenādayaḥ sabhyā uccakair jahasus tadā
BhP uvāca dūtaṃ bhagavān parihāsakathām anu
BhP utsrakṣye mūḍha cihnāni yais tvam evaṃ vikatthase
BhP mukhaṃ tad apidhāyājña kaṅkagṛdhravaṭair vṛtaḥ
BhP śayiṣyase hatas tatra bhavitā śaraṇaṃ śunām
BhP iti dūtas tam ākṣepaṃ svāmine sarvam āharat
BhP kṛṣṇo 'pi ratham āsthāya kāśīm upajagāma ha
BhP pauṇḍrako 'pi tadudyogam upalabhya mahārathaḥ
BhP akṣauhiṇībhyāṃ saṃyukto niścakrāma purād drutam
BhP tasya kāśīpatir mitraṃ pārṣṇigrāho 'nvayān nṛpa
BhP akṣauhiṇībhis tisṛbhir apaśyat pauṇḍrakaṃ hariḥ
BhP śaṅkhāryasigadāśārṅga śrīvatsādyupalakṣitam
BhP bibhrāṇaṃ kaustubhamaṇiṃ vanamālāvibhūṣitam
BhP kauśeyavāsasī pīte vasānaṃ garuḍadhvajam
BhP amūlyamaulyābharaṇaṃ sphuranmakarakuṇḍalam
BhP dṛṣṭvā tam ātmanas tulyaṃ veṣaṃ kṛtrimam āsthitam
BhP yathā naṭaṃ raṅgagataṃ vijahāsa bhṛśaṃ harīḥ
BhP śulair gadābhiḥ parighaiḥ śaktyṛṣṭiprāsatomaraiḥ
BhP asibhiḥ paṭṭiśair bāṇaiḥ prāharann arayo harim
BhP kṛṣṇas tu tat pauṇḍrakakāśirājayor
BhP balaṃ gajasyandanavājipattimat
BhP gadāsicakreṣubhir ārdayad bhṛśaṃ
BhP yathā yugānte hutabhuk pṛthak prajāḥ
BhP āyodhanaṃ tad rathavājikuñjara dvipatkharoṣṭrair ariṇāvakhaṇḍitaiḥ
BhP babhau citaṃ modavahaṃ manasvinām ākrīḍanaṃ bhūtapater ivolbaṇam
BhP athāha pauṇḍrakaṃ śaurir bho bho pauṇḍraka yad bhavān
BhP dūtavākyena mām āha tāny astraṇy utsṛjāmi te
BhP tyājayiṣye 'bhidhānaṃ me yat tvayājña mṛṣā dhṛtam
BhP vrajāmi śaranaṃ te 'dya yadi necchāmi saṃyugam
BhP iti kṣiptvā śitair bāṇair virathīkṛtya pauṇḍrakam
BhP śiro 'vṛścad rathāṅgena vajreṇendro yathā gireḥ
BhP tathā kāśīpateḥ kāyāc chira utkṛtya patribhiḥ
BhP nyapātayat kāśīpuryāṃ padmakośam ivānilaḥ
BhP evaṃ matsariṇam hatvā pauṇḍrakaṃ sasakhaṃ hariḥ
BhP dvārakām āviśat siddhair gīyamānakathāmṛtaḥ
BhP sa nityaṃ bhagavaddhyāna pradhvastākhilabandhanaḥ
BhP bibhrāṇaś ca hare rājan svarūpaṃ tanmayo 'bhavat
BhP śiraḥ patitam ālokya rājadvāre sakuṇḍalam
BhP kim idaṃ kasya vā vaktram iti saṃśiśire janāḥ
BhP rājñaḥ kāśīpater jñātvā mahiṣyaḥ putrabāndhavāḥ
BhP paurāś ca hā hatā rājan nātha nātheti prārudan
BhP sudakṣiṇas tasya sutaḥ kṛtvā saṃsthāvidhiṃ pateḥ
BhP nihatya pitṛhantāraṃ yāsyāmy apacitiṃ pituḥ
BhP ity ātmanābhisandhāya sopādhyāyo maheśvaram
BhP sudakṣiṇo 'rcayām āsa parameṇa samādhinā
BhP prīto 'vimukte bhagavāṃs tasmai varam adād vibhuḥ
BhP pitṛhantṛvadhopāyaṃ sa vavre varam īpsitam
BhP dakṣiṇāgniṃ paricara brāhmaṇaiḥ samam ṛtvijam
BhP abhicāravidhānena sa cāgniḥ pramathair vṛtaḥ
BhP sādhayiṣyati saṅkalpam abrahmaṇye prayojitaḥ
BhP ity ādiṣṭas tathā cakre kṛṣṇāyābhicaran vratī
BhP tato 'gnir utthitaḥ kuṇḍān mūrtimān atibhīṣaṇaḥ
BhP taptatāmraśikhāśmaśrur aṅgārodgārilocanaḥ
BhP daṃṣṭrograbhrukuṭīdaṇḍa kaṭhorāsyaḥ svajihvayā
BhP ālihan sṛkvaṇī nagno vidhunvaṃs triśikhaṃ jvalat
BhP padbhyāṃ tālapramāṇābhyāṃ kampayann avanītalam
BhP so 'bhyadhāvad vṛto bhūtair dvārakāṃ pradahan diśaḥ
BhP tam ābhicāradahanam āyāntaṃ dvārakaukasaḥ
BhP vilokya tatrasuḥ sarve vanadāhe mṛgā yathā
BhP akṣaiḥ sabhāyāṃ krīḍantaṃ bhagavantaṃ bhayāturāḥ
BhP trāhi trāhi trilokeśa vahneḥ pradahataḥ puram
BhP śrutvā taj janavaiklavyaṃ dṛṣṭvā svānāṃ ca sādhvasam
BhP śaraṇyaḥ samprahasyāha mā bhaiṣṭety avitāsmy aham
BhP sarvasyāntarbahiḥsākṣī kṛtyāṃ māheśvarīṃ vibhuḥ
BhP vijñāya tadvighātārthaṃ pārśvasthaṃ cakram ādiśat
BhP tat sūryakoṭipratimaṃ sudarśanaṃ jājvalyamānaṃ pralayānalaprabham
BhP svatejasā khaṃ kakubho 'tha rodasī cakraṃ mukundāstraṃ athāgnim ārdayat
BhP kṛtyānalaḥ pratihataḥ sa rathāngapāṇer
BhP astraujasā sa nṛpa bhagnamukho nivṛttaḥ
BhP vārāṇasīṃ parisametya sudakṣiṇaṃ taṃ
BhP sartvigjanaṃ samadahat svakṛto 'bhicāraḥ
BhP cakraṃ ca viṣṇos tadanupraviṣṭaṃ vārānasīṃ sāṭṭasabhālayāpaṇām
BhP sagopurāṭṭālakakoṣṭhasaṅkulāṃ sakośahastyaśvarathānnaśālinīm
BhP dagdhvā vārāṇasīṃ sarvāṃ viṣṇoś cakraṃ sudarśanam
BhP bhūyaḥ pārśvam upātiṣṭhat kṛṣṇasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
BhP ya enaṃ śrāvayen martya uttamaḥślokavikramam
BhP samāhito vā śṛṇuyāt sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP bhuyo 'haṃ śrotum icchāmi rāmasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ
BhP anantasyāprameyasya yad anyat kṛtavān prabhuḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP narakasya sakhā kaścid dvivido nāma vānaraḥ
BhP sugrīvasacivaḥ so 'tha bhrātā maindasya vīryavān
BhP sakhyuḥ so 'pacitiṃ kurvan vānaro rāṣṭraviplavam
BhP puragrāmākarān ghoṣān adahad vahnim utsṛjan
BhP kvacit sa śailān utpāṭya tair deśān samacūrṇayat
BhP ānartān sutarām eva yatrāste mitrahā hariḥ
BhP kvacit samudramadhyastho dorbhyām utkṣipya tajjalam
BhP deśān nāgāyutaprāṇo velākūle nyamajjayat
BhP āśramān ṛṣimukhyānāṃ kṛtvā bhagnavanaspatīn
BhP adūṣayac chakṛnmūtrair agnīn vaitānikān khalaḥ
BhP puruṣān yoṣito dṛptaḥ kṣmābhṛddronīguhāsu saḥ
BhP nikṣipya cāpyadhāc chailaiḥ peśaṣkārīva kīṭakam
BhP evaṃ deśān viprakurvan dūṣayaṃś ca kulastriyaḥ
BhP śrutvā sulalitaṃ gītaṃ giriṃ raivatakaṃ yayau
BhP tatrāpaśyad yadupatiṃ rāmaṃ puṣkaramālinam
BhP sudarśanīyasarvāṅgaṃ lalanāyūthamadhyagam
BhP gāyantaṃ vāruṇīṃ pītvā madavihvalalocanam
BhP vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā prabhinnam iva vāraṇam
BhP duṣṭaḥ śākhāmṛgaḥ śākhām ārūḍhaḥ kampayan drumān
BhP cakre kilakilāśabdam ātmānaṃ sampradarśayan
BhP tasya dhārṣṭyaṃ kaper vīkṣya taruṇyo jāticāpalāḥ
BhP hāsyapriyā vijahasur baladevaparigrahāḥ
BhP tā helayām āsa kapir bhrūkṣepair sammukhādibhiḥ
BhP darśayan svagudaṃ tāsāṃ rāmasya ca nirīkṣitaḥ
BhP taṃ grāvṇā prāharat kruddho balaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
BhP sa vañcayitvā grāvāṇaṃ madirākalaśaṃ kapiḥ
BhP gṛhītvā helayām āsa dhūrtas taṃ kopayan hasan
BhP nirbhidya kalaśaṃ duṣṭo vāsāṃsy āsphālayad balam
BhP kadarthīkṛtya balavān vipracakre madoddhataḥ
BhP taṃ tasyāvinayaṃ dṛṣṭvā deśāṃś ca tadupadrutān
BhP kruddho muṣalam ādatta halaṃ cārijighāṃsayā
BhP dvivido 'pi mahāvīryaḥ śālam udyamya pāṇinā
BhP abhyetya tarasā tena balaṃ mūrdhany atāḍayat
BhP taṃ tu saṅkarṣaṇo mūrdhni patantam acalo yathā
BhP pratijagrāha balavān sunandenāhanac ca tam
BhP mūṣalāhatamastiṣko vireje raktadhārayā
BhP girir yathā gairikayā prahāraṃ nānucintayan
BhP punar anyaṃ samutkṣipya kṛtvā niṣpatram ojasā
BhP tenāhanat susaṅkruddhas taṃ balaḥ śatadhācchinat
BhP tato 'nyena ruṣā jaghne taṃ cāpi śatadhācchinat
BhP evaṃ yudhyan bhagavatā bhagne bhagne punaḥ punaḥ
BhP ākṛṣya sarvato vṛkṣān nirvṛkṣam akarod vanam
BhP tato 'muñcac chilāvarṣaṃ balasyopary amarṣitaḥ
BhP tat sarvaṃ cūrṇayāṃ āsa līlayā muṣalāyudhaḥ
BhP sa bāhū tālasaṅkāśau muṣṭīkṛtya kapīśvaraḥ
BhP āsādya rohiṇīputraṃ tābhyāṃ vakṣasy arūrujat
BhP yādavendro 'pi taṃ dorbhyāṃ tyaktvā muṣalalāṅgale
BhP jatrāv abhyardayat kruddhaḥ so 'patad rudhiraṃ vaman
BhP cakampe tena patatā saṭaṅkaḥ savanaspatiḥ
BhP parvataḥ kuruśārdūla vāyunā naur ivāmbhasi
BhP jayaśabdo namaḥśabdaḥ sādhu sādhv iti cāmbare
BhP surasiddhamunīndrāṇām āsīt kusumavarṣiṇām
BhP evaṃ nihatya dvividaṃ jagadvyatikarāvaham
BhP saṃstūyamāno bhagavān janaiḥ svapuram āviśat
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP duryodhanasutāṃ rājan lakṣmaṇāṃ samitiṃjayaḥ
BhP svayaṃvarasthām aharat sāmbo jāmbavatīsutaḥ
BhP kauravāḥ kupitā ūcur durvinīto 'yam arbhakaḥ
BhP kadarthīkṛtya naḥ kanyām akāmām aharad balāt
BhP badhnītemaṃ durvinītaṃ kiṃ kariṣyanti vṛṣṇayaḥ
BhP ye 'smatprasādopacitāṃ dattāṃ no bhuñjate mahīm
BhP nigṛhītaṃ sutaṃ śrutvā yady eṣyantīha vṛṣṇayaḥ
BhP bhagnadarpāḥ śamaṃ yānti prāṇā iva susaṃyatāḥ
BhP iti karṇaḥ śalo bhūrir yajñaketuḥ suyodhanaḥ
BhP sāmbam ārebhire yoddhuṃ kuruvṛddhānumoditāḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvānudhāvataḥ sāmbo dhārtarāṣṭrān mahārathaḥ
BhP pragṛhya ruciraṃ cāpaṃ tasthau siṃha ivaikalaḥ
BhP taṃ te jighṛkṣavaḥ kruddhās tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti bhāṣiṇaḥ
BhP āsādya dhanvino bāṇaiḥ karṇāgraṇyaḥ samākiran
BhP so 'paviddhaḥ kuruśreṣṭha kurubhir yadunandanaḥ
BhP nāmṛṣyat tad acintyārbhaḥ siṃha kṣudramṛgair iva
BhP visphūrjya ruciraṃ cāpaṃ sarvān vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
BhP karṇādīn ṣaḍ rathān vīras tāvadbhir yugapat pṛthak
BhP caturbhiś caturo vāhān ekaikena ca sārathīn
BhP rathinaś ca maheṣvāsāṃs tasya tat te 'bhyapūjayan
BhP taṃ tu te virathaṃ cakruś catvāraś caturo hayān
BhP ekas tu sārathiṃ jaghne cicchedaṇyaḥ śarāsanam
BhP taṃ baddhvā virathīkṛtya kṛcchreṇa kuravo yudhi
BhP kumāraṃ svasya kanyāṃ ca svapuraṃ jayino 'viśan
BhP tac chrutvā nāradoktena rājan sañjātamanyavaḥ
BhP kurūn praty udyamaṃ cakrur ugrasenapracoditāḥ
BhP sāntvayitvā tu tān rāmaḥ sannaddhān vṛṣṇipuṅgavān
BhP naicchat kurūṇāṃ vṛṣṇīnāṃ kaliṃ kalimalāpahaḥ
BhP jagāma hāstinapuraṃ rathenādityavarcasā
BhP brāhmaṇaiḥ kulavṛddhaiś ca vṛtaś candra iva grahaiḥ
BhP gatvā gajāhvayaṃ rāmo bāhyopavanam āsthitaḥ
BhP uddhavaṃ preṣayām āsa dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ bubhutsayā
BhP so 'bhivandyāmbikāputraṃ bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ ca bāhlikam
BhP duryodhanaṃ ca vidhivad rāmam āgataṃ abravīt
BhP te 'tiprītās tam ākarṇya prāptaṃ rāmaṃ suhṛttamam
BhP tam arcayitvābhiyayuḥ sarve maṅgalapāṇayaḥ
BhP taṃ saṅgamya yathānyāyaṃ gām arghyaṃ ca nyavedayan
BhP teṣāṃ ye tatprabhāvajñāḥ praṇemuḥ śirasā balam
BhP bandhūn kuśalinaḥ śrutvā pṛṣṭvā śivam anāmayam
BhP parasparam atho rāmo babhāṣe 'viklavaṃ vacaḥ
BhP ugrasenaḥ kṣiteśeśo yad va ājñāpayat prabhuḥ
BhP tad avyagradhiyaḥ śrutvā kurudhvam avilambitam
BhP yad yūyaṃ bahavas tv ekaṃ jitvādharmeṇa dhārmikam
BhP abadhnītātha tan mṛṣye bandhūnām aikyakāmyayā
BhP vīryaśauryabalonnaddham ātmaśaktisamaṃ vacaḥ
BhP kuravo baladevasya niśamyocuḥ prakopitāḥ
BhP aho mahac citram idaṃ kālagatyā duratyayā
BhP ārurukṣaty upānad vai śiro mukuṭasevitam
BhP ete yaunena sambaddhāḥ sahaśayyāsanāśanāḥ
BhP vṛṣṇayas tulyatāṃ nītā asmaddattanṛpāsanāḥ
BhP cāmaravyajane śaṅkham ātapatraṃ ca pāṇḍuram
BhP kirīṭam āsanaṃ śayyāṃ bhuñjate 'smadupekṣayā
BhP alaṃ yadūnāṃ naradevalāñchanair dātuḥ pratīpaiḥ phaṇinām ivāmṛtam
BhP ye 'smatprasādopacitā hi yādavā ājñāpayanty adya gatatrapā bata
BhP katham indro 'pi kurubhir bhīṣmadroṇārjunādibhiḥ
BhP adattam avarundhīta siṃhagrastam ivoraṇaḥ
BhP śrībādarāyaṇir uvāca
BhP janmabandhuśrīyonnaddha madās te bharatarṣabha
BhP āśrāvya rāmaṃ durvācyam asabhyāḥ puram āviśan
BhP dṛṣṭvā kurūnāṃ dauḥśīlyaṃ śrutvāvācyāni cācyutaḥ
BhP avocat kopasaṃrabdho duṣprekṣyaḥ prahasan muhuḥ
BhP nūnaṃ nānāmadonnaddhāḥ śāntiṃ necchanty asādhavaḥ
BhP teṣāṃ hi praśamo daṇḍaḥ paśūnāṃ laguḍo yathā
BhP aho yadūn susaṃrabdhān kṛṣṇaṃ ca kupitaṃ śanaiḥ
BhP sāntvayitvāham eteṣāṃ śamam icchann ihāgataḥ
BhP ta ime mandamatayaḥ kalahābhiratāḥ khalāḥ
BhP taṃ mām avajñāya muhur durbhāṣān mānino 'bruvan
BhP nograsenaḥ kila vibhur bhojavṛṣṇyandhakeśvaraḥ
BhP śakrādayo lokapālā yasyādeśānuvartinaḥ
BhP sudharmākramyate yena pārijāto 'marāṅghripaḥ
BhP ānīya bhujyate so 'sau na kilādhyāsanārhaṇaḥ
BhP yasya pādayugaṃ sākṣāc chrīr upāste 'khileśvarī
BhP sa nārhati kila śrīśo naradevaparicchadān
BhP yasyāṅghripaṅkajarajo 'khilalokapālair
BhP maulyuttamair dhṛtam upāsitatīrthatīrtham
BhP brahmā bhavo 'ham api yasya kalāḥ kalāyāḥ
BhP śrīś codvahema ciram asya nṛpāsanaṃ kva
BhP bhuñjate kurubhir dattaṃ bhūkhaṇḍaṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ kila
BhP upānahaḥ kila vayaṃ svayaṃ tu kuravaḥ śiraḥ
BhP aho aiśvaryamattānāṃ mattānām iva māninām
BhP asambaddhā giṛo rukṣāḥ kaḥ sahetānuśāsītā
BhP adya niṣkauravaṃ pṛthvīṃ kariṣyāmīty amarṣitaḥ
BhP gṛhītvā halam uttasthau dahann iva jagattrayam
BhP lāṅgalāgreṇa nagaram udvidārya gajāhvayam
BhP vicakarṣa sa gaṅgāyāṃ prahariṣyann amarṣitaḥ
BhP jalayānam ivāghūrṇaṃ gaṅgāyāṃ nagaraṃ patat
BhP ākṛṣyamāṇam ālokya kauravāḥ jātasambhramāḥ
BhP tam eva śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ sakuṭumbā jijīviṣavaḥ
BhP salakṣmaṇaṃ puraskṛtya sāmbaṃ prāñjalayaḥ prabhum
BhP rāma rāmākhilādhāra prabhāvaṃ na vidāma te
BhP mūḍhānāṃ naḥ kubuddhīnāṃ kṣantum arhasy atikramam
BhP sthityutpattyapyayānāṃ tvam eko hetur nirāśrayaḥ
BhP lokān krīḍanakān īśa krīḍatas te vadanti hi
BhP tvam eva mūrdhnīdam ananta līlayā bhūmaṇḍalaṃ bibharṣi sahasramūrdhan
BhP ante ca yaḥ svātmaniruddhaviśvaḥ śeṣe 'dvitīyaḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ
BhP kopas te 'khilaśikṣārthaṃ na dveṣān na ca matsarāt
BhP bibhrato bhagavan sattvaṃ sthitipālanatatparaḥ
BhP namas te sarvabhūtātman sarvaśaktidharāvyaya
BhP viśvakarman namas te 'stu tvāṃ vayaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ prapannaiḥ saṃvignair vepamānāyanair balaḥ
BhP prasāditaḥ suprasanno mā bhaiṣṭety abhayaṃ dadau
BhP duryodhanaḥ pāribarhaṃ kuñjarān ṣaṣṭihāyanān
BhP dadau ca dvādaśaśatāny ayutāni turaṅgamān
BhP rathānāṃ ṣaṭsahasrāṇi raukmāṇāṃ sūryavarcasām
BhP dāsīnāṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīnāṃ sahasraṃ duhitṛvatsalaḥ
BhP pratigṛhya tu tat sarvaṃ bhagavān sātvatarṣabhaḥ
BhP sasutaḥ sasnuṣaḥ prāyāt suhṛdbhir abhinanditaḥ
BhP tataḥ praviṣṭaḥ svapuraṃ halāyudhaḥ
BhP sametya bandhūn anuraktacetasaḥ
BhP śaśaṃsa sarvaṃ yadupuṅgavānāṃ
BhP madhye sabhāyāṃ kuruṣu svaceṣṭitam
BhP adyāpi ca puraṃ hy etat sūcayad rāmavikramam
BhP samunnataṃ dakṣiṇato gaṅgāyām anudṛśyate
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP narakaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā tathodvāhaṃ ca yoṣitām
BhP kṛṣṇenaikena bahvīnāṃ taddidṛkṣuḥ sma nāradaḥ
BhP citraṃ bataitad ekena vapuṣā yugapat pṛthak
BhP gṛheṣu dvyaṣṭasāhasraṃ striya eka udāvahat
BhP ity utsuko dvāravatīṃ devarṣir draṣṭum āgamat
BhP puṣpitopavanārāma dvijālikulanāditām
BhP utphullendīvarāmbhoja kahlārakumudotpalaiḥ
BhP churiteṣu saraḥsūccaiḥ kūjitāṃ haṃsasārasaiḥ
BhP prāsādalakṣair navabhir juṣṭāṃ sphāṭikarājataiḥ
BhP mahāmarakataprakhyaiḥ svarṇaratnaparicchadaiḥ
BhP vibhaktarathyāpathacatvarāpaṇaiḥ śālāsabhābhī rucirāṃ surālayaiḥ
BhP saṃsiktamārgāṅganavīthidehalīṃ patatpatākadhvajavāritātapām
BhP tasyām antaḥpuraṃ śrīmad arcitaṃ sarvadhiṣṇyapaiḥ
BhP hareḥ svakauśalaṃ yatra tvaṣṭrā kārtsnyena darśitam
BhP tatra ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sadma sahasraiḥ samalaṅkṛtam
BhP viveśaikatomaṃ śaureḥ patnīnāṃ bhavanaṃ mahat
BhP viṣṭabdhaṃ vidrumastambhair vaidūryaphalakottamaiḥ
BhP indranīlamayaiḥ kuḍyair jagatyā cāhatatviṣā
BhP vitānair nirmitais tvaṣṭrā muktādāmavilambibhiḥ
BhP dāntair āsanaparyaṅkair maṇyuttamapariṣkṛtaiḥ
BhP dāsībhir niṣkakaṇṭhībhiḥ suvāsobhir alaṅkṛtam
BhP pumbhiḥ sakañcukoṣṇīṣa suvastramaṇikuṇḍalaiḥ
BhP ratnapradīpanikaradyutibhir nirasta dhvāntaṃ vicitravalabhīṣu śikhaṇḍino 'ṅga
BhP nṛtyanti yatra vihitāgurudhūpam akṣair niryāntam īkṣya ghanabuddhaya unnadantaḥ
BhP tasmin samānaguṇarūpavayaḥsuveṣa
BhP dāsīsahasrayutayānusavaṃ gṛhiṇyā
BhP vipro dadarśa camaravyajanena rukma
BhP daṇḍena sātvatapatiṃ parivījayantyā
BhP taṃ sannirīkṣya bhagavān sahasotthitaśrī
BhP paryaṅkataḥ sakaladharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
BhP ānamya pādayugalaṃ śirasā kirīṭa
BhP juṣṭena sāñjalir avīviśad āsane sve
BhP tasyāvanijya caraṇau tadapaḥ svamūrdhnā
BhP bibhraj jagadgurutamo 'pi satāṃ patir hi
BhP brahmaṇyadeva iti yad guṇanāma yuktaṃ
BhP tasyaiva yaccaraṇaśaucam aśeṣatīrtham
BhP sampūjya devaṛṣivaryam ṛṣiḥ purāṇo
BhP nārāyaṇo narasakho vidhinoditena
BhP vāṇyābhibhāṣya mitayāmṛtamiṣṭayā taṃ
BhP prāha prabho bhagavate karavāma he kim
BhP śrīnārada uvāca
BhP naivādbhutaṃ tvayi vibho 'khilalokanāthe
BhP maitrī janeṣu sakaleṣu damaḥ khalānām
BhP niḥśreyasāya hi jagatsthitirakṣaṇābhyāṃ
BhP svairāvatāra urugāya vidāma suṣṭhu
BhP dṛṣṭaṃ tavāṅghriyugalaṃ janatāpavargaṃ
BhP brahmādibhir hṛdi vicintyam agādhabodhaiḥ
BhP saṃsārakūpapatitottaraṇāvalambaṃ
BhP dhyāyaṃś carāmy anugṛhāṇa yathā smṛtiḥ syāt
BhP tato 'nyad āviśad gehaṃ kṛṣṇapatnyāḥ sa nāradaḥ
BhP yogeśvareśvarasyāṅga yogamāyāvivitsayā
BhP dīvyantam akṣais tatrāpi priyayā coddhavena ca
BhP pūjitaḥ parayā bhaktyā pratyutthānāsanādibhiḥ
BhP pṛṣṭaś cāviduṣevāsau kadāyāto bhavān iti
BhP kriyate kiṃ nu pūrṇānām apūrṇair asmadādibhiḥ
BhP athāpi brūhi no brahman janmaitac chobhanaṃ kuru
BhP sa tu vismita utthāya tūṣṇīm anyad agād gṛham
BhP tatrāpy acaṣṭa govindaṃ lālayantaṃ sutān śiśūn
BhP tato 'nyasmin gṛhe 'paśyan majjanāya kṛtodyamam
BhP juhvantaṃ ca vitānāgnīn yajantaṃ pañcabhir makhaiḥ
BhP bhojayantaṃ dvijān kvāpi bhuñjānam avaśeṣitam
BhP kvāpi sandhyām upāsīnaṃ japantaṃ brahma vāgyatam
BhP ekatra cāsicarmābhyāṃ carantam asivartmasu
BhP aśvair gajai rathaiḥ kvāpi vicarantaṃ gadāgrajam
BhP kvacic chayānaṃ paryaṅke stūyamānaṃ ca vandibhiḥ
BhP mantrayantaṃ ca kasmiṃścin mantribhiś coddhavādibhiḥ
BhP jalakrīḍārataṃ kvāpi vāramukhyābalāvṛtam
BhP kutracid dvijamukhyebhyo dadataṃ gāḥ svalaṅkṛtāḥ
BhP itihāsapurāṇāni śṛṇvantaṃ maṅgalāni ca
BhP hasantaṃ hāsakathayā kadācit priyayā gṛhe
BhP kvāpi dharmaṃ sevamānam arthakāmau ca kutracit
BhP dhyāyantam ekam āsīnaṃ puruṣaṃ prakṛteḥ param
BhP śuśrūṣantaṃ gurūn kvāpi kāmair bhogaiḥ saparyayā
BhP kurvantaṃ vigrahaṃ kaiścit sandhiṃ cānyatra keśavam
BhP kutrāpi saha rāmeṇa cintayantaṃ satāṃ śivam
BhP putrāṇāṃ duhitṝṇāṃ ca kāle vidhyupayāpanam
BhP dārair varais tatsadṛśaiḥ kalpayantaṃ vibhūtibhiḥ
BhP prasthāpanopanayanair apatyānāṃ mahotsavān
BhP vīkṣya yogeśvareśasya yeṣāṃ lokā visismire
BhP yajantaṃ sakalān devān kvāpi kratubhir ūrjitaiḥ
BhP pūrtayantaṃ kvacid dharmaṃ kūrpārāmamaṭhādibhiḥ
BhP carantaṃ mṛgayāṃ kvāpi hayam āruhya saindhavam
BhP ghnantaṃ tatra paśūn medhyān parītaṃ yadupuṅgavaiḥ
BhP avyaktalingaṃ prakṛtiṣv antaḥpuragṛhādiṣu
BhP kvacic carantaṃ yogeśaṃ tattadbhāvabubhutsayā
BhP athovāca hṛṣīkeśaṃ nāradaḥ prahasann iva
BhP yogamāyodayaṃ vīkṣya mānuṣīm īyuṣo gatim
BhP vidāma yogamāyās te durdarśā api māyinām
BhP yogeśvarātman nirbhātā bhavatpādaniṣevayā
BhP anujānīhi māṃ deva lokāṃs te yaśasāplutān
BhP paryaṭāmi tavodgāyan līlā bhuvanapāvanīḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP brahman dhannasya vaktāhaṃ kartā tadanumoditā
BhP tac chikṣayan lokam imam āsthitaḥ putra mā khidaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity ācarantaṃ saddharmān pāvanān gṛhamedhinām
BhP tam eva sarvageheṣu santam ekaṃ dadarśa ha
BhP kṛṣṇasyānantavīryasya yogamāyāmahodayam
BhP muhur dṛṣṭvā ṛṣir abhūd vismito jātakautukaḥ
BhP ity arthakāmadharmeṣu kṛṣṇena śraddhitātmanā
BhP samyak sabhājitaḥ prītas tam evānusmaran yayau
BhP evaṃ manuṣyapadavīm anuvartamāno nārāyaṇo 'khilabhavāya gṛhītaśaktiḥ
BhP reme 'ṇga ṣoḍaśasahasravarāṅganānāṃ savrīḍasauhṛdanirīkṣaṇahāsajuṣṭaḥ
BhP yānīha viśvavilayodbhavavṛttihetuḥ
BhP karmāṇy ananyaviṣayāṇi harīś cakāra
BhP yas tv aṅga gāyati śṛṇoty anumodate vā
BhP bhaktir bhaved bhagavati hy apavargamārge
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP athoṣasy upavṛttāyāṃ kukkuṭān kūjato 'śapan
BhP gṛhītakaṇṭhyaḥ patibhir mādhavyo virahāturāḥ
BhP vayāṃsy aroruvan kṛṣṇaṃ bodhayantīva vandinaḥ
BhP gāyatsv aliṣv anidrāṇi mandāravanavāyubhiḥ
BhP muhūrtaṃ taṃ tu vaidarbhī nāmṛṣyad atiśobhanam
BhP parirambhaṇaviśleṣāt priyabāhvantaraṃ gatā
BhP brāhme muhūrta utthāya vāry upaspṛśya mādhavaḥ
BhP dadhyau prasannakaraṇa ātmānaṃ tamasaḥ param
BhP ekaṃ svayaṃjyotir ananyam avyayaṃ svasaṃsthayā nityanirastakalmaṣam
BhP brahmākhyam asyodbhavanāśahetubhiḥ svaśaktibhir lakṣitabhāvanirvṛtim
BhP athāpluto 'mbhasy amale yathāvidhi
BhP kriyākalāpaṃ paridhāya vāsasī
BhP cakāra sandhyopagamādi sattamo
BhP hutānalo brahma jajāpa vāgyataḥ
BhP upasthāyārkam udyantaṃ tarpayitvātmanaḥ kalāḥ
BhP devān ṛṣīn pitṝn vṛddhān viprān abhyarcya cātmavān
BhP dhenūnāṃ rukmaśṛṅgīnāṃ sādhvīnāṃ mauktikasrajām
BhP payasvinīnāṃ gṛṣṭīnāṃ savatsānāṃ suvāsasām
BhP dadau rūpyakhurāgrāṇāṃ kṣaumājinatilaiḥ saha
BhP alaṅkṛtebhyo viprebhyo badvaṃ badvaṃ dine dine
BhP govipradevatāvṛddha gurūn bhūtāni sarvaśaḥ
BhP namaskṛtyātmasambhūtīr maṅgalāni samaspṛśat
BhP ātmānaṃ bhūṣayām āsa naralokavibhūṣaṇam
BhP vāsobhir bhūṣaṇaiḥ svīyair divyasraganulepanaiḥ
BhP avekṣyājyaṃ tathādarśaṃ govṛṣadvijadevatāḥ
BhP kāmāṃś ca sarvavarṇānāṃ paurāntaḥpuracāriṇām
BhP pradāpya prakṛtīḥ kāmaiḥ pratoṣya pratyanandata
BhP saṃvibhajyāgrato viprān sraktāmbūlānulepanaiḥ
BhP suhṛdaḥ prakṛtīr dārān upāyuṅkta tataḥ svayam
BhP tāvat sūta upānīya syandanaṃ paramādbhutam
BhP sugrīvādyair hayair yuktaṃ praṇamyāvasthito 'grataḥ
BhP gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇī sārathes tam athāruhat
BhP sātyakyuddhavasaṃyuktaḥ pūrvādrim iva bhāskaraḥ
BhP īkṣito 'ntaḥpurastrīṇāṃ savrīḍapremavīkṣitaiḥ
BhP kṛcchrād visṛṣṭo niragāj jātahāso haran manaḥ
BhP sudharmākhyāṃ sabhāṃ sarvair vṛṣṇibhiḥ parivāritaḥ
BhP prāviśad yanniviṣṭānāṃ na santy aṅga ṣaḍ ūrmayaḥ
BhP tatropavistaḥ paramāsane vibhur babhau svabhāsā kakubho 'vabhāsayan
BhP vṛto nṛsiṃhair yadubhir yadūttamo yathoḍurājo divi tārakāgaṇaiḥ
BhP tatropamantriṇo rājan nānāhāsyarasair vibhum
BhP upatasthur naṭācāryā nartakyas tāṇḍavaiḥ pṛthak
BhP mṛdaṅgavīṇāmuraja veṇutāladarasvanaiḥ
BhP nanṛtur jagus tuṣṭuvuś ca sūtamāgadhavandinaḥ
BhP tatrāhur brāhmaṇāḥ kecid āsīnā brahmavādinaḥ
BhP pūrveṣāṃ puṇyayaśasāṃ rājñāṃ cākathayan kathāḥ
BhP tatraikaḥ puruṣo rājann āgato 'pūrvadarśanaḥ
BhP vijñāpito bhagavate pratīhāraiḥ praveśitaḥ
BhP sa namaskṛtya kṛṣṇāya pareśāya kṛtāñjaliḥ
BhP rājñām āvedayad duḥkhaṃ jarāsandhanirodhajam
BhP ye ca digvijaye tasya sannatiṃ na yayur nṛpāḥ
BhP prasahya ruddhās tenāsann ayute dve girivraje
BhP rājāna ūcuḥ
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇāprameyātman prapannabhayabhañjana
BhP vayaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmo bhavabhītāḥ pṛthagdhiyaḥ
BhP loko vikarmanirataḥ kuśale pramattaḥ
BhP karmaṇy ayaṃ tvadudite bhavadarcane sve
BhP yas tāvad asya balavān iha jīvitāśāṃ
BhP sadyaś chinatty animiṣāya namo 'stu tasmai
BhP loke bhavāñ jagadinaḥ kalayāvatīrṇaḥ
BhP sadrakṣaṇāya khalanigrahaṇāya cānyaḥ
BhP kaścit tvadīyam atiyāti nideśam īśa
BhP kiṃ vā janaḥ svakṛtam ṛcchati tan na vidmaḥ
BhP svapnāyitaṃ nṛpasukhaṃ paratantram īśa
BhP śaśvadbhayena mṛtakena dhuraṃ vahāmaḥ
BhP hitvā tad ātmani sukhaṃ tvadanīhalabhyaṃ
BhP kliśyāmahe 'tikṛpaṇās tava māyayeha
BhP tan no bhavān praṇataśokaharāṅghriyugmo
BhP baddhān viyuṅkṣva magadhāhvayakarmapāśāt
BhP yo bhūbhujo 'yutamataṅgajavīryam eko
BhP bibhrad rurodha bhavane mṛgarāḍ ivāvīḥ
BhP yo vai tvayā dvinavakṛtva udāttacakra
BhP bhagno mṛdhe khalu bhavantam anantavīryam
BhP jitvā nṛlokanirataṃ sakṛd ūḍhadarpo
BhP yuṣmatprajā rujati no 'jita tad vidhehi
BhP dūta uvāca
BhP iti māgadhasaṃruddhā bhavaddarśanakaṅkṣiṇaḥ
BhP prapannāḥ pādamūlaṃ te dīnānāṃ śaṃ vidhīyatām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP rājadūte bruvaty evaṃ devarṣiḥ paramadyutiḥ
BhP bibhrat piṅgajaṭābhāraṃ prādurāsīd yathā raviḥ
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ sarvalokeśvareśvaraḥ
BhP vavanda utthitaḥ śīrṣṇā sasabhyaḥ sānugo mudā
BhP sabhājayitvā vidhivat kṛtāsanaparigraham
BhP babhāṣe sunṛtair vākyaiḥ śraddhayā tarpayan munim
BhP api svid adya lokānāṃ trayāṇām akutobhayam
BhP nanu bhūyān bhagavato lokān paryaṭato guṇaḥ
BhP na hi te 'viditaṃ kiñcil lokeṣv īśvarakartṛṣu
BhP atha pṛcchāmahe yuṣmān pāṇḍavānāṃ cikīrṣitam
BhP śrīnārada uvāca
BhP dṛṣṭā māyā te bahuśo duratyayā māyā vibho viśvasṛjaś ca māyinaḥ
BhP bhūteṣu bhūmaṃś carataḥ svaśaktibhir vahner iva cchannaruco na me 'dbhutam
BhP tavehitaṃ ko 'rhati sādhu vedituṃ svamāyayedaṃ sṛjato niyacchataḥ
BhP yad vidyamānātmatayāvabhāsate tasmai namas te svavilakṣaṇātmane
BhP jīvasya yaḥ saṃsarato vimokṣaṇaṃ na jānato 'narthavahāc charīrataḥ
BhP līlāvatāraiḥ svayaśaḥ pradīpakaṃ prājvālayat tvā tam ahaṃ prapadye
BhP athāpy āśrāvaye brahma naralokaviḍambanam
BhP rājñaḥ paitṛṣvasreyasya bhaktasya ca cikīrṣitam
BhP yakṣyati tvāṃ makhendreṇa rājasūyena pāṇḍavaḥ
BhP pārameṣṭhyakāmo nṛpatis tad bhavān anumodatām
BhP tasmin deva kratuvare bhavantaṃ vai surādayaḥ
BhP didṛkṣavaḥ sameṣyanti rājānaś ca yaśasvinaḥ
BhP śravaṇāt kīrtanād dhyānāt pūyante 'ntevasāyinaḥ
BhP tava brahmamayasyeśa kim utekṣābhimarśinaḥ
BhP yasyāmalaṃ divi yaśaḥ prathitaṃ rasāyāṃ
BhP bhūmau ca te bhuvanamaṅgala digvitānam
BhP mandākinīti divi bhogavatīti cādho
BhP gaṅgeti ceha caraṇāmbu punāti viśvam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP tatra teṣv ātmapakṣeṣv a gṛṇatsu vijigīṣayā
BhP vācaḥ peśaiḥ smayan bhṛtyam uddhavaṃ prāha keśavaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP tvaṃ hi naḥ paramaṃ cakṣuḥ suhṛn mantrārthatattvavit

BhP ity upāmantrito bhartrā sarvajñenāpi mugdhavat
BhP nideśaṃ śirasādhāya uddhavaḥ pratyabhāṣata
BhP śrīśuka uvāca

BhP sabhyānāṃ matam ājñāya kṛṣṇasya ca mahāmatiḥ
BhP śrīuddhava uvāca
BhP yad uktam ṛṣinā deva sācivyaṃ yakṣyatas tvayā
BhP kāryaṃ paitṛṣvasreyasya rakṣā ca śaraṇaiṣiṇām
BhP yaṣṭavyam rājasūyena dikcakrajayinā vibho
BhP ato jarāsutajaya ubhayārtho mato mama
BhP asmākaṃ ca mahān artho hy etenaiva bhaviṣyati
BhP yaśaś ca tava govinda rājño baddhān vimuñcataḥ
BhP sa vai durviṣaho rājā nāgāyutasamo bale
BhP balinām api cānyeṣāṃ bhīmaṃ samabalaṃ vinā
BhP dvairathe sa tu jetavyo mā śatākṣauhiṇīyutaḥ
BhP brāhmaṇyo 'bhyarthito viprair na pratyākhyāti karhicit

BhP haniṣyati na sandeho dvairathe tava sannidhau

BhP hiraṇyagarbhaḥ śarvaś ca kālasyārūpiṇas tava

BhP gopyaś ca kuñjarapater janakātmajāyāḥ
BhP pitroś ca labdhaśaraṇā munayo vayaṃ ca
BhP jarāsandhavadhaḥ kṛṣṇa bhūryarthāyopakalpate
BhP prāyaḥ pākavipākena tava cābhimataḥ kratuḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity uddhavavaco rājan sarvatobhadram acyutam
BhP devarṣir yaduvṛddhāś ca kṛṣṇaś ca pratyapūjayan
BhP athādiśat prayāṇāya bhagavān devakīsutaḥ
BhP bhṛtyān dārukajaitrādīn anujñāpya gurūn vibhuḥ
BhP nirgamayyāvarodhān svān sasutān saparicchadān
BhP saṅkarṣaṇam anujñāpya yadurājaṃ ca śatruhan
BhP sūtopanītaṃ svaratham āruhad garuḍadhvajam
BhP tato rathadvipabhaṭasādināyakaiḥ
BhP karālayā parivṛta ātmasenayā
BhP mṛdaṅgabheryānakaśaṅkhagomukhaiḥ
BhP praghoṣaghoṣitakakubho nirakramat
BhP nṛvājikāñcanaśibikābhir acyutaṃ sahātmajāḥ patim anu suvratā yayuḥ
BhP varāmbarābharaṇavilepanasrajaḥ susaṃvṛtā nṛbhir asicarmapāṇibhiḥ
BhP naroṣṭragomahiṣakharāśvataryanaḥ
BhP kareṇubhiḥ parijanavārayoṣitaḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtāḥ kaṭakuṭikambalāmbarādy
BhP upaskarā yayur adhiyujya sarvataḥ
BhP balaṃ bṛhaddhvajapaṭachatracāmarair
BhP varāyudhābharaṇakirīṭavarmabhiḥ
BhP divāṃśubhis tumularavaṃ babhau raver
BhP yathārṇavaḥ kṣubhitatimiṅgilormibhiḥ
BhP atho munir yadupatinā sabhājitaḥ praṇamya taṃ hṛdi vidadhad vihāyasā
BhP niśamya tadvyavasitam āhṛtārhaṇo mukundasandaraśananirvṛtendriyaḥ
BhP rājadūtam uvācedaṃ bhagavān prīṇayan girā
BhP mā bhaiṣṭa dūta bhadraṃ vo ghātayiṣyāmi māgadham
BhP ity uktaḥ prasthito dūto yathāvad avadan nṛpān
BhP te 'pi sandarśanaṃ śaureḥ pratyaikṣan yan mumukṣavaḥ
BhP ānartasauvīramarūṃs tīrtvā vinaśanaṃ hariḥ
BhP girīn nadīr atīyāya puragrāmavrajākarān
BhP tato dṛṣadvatīṃ tīrtvā mukundo 'tha sarasvatīm
BhP pañcālān atha matsyāṃś ca śakraprastham athāgamat
BhP tam upāgatam ākarṇya prīto durdarśanaṃ nṛnām
BhP ajātaśatrur niragāt sopadhyāyaḥ suhṛdvṛtaḥ
BhP gītavāditraghoṣeṇa brahmaghoṣeṇa bhūyasā
BhP abhyayāt sa hṛṣīkeśaṃ prāṇāḥ prāṇam ivādṛtaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā viklinnahṛdayaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ snehena pāṇḍavaḥ
BhP cirād dṛṣṭaṃ priyatamaṃ sasvaje 'tha punaḥ punaḥ
BhP dorbhyāṃ pariṣvajya ramāmalālayaṃ mukundagātraṃ nṛpatir hatāśubhaḥ
BhP lebhe parāṃ nirvṛtim aśrulocano hṛṣyattanur vismṛtalokavibhramaḥ
BhP taṃ mātuleyaṃ parirabhya nirvṛto bhīmaḥ smayan premajalākulendriyaḥ
BhP yamau kirīṭī ca suhṛttamaṃ mudā pravṛddhabāṣpāḥ parirebhire 'cyutam
BhP arjunena pariṣvakto yamābhyām abhivāditaḥ
BhP brāhmaṇebhyo namaskṛtya vṛddhebhyaś ca yathārhataḥ
BhP mānino mānayām āsa kurusṛñjayakaikayān
BhP sūtamāgadhagandharvā vandinaś copamantriṇaḥ
BhP mṛdaṅgaśaṅkhapaṭaha vīṇāpaṇavagomukhaiḥ
BhP brāhmaṇāś cāravindākṣaṃ tuṣṭuvur nanṛtur jaguḥ
BhP evaṃ suhṛdbhiḥ paryastaḥ puṇyaślokaśikhāmaṇiḥ
BhP saṃstūyamāno bhagavān viveśālaṅkṛtaṃ puram
BhP saṃsiktavartma kariṇāṃ madagandhatoyaiś
BhP citradhvajaiḥ kanakatoraṇapūrṇakumbhaiḥ
BhP mṛṣṭātmabhir navadukūlavibhūṣaṇasrag
BhP gandhair nṛbhir yuvatibhiś ca virājamānam
BhP uddīptadīpabalibhiḥ pratisadma jāla
BhP niryātadhūparuciraṃ vilasatpatākam
BhP mūrdhanyahemakalaśai rajatoruśṛṅgair
BhP juṣṭaṃ dadarśa bhavanaiḥ kururājadhāma

BhP autsukyaviślathitakeśadukūlabandhāḥ
BhP sadyo visṛjya gṛhakarma patīṃś ca talpe
BhP draṣṭuṃ yayur yuvatayaḥ sma narendramārge
BhP tasmin susaṅkula ibhāśvarathadvipadbhiḥ
BhP kṛṣṇam sabhāryam upalabhya gṛhādhirūḍhāḥ
BhP nāryo vikīrya kusumair manasopaguhya
BhP susvāgataṃ vidadhur utsmayavīkṣitena
BhP ūcuḥ striyaḥ pathi nirīkṣya mukundapatnīs
BhP tārā yathoḍupasahāḥ kim akāry amūbhiḥ
BhP yac cakṣuṣāṃ puruṣamaulir udārahāsa

BhP cakruḥ saparyāṃ kṛṣṇāya śreṇīmukhyā hatainasaḥ
BhP antaḥpurajanaiḥ prītyā mukundaḥ phullalocanaiḥ
BhP sasambhramair abhyupetaḥ prāviśad rājamandiram

BhP govindaṃ gṛham ānīya devadeveśam ādṛtaḥ
BhP pūjāyāṃ nāvidat kṛtyaṃ pramodopahato nṛpaḥ

BhP svayaṃ ca kṛṣṇayā rājan bhaginyā cābhivanditaḥ
BhP śvaśṛvā sañcoditā kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇapatnīś ca sarvaśaḥ
BhP ānarca rukmiṇīṃ satyāṃ bhadrāṃ jāmbavatīṃ tathā
BhP kālindīṃ mitravindāṃ ca śaibyāṃ nāgnajitīṃ satīm
BhP anyāś cābhyāgatā yās tu vāsaḥsraṅmaṇḍanādibhiḥ
BhP sukhaṃ nivāsayām āsa dharmarājo janārdanam
BhP sasainyaṃ sānugāmatyaṃ sabhāryaṃ ca navaṃ navam

BhP mocayitvā mayaṃ yena rājñe divyā sabhā kṛtā
BhP uvāsa katicin māsān rājñaḥ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP viharan ratham āruhya phālgunena bhaṭair vṛtaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ekadā tu sabhāmadhya āsthito munibhir vṛtaḥ
BhP brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyair bhrātṛbhiś ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
BhP ācāryaiḥ kulavṛddhaiś ca jñātisambandhibāndhavaiḥ
BhP śṛṇvatām eva caiteṣām ābhāṣyedam uvāca ha
BhP śrīyudhiṣṭhira uvāca

BhP na kaścin matparaṃ loke tejasā yaśasā śriyā

BhP diśi pratīcyāṃ nakulam udīcyāṃ savyasācinam

BhP jagmur girivrajaṃ tāta bṛhadrathasuto yataḥ

BhP rājan viddhy atithīn prāptān arthino dūram āgatān

BhP kiṃ na deyaṃ vadānyānāṃ kaḥ paraḥ samadarśinām

BhP śrīśuka uvāca

BhP aiśvaryād bhraṃśitasyāpi vipravyājena viṣṇunā

BhP jīvatā brāhmaṇārthāya ko nv arthaḥ kṣatrabandhunā
BhP dehena patamānena nehatā vipulaṃ yaśaḥ
BhP ity udāramatiḥ prāha kṛṣṇārjunavṛkodarān
BhP he viprā vriyatāṃ kāmo dadāmy ātmaśiro 'pi vaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca

BhP asau vṛkodaraḥ pārthas tasya bhrātārjuno hy ayam

BhP dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sahasuto viduraś ca mahāmatiḥ

BhP kṛṣṭvā tatra yathāmnāyaṃ dīkṣayāṃ cakrire nṛpam

BhP indrādayo lokapālā viriñcibhavasaṃyutāḥ
BhP sagaṇāḥ siddhagandharvā vidyādharamahoragāḥ
BhP munayo yakṣarakṣāṃsi khagakinnaracāraṇāḥ
BhP rājānaś ca samāhūtā rājapatnyaś ca sarvaśaḥ
BhP rājasūyaṃ samīyuḥ sma rājñaḥ pāṇḍusutasya vai
