BhP ayājayan mahārājaṃ yājakā devavarcasaḥ
BhP rājasūyena vidhivat pracetasam ivāmarāḥ
BhP sūtye 'hany avanīpālo yājakān sadasaspatīn
BhP apūjayan mahābhāgān yathāvat susamāhitaḥ
BhP sadasyāgryārhaṇārhaṃ vai vimṛśantaḥ sabhāsadaḥ
BhP nādhyagacchann anaikāntyāt sahadevas tadābravīt
BhP arhati hy acyutaḥ śraiṣṭhyaṃ bhagavān sātvatāṃ patiḥ
BhP eṣa vai devatāḥ sarvā deśakāladhanādayaḥ
BhP yadātmakam idaṃ viśvaṃ kratavaś ca yadātmakāḥ
BhP agnir āhutayo mantrā sāṅkhyaṃ yogaś ca yatparaḥ
BhP eka evādvitīyo 'sāv aitadātmyam idaṃ jagat
BhP ātmanātmāśrayaḥ sabhyāḥ sṛjaty avati hanty ajaḥ
BhP vividhānīha karmāṇi janayan yadavekṣayā
BhP īhate yad ayaṃ sarvaḥ śreyo dharmādilakṣaṇam
BhP tasmāt kṛṣṇāya mahate dīyatāṃ paramārhaṇam
BhP evaṃ cet sarvabhūtānām ātmanaś cārhaṇaṃ bhavet
BhP sarvabhūtātmabhūtāya kṛṣṇāyānanyadarśine
BhP deyaṃ śāntāya pūrṇāya dattasyānantyam icchatā
BhP ity uktvā sahadevo 'bhūt tūṣṇīṃ kṛṣṇānubhāvavit
BhP tac chrutvā tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve sādhu sādhv iti sattamāḥ
BhP śrutvā dvijeritaṃ rājā jñātvā hārdaṃ sabhāsadām
BhP samarhayad dhṛṣīkeśaṃ prītaḥ praṇayavihvalaḥ
BhP tatpādāv avanijyāpaḥ śirasā lokapāvanīḥ
BhP sabhāryaḥ sānujāmātyaḥ sakuṭumbo vahan mudā
BhP vāsobhiḥ pītakauṣeyair bhūṣaṇaiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
BhP arhayitvāśrupūrṇākṣo nāśakat samavekṣitum
BhP itthaṃ sabhājitaṃ vīkṣya sarve prāñjalayo janāḥ
BhP namo jayeti nemus taṃ nipetuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭayaḥ
BhP itthaṃ niśamya damaghoṣasutaḥ svapīṭhād
BhP utthāya kṛṣṇaguṇavarṇanajātamanyuḥ
BhP utkṣipya bāhum idam āha sadasy amarṣī
BhP saṃśrāvayan bhagavate paruṣāṇy abhītaḥ
BhP īśo duratyayaḥ kāla iti satyavatī srutiḥ
BhP vṛddhānām api yad buddhir bālavākyair vibhidyate
BhP yūyaṃ pātravidāṃ śreṣṭhā mā mandhvaṃ bālabhāṣītam
BhP sadasaspatayaḥ sarve kṛṣṇo yat sammato 'rhaṇe
BhP tapovidyāvratadharān jñānavidhvastakalmaṣān
BhP paramaṛṣīn brahmaniṣṭhāṃl lokapālaiś ca pūjitān
BhP sadaspatīn atikramya gopālaḥ kulapāṃsanaḥ
BhP yathā kākaḥ puroḍāśaṃ saparyāṃ katham arhati
BhP varṇāśramakulāpetaḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtaḥ
BhP svairavartī guṇair hīnaḥ saparyāṃ katham arhati
BhP yayātinaiṣāṃ hi kulaṃ śaptaṃ sadbhir bahiṣkṛtam
BhP vṛthāpānarataṃ śaśvat saparyāṃ katham arhati
BhP brahmarṣisevitān deśān hitvaite 'brahmavarcasam
BhP samudraṃ durgam āśritya bādhante dasyavaḥ prajāḥ
BhP evamādīny abhadrāṇi babhāṣe naṣṭamaṅgalaḥ
BhP novāca kiñcid bhagavān yathā siṃhaḥ śivārutam
BhP bhagavannindanaṃ śrutvā duḥsahaṃ tat sabhāsadaḥ
BhP karṇau pidhāya nirjagmuḥ śapantaś cedipaṃ ruṣā
BhP nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śṛṇvaṃs tatparasya janasya vā
BhP tato nāpaiti yaḥ so 'pi yāty adhaḥ sukṛtāc cyutaḥ
BhP tataḥ pāṇḍusutāḥ kruddhā matsyakaikayasṛñjayāḥ
BhP udāyudhāḥ samuttasthuḥ śiśupālajighāṃsavaḥ
BhP tataś caidyas tv asambhrānto jagṛhe khaḍgacarmaṇī
BhP bhartsayan kṛṣṇapakṣīyān rājñaḥ sadasi bhārata
BhP tāvad utthāya bhagavān svān nivārya svayaṃ ruṣā
BhP śiraḥ kṣurāntacakreṇa jahāra patato ripoḥ
BhP śabdaḥ kolāhalo 'thāsīc chiśupāle hate mahān
BhP tasyānuyāyino bhūpā dudruvur jīvitaiṣiṇaḥ
BhP caidyadehotthitaṃ jyotir vāsudevam upāviśat
BhP paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānām ulkeva bhuvi khāc cyutā
BhP janmatrayānuguṇita vairasaṃrabdhayā dhiyā
BhP dhyāyaṃs tanmayatāṃ yāto bhāvo hi bhavakāraṇam
BhP ṛtvigbhyaḥ sasadasyebhyo dakṣināṃ vipulām adāt
BhP sarvān sampūjya vidhivac cakre 'vabhṛtham ekarāṭ
BhP sādhayitvā kratuḥ rājñaḥ kṛṣṇo yogeśvareśvaraḥ
BhP uvāsa katicin māsān suhṛdbhir abhiyācitaḥ
BhP tato 'nujñāpya rājānam anicchantam apīśvaraḥ
BhP yayau sabhāryaḥ sāmātyaḥ svapuraṃ devakīsutaḥ
BhP varṇitaṃ tad upākhyānaṃ mayā te bahuvistaram
BhP vaikuṇṭhavāsinor janma vipraśāpāt punaḥ punaḥ
BhP rājasūyāvabhṛthyena snāto rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
BhP brahmakṣatrasabhāmadhye śuśubhe surarāḍ iva
BhP rājñā sabhājitāḥ sarve suramānavakhecarāḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaṃ kratuṃ ca śaṃsantaḥ svadhāmāni yayur mudā
BhP duryodhanam ṛte pāpaṃ kaliṃ kurukulāmayam
BhP yo na sehe śrīyaṃ sphītāṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍusutasya tām
BhP ya idaṃ kīrtayed viṣṇoḥ karma caidyavadhādikam
BhP rājamokṣaṃ vitānaṃ ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
BhP śrīrājovāca ajātaśatros tam dṛṣṭvā rājasūyamahodayam
BhP sarve mumudire brahman nṛdevā ye samāgatāḥ
BhP duryodhanaṃ varjayitvā rājānaḥ sarṣayaḥ surāḥ
BhP iti śrutaṃ no bhagavaṃs tatra kāraṇam ucyatām
BhP śrībādarāyaṇir uvāca
BhP pitāmahasya te yajñe rājasūye mahātmanaḥ
BhP bāndhavāḥ paricaryāyāṃ tasyāsan premabandhanāḥ
BhP bhīmo mahānasādhyakṣo dhanādhyakṣaḥ suyodhanaḥ
BhP sahadevas tu pūjāyāṃ nakulo dravyasādhane
BhP guruśuśrūṣaṇe jiṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pādāvanejane
BhP pariveṣaṇe drupadajā karṇo dāne mahāmanāḥ
BhP yuyudhāno vikarṇaś ca hārdikyo vidurādayaḥ
BhP bāhlīkaputrā bhūryādyā ye ca santardanādayaḥ
BhP nirūpitā mahāyajñe nānākarmasu te tadā
BhP pravartante sma rājendra rājñaḥ priyacikīrṣavaḥ
BhP ṛtviksadasyabahuvitsu suhṛttameṣu
BhP sviṣṭeṣu sūnṛtasamarhaṇadakṣiṇābhiḥ
BhP caidye ca sātvatapateś caraṇaṃ praviṣṭe
BhP cakrus tatas tv avabhṛthasnapanaṃ dyunadyām
BhP mṛdaṅgaśaṅkhapaṇava dhundhuryānakagomukhāḥ
BhP vāditrāṇi vicitrāṇi nedur āvabhṛthotsave
BhP nārtakyo nanṛtur hṛṣṭā gāyakā yūthaśo jaguḥ
BhP vīṇāveṇutalonnādas teṣāṃ sa divam aspṛśat
BhP citradhvajapatākāgrair ibhendrasyandanārvabhiḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtair bhaṭair bhūpā niryayū rukmamālinaḥ
BhP yadusṛñjayakāmboja kurukekayakośalāḥ
BhP kampayanto bhuvaṃ sainyair yayamānapuraḥsarāḥ
BhP sadasyartvigdvijaśreṣṭhā brahmaghoṣeṇa bhūyasā
BhP devarṣipitṛgandharvās tuṣṭuvuḥ puṣpavarṣiṇaḥ
BhP svalaṇkṛtā narā nāryo gandhasragbhūṣaṇāmbaraiḥ
BhP vilimpantyo 'bhisiñcantyo vijahrur vividhai rasaiḥ
BhP tailagorasagandhoda haridrāsāndrakuṅkumaiḥ
BhP pumbhir liptāḥ pralimpantyo vijahrur vārayoṣitaḥ
BhP guptā nṛbhir niragamann upalabdhum etad
BhP devyo yathā divi vimānavarair nṛdevyo
BhP tā mātuleyasakhibhiḥ pariṣicyamānāḥ
BhP savrīḍahāsavikasadvadanā virejuḥ
BhP tā devarān uta sakhīn siṣicur dṛtībhiḥ
BhP klinnāmbarā vivṛtagātrakucorumadhyāḥ
BhP autsukyamuktakavarāc cyavamānamālyāḥ
BhP kṣobhaṃ dadhur maladhiyāṃ rucirair vihāraiḥ
BhP sa samrāḍ ratham āruḍhaḥ sadaśvaṃ rukmamālinam
BhP vyarocata svapatnībhiḥ kriyābhiḥ kraturāḍ iva
BhP patnīsamyājāvabhṛthyaiś caritvā te tam ṛtvijaḥ
BhP ācāntaṃ snāpayāṃ cakrur gaṅgāyāṃ saha kṛṣṇayā
BhP devadundubhayo nedur naradundubhibhiḥ samam
BhP mumucuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi devarṣipitṛmānavāḥ
BhP sasnus tatra tataḥ sarve varṇāśramayutā narāḥ
BhP mahāpātaky api yataḥ sadyo mucyeta kilbiṣāt
BhP atha rājāhate kṣaume paridhāya svalaṅkṛtaḥ
BhP ṛtviksadasyaviprādīn ānarcābharaṇāmbaraiḥ
BhP bandhūñ jñātīn nṛpān mitra suhṛdo 'nyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
BhP abhīkṣnaṃ pūjayām āsa nārāyaṇaparo nṛpaḥ
BhP sarve janāḥ suraruco maṇikuṇḍalasrag
BhP uṣṇīṣakañcukadukūlamahārghyahārāḥ
BhP nāryaś ca kuṇḍalayugālakavṛndajuṣṭa
BhP vaktraśriyaḥ kanakamekhalayā virejuḥ
BhP athartvijo mahāśīlāḥ sadasyā brahmavādinaḥ
BhP brahmakṣatriyaviṭśudrā rājāno ye samāgatāḥ
BhP devarṣipitṛbhūtāni lokapālāḥ sahānugāḥ
BhP pūjitās tam anujñāpya svadhāmāni yayur nṛpa
BhP haridāsasya rājarṣe rājasūyamahodayam
BhP naivātṛpyan praśaṃsantaḥ piban martyo 'mṛtaṃ yathā
BhP tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā suhṛtsambandhibāndhavān
BhP premṇā nivārayām āsa kṛṣṇaṃ ca tyāgakātaraḥ
BhP bhagavān api tatrāṅga nyāvātsīt tatpriyaṃkaraḥ
BhP prasthāpya yaduvīrāṃś ca sāmbādīṃś ca kuśasthalīm
BhP itthaṃ rājā dharmasuto manorathamahārṇavam
BhP sudustaraṃ samuttīrya kṛṣṇenāsīd gatajvaraḥ
BhP ekadāntaḥpure tasya vīkṣya duryodhanaḥ śriyam
BhP atapyad rājasūyasya mahitvaṃ cācyutātmanaḥ
BhP yasmiṃs narendraditijendrasurendralakṣmīr
BhP nānā vibhānti kila viśvasṛjopakḷptāḥ
BhP tābhiḥ patīn drupadarājasutopatasthe
BhP yasyāṃ viṣaktahṛdayaḥ kururāḍ atapyat
BhP yasmin tadā madhupater mahiṣīsahasraṃ
BhP śroṇībhareṇa śanakaiḥ kvaṇadaṅghriśobham
BhP madhye sucāru kucakuṅkumaśoṇahāraṃ
BhP śrīmanmukhaṃ pracalakuṇḍalakuntalāḍhyam
BhP sabhāyāṃ mayakḷptāyāṃ kvāpi dharmasuto 'dhirāṭ
BhP vṛto 'nugair bandhubhiś ca kṛṣṇenāpi svacakṣuṣā
BhP āsīnaḥ kāñcane sākṣād āsane maghavān iva
BhP pārameṣṭhyaśrīyā juṣṭaḥ stūyamānaś ca vandibhiḥ
BhP tatra duryodhano mānī parīto bhrātṛbhir nṛpa
BhP kirīṭamālī nyaviśad asihastaḥ kṣipan ruṣā
BhP sthale 'bhyagṛhṇād vastrāntaṃ jalaṃ matvā sthale 'patat
BhP jale ca sthalavad bhrāntyā mayamāyāvimohitaḥ
BhP jahāsa bhīmas taṃ dṛṣṭvā striyo nṛpatayo pare
BhP nivāryamāṇā apy aṅga rājñā kṛṣṇānumoditāḥ
BhP sa vrīḍito 'vagvadano ruṣā jvalan niṣkramya tūṣṇīṃ prayayau gajāhvayam
BhP hāheti śabdaḥ sumahān abhūt satām ajātaśatrur vimanā ivābhavat
BhP babhūva tūṣṇīṃ bhagavān bhuvo bharaṃ samujjihīrṣur bhramati sma yaddṛśā
BhP etat te 'bhihitaṃ rājan yat pṛṣṭo 'ham iha tvayā
BhP suyodhanasya daurātmyaṃ rājasūye mahākratau
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP athānyad api kṛṣṇasya śṛṇu karmādbhutaṃ nṛpa
BhP krīḍānaraśarīrasya yathā saubhapatir hataḥ
BhP śiśupālasakhaḥ śālvo rukmiṇyudvāha āgataḥ
BhP yadubhir nirjitaḥ saṅkhye jarāsandhādayas tathā
BhP śālvaḥ pratijñām akaroc chṛṇvatāṃ sarvabhūbhujām
BhP ayādavāṃ kṣmāṃ kariṣye pauruṣaṃ mama paśyata
BhP iti mūḍhaḥ pratijñāya devaṃ paśupatiṃ prabhum
BhP ārādhayām āsa nṛpaḥ pāṃśumuṣṭiṃ sakṛd grasan
BhP saṃvatsarānte bhagavān āśutoṣa umāpatiḥ
BhP vareṇa cchandayām āsa śālvaṃ śaraṇam āgatam
BhP devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām
BhP abhedyaṃ kāmagaṃ vavre sa yānaṃ vṛṣṇibhīṣaṇam
BhP tatheti giriśādiṣṭo mayaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
BhP puraṃ nirmāya śālvāya prādāt saubham ayasmayam
BhP sa labdhvā kāmagaṃ yānaṃ tamodhāma durāsadam
BhP yayas dvāravatīṃ śālvo vairaṃ vṛṣṇikṛtaṃ smaran
BhP nirudhya senayā śālvo mahatyā bharatarṣabha
BhP purīṃ babhañjopavanān udyānāni ca sarvaśaḥ
BhP sagopurāṇi dvārāṇi prāsādāṭṭālatolikāḥ
BhP vihārān sa vimānāgryān nipetuḥ śastravṛṣṭayaḥ
BhP śilādrumāś cāśanayaḥ sarpā āsāraśarkarāḥ
BhP pracaṇḍaś cakravāto 'bhūd rajasācchāditā diśaḥ
BhP ity ardyamānā saubhena kṛṣṇasya nagarī bhṛśam
BhP nābhyapadyata śaṃ rājaṃs tripureṇa yathā mahī
BhP pradyumno bhagavān vīkṣya bādhyamānā nijāḥ prajāḥ
BhP ma bhaiṣṭety abhyadhād vīro rathārūḍho mahāyaśāḥ
BhP sātyakiś cārudeṣṇaś ca sāmbo 'krūraḥ sahānujaḥ
BhP hārdikyo bhānuvindaś ca gadaś ca śukasāraṇau
BhP apare ca maheṣvāsā rathayūthapayūthapāḥ
BhP niryayur daṃśitā guptā rathebhāśvapadātibhiḥ
BhP tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ śālvānāṃ yadubhiḥ saha
BhP yathāsurāṇāṃ vibudhais tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
BhP tāś ca saubhapater māyā divyāstrai rukmiṇīsutaḥ
BhP kṣaṇena nāśayām āsa naiśaṃ tama ivoṣṇaguḥ
BhP vivyādha pañcaviṃśatyā svarṇapuṅkhair ayomukhaiḥ
BhP śālvasya dhvajinīpālaṃ śaraiḥ sannataparvabhiḥ
BhP śatenātāḍayac chālvam ekaikenāsya sainikān
BhP daśabhir daśabhir netṝn vāhanāni tribhis tribhiḥ
BhP tad adbhutaṃ mahat karma pradyumnasya mahātmanaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā taṃ pūjayām āsuḥ sarve svaparasainikāḥ
BhP bahurūpaikarūpaṃ tad dṛśyate na ca dṛśyate
BhP māyāmayaṃ mayakṛtaṃ durvibhāvyaṃ parair abhūt
BhP kvacid bhūmau kvacid vyomni girimūrdhni jale kvacit
BhP alātacakravad bhrāmyat saubhaṃ tad duravasthitam
BhP yatra yatropalakṣyeta sasaubhaḥ sahasainikaḥ
BhP śālvas tatas tato 'muñcañ charān sātvatayūthapāḥ
BhP śarair agnyarkasaṃsparśair āśīviṣadurāsadaiḥ
BhP pīḍyamānapurānīkaḥ śālvo 'muhyat pareritaiḥ
BhP śālvānīkapaśastraughair vṛṣṇivīrā bhṛśārditāḥ
BhP na tatyajū raṇaṃ svaṃ svaṃ lokadvayajigīṣavaḥ
BhP śālvāmātyo dyumān nāma pradyumnaṃ prak prapīḍitaḥ
BhP āsādya gadayā maurvyā vyāhatya vyanadad balī
BhP pradyumnaṃ gadayā sīrṇa vakṣaḥsthalam ariṃdamam
BhP apovāha raṇāt sūto dharmavid dārukātmajaḥ
BhP labdhasamjño muhūrtena kārṣṇiḥ sārathim abravīt
BhP aho asādhv idaṃ sūta yad raṇān me 'pasarpaṇam
BhP na yadūnāṃ kule jātaḥ śrūyate raṇavicyutaḥ
BhP vinā mat klībacittena sūtena prāptakilbiṣāt
BhP kiṃ nu vakṣye 'bhisaṅgamya pitarau rāmakeśavau
BhP yuddhāt samyag apakrāntaḥ pṛṣṭas tatrātmanaḥ kṣamam
BhP vyaktaṃ me kathayiṣyanti hasantyo bhrātṛjāmayaḥ
BhP klaibyaṃ kathaṃ kathaṃ vīra tavānyaiḥ kathyatāṃ mṛdhe
BhP sārathir uvāca
BhP dharmaṃ vijānatāyuṣman kṛtam etan mayā vibho
BhP sūtaḥ kṛcchragataṃ rakṣed rathinaṃ sārathiṃ rathī
BhP etad viditvā tu bhavān mayāpovāhito raṇāt
BhP upasṛṣṭaḥ pareṇeti mūrcchito gadayā hataḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa upaspṛśya salilaṃ daṃśito dhṛtakārmukaḥ
BhP naya māṃ dyumataḥ pārśvaṃ vīrasyety āha sārathim
BhP vidhamantaṃ svasainyāni dyumantaṃ rukmiṇīsutaḥ
BhP pratihatya pratyavidhyān nārācair aṣṭabhiḥ smayan
BhP caturbhiś caturo vāhān sūtam ekena cāhanat
BhP dvābhyaṃ dhanuś ca ketuṃ ca śareṇānyena vai śiraḥ
BhP gadasātyakisāmbādyā jaghnuḥ saubhapater balam
BhP petuḥ samudre saubheyāḥ sarve sañchinnakandharāḥ
BhP evaṃ yadūnāṃ śālvānāṃ nighnatām itaretaram
BhP yuddhaṃ trinavarātraṃ tad abhūt tumulam ulbaṇam
BhP indraprasthaṃ gataḥ kṛṣṇa āhūto dharmasūnunā
BhP rājasūye 'tha nivṛtte śiśupāle ca saṃsthite
BhP kuruvṛddhān anujñāpya munīṃś ca sasutāṃ pṛthām
BhP nimittāny atighorāṇi paśyan dvāravatīṃ yayau
BhP āha cāham ihāyāta āryamiśrābhisaṅgataḥ
BhP rājanyāś caidyapakṣīyā nūnaṃ hanyuḥ purīṃ mama
BhP vīkṣya tat kadanaṃ svānāṃ nirūpya purarakṣaṇam
BhP saubhaṃ ca śālvarājaṃ ca dārukaṃ prāha keśavaḥ
BhP rathaṃ prāpaya me sūta śālvasyāntikam āśu vai
BhP sambhramas te na kartavyo māyāvī saubharāḍ ayam
BhP ity uktaś codayām āsa ratham āsthāya dārukaḥ
BhP viśantaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarve sve pare cāruṇānujam
BhP śālvaś ca kṛṣṇam ālokya hataprāyabaleśvaraḥ
BhP prāharat kṛṣṇasūtaya śaktiṃ bhīmaravāṃ mṛdhe
BhP tām āpatantīṃ nabhasi maholkām iva raṃhasā
BhP bhāsayantīṃ diśaḥ śauriḥ sāyakaiḥ śatadhācchinat
BhP taṃ ca ṣoḍaśabhir viddhvā bānaiḥ saubhaṃ ca khe bhramat
BhP avidhyac charasandohaiḥ khaṃ sūrya iva raśmibhiḥ
BhP śālvaḥ śaures tu doḥ savyaṃ saśārṅgaṃ śārṅgadhanvanaḥ
BhP bibheda nyapatad dhastāc chārṅgam āsīt tad adbhutam
BhP hāhākāro mahān āsīd bhūtānāṃ tatra paśyatām
BhP ninadya saubharāḍ uccair idam āha janārdanam
BhP yat tvayā mūḍha naḥ sakhyur bhrātur bhāryā hṛtekṣatām
BhP pramattaḥ sa sabhāmadhye tvayā vyāpāditaḥ sakhā
BhP taṃ tvādya niśitair bāṇair aparājitamāninam
BhP nayāmy apunarāvṛttiṃ yadi tiṣṭher mamāgrataḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP vṛthā tvaṃ katthase manda na paśyasy antike 'ntakam
BhP paurusaṃ darśayanti sma śūrā na bahubhāṣiṇaḥ
BhP ity uktvā bhagavāñ chālvaṃ gadayā bhīmavegayā
BhP tatāḍa jatrau saṃrabdhaḥ sa cakampe vamann asṛk
BhP gadāyāṃ sannivṛttāyāṃ śālvas tv antaradhīyata
BhP tato muhūrta āgatya puruṣaḥ śirasācyutam
BhP devakyā prahito 'smīti natvā prāha vaco rudan
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahābāho pitā te pitṛvatsala
BhP baddhvāpanītaḥ śālvena saunikena yathā paśuḥ
BhP niśamya vipriyaṃ kṛṣṇo mānusīṃ prakṛtiṃ gataḥ
BhP vimanasko ghṛṇī snehād babhāṣe prākṛto yathā
BhP kathaṃ rāmam asambhrāntaṃ jitvājeyaṃ surāsuraiḥ
BhP śālvenālpīyasā nītaḥ pitā me balavān vidhiḥ
BhP iti bruvāṇe govinde saubharāṭ pratyupasthitaḥ
BhP vasudevam ivānīya kṛṣṇaṃ cedam uvāca saḥ
BhP eṣa te janitā tāto yadartham iha jīvasi
BhP vadhiṣye vīkṣatas te 'mum īśaś cet pāhi bāliśa
BhP evaṃ nirbhartsya māyāvī khaḍgenānakadundubheḥ
BhP utkṛtya śira ādāya khasthaṃ saubhaṃ samāviśat
BhP tato muhūrtaṃ prakṛtāv upaplutaḥ svabodha āste svajanānuṣaṅgataḥ
BhP mahānubhāvas tad abudhyad āsurīṃ māyāṃ sa śālvaprasṛtāṃ mayoditām
BhP na tatra dūtaṃ na pituḥ kalevaraṃ prabuddha ājau samapaśyad acyutaḥ
BhP svāpnaṃ yathā cāmbaracāriṇaṃ ripuṃ saubhastham ālokya nihantum udyataḥ
BhP evaṃ vadanti rājarṣe ṛṣayaḥ ke ca nānvitāḥ
BhP yat svavāco virudhyeta nūnaṃ te na smaranty uta
BhP kva śokamohau sneho vā bhayaṃ vā ye 'jñasambhavāḥ
BhP kva cākhaṇḍitavijñāna jñānaiśvaryas tv akhaṇḍitaḥ
BhP yatpādasevorjitayātmavidyayā hinvanty anādyātmaviparyayagraham
BhP labhanta ātmīyam anantam aiśvaraṃ kuto nu mohaḥ paramasya sadgateḥ
BhP taṃ śastrapūgaiḥ praharantam ojasā
BhP śālvaṃ śaraiḥ śaurir amoghavikramaḥ
BhP viddhvācchinad varma dhanuḥ śiromaṇiṃ
BhP saubhaṃ ca śatror gadayā ruroja ha
BhP tat kṛṣṇahasteritayā vicūrṇitaṃ papāta toye gadayā sahasradhā
BhP visṛjya tad bhūtalam āsthito gadām udyamya śālvo 'cyutam abhyagād drutam
BhP ādhāvataḥ sagadaṃ tasya bāhuṃ bhallena chittvātha rathāṅgam adbhutam
BhP vadhāya śālvasya layārkasannibhaṃ bibhrad babhau sārka ivodayācalaḥ
BhP jahāra tenaiva śiraḥ sakuṇḍalaṃ kirīṭayuktaṃ purumāyino hariḥ
BhP vajreṇa vṛtrasya yathā purandaro babhūva hāheti vacas tadā nṛṇām
BhP tasmin nipatite pāpe saubhe ca gadayā hate
BhP nedur dundubhayo rājan divi devagaṇeritāḥ
BhP sakhīnām apacitiṃ kurvan dantavakro ruṣābhyagāt
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP śiśupālasya śālvasya pauṇḍrakasyāpi durmatiḥ
BhP paralokagatānāṃ ca kurvan pārokṣyasauhṛdam
BhP ekaḥ padātiḥ saṅkruddho gadāpāṇiḥ prakampayan
BhP padbhyām imāṃ mahārāja mahāsattvo vyadṛśyata
BhP taṃ tathāyāntam ālokya gadām ādāya satvaraḥ
BhP avaplutya rathāt kṛṣṇaḥ sindhuṃ veleva pratyadhāt
BhP gadām udyamya kārūṣo mukundaṃ prāha durmadaḥ
BhP diṣṭyā diṣṭyā bhavān adya mama dṛṣṭipathaṃ gataḥ
BhP tvaṃ mātuleyo naḥ kṛṣṇa mitradhruṅ māṃ jighāṃsasi
BhP atas tvāṃ gadayā manda haniṣye vajrakalpayā
BhP tarhy ānṛṇyam upaimy ajña mitrāṇāṃ mitravatsalaḥ
BhP bandhurūpam ariṃ hatvā vyādhiṃ dehacaraṃ yathā
BhP evaṃ rūkṣais tudan vākyaiḥ kṛṣṇaṃ totrair iva dvipam
BhP gadayātāḍayan mūrdhni siṃhavad vyanadac ca saḥ
BhP gadayābhihato 'py ājau na cacāla yadūdvahaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇo 'pi tam ahan gurvyā kaumodakyā stanāntare
BhP gadānirbhinnahṛdaya udvaman rudhiraṃ mukhāt
BhP prasārya keśabāhvaṅghrīn dharaṇyāṃ nyapatad vyasuḥ
BhP tataḥ sūkṣmataraṃ jyotiḥ kṛṣṇam āviśad adbhutam
BhP paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yathā caidyavadhe nṛpa
BhP vidūrathas tu tadbhrātā bhrātṛśokapariplutaḥ
BhP āgacchad asicarmābhyām ucchvasaṃs tajjighāṃsayā
BhP tasya cāpatataḥ kṛṣṇaś cakreṇa kṣuraneminā
BhP śiro jahāra rājendra sakirīṭaṃ sakuṇḍalam
BhP evaṃ saubhaṃ ca śālvaṃ ca dantavakraṃ sahānujam
BhP hatvā durviṣahān anyair īḍitaḥ suramānavaiḥ
BhP munibhiḥ siddhagandharvair vidyādharamahoragaiḥ
BhP apsarobhiḥ pitṛgaṇair yakṣaiḥ kinnaracāraṇaiḥ
BhP upagīyamānavijayaḥ kusumair abhivarṣitaḥ
BhP vṛtaś ca vṛṣṇipravarair viveśālaṅkṛtāṃ purīm
BhP evaṃ yogeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇo bhagavān jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP īyate paśudṛṣṭīnāṃ nirjito jayatīti saḥ
BhP śrutvā yuddhodyamaṃ rāmaḥ kurūṇāṃ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
BhP tīrthābhiṣekavyājena madhyasthaḥ prayayau kila
BhP snātvā prabhāse santarpya devarṣipitṛmānavān
BhP sarasvatīṃ pratisrotaṃ yayau brāhmaṇasaṃvṛtaḥ
BhP pṛthūdakaṃ bindusaras tritakūpaṃ sudarśanam
BhP viśālaṃ brahmatīrthaṃ ca cakraṃ prācīṃ sarasvatīm
BhP yamunām anu yāny eva gaṅgām anu ca bhārata
BhP jagāma naimiṣaṃ yatra ṛṣayaḥ satram āsate
BhP tam āgatam abhipretya munayo dīrghasatriṇaḥ
BhP abhinandya yathānyāyaṃ praṇamyotthāya cārcayan
BhP so 'rcitaḥ saparīvāraḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ
BhP romaharṣaṇam āsīnaṃ maharṣeḥ śiṣyam aikṣata
BhP apratyutthāyinaṃ sūtam akṛtaprahvaṇāñjalim
BhP adhyāsīnaṃ ca tān viprāṃś cukopodvīkṣya mādhavaḥ
BhP yasmād asāv imān viprān adhyāste pratilomajaḥ
BhP dharmapālāṃs tathaivāsmān vadham arhati durmatiḥ
BhP ṛṣer bhagavato bhūtvā śiṣyo 'dhītya bahūni ca
BhP setihāsapurāṇāni dharmaśāstrāṇi sarvaśaḥ
BhP adāntasyāvinītasya vṛthā paṇḍitamāninaḥ
BhP na guṇāya bhavanti sma naṭasyevājitātmanaḥ
BhP etadartho hi loke 'sminn avatāro mayā kṛtaḥ
BhP vadhyā me dharmadhvajinas te hi pātakino 'dhikāḥ
BhP etāvad uktvā bhagavān nivṛtto 'sadvadhād api
BhP bhāvitvāt taṃ kuśāgreṇa karasthenāhanat prabhuḥ
BhP hāhetivādinaḥ sarve munayaḥ khinnamānasāḥ
BhP ūcuḥ saṅkarṣaṇaṃ devam adharmas te kṛtaḥ prabho
BhP asya brahmāsanaṃ dattam asmābhir yadunandana
BhP āyuś cātmāklamaṃ tāvad yāvat satraṃ samāpyate
BhP ajānataivācaritas tvayā brahmavadho yathā
BhP yogeśvarasya bhavato nāmnāyo 'pi niyāmakaḥ
BhP yady etadbrahmahatyāyāḥ pāvanaṃ lokapāvana
BhP cariṣyati bhavāṃl loka saṅgraho 'nanyacoditaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP cariṣye vadhanirveśaṃ lokānugrahakāmyayā
BhP niyamaḥ prathame kalpe yāvān sa tu vidhīyatām
BhP dīrgham āyur bataitasya sattvam indriyam eva ca
BhP āśāsitaṃ yat tad brūte sādhaye yogamāyayā
BhP ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
BhP astrasya tava vīryasya mṛtyor asmākam eva ca
BhP yathā bhaved vacaḥ satyaṃ tathā rāma vidhīyatām
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP ātmā vai putra utpanna iti vedānuśāsanam
BhP tasmād asya bhaved vaktā āyurindriyasattvavān
BhP kiṃ vaḥ kāmo muniśreṣṭhā brūtāhaṃ karavāṇy atha
BhP ajānatas tv apacitiṃ yathā me cintyatāṃ budhāḥ
BhP ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
BhP ilvalasya suto ghoro balvalo nāma dānavaḥ
BhP sa dūṣayati naḥ satram etya parvaṇi parvaṇi
BhP taṃ pāpaṃ jahi dāśārha tan naḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ param
BhP pūyaśoṇitavinmūtra surāmāṃsābhivarṣiṇam
BhP tataś ca bhārataṃ varṣaṃ parītya susamāhitaḥ
BhP caritvā dvādaśamāsāṃs tīrthasnāyī viśudhyasi
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP tataḥ parvaṇy upāvṛtte pracaṇḍaḥ pāṃśuvarṣaṇaḥ
BhP bhīmo vāyur abhūd rājan pūyagandhas tu sarvaśaḥ
BhP tato 'medhyamayaṃ varṣaṃ balvalena vinirmitam
BhP abhavad yajñaśālāyāṃ so 'nvadṛśyata śūladhṛk
BhP taṃ vilokya bṛhatkāyaṃ bhinnāñjanacayopamam
BhP taptatāmraśikhāśmaśruṃ daṃṣṭrograbhrukuṭīmukham
BhP sasmāra mūṣalaṃ rāmaḥ parasainyavidāraṇam
BhP halaṃ ca daityadamanaṃ te tūrṇam upatasthatuḥ
BhP tam ākṛṣya halāgreṇa balvalaṃ gaganecaram
BhP mūṣalenāhanat kruddho mūrdhni brahmadruhaṃ balaḥ
BhP so 'patad bhuvi nirbhinna lalāṭo 'sṛk samutsṛjan
BhP muñcann ārtasvaraṃ śailo yathā vajrahato 'ruṇaḥ
BhP saṃstutya munayo rāmaṃ prayujyāvitathāśiṣaḥ
BhP abhyaṣiñcan mahābhāgā vṛtraghnaṃ vibudhā yathā
BhP vaijayantīṃ dadur mālāṃ śrīdhāmāmlānapaṅkajāṃ
BhP rāmāya vāsasī divye divyāny ābharaṇāni ca
BhP atha tair abhyanujñātaḥ kauśikīm etya brāhmaṇaiḥ
BhP snātvā sarovaram agād yataḥ sarayūr āsravat
BhP anusrotena sarayūṃ prayāgam upagamya saḥ
BhP snātvā santarpya devādīn jagāma pulahāśramam
BhP gomatīṃ gaṇḍakīṃ snātvā vipāśāṃ śoṇa āplutaḥ
BhP gayāṃ gatvā pitṝn iṣṭvā gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame
BhP upaspṛśya mahendrādrau rāmaṃ dṛṣṭvābhivādya ca
BhP saptagodāvarīṃ veṇāṃ pampāṃ bhīmarathīṃ tataḥ
BhP skandaṃ dṛṣṭvā yayau rāmaḥ śrīśailaṃ giriśālayam
BhP draviḍeṣu mahāpuṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvādriṃ veṅkaṭaṃ prabhuḥ
BhP kāmakoṣṇīṃ purīṃ kāñcīṃ kāverīṃ ca saridvarām
BhP śrīrangākhyaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ yatra sannihito hariḥ
BhP ṛṣabhādriṃ hareḥ kṣetraṃ dakṣiṇāṃ mathurāṃ tathā
BhP sāmudraṃ setum agamat mahāpātakanāśanam
BhP tatrāyutam adād dhenūr brāhmaṇebhyo halāyudhaḥ
BhP kṛtamālāṃ tāmraparṇīṃ malayaṃ ca kulācalam
BhP tatrāgastyaṃ samāsīnaṃ namaskṛtyābhivādya ca
BhP yojitas tena cāśīrbhir anujñāto gato 'rṇavam
BhP dakṣiṇaṃ tatra kanyākhyāṃ durgāṃ devīṃ dadarśa saḥ
BhP tataḥ phālgunam āsādya pañcāpsarasam uttamam
BhP viṣṇuḥ sannihito yatra snātvāsparśad gavāyutam
BhP tato 'bhivrajya bhagavān keralāṃs tu trigartakān
BhP gokarṇākhyaṃ śivakṣetraṃ sānnidhyaṃ yatra dhūrjaṭeḥ
BhP āryāṃ dvaipāyanīṃ dṛṣṭvā śūrpārakam agād balaḥ
BhP tāpīṃ payoṣṇīṃ nirvindhyām upaspṛśyātha daṇḍakam
BhP praviśya revām agamad yatra māhiṣmatī purī
BhP manutīrtham upaspṛśya prabhāsaṃ punar āgamat
BhP śrutvā dvijaiḥ kathyamānaṃ kurupāṇḍavasaṃyuge
BhP sarvarājanyanidhanaṃ bhāraṃ mene hṛtaṃ bhuvaḥ
BhP sa bhīmaduryodhanayor gadābhyāṃ yudhyator mṛdhe
BhP vārayiṣyan vinaśanaṃ jagāma yadunandanaḥ
BhP yudhiṣṭhiras tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā yamau kṛṣṇārjunāv api
BhP abhivādyābhavaṃs tuṣṇīṃ kiṃ vivakṣur ihāgataḥ
BhP gadāpāṇī ubhau dṛṣṭvā saṃrabdhau vijayaiṣiṇau
BhP maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi carantāv idam abravīt
BhP yuvāṃ tulyabalau vīrau he rājan he vṛkodara
BhP ekaṃ prāṇādhikaṃ manye utaikaṃ śikṣayādhikam
BhP tasmād ekatarasyeha yuvayoḥ samavīryayoḥ
BhP na lakṣyate jayo 'nyo vā viramatv aphalo raṇaḥ
BhP na tadvākyaṃ jagṛhatur baddhavairau nṛpārthavat
BhP anusmarantāv anyonyaṃ duruktaṃ duṣkṛtāni ca
BhP diṣṭaṃ tad anumanvāno rāmo dvāravatīṃ yayau
BhP ugrasenādibhiḥ prītair jñātibhiḥ samupāgataḥ
BhP taṃ punar naimiṣaṃ prāptam ṛṣayo 'yājayan mudā
BhP kratvaṅgaṃ kratubhiḥ sarvair nivṛttākhilavigraham
BhP tebhyo viśuddhaṃ vijñānaṃ bhagavān vyatarad vibhuḥ
BhP yenaivātmany ado viśvam ātmānaṃ viśvagaṃ viduḥ
BhP svapatyāvabhṛthasnāto jñātibandhusuhṛdvṛtaḥ
BhP reje svajyotsnayevenduḥ suvāsāḥ suṣṭhv alaṅkṛtaḥ
BhP īdṛgvidhāny asaṅkhyāni balasya balaśālinaḥ
BhP anantasyāprameyasya māyāmartyasya santi hi
BhP yo 'nusmareta rāmasya karmāṇy adbhutakarmaṇaḥ
BhP sāyaṃ prātar anantasya viṣṇoḥ sa dayito bhavet
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP bhagavan yāni cānyāni mukundasya mahātmanaḥ
BhP vīryāṇy anantavīryasya śrotum icchāmi he prabho
BhP ko nu śrutvāsakṛd brahmann uttamaḥślokasatkathāḥ
BhP virameta viśeṣajño viṣaṇṇaḥ kāmamārgaṇaiḥ
BhP sā vāg yayā tasya guṇān gṛṇīte karau ca tatkarmakarau manaś ca
BhP smared vasantaṃ sthirajaṅgameṣu śṛṇoti tatpuṇyakathāḥ sa karṇaḥ
BhP śiras tu tasyobhayaliṅgam ānamet tad eva yat paśyati tad dhi cakṣuḥ
BhP aṅgāni viṣṇor atha tajjanānāṃ pādodakaṃ yāni bhajanti nityam
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP viṣṇurātena sampṛṣṭo bhagavān bādarāyaṇiḥ
BhP vāsudeve bhagavati nimagnahṛdayo 'bravīt
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP kṛṣṇasyāsīt sakhā kaścid brāhmaṇo brahmavittamaḥ
BhP virakta indriyārtheṣu praśāntātmā jitendriyaḥ
BhP yadṛcchayopapannena vartamāno gṛhāśramī
BhP tasya bhāryā kucailasya kṣutkṣāmā ca tathāvidhā
BhP pativratā patiṃ prāha mlāyatā vadanena sā
BhP daridraṃ sīdamānā vai vepamānābhigamya ca
BhP nanu brahman bhagavataḥ sakhā sākṣāc chriyaḥ patiḥ
BhP brahmaṇyaś ca śaraṇyaś ca bhagavān sātvatarṣabhaḥ
BhP tam upaihi mahābhāga sādhūnāṃ ca parāyaṇam
BhP dāsyati draviṇaṃ bhūri sīdate te kuṭumbine
BhP āste 'dhunā dvāravatyāṃ bhojavṛṣṇyandhakeśvaraḥ
BhP smarataḥ pādakamalam ātmānam api yacchati
BhP kiṃ nv arthakāmān bhajato nātyabhīṣṭān jagadguruḥ
BhP sa evaṃ bhāryayā vipro bahuśaḥ prārthito muhuḥ
BhP ayaṃ hi paramo lābha uttamaḥślokadarśanam
BhP iti sañcintya manasā gamanāya matiṃ dadhe
BhP apy asty upāyanaṃ kiñcid gṛhe kalyāṇi dīyatām
BhP yācitvā caturo muṣṭīn viprān pṛthukataṇḍulān
BhP cailakhaṇḍena tān baddhvā bhartre prādād upāyanam
BhP sa tān ādāya viprāgryaḥ prayayau dvārakāṃ kila
BhP kṛṣṇasandarśanaṃ mahyaṃ kathaṃ syād iti cintayan
BhP trīṇi gulmāny atīyāya tisraḥ kakṣāś ca sadvijaḥ
BhP vipro 'gamyāndhakavṛṣṇīnāṃ gṛheṣv acyutadharmiṇām
BhP gṛhaṃ dvyaṣṭasahasrāṇāṃ mahiṣīṇāṃ harer dvijaḥ
BhP viveśaikatamaṃ śrīmad brahmānandaṃ gato yathā
BhP taṃ vilokyācyuto dūrāt priyāparyaṅkam āsthitaḥ
BhP sahasotthāya cābhyetya dorbhyāṃ paryagrahīn mudā
BhP sakhyuḥ priyasya viprarṣer aṅgasaṅgātinirvṛtaḥ
BhP prīto vyamuñcad abbindūn netrābhyāṃ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
BhP athopaveśya paryaṅke svayam sakhyuḥ samarhaṇam
BhP upahṛtyāvanijyāsya pādau pādāvanejanīḥ
BhP agrahīc chirasā rājan bhagavāṃl lokapāvanaḥ
BhP vyalimpad divyagandhena candanāgurukuṅkamaiḥ
BhP dhūpaiḥ surabhibhir mitraṃ pradīpāvalibhir mudā
BhP arcitvāvedya tāmbūlaṃ gāṃ ca svāgatam abravīt
BhP kucailaṃ malinaṃ kṣāmaṃ dvijaṃ dhamanisantatam
BhP devī paryacarat sākṣāc cāmaravyajanena vai
BhP antaḥpurajano dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇenāmalakīrtinā
BhP vismito 'bhūd atiprītyā avadhūtaṃ sabhājitam
BhP kim anena kṛtaṃ puṇyam avadhūtena bhikṣuṇā
BhP śriyā hīnena loke 'smin garhitenādhamena ca
BhP yo 'sau trilokaguruṇā śrīnivāsena sambhṛtaḥ
BhP paryaṅkasthāṃ śriyaṃ hitvā pariṣvakto 'grajo yathā
BhP kathayāṃ cakratur gāthāḥ pūrvā gurukule satoḥ
BhP ātmanor lalitā rājan karau gṛhya parasparam
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP api brahman gurukulād bhavatā labdhadakṣiṇāt
BhP samāvṛttena dharmajña bhāryoḍhā sadṛśī na vā
BhP prāyo gṛheṣu te cittam akāmavihitaṃ tathā
BhP naivātiprīyase vidvan dhaneṣu viditaṃ hi me
BhP kecit kurvanti karmāṇi kāmair ahatacetasaḥ
BhP tyajantaḥ prakṛtīr daivīr yathāhaṃ lokasaṅgraham
BhP kaccid gurukule vāsaṃ brahman smarasi nau yataḥ
BhP dvijo vijñāya vijñeyaṃ tamasaḥ pāram aśnute
BhP sa vai satkarmaṇāṃ sākṣād dvijāter iha sambhavaḥ
BhP ādyo 'ṅga yatrāśramiṇāṃ yathāhaṃ jñānado guruḥ
BhP nanv arthakovidā brahman varṇāśramavatām iha
BhP ye mayā guruṇā vācā taranty añjo bhavārṇavam
BhP nāham ijyāprajātibhyāṃ tapasopaśamena vā
BhP tuṣyeyaṃ sarvabhūtātmā guruśuśrūṣayā yathā
BhP api naḥ smaryate brahman vṛttaṃ nivasatāṃ gurau
BhP gurudāraiś coditānām indhanānayane kvacit
BhP praviṣṭānāṃ mahāraṇyam apartau sumahad dvija
BhP vātavarṣam abhūt tīvraṃ niṣṭhurāḥ stanayitnavaḥ
BhP sūryaś cāstaṃ gatas tāvat tamasā cāvṛtā diśaḥ
BhP nimnaṃ kūlaṃ jalamayaṃ na prājñāyata kiñcana
BhP vayaṃ bhṛśam tatra mahānilāmbubhir nihanyamānā mahur ambusamplave
BhP diśo 'vidanto 'tha parasparaṃ vane gṛhītahastāḥ paribabhrimāturāḥ
BhP etad viditvā udite ravau sāndīpanir guruḥ
BhP anveṣamāṇo naḥ śiṣyān ācāryo 'paśyad āturān
BhP aho he putrakā yūyam asmadarthe 'tiduḥkhitāḥ
BhP ātmā vai prāṇinām preṣṭhas tam anādṛtya matparāḥ
BhP etad eva hi sacchiṣyaiḥ kartavyaṃ guruniṣkṛtam
BhP yad vai viśuddhabhāvena sarvārthātmārpaṇaṃ gurau
BhP tuṣṭo 'haṃ bho dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ satyāḥ santu manorathāḥ
BhP chandāṃsy ayātayāmāni bhavantv iha paratra ca
BhP itthaṃvidhāny anekāni vasatāṃ guruveśmani
BhP guror anugraheṇaiva pumān pūrṇaḥ praśāntaye
BhP śrībrāhmaṇa uvāca
BhP kim asmābhir anirvṛttaṃ devadeva jagadguro
BhP bhavatā satyakāmena yeṣāṃ vāso guror abhūt
BhP yasya cchandomayaṃ brahma deha āvapanaṃ vibho
BhP śreyasāṃ tasya guruṣu vāso 'tyantaviḍambanam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa itthaṃ dvijamukhyena saha saṅkathayan hariḥ
BhP sarvabhūtamano'bhijñaḥ smayamāna uvāca tam
BhP brahmaṇyo brāhmaṇaṃ kṛṣṇo bhagavān prahasan priyam
BhP premṇā nirīkṣaṇenaiva prekṣan khalu satāṃ gatiḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP kim upāyanam ānītaṃ brahman me bhavatā gṛhāt
BhP aṇv apy upāhṛtaṃ bhaktaiḥ premṇā bhury eva me bhavet
BhP bhūry apy abhaktopahṛtaṃ na me toṣāya kalpate
BhP patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati
BhP tad ahaṃ bhaktyupahṛtam aśnāmi prayatātmanaḥ
BhP ity ukto 'pi dviyas tasmai vrīḍitaḥ pataye śriyaḥ
BhP pṛthukaprasṛtiṃ rājan na prāyacchad avāṅmukhaḥ
BhP sarvabhūtātmadṛk sākṣāt tasyāgamanakāraṇam
BhP vijṅāyācintayan nāyaṃ śrīkāmo mābhajat purā
BhP patnyāḥ pativratāyās tu sakhā priyacikīrṣayā
BhP prāpto mām asya dāsyāmi sampado 'martyadurlabhāḥ
BhP itthaṃ vicintya vasanāc cīrabaddhān dvijanmanaḥ
BhP svayaṃ jahāra kim idam iti pṛthukataṇḍulān
BhP nanv etad upanītaṃ me paramaprīṇanaṃ sakhe
BhP tarpayanty aṅga māṃ viśvam ete pṛthukataṇḍulāḥ
BhP iti muṣṭiṃ sakṛj jagdhvā dvitīyāṃ jagdhum ādade
BhP tāvac chrīr jagṛhe hastaṃ tatparā parameṣṭhinaḥ
BhP etāvatālaṃ viśvātman sarvasampatsamṛddhaye
BhP asmin loke 'tha vāmuṣmin puṃsas tvattoṣakāraṇam
BhP brāhmaṇas tāṃ tu rajanīm uṣitvācyutamandire
BhP bhuktvā pītvā sukhaṃ mene ātmānaṃ svargataṃ yathā
BhP śvobhūte viśvabhāvena svasukhenābhivanditaḥ
BhP jagāma svālayaṃ tāta pathy anavrajya nanditaḥ
BhP sa cālabdhvā dhanaṃ kṛṣṇān na tu yācitavān svayam
BhP svagṛhān vrīḍito 'gacchan mahaddarśananirvṛtaḥ
BhP aho brahmaṇyadevasya dṛṣṭā brahmaṇyatā mayā
BhP yad daridratamo lakṣmīm āśliṣṭo bibhratorasi
BhP kvāhaṃ daridraḥ pāpīyān kva kṛṣṇaḥ śrīniketanaḥ
BhP brahmabandhur iti smāhaṃ bāhubhyāṃ parirambhitaḥ
BhP nivāsitaḥ priyājuṣṭe paryaṅke bhrātaro yathā
BhP mahiṣyā vījitaḥ śrānto bālavyajanahastayā
BhP śuśrūṣayā paramayā pādasaṃvāhanādibhiḥ
BhP pūjito devadevena vipradevena devavat
BhP svargāpavargayoḥ puṃsāṃ rasāyāṃ bhuvi sampadām
BhP sarvāsām api siddhīnāṃ mūlaṃ taccaraṇārcanam
BhP adhano 'yaṃ dhanaṃ prāpya mādyann uccair na māṃ smaret
BhP iti kāruṇiko nūnaṃ dhanaṃ me 'bhūri nādadāt
BhP iti tac cintayann antaḥ prāpto niyagṛhāntikam
BhP sūryānalendusaṅkāśair vimānaiḥ sarvato vṛtam
BhP vicitropavanodyānaiḥ kūjaddvijakulākulaiḥ
BhP protphullakamudāmbhoja kahlārotpalavāribhiḥ
BhP juṣṭaṃ svalaṅkṛtaiḥ pumbhiḥ strībhiś ca hariṇākṣibhiḥ
BhP kim idaṃ kasya vā sthānaṃ kathaṃ tad idam ity abhūt
BhP evaṃ mīmāṃsamānaṃ taṃ narā nāryo 'maraprabhāḥ
BhP pratyagṛhṇan mahābhāgaṃ gītavādyena bhūyasā
BhP patim āgatam ākarṇya patny uddharṣātisambhramā
BhP niścakrāma gṛhāt tūrṇaṃ rūpiṇī śrīr ivālayāt
BhP pativratā patiṃ dṛṣṭvā premotkaṇṭhāśrulocanā
BhP mīlitākṣy anamad buddhyā manasā pariṣasvaje
BhP patnīṃ vīkṣya visphurantīṃ devīṃ vaimānikīm iva
BhP dāsīnāṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīnāṃ madhye bhāntīṃ sa vismitaḥ
BhP prītaḥ svayaṃ tayā yuktaḥ praviṣṭo nijamandiram
BhP maṇistambhaśatopetaṃ mahendrabhavanaṃ yathā
BhP payaḥphenanibhāḥ śayyā dāntā rukmaparicchadāḥ
BhP paryaṅkā hemadaṇḍāni cāmaravyajanāni ca
BhP āsanāni ca haimāni mṛdūpastaraṇāni ca
BhP muktādāmavilambīni vitānāni dyumanti ca
BhP svacchasphaṭikakuḍyeṣu mahāmārakateṣu ca
BhP ratnadīpān bhrājamānān lalanā ratnasaṃyutāḥ
BhP vilokya brāhmaṇas tatra samṛddhīḥ sarvasampadām
BhP tarkayām āsa nirvyagraḥ svasamṛddhim ahaitukīm
BhP nūnaṃ bataitan mama durbhagasya śaśvad daridrasya samṛddhihetuḥ
BhP mahāvibhūter avalokato 'nyo naivopapadyeta yadūttamasya
BhP nanv abruvāṇo diśate samakṣaṃ yāciṣṇave bhūry api bhūribhojaḥ
BhP parjanyavat tat svayam īkṣamāṇo dāśārhakāṇām ṛṣabhaḥ sakhā me
BhP kiñcit karoty urv api yat svadattaṃ
BhP suhṛtkṛtaṃ phalgv api bhūrikārī
BhP mayopaṇītaṃ pṛthukaikamuṣṭiṃ
BhP pratyagrahīt prītiyuto mahātmā
BhP tasyaiva me sauhṛdasakhyamaitrī dāsyaṃ punar janmani janmani syāt
BhP mahānubhāvena guṇālayena viṣajjatas tatpuruṣaprasaṅgaḥ
BhP bhaktāya citrā bhagavān hi sampado rājyaṃ vibhūtīr na samarthayaty ajaḥ
BhP adīrghabodhāya vicakṣaṇaḥ svayaṃ paśyan nipātaṃ dhanināṃ madodbhavam
BhP itthaṃ vyavasito buddhyā bhakto 'tīva janārdane
BhP viṣayān jāyayā tyakṣyan bubhuje nātilampaṭaḥ
BhP tasya vai devadevasya harer yajñapateḥ prabhoḥ
BhP brāhmaṇāḥ prabhavo daivaṃ na tebhyo vidyate param
BhP evaṃ sa vipro bhagavatsuhṛt tadā dṛṣṭvā svabhṛtyair ajitaṃ parājitam
BhP taddhyānavegodgrathitātmabandhanas taddhāma lebhe 'cirataḥ satāṃ gatim
BhP etad brahmaṇyadevasya śrutvā brahmaṇyatāṃ naraḥ
BhP labdhabhāvo bhagavati karmabandhād vimucyate
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP athaikadā dvāravatyāṃ vasato rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP sūryoparāgaḥ sumahān āsīt kalpakṣaye yathā
BhP taṃ jñātvā manujā rājan purastād eva sarvataḥ
BhP samantapañcakaṃ kṣetraṃ yayuḥ śreyovidhitsayā
BhP niḥkṣatriyāṃ mahīṃ kurvan rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
BhP nṛpāṇāṃ rudhiraugheṇa yatra cakre mahāhradān
BhP īje ca bhagavān rāmo yatrāspṛṣṭo 'pi karmaṇā
BhP lokaṃ saṅgrāhayann īśo yathānyo 'ghāpanuttaye
BhP mahatyāṃ tīrthayātrāyāṃ tatrāgan bhāratīḥ prajāḥ
BhP vṛṣṇayaś ca tathākrūra vasudevāhukādayaḥ
BhP yayur bhārata tat kṣetraṃ svam aghaṃ kṣapayiṣṇavaḥ
BhP gadapradyumnasāmbādyāḥ sucandraśukasāraṇaiḥ
BhP āste 'niruddho rakṣāyāṃ kṛtavarmā ca yūthapaḥ
BhP te rathair devadhiṣṇyābhair hayaiś ca taralaplavaiḥ
BhP gajair nadadbhir abhrābhair nṛbhir vidyādharadyubhiḥ
BhP vyarocanta mahātejāḥ pathi kāñcanamālinaḥ
BhP divyasragvastrasannāhāḥ kalatraiḥ khecarā iva
BhP tatra snātvā mahābhāgā upoṣya susamāhitāḥ
BhP brāhmaṇebhyo dadur dhenūr vāsaḥsragrukmamālinīḥ
BhP rāmahradeṣu vidhivat punar āplutya vṛṣṇayaḥ
BhP dadaḥ svannaṃ dvijāgryebhyaḥ kṛṣṇe no bhaktir astv iti
BhP svayaṃ ca tadanujñātā vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇadevatāḥ
BhP bhuktvopaviviśuḥ kāmaṃ snigdhacchāyāṅghripāṅghriṣu
BhP tatrāgatāṃs te dadṛśuḥ suhṛtsambandhino nṛpān
BhP matsyośīnarakauśalya vidarbhakurusṛñjayān
BhP kāmbojakaikayān madrān kuntīn ānartakeralān
BhP anyāṃś caivātmapakṣīyān parāṃś ca śataśo nṛpa
BhP nandādīn suhṛdo gopān gopīś cotkaṇṭhitāś ciram
BhP anyonyasandarśanaharṣaraṃhasā protphullahṛdvaktrasaroruhaśriyaḥ
BhP āśliṣya gāḍhaṃ nayanaiḥ sravajjalā hṛṣyattvaco ruddhagiro yayur mudam
BhP striyaś ca saṃvīkṣya mitho 'tisauhṛda
BhP smitāmalāpāṅgadṛśo 'bhirebhire
BhP stanaiḥ stanān kuṅkumapaṅkarūṣitān
BhP nihatya dorbhiḥ praṇayāśrulocanāḥ
BhP tato 'bhivādya te vṛddhān yaviṣṭhair abhivāditāḥ
BhP svāgataṃ kuśalaṃ pṛṣṭvā cakruḥ kṛṣṇakathā mithaḥ
BhP pṛthā bhrātṝn svasṝr vīkṣya tatputrān pitarāv api
BhP bhrātṛpatnīr mukundaṃ ca jahau saṅkathayā śucaḥ
BhP kunty uvāca
BhP ārya bhrātar ahaṃ manye ātmānam akṛtāśiṣam
BhP yad vā āpatsu madvārtāṃ nānusmaratha sattamāḥ
BhP suhṛdo jñātayaḥ putrā bhrātaraḥ pitarāv api
BhP nānusmaranti svajanaṃ yasya daivam adakṣiṇam
BhP śrīvasudeva uvāca
BhP amba māsmān asūyethā daivakrīḍanakān narān
BhP īśasya hi vaśe lokaḥ kurute kāryate 'tha vā
BhP kaṃsapratāpitāḥ sarve vayaṃ yātā diśaṃ diśam
BhP etarhy eva punaḥ sthānaṃ daivenāsāditāḥ svasaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP vasudevograsenādyair yadubhis te 'rcitā nṛpāḥ
BhP āsann acyutasandarśa paramānandanirvṛtāḥ
BhP bhīṣmo droṇo 'mbikāputro gāndhārī sasutā tathā
BhP sadārāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kuntī sañjayo viduraḥ kṛpaḥ
BhP kuntībhojo virāṭaś ca bhīṣmako nagnajin mahān
BhP purujid drupadaḥ śalyo dhṛṣṭaketuḥ sa kāśirāṭ
BhP damaghoṣo viśālākṣo maithilo madrakekayau
BhP yudhāmanyuḥ suśarmā ca sasutā bāhlikādayaḥ
BhP rājāno ye ca rājendra yudhiṣṭhiram anuvratāḥ
BhP śrīniketaṃ vapuḥ śaureḥ sastrīkaṃ vīkṣya vismitāḥ
BhP atha te rāmakṛṣṇābhyāṃ samyak prāptasamarhaṇāḥ
BhP praśaśaṃsur mudā yuktā vṛṣṇīn kṛṣṇaparigrahān
BhP aho bhojapate yūyaṃ janmabhājo nṛṇām iha
BhP yat paśyathāsakṛt kṛṣṇaṃ durdarśam api yoginām
BhP yadviśrutiḥ śrutinutedam alaṃ punāti
BhP pādāvanejanapayaś ca vacaś ca śāstram
BhP bhūḥ kālabharjitabhagāpi yadaṅghripadma
BhP sparśotthaśaktir abhivarṣati no 'khilārthān
BhP taddarśanasparśanānupathaprajalpa
BhP śayyāsanāśanasayaunasapiṇḍabandhaḥ
BhP yeṣāṃ gṛhe nirayavartmani vartatāṃ vaḥ
BhP svargāpavargaviramaḥ svayam āsa viṣṇuḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP nandas tatra yadūn prāptān jñātvā kṛṣṇapurogamān
BhP tatrāgamad vṛto gopair anaḥsthārthair didṛkṣayā
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvā vṛṣṇayo hṛṣṭās tanvaḥ prāṇam ivotthitāḥ
BhP pariṣasvajire gāḍhaṃ ciradarśanakātarāḥ
BhP vasudevaḥ pariṣvajya samprītaḥ premavihvalaḥ
BhP smaran kaṃsakṛtān kleśān putranyāsaṃ ca gokule
BhP kṛṣṇarāmau pariṣvajya pitarāv abhivādya ca
BhP na kiñcanocatuḥ premṇā sāśrukaṇṭhau kurūdvaha
BhP tāv ātmāsanam āropya bāhubhyāṃ parirabhya ca
BhP yaśodā ca mahābhāgā sutau vijahatuḥ śucaḥ
BhP rohiṇī devakī cātha pariṣvajya vrajeśvarīm
BhP smarantyau tatkṛtāṃ maitrīṃ bāṣpakaṇṭhyau samūcatuḥ
BhP kā vismareta vāṃ maitrīm anivṛttāṃ vrajeśvari
BhP avāpyāpy aindram aiśvaryaṃ yasyā neha pratikriyā
BhP etāv adṛṣṭapitarau yuvayoḥ sma pitroḥ
BhP samprīṇanābhyudayapoṣaṇapālanāni
BhP prāpyoṣatur bhavati pakṣma ha yadvad akṣṇor
BhP nyastāv akutra ca bhayau na satāṃ paraḥ svaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP gopyaś ca kṛṣṇam upalabhya cirād abhīṣṭaṃ
BhP yatprekṣaṇe dṛśiṣu pakṣmakṛtaṃ śapanti
BhP dṛgbhir hṛdīkṛtam alaṃ parirabhya sarvās
BhP tadbhāvam āpur api nityayujāṃ durāpam
BhP bhagavāṃs tās tathābhūtā vivikta upasaṅgataḥ
BhP āśliṣyānāmayaṃ pṛṣṭvā prahasann idam abravīt
BhP api smaratha naḥ sakhyaḥ svānām arthacikīrṣayā
BhP gatāṃś cirāyitāñ chatru pakṣakṣapaṇacetasaḥ
BhP apy avadhyāyathāsmān svid akṛtajñāviśaṅkayā
BhP nūnaṃ bhūtāni bhagavān yunakti viyunakti ca
BhP vāyur yathā ghanānīkaṃ tṛṇaṃ tūlaṃ rajāṃsi ca
BhP saṃyojyākṣipate bhūyas tathā bhūtāni bhūtakṛt
BhP mayi bhaktir hi bhūtānām amṛtatvāya kalpate
BhP diṣṭyā yad āsīn matsneho bhavatīnāṃ madāpanaḥ
BhP ahaṃ hi sarvabhūtānām ādir anto 'ntaraṃ bahiḥ
BhP bhautikānāṃ yathā khaṃ vār bhūr vāyur jyotir aṅganāḥ
BhP evaṃ hy etāni bhūtāni bhūteṣv ātmātmanā tataḥ
BhP ubhayaṃ mayy atha pare paśyatābhātam akṣare
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP adhyātmaśikṣayā gopya evaṃ kṛṣṇena śikṣitāḥ
BhP tadanusmaraṇadhvasta jīvakośās tam adhyagan
BhP āhuś ca te nalinanābha padāravindaṃ
BhP yogeśvarair hṛdi vicintyam agādhabodhaiḥ
BhP saṃsārakūpapatitottaraṇāvalambaṃ
BhP gehaṃ juṣām api manasy udiyāt sadā naḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP tathānugṛhya bhagavān gopīnāṃ sa gurur gatiḥ
BhP yudhiṣṭhiram athāpṛcchat sarvāṃś ca suhṛdo 'vyayam
BhP ta evaṃ lokanāthena paripṛṣṭāḥ susatkṛtāḥ
BhP pratyūcur hṛṣṭamanasas tatpādekṣāhatāṃhasaḥ
BhP kuto 'śivaṃ tvaccaraṇāmbujāsavaṃ mahanmanasto mukhaniḥsṛtaṃ kvacit
BhP pibanti ye karṇapuṭair alaṃ prabho dehaṃbhṛtāṃ dehakṛdasmṛticchidam
BhP hi tvātma dhāmavidhutātmakṛtatryavasthām
BhP ānandasamplavam akhaṇḍam akuṇṭhabodham
BhP kālopasṛṣṭanigamāvana āttayoga
BhP māyākṛtiṃ paramahaṃsagatiṃ natāḥ sma
BhP śrīṛṣir uvāca
BhP ity uttamaḥślokaśikhāmaṇiṃ janeṣv
BhP abhiṣṭuvatsv andhakakauravastriyaḥ
BhP sametya govindakathā mitho 'gṛnaṃs
BhP trilokagītāḥ śṛṇu varṇayāmi te
BhP śrīdraupady uvāca
BhP he vaidarbhy acyuto bhadre he jāmbavati kauśale
BhP he satyabhāme kālindi śaibye rohiṇi lakṣmaṇe
BhP he kṛṣṇapatnya etan no brūte vo bhagavān svayam
BhP upayeme yathā lokam anukurvan svamāyayā
BhP śrīrukmiṇy uvāca
BhP caidyāya mārpayitum udyatakārmukeṣu
BhP rājasv ajeyabhaṭaśekharitāṅghrireṇuḥ
BhP ninye mṛgendra iva bhāgam ajāviyūthāt
BhP tacchrīniketacaraṇo 'stu mamārcanāya
BhP śrīsatyabhāmovāca
BhP yo me sanābhivadhataptahṛdā tatena
BhP liptābhiśāpam apamārṣṭum upājahāra
BhP jitvarkṣarājam atha ratnam adāt sa tena
BhP bhītaḥ pitādiśata māṃ prabhave 'pi dattām
BhP śrījāmbavaty uvāca
BhP prājñāya dehakṛd amuṃ nijanāthadaivaṃ
BhP sītāpatiṃ trinavahāny amunābhyayudhyat
BhP jñātvā parīkṣita upāharad arhaṇaṃ māṃ
BhP pādau pragṛhya maṇināham amuṣya dāsī
BhP śrīkālindy uvāca
BhP tapaś carantīm ājñāya svapādasparśanāśayā
BhP sakhyopetyāgrahīt pāṇiṃ yo 'haṃ tadgṛhamārjanī
BhP śrīmitravindovāca
BhP yo māṃ svayaṃvara upetya vijitya bhūpān
BhP ninye śvayūthagaṃ ivātmabaliṃ dvipāriḥ
BhP bhrātṝṃś ca me 'pakurutaḥ svapuraṃ śriyaukas
BhP tasyāstu me 'nubhavam aṅghryavanejanatvam
BhP śrīsatyovāca
BhP saptokṣaṇo 'tibalavīryasutīkṣṇaśṛṅgān
BhP pitrā kṛtān kṣitipavīryaparīkṣaṇāya
BhP tān vīradurmadahanas tarasā nigṛhya
BhP krīḍan babandha ha yathā śiśavo 'jatokān
BhP ya itthaṃ vīryaśulkāṃ māṃ
BhP dāsībhiś caturangiṇīm
BhP pathi nirjitya rājanyān
BhP ninye taddāsyam astu me
BhP śrībhadrovāca pitā me mātuleyāya svayam āhūya dattavān
BhP kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇāya taccittām akṣauhiṇyā sakhījanaiḥ
BhP asya me pādasaṃsparśo bhavej janmani janmani
BhP karmabhir bhrāmyamāṇāyā yena tac chreya ātmanaḥ
BhP śrīlakṣmaṇovāca
BhP mamāpi rājñy acyutajanmakarma śrutvā muhur nāradagītam āsa ha
BhP cittaṃ mukunde kila padmahastayā vṛtaḥ susammṛśya vihāya lokapān
BhP jñātvā mama mataṃ sādhvi pitā duhitṛvatsalaḥ
BhP bṛhatsena iti khyātas tatropāyam acīkarat
BhP yathā svayaṃvare rājñi matsyaḥ pārthepsayā kṛtaḥ
BhP ayaṃ tu bahir ācchanno dṛśyate sa jale param
BhP śrutvaitat sarvato bhūpā āyayur matpituḥ puram
BhP sarvāstraśastratattvajñāḥ sopādhyāyāḥ sahasraśaḥ
BhP pitrā sampūjitāḥ sarve yathāvīryaṃ yathāvayaḥ
BhP ādaduḥ saśaraṃ cāpaṃ veddhuṃ parṣadi maddhiyaḥ
BhP ādāya vyasṛjan kecit sajyaṃ kartum anīśvarāḥ
BhP ākoṣṭhaṃ jyāṃ samutkṛṣya petur eke 'munāhatāḥ
BhP sajyaṃ kṛtvāpare vīrā māgadhāmbaṣṭhacedipāḥ
BhP bhīmo duryodhanaḥ karṇo nāvidaṃs tadavasthitim
BhP matsyābhāsaṃ jale vīkṣya jñātvā ca tadavasthitim
BhP pārtho yatto 'sṛjad bāṇaṃ nācchinat paspṛśe param
BhP rājanyeṣu nivṛtteṣu bhagnamāneṣu māniṣu
BhP bhagavān dhanur ādāya sajyaṃ kṛtvātha līlayā
BhP tasmin sandhāya viśikhaṃ matsyaṃ vīkṣya sakṛj jale
BhP chittveṣuṇāpātayat taṃ sūrye cābhijiti sthite
BhP divi dundubhayo nedur jayaśabdayutā bhuvi
BhP devāś ca kusumāsārān mumucur harṣavihvalāḥ
BhP tad raṅgam āviśam ahaṃ kalanūpurābhyāṃ
BhP padbhyāṃ pragṛhya kanakoijvalaratnamālām
BhP nūtne nivīya paridhāya ca kauśikāgrye
BhP savrīḍahāsavadanā kavarīdhṛtasrak
BhP unnīya vaktram urukuntalakuṇḍalatviḍ
BhP gaṇḍasthalaṃ śiśirahāsakaṭākṣamokṣaiḥ
BhP rājño nirīkṣya paritaḥ śanakair murārer
BhP aṃse 'nuraktahṛdayā nidadhe svamālām
BhP tāvan mṛdaṅgapaṭahāḥ śaṅkhabheryānakādayaḥ
BhP ninedur naṭanartakyo nanṛtur gāyakā jaguḥ
BhP evaṃ vṛte bhagavati mayeśe nṛpayūthapāḥ
BhP na sehire yājñaseni spardhanto hṛcchayāturāḥ
BhP māṃ tāvad ratham āropya hayaratnacatuṣṭayam
BhP śārṅgam udyamya sannaddhas tasthāv ājau caturbhujaḥ
BhP dārukaś codayām āsa kāñcanopaskaraṃ ratham
BhP miṣatāṃ bhūbhujāṃ rājñi mṛgāṇāṃ mṛgarāḍ iva
BhP te 'nvasajjanta rājanyā niṣeddhuṃ pathi kecana
BhP saṃyattā uddhṛteṣvāsā grāmasiṃhā yathā harim
BhP te śārṅgacyutabāṇaughaiḥ kṛttabāhvaṅghrikandharāḥ
BhP nipetuḥ pradhane kecid eke santyajya dudruvuḥ
BhP tataḥ purīṃ yadupatir atyalaṅkṛtāṃ
BhP ravicchadadhvajapaṭacitratoraṇām
BhP kuśasthalīṃ divi bhuvi cābhisaṃstutāṃ
BhP samāviśat taraṇir iva svaketanam
BhP pitā me pūjayām āsa suhṛtsambandhibāndhavān
BhP mahārhavāso'laṅkāraiḥ śayyāsanaparicchadaiḥ
BhP dāsībhiḥ sarvasampadbhir bhaṭebharathavājibhiḥ
BhP āyudhāni mahārhāṇi dadau pūrṇasya bhaktitaḥ
BhP ātmārāmasya tasyemā vayaṃ vai gṛhadāsikāḥ
BhP sarvasaṅganivṛttyāddhā tapasā ca babhūvima
BhP mahiṣya ūcuḥ
BhP bhaumaṃ nihatya sagaṇaṃ yudhi tena ruddhā
BhP jñātvātha naḥ kṣitijaye jitarājakanyāḥ
BhP nirmucya saṃsṛtivimokṣam anusmarantīḥ
BhP pādāmbujaṃ pariṇināya ya āptakāmaḥ
BhP na vayaṃ sādhvi sāmrājyaṃ svārājyaṃ bhaujyam apy uta
BhP vairājyaṃ pārameṣṭhyaṃ ca ānantyaṃ vā hareḥ padam
BhP kāmayāmaha etasya śrīmatpādarajaḥ śriyaḥ
BhP kucakuṅkumagandhāḍhyaṃ mūrdhnā voḍhuṃ gadābhṛtaḥ
BhP vrajastriyo yad vāñchanti pulindyas tṛṇavīrudhaḥ
BhP gāvaś cārayato gopāḥ padasparśaṃ mahātmanaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP śrutvā pṛthā subalaputry atha yājñasenī
BhP mādhavy atha kṣitipapatnya uta svagopyaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇe 'khilātmani harau praṇayānubandhaṃ
BhP sarvā visismyur alam aśrukalākulākṣyaḥ
BhP iti sambhāṣamāṇāsu strībhiḥ strīṣu nṛbhir nṛṣu
BhP āyayur munayas tatra kṛṣṇarāmadidṛkṣayā
BhP dvaipāyano nāradaś ca cyavano devalo 'sitaḥ
BhP viśvāmitraḥ śatānando bharadvājo 'tha gautamaḥ
BhP rāmaḥ saśiṣyo bhagavān vasiṣṭho gālavo bhṛguḥ
BhP pulastyaḥ kaśyapo 'triś ca mārkaṇḍeyo bṛhaspatiḥ
BhP dvitas tritaś caikataś ca brahmaputrās tathāṅgirāḥ
BhP agastyo yājñavalkyaś ca vāmadevādayo 'pare
BhP tān dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya prāg āsīnā nṛpādayaḥ
BhP pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇarāmau ca praṇemur viśvavanditān
BhP tān ānarcur yathā sarve saharāmo 'cyuto 'rcayat
BhP svāgatāsanapādyārghya mālyadhūpānulepanaiḥ
BhP uvāca sukham āsīnān bhagavān dharmaguptanuḥ
BhP sadasas tasya mahato yatavāco 'nuśṛṇvataḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP aho vayaṃ janmabhṛto labdhaṃ kārtsnyena tatphalam
BhP devānām api duṣprāpaṃ yad yogeśvaradarśanam
BhP kiṃ svalpatapasāṃ nṝṇām arcāyāṃ devacakṣuṣām
BhP darśanasparśanapraśna prahvapādārcanādikam
BhP na hy ammayāni tīrthāni na devā mṛcchilāmayāḥ
BhP te punanty urukālena darśanād eva sādhavaḥ
BhP nāgnir na sūryo na ca candratārakā
BhP na bhūr jalaṃ khaṃ śvasano 'tha vāṅ manaḥ
BhP upāsitā bhedakṛto haranty aghaṃ
BhP vipaścito ghnanti muhūrtasevayā
BhP yasyātmabuddhiḥ kuṇape tridhātuke
BhP svadhīḥ kalatrādiṣu bhauma ijyadhīḥ
BhP yattīrthabuddhiḥ salile na karhicij
BhP janeṣv abhijñeṣu sa eva gokharaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP niśamyetthaṃ bhagavataḥ kṛṣṇasyākuṇthamedhasaḥ
BhP vaco duranvayaṃ viprās tūṣṇīm āsan bhramaddhiyaḥ
BhP ciraṃ vimṛśya munaya īśvarasyeśitavyatām
BhP janasaṅgraha ity ūcuḥ smayantas taṃ jagadgurum
BhP śrīmunaya ūcuḥ
BhP yanmāyayā tattvaviduttamā vayaṃ vimohitā viśvasṛjām adhīśvarāḥ
BhP yad īśitavyāyati gūḍha īhayā aho vicitram bhagavadviceṣṭitam
BhP anīha etad bahudhaika ātmanā sṛjaty avaty atti na badhyate yathā
BhP bhaumair hi bhūmir bahunāmarūpiṇī aho vibhūmnaś caritaṃ viḍambanam
BhP athāpi kāle svajanābhiguptaye bibharṣi sattvaṃ khalanigrahāya ca
BhP svalīlayā vedapathaṃ sanātanaṃ varṇāśramātmā puruṣaḥ paro bhavān
BhP brahma te hṛdayaṃ śuklaṃ tapaḥsvādhyāyasaṃyamaiḥ
BhP yatropalabdhaṃ sad vyaktam avyaktaṃ ca tataḥ param
BhP tasmād brahmakulaṃ brahman śāstrayones tvam ātmanaḥ
BhP sabhājayasi sad dhāma tad brahmaṇyāgraṇīr bhavān
BhP adya no janmasāphalyaṃ vidyāyās tapaso dṛśaḥ
BhP tvayā saṅgamya sadgatyā yad antaḥ śreyasāṃ paraḥ
BhP namas tasmai bhagavate kṛṣṇāyākuṇṭhamedhase
BhP svayogamāyayācchanna mahimne paramātmane
BhP na yaṃ vidanty amī bhūpā ekārāmāś ca vṛṣṇayaḥ
BhP māyājavanikācchannam ātmānaṃ kālam īśvaram
BhP yathā śayānaḥ puruṣa ātmānaṃ guṇatattvadṛk
BhP nāmamātrendriyābhātaṃ na veda rahitaṃ param
BhP evaṃ tvā nāmamātreṣu viṣayeṣv indriyehayā
BhP māyayā vibhramaccitto na veda smṛtyupaplavāt
BhP tasyādya te dadṛśimāṅghrim aghaughamarṣa
BhP tīrthāspadaṃ hṛdi kṛtaṃ suvipakvayogaiḥ
BhP utsiktabhaktyupahatāśaya jīvakośā
BhP āpur bhavadgatim athānugṛhāna bhaktān
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity anujñāpya dāśārhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
BhP rājarṣe svāśramān gantuṃ munayo dadhire manaḥ
BhP tad vīkṣya tān upavrajya vasudevo mahāyaśāḥ
BhP praṇamya copasaṅgṛhya babhāṣedaṃ suyantritaḥ
BhP śrīvasudeva uvāca
BhP namo vaḥ sarvadevebhya ṛṣayaḥ śrotum arhatha
BhP karmaṇā karmanirhāro yathā syān nas tad ucyatām
BhP śrīnārada uvāca
BhP nāticitram idaṃ viprā vasudevo bubhutsayā
BhP kṛṣṇam matvārbhakaṃ yan naḥ pṛcchati śreya ātmanaḥ
BhP sannikarṣo 'tra martyānām anādaraṇakāraṇam
BhP gāṅgaṃ hitvā yathānyāmbhas tatratyo yāti śuddhaye
BhP yasyānubhūtiḥ kālena layotpattyādināsya vai
BhP svato 'nyasmāc ca guṇato na kutaścana riṣyati
BhP taṃ kleśakarmaparipākaguṇapravāhair avyāhatānubhavam īśvaram advitīyam
BhP prāṇādibhiḥ svavibhavair upagūḍham anyo manyeta sūryam iva meghahimoparāgaiḥ
BhP athocur munayo rājann ābhāṣyānalsadundabhim
BhP sarveṣāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ rājñāṃ tathaivācyutarāmayoḥ
BhP karmaṇā karmanirhāra eṣa sādhunirūpitaḥ
BhP yac chraddhayā yajed viṣṇuṃ sarvayajñeśvaraṃ makhaiḥ
BhP cittasyopaśamo 'yaṃ vai kavibhiḥ śāstracakṣusā
BhP darśitaḥ sugamo yogo dharmaś cātmamudāvahaḥ
BhP ayaṃ svastyayanaḥ panthā dvijāter gṛhamedhinaḥ
BhP yac chraddhayāptavittena śuklenejyeta pūruṣaḥ
BhP vittaiṣaṇāṃ yajñadānair gṛhair dārasutaiṣaṇām
BhP ātmalokaiṣaṇāṃ deva kālena visṛjed budhaḥ
BhP grāme tyaktaiṣaṇāḥ sarve yayur dhīrās tapovanam
BhP ṛṇais tribhir dvijo jāto devarṣipitṝṇāṃ prabho
BhP yajñādhyayanaputrais tāny anistīrya tyajan patet
BhP tvaṃ tv adya mukto dvābhyāṃ vai ṛṣipitror mahāmate
BhP yajñair devarṇam unmucya nirṛṇo 'śaraṇo bhava
BhP vasudeva bhavān nūnaṃ bhaktyā paramayā harim
BhP jagatām īśvaraṃ prārcaḥ sa yad vāṃ putratāṃ gataḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vasudevo mahāmanāḥ
BhP tān ṛṣīn ṛtvijo vavre mūrdhnānamya prasādya ca
BhP ta enam ṛṣayo rājan vṛtā dharmeṇa dhārmikam
BhP tasminn ayājayan kṣetre makhair uttamakalpakaiḥ
BhP taddīkṣāyāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ puṣkarasrajaḥ
BhP snātāḥ suvāsaso rājan rājānaḥ suṣṭhvalaṅkṛtāḥ
BhP tanmahiṣyaś ca muditā niṣkakaṇṭhyaḥ suvāsasaḥ
BhP dīkṣāśālām upājagmur āliptā vastupāṇayaḥ
BhP nedur mṛdaṅgapaṭaha śaṅkhabheryānakādayaḥ
BhP nanṛtur naṭanartakyas tuṣṭuvuḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ
BhP jaguḥ sukaṇṭhyo gandharvyaḥ saṅgītaṃ sahabhartṛkāḥ
BhP tam abhyaṣiñcan vidhivad aktam abhyaktam ṛtvijaḥ
BhP patnībhir aṣṭādaśabhiḥ somarājam ivoḍubhiḥ
BhP tābhir dukūlavalayair hāranūpurakuṇḍalaiḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtābhir vibabhau dīkṣito 'jinasaṃvṛtaḥ
BhP tasyartvijo mahārāja ratnakauśeyavāsasaḥ
BhP sasadasyā virejus te yathā vṛtrahaṇo 'dhvare
BhP tadā rāmaś ca kṛṣṇaś ca svaiḥ svair bandhubhir anvitau
BhP rejatuḥ svasutair dārair jīveśau svavibhūtibhiḥ
BhP īje 'nuyajñaṃ vidhinā agnihotrādilakṣaṇaiḥ
BhP prākṛtair vaikṛtair yajñair dravyajñānakriyeśvaram
BhP athartvigbhyo 'dadāt kāle yathāmnātaṃ sa dakṣiṇāḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtebhyo 'laṅkṛtya gobhūkanyā mahādhanāḥ
BhP patnīsaṃyājāvabhṛthyaiś caritvā te maharṣayaḥ
BhP sasnū rāmahrade viprā yajamānapuraḥsarāḥ
BhP snāto 'laṅkāravāsāṃsi vandibhyo 'dāt tathā striyaḥ
BhP tataḥ svalaṅkṛto varṇān āśvabhyo 'nnena pūjayat
BhP bandhūn sadārān sasutān pāribarheṇa bhūyasā
BhP vidarbhakośalakurūn kāśikekayasṛñjayān
BhP sadasyartviksuragaṇān nṛbhūtapitṛcāraṇān
BhP śrīniketam anujñāpya śaṃsantaḥ prayayuḥ kratum
BhP dhṛtarāṣṭro 'nujaḥ pārthā bhīṣmo droṇaḥ pṛthā yamau
BhP nārado bhagavān vyāsaḥ suhṛtsambandhibāndhavāḥ
BhP bandhūn pariṣvajya yadūn sauhṛdāklinnacetasaḥ
BhP yayur virahakṛcchreṇa svadeśāṃś cāpare janāḥ
BhP nandas tu saha gopālair bṛhatyā pūjayārcitaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇarāmograsenādyair nyavātsīd bandhuvatsalaḥ
BhP vasudevo 'ñjasottīrya manorathamahārṇavam
BhP suhṛdvṛtaḥ prītamanā nandam āha kare spṛśan
BhP śrīvasudeva uvāca
BhP bhrātar īśakṛtaḥ pāśo nṛnāṃ yaḥ snehasaṃjñitaḥ
BhP taṃ dustyajam ahaṃ manye śūrāṇām api yoginām
BhP asmāsv apratikalpeyaṃ yat kṛtājñeṣu sattamaiḥ
BhP maitry arpitāphalā cāpi na nivarteta karhicit
BhP prāg akalpāc ca kuśalaṃ bhrātar vo nācarāma hi
BhP adhunā śrīmadāndhākṣā na paśyāmaḥ puraḥ sataḥ
BhP mā rājyaśrīr abhūt puṃsaḥ śreyaskāmasya mānada
BhP svajanān uta bandhūn vā na paśyati yayāndhadṛk
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ sauhṛdaśaithilya citta ānakadundubhiḥ
BhP ruroda tatkṛtāṃ maitrīṃ smarann aśruvilocanaḥ
BhP nandas tu sakhyuḥ priyakṛt premṇā govindarāmayoḥ
BhP adya śva iti māsāṃs trīn yadubhir mānito 'vasat
BhP tataḥ kāmaiḥ pūryamāṇaḥ savrajaḥ sahabāndhavaḥ
BhP parārdhyābharaṇakṣauma nānānarghyaparicchadaiḥ
BhP vasudevograsenābhyāṃ kṛṣṇoddhavabalādibhiḥ
BhP dattam ādāya pāribarhaṃ yāpito yadubhir yayau
BhP nando gopāś ca gopyaś ca govindacaraṇāmbuje
BhP manaḥ kṣiptaṃ punar hartum anīśā mathurāṃ yayuḥ
BhP bandhuṣu pratiyāteṣu vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇadevatāḥ
BhP vīkṣya prāvṛṣam āsannād yayur dvāravatīṃ punaḥ
BhP janebhyaḥ kathayāṃ cakrur yadudevamahotsavam
BhP yad āsīt tīrthayātrāyāṃ suhṛtsandarśanādikam
BhP śrībādarāyaṇir uvāca
BhP athaikadātmajau prāptau kṛtapādābhivandanau
BhP vasudevo 'bhinandyāha prītyā saṅkarṣaṇācyutau
BhP munīnāṃ sa vacaḥ śrutvā putrayor dhāmasūcakam
BhP tadvīryair jātaviśrambhaḥ paribhāṣyābhyabhāṣata
BhP kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahāyogin saṅkarṣaṇa sanātana
BhP jāne vām asya yat sākṣāt pradhānapuruṣau parau
BhP yatra yena yato yasya yasmai yad yad yathā yadā
BhP syād idaṃ bhagavān sākṣāt pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ
BhP etan nānāvidhaṃ viśvam ātmasṛṣṭam adhokṣaja
BhP ātmanānupraviśyātman prāṇo jīvo bibharṣy aja
BhP prāṇādīnāṃ viśvasṛjāṃ śaktayo yāḥ parasya tāḥ
BhP pāratantryād vaisādṛṣyād dvayoś ceṣṭaiva ceṣṭatām
BhP kāntis tejaḥ prabhā sattā candrāgnyarkarkṣavidyutām
BhP yat sthairyaṃ bhūbhṛtāṃ bhūmer vṛttir gandho 'rthato bhavān
BhP tarpaṇaṃ prāṇanam apāṃ deva tvaṃ tāś ca tadrasaḥ
BhP ojaḥ saho balaṃ ceṣṭā gatir vāyos taveśvara
BhP diśāṃ tvam avakāśo 'si diśaḥ khaṃ sphoṭa āśrayaḥ
BhP nādo varṇas tvam oṃkāra ākṛtīnāṃ pṛthakkṛtiḥ
BhP indriyaṃ tv indriyāṇāṃ tvaṃ devāś ca tadanugrahaḥ
BhP avabodho bhavān buddher jīvasyānusmṛtiḥ satī
BhP bhūtānām asi bhūtādir indriyāṇāṃ ca taijasaḥ
BhP vaikāriko vikalpānāṃ pradhānam anuśāyinam
BhP naśvareṣv iha bhāveṣu tad asi tvam anaśvaram
BhP yathā dravyavikāreṣu dravyamātraṃ nirūpitam
BhP sattvam rajas tama iti guṇās tadvṛttayaś ca yāḥ
BhP tvayy addhā brahmaṇi pare kalpitā yogamāyayā
BhP tasmān na santy amī bhāvā yarhi tvayi vikalpitāḥ
BhP tvaṃ cāmīṣu vikāreṣu hy anyadāvyāvahārikaḥ
BhP guṇapravāha etasminn abudhās tv akhilātmanaḥ
BhP gatiṃ sūkṣmām abodhena saṃsarantīha karmabhiḥ
BhP yadṛcchayā nṛtāṃ prāpya sukalpām iha durlabhām
BhP svārthe pramattasya vayo gataṃ tvanmāyayeśvara
BhP asāv aham mamaivaite dehe cāsyānvayādiṣu
BhP snehapāśair nibadhnāti bhavān sarvam idaṃ jagat
BhP yuvāṃ na naḥ sutau sākṣāt pradhānapuruṣeśvarau
BhP bhūbhārakṣatrakṣapaṇa avatīrṇau tathāttha ha
BhP tat te gato 'smy araṇam adya padāravindam
BhP āpannasaṃsṛtibhayāpaham ārtabandho
BhP etāvatālam alam indriyalālasena
BhP martyātmadṛk tvayi pare yad apatyabuddhiḥ
BhP sūtīgṛhe nanu jagāda bhavān ajo nau
BhP sañjajña ity anuyugaṃ nijadharmaguptyai
BhP nānātanūr gaganavad vidadhaj jahāsi
BhP ko veda bhūmna urugāya vibhūtimāyām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ākarṇyetthaṃ pitur vākyaṃ bhagavān sātvatarṣabhaḥ
BhP pratyāha praśrayānamraḥ prahasan ślakṣṇayā girā
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP vaco vaḥ samavetārthaṃ tātaitad upamanmahe
BhP yan naḥ putrān samuddiśya tattvagrāma udāhṛtaḥ
BhP ahaṃ yūyam asāv ārya ime ca dvārakāukasaḥ
BhP sarve 'py evaṃ yaduśreṣṭha vimṛgyāḥ sacarācaram
BhP ātmā hy ekaḥ svayaṃjyotir nityo 'nyo nirguṇo guṇaiḥ
BhP ātmasṛṣṭais tatkṛteṣu bhūteṣu bahudheyate
BhP khaṃ vāyur jyotir āpo bhūs tatkṛteṣu yathāśayam
BhP āvistiro'lpabhūry eko nānātvaṃ yāty asāv api
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ bhagavatā rājan vasudeva udāhṛtaḥ
BhP śrutvā vinaṣṭanānādhīs tūṣṇīṃ prītamanā abhūt
BhP atha tatra kuruśreṣṭha devakī sarvadevatā
BhP śrutvānītaṃ guroḥ putram ātmajābhyāṃ suvismitā
BhP kṛṣṇarāmau samāśrāvya putrān kaṃsavihiṃsitān
BhP smarantī kṛpaṇaṃ prāha vaiklavyād aśrulocanā
BhP śrīdevaky uvāca
BhP rāma rāmāprameyātman kṛṣṇa yogeśvareśvara
BhP vedāhaṃ vāṃ viśvasṛjām īśvarāv ādipūruṣau
BhP kalavidhvastasattvānāṃ rājñām ucchāstravartinām
BhP bhūmer bhārāyamāṇānām avatīrṇau kilādya me
BhP yasyāṃśāṃśāṃśabhāgena viśvotpattilayodayāḥ
BhP bhavanti kila viśvātmaṃs taṃ tvādyāhaṃ gatiṃ gatā
BhP cirān mṛtasutādāne guruṇā kila coditau
BhP āninyathuḥ pitṛsthānād gurave gurudakṣiṇām
BhP tathā me kurutaṃ kāmaṃ yuvāṃ yogeśvareśvarau
BhP bhojarājahatān putrān kāmaye draṣṭum āhṛtān
BhP ṛṣir uvāca
BhP evaṃ sañcoditau mātrā rāmaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca bhārata
BhP sutalaṃ saṃviviśatur yogamāyām upāśritau
BhP tasmin praviṣṭāv upalabhya daityarāḍ
BhP viśvātmadaivaṃ sutarāṃ tathātmanaḥ
BhP taddarśanāhlādapariplutāśayaḥ
BhP sadyaḥ samutthāya nanāma sānvayaḥ
BhP tayoḥ samānīya varāsanaṃ mudā niviṣṭayos tatra mahātmanos tayoḥ
BhP dadhāra pādāv avanijya taj jalaṃ savṛnda ābrahma punad yad ambu ha
BhP samarhayām āsa sa tau vibhūtibhir mahārhavastrābharaṇānulepanaiḥ
BhP tāmbūladīpāmṛtabhakṣaṇādibhiḥ svagotravittātmasamarpaṇena ca
BhP sa indraseno bhagavatpadāmbujaṃ bibhran muhuḥ premavibhinnayā dhiyā
BhP uvāca hānandajalākulekṣaṇaḥ prahṛṣṭaromā nṛpa gadgadākṣaram
BhP balir uvāca
BhP namo 'nantāya bṛhate namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase
BhP sāṅkhyayogavitānāya brahmaṇe paramātmane
BhP darśanaṃ vāṃ hi bhūtānāṃ duṣprāpaṃ cāpy adurlabham
BhP rajastamaḥsvabhāvānāṃ yan naḥ prāptau yadṛcchayā
BhP daityadānavagandharvāḥ siddhavidyādhracāraṇāḥ
BhP yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāś ca bhūtapramathanāyakāḥ
BhP viśuddhasattvadhāmny addhā tvayi śāstraśarīriṇi
BhP nityaṃ nibaddhavairās te vayaṃ cānye ca tādṛśāḥ
BhP kecanodbaddhavaireṇa bhaktyā kecana kāmataḥ
BhP na tathā sattvasaṃrabdhāḥ sannikṛṣṭāḥ surādayaḥ
BhP idam ittham iti prāyas tava yogeśvareśvara
BhP na vidanty api yogeśā yogamāyāṃ kuto vayam
BhP tan naḥ prasīda nirapekṣavimṛgyayuṣmat
BhP pādāravindadhiṣaṇānyagṛhāndhakūpāt
BhP niṣkramya viśvaśaraṇāṅghryupalabdhavṛttiḥ
BhP śānto yathaika uta sarvasakhaiś carāmi
BhP śādhy asmān īśitavyeśa niṣpāpān kuru naḥ prabho
BhP pumān yac chraddhayātiṣṭhaṃś codanāyā vimucyate
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP āsan marīceḥ ṣaṭ putrā ūrṇāyāṃ prathame 'ntare
BhP devāḥ kaṃ jahasur vīkṣya sutaṃ yabhitum udyatam
BhP tenāsurīm agan yonim adhunāvadyakarmaṇā
BhP hiraṇyakaśipor jātā nītās te yogamāyayā
BhP devakyā udare jātā rājan kaṃsavihiṃsitāḥ
BhP sā tān śocaty ātmajān svāṃs ta ime 'dhyāsate 'ntike
BhP ita etān praṇeṣyāmo mātṛśokāpanuttaye
BhP tataḥ śāpād vinirmaktā lokaṃ yāsyanti vijvarāḥ
BhP smarodgīthaḥ pariṣvaṅgaḥ pataṅgaḥ kṣudrabhṛd ghṛṇī
BhP ṣaḍ ime matprasādena punar yāsyanti sadgatim
BhP ity uktvā tān samādāya indrasenena pūjitau
BhP punar dvāravatīm etya mātuḥ putrān ayacchatām
BhP tān dṛṣṭvā bālakān devī putrasnehasnutastanī
BhP pariṣvajyāṅkam āropya mūrdhny ajighrad abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
BhP apāyayat stanaṃ prītā sutasparśaparisnutam
BhP mohitā māyayā viṣṇor yayā sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate
BhP pītvāmṛtaṃ payas tasyāḥ pītaśeṣaṃ gadābhṛtaḥ
BhP nārāyaṇāṅgasaṃsparśa pratilabdhātmadarśanāḥ
BhP te namaskṛtya govindaṃ devakīṃ pitaraṃ balam
BhP miṣatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yayur dhāma divaukasām
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvā devakī devī mṛtāgamananirgamam
BhP mene suvismitā māyāṃ kṛṣṇasya racitāṃ nṛpa
BhP evaṃvidhāny adbhutāni kṛṣṇasya paramātmanaḥ
BhP vīryāṇy anantavīryasya santy anantāni bhārata
BhP śrīsūta uvāca
BhP ya idam anuśṛṇoti śrāvayed vā murāreś
BhP caritam amṛtakīrter varṇitaṃ vyāsaputraiḥ
BhP jagadaghabhid alaṃ tadbhaktasatkarṇapūraṃ
BhP bhagavati kṛtacitto yāti tatkṣemadhāma
BhP śrīrājovāca
BhP brahman veditum icchāmaḥ svasārāṃ rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ
BhP yathopayeme vijayo yā mamāsīt pitāmahī
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP arjunas tīrthayātrāyāṃ paryaṭann avanīṃ prabhuḥ
BhP gataḥ prabhāsam aśṛṇon mātuleyīṃ sa ātmanaḥ
BhP duryodhanāya rāmas tāṃ dāsyatīti na cāpare
BhP tallipsuḥ sa yatir bhūtvā tridaṇḍī dvārakām agāt
BhP tatra vai vārṣitān māsān avātsīt svārthasādhakaḥ
BhP pauraiḥ sabhājito 'bhīkṣṇaṃ rāmeṇājānatā ca saḥ
BhP ekadā gṛham ānīya ātithyena nimantrya tam
BhP śraddhayopahṛtaṃ bhaikṣyaṃ balena bubhuje kila
BhP so 'paśyat tatra mahatīṃ kanyāṃ vīramanoharām
BhP prītyutphullekṣaṇas tasyāṃ bhāvakṣubdhaṃ mano dadhe
BhP sāpi taṃ cakame vīkṣya nārīṇāṃ hṛdayaṃgamam
BhP hasantī vrīḍitāpaṅgī tannyastahṛdayekṣaṇā
BhP tāṃ paraṃ samanudhyāyann antaraṃ prepsur arjunaḥ
BhP na lebhe śaṃ bhramaccittaḥ kāmenātibalīyasā
BhP mahatyāṃ devayātrāyāṃ rathasthāṃ durganirgatāṃ
BhP jahārānumataḥ pitroḥ kṛṣṇasya ca mahārathaḥ
BhP rathastho dhanur ādāya śūrāṃś cārundhato bhaṭān
BhP vidrāvya krośatāṃ svānāṃ svabhāgaṃ mṛgarāḍ iva
BhP tac chrutvā kṣubhito rāmaḥ parvaṇīva mahārṇavaḥ
BhP gṛhītapādaḥ kṛṣṇena suhṛdbhiś cānusāntvitaḥ
BhP prāhiṇot pāribarhāṇi varavadhvor mudā balaḥ
BhP mahādhanopaskarebha rathāśvanarayoṣitaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP kṛṣṇasyāsīd dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ śrutadeva iti śrutaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇaikabhaktyā pūrṇārthaḥ śāntaḥ kavir alampataḥ
BhP sa uvāsa videheṣu mithilāyāṃ gṛhāśramī
BhP anīhayāgatāhārya nirvartitanijakriyaḥ
BhP yātrāmātraṃ tv ahar ahar daivād upanamaty uta
BhP nādhikaṃ tāvatā tuṣṭaḥ kriyā cakre yathocitāḥ
BhP tathā tadrāṣṭrapālo 'ṅga bahulāśva iti śrutaḥ
BhP maithilo nirahammāna ubhāv apy acyutapriyau
BhP tayoḥ prasanno bhagavān dārukeṇāhṛtaṃ ratham
BhP āruhya sākaṃ munibhir videhān prayayau prabhuḥ
BhP nārado vāmadevo 'triḥ kṛṣṇo rāmo 'sito 'ruṇiḥ
BhP ahaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ kaṇvo maitreyaś cyavanādayaḥ
BhP tatra tatra tam āyāntaṃ paurā jānapadā nṛpa
BhP upatasthuḥ sārghyahastā grahaiḥ sūryam ivoditam
BhP ānartadhanvakurujāṅgalakaṅkamatsya

BhP anye ca tanmukhasarojam udārahāsa
BhP snigdhekṣaṇaṃ nṛpa papur dṛśibhir nrnāryaḥ
BhP tebhyaḥ svavīkṣaṇavinaṣṭatamisradṛgbhyaḥ
BhP kṣemaṃ trilokagurur arthadṛśaṃ ca yacchan
BhP śṛṇvan digantadhavalaṃ svayaśo 'śubhaghnaṃ
BhP gītaṃ surair nṛbhir agāc chanakair videhān
BhP te 'cyutaṃ prāptam ākarṇya paurā jānapadā nṛpa
BhP abhīyur muditās tasmai gṛhītārhaṇapāṇayaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā ta uttamaḥślokaṃ prītyutphulānanāśayāḥ
BhP kair dhṛtāñjalibhir nemuḥ śrutapūrvāṃs tathā munīn
BhP svānugrahāya samprāptaṃ manvānau taṃ jagadgurum
BhP maithilaḥ śrutadevaś ca pādayoḥ petatuḥ prabhoḥ
BhP nyamantrayetāṃ dāśārham ātithyena saha dvijaiḥ
BhP maithilaḥ śrutadevaś ca yugapat saṃhatāñjalī
BhP bhagavāṃs tad abhipretya dvayoḥ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP ubhayor āviśad geham ubhābhyāṃ tadalakṣitaḥ
BhP śrāntān apy atha tān dūrāj janakaḥ svagṛhāgatān
BhP ānīteṣv āsanāgryeṣu sukhāsīnān mahāmanāḥ
BhP pravṛddhabhaktyā uddharṣa hṛdayāsrāvilekṣaṇaḥ
BhP natvā tadaṅghrīn prakṣālya tadapo lokapāvanīḥ
BhP sakuṭumbo vahan mūrdhnā pūjayāṃ cakra īśvarān
BhP gandhamālyāmbarākalpa dhūpadīpārghyagovṛṣaiḥ
BhP vācā madhurayā prīṇann idam āhānnatarpitān
BhP pādāv aṅkagatau viṣṇoḥ saṃspṛśañ chanakair mudā
BhP śrībahulāśva uvāca
BhP bhavān hi sarvabhūtānām ātmā sākṣī svadṛg vibho
BhP atha nas tvatpadāmbhojaṃ smaratāṃ darśanaṃ gataḥ
BhP svavacas tad ṛtaṃ kartum asmaddṛggocaro bhavān
BhP yad ātthaikāntabhaktān me nānantaḥ śrīr ajaḥ priyaḥ
BhP ko nu tvaccaraṇāmbhojam evaṃvid visṛjet pumān
BhP niṣkiñcanānāṃ śāntānāṃ munīnāṃ yas tvam ātmadaḥ
BhP yo 'vatīrya yador vaṃśe nṛṇāṃ saṃsaratām iha
BhP yaśo vitene tacchāntyai trailokyavṛjināpaham
BhP namas tubhyaṃ bhagavate kṛṣṇāyākuṇṭhamedhase
BhP nārāyaṇāya ṛṣaye suśāntaṃ tapa īyuṣe
BhP dināni katicid bhūman gṛhān no nivasa dvijaiḥ
BhP sametaḥ pādarajasā punīhīdaṃ nimeḥ kulam
BhP ity upāmantrito rājñā bhagavāṃl lokabhāvanaḥ
BhP uvāsa kurvan kalyāṇaṃ mithilānarayoṣitām
BhP śrutadevo 'cyutaṃ prāptaṃ svagṛhāñ janako yathā
BhP natvā munīn susaṃhṛṣṭo dhunvan vāso nanarta ha
BhP tṛṇapīṭhabṛṣīṣv etān ānīteṣūpaveśya saḥ
BhP svāgatenābhinandyāṅghrīn sabhāryo 'vanije mudā
BhP tadambhasā mahābhāga ātmānaṃ sagṛhānvayam
BhP snāpayāṃ cakra uddharṣo labdhasarvamanorathaḥ
BhP phalārhaṇośīraśivāmṛtāmbubhir mṛdā surabhyā tulasīkuśāmbuyaiḥ
BhP ārādhayām āsa yathopapannayā saparyayā sattvavivardhanāndhasā
BhP sa tarkayām āsa kuto mamānv abhūt gṛhāndhakupe patitasya saṅgamaḥ
BhP yaḥ sarvatīrthāspadapādareṇubhiḥ kṛṣṇena cāsyātmaniketabhūsuraiḥ
BhP sūpaviṣṭān kṛtātithyān śrutadeva upasthitaḥ
BhP sabhāryasvajanāpatya uvācāṅghryabhimarśanaḥ
BhP śrutadeva uvāca
BhP nādya no darśanaṃ prāptaḥ paraṃ paramapūruṣaḥ
BhP yarhīdaṃ śaktibhiḥ sṛṣṭvā praviṣṭo hy ātmasattayā
BhP yathā śayānaḥ puruṣo manasaivātmamāyayā
BhP sṛṣṭvā lokaṃ paraṃ svāpnam anuviśyāvabhāsate
BhP śṛṇvatāṃ gadatāṃ śaśvad arcatāṃ tvābhivandatām
BhP ṇṛṇāṃ saṃvadatām antar hṛdi bhāsy amalātmanām
BhP hṛdistho 'py atidūrasthaḥ karmavikṣiptacetasām
BhP ātmaśaktibhir agrāhyo 'py anty upetaguṇātmanām
BhP namo 'stu te 'dhyātmavidāṃ parātmane
BhP anātmane svātmavibhaktamṛtyave
BhP sakāraṇākāraṇaliṅgam īyuṣe
BhP svamāyayāsaṃvṛtaruddhadṛṣṭaye
BhP sa tvaṃ śādhi svabhṛtyān naḥ kiṃ deva karavāma he
BhP etadanto nṛṇāṃ kleśo yad bhavān akṣigocaraḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP taduktam ity upākarṇya bhagavān praṇatārtihā
BhP gṛhītvā pāṇinā pāṇiṃ prahasaṃs tam uvāca ha
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP brahmaṃs te 'nugrahārthāya samprāptān viddhy amūn munīn
BhP sañcaranti mayā lokān punantaḥ pādareṇubhiḥ
BhP devāḥ kṣetrāṇi tīrthāni darśanasparśanārcanaiḥ
BhP śanaiḥ punanti kālena tad apy arhattamekṣayā
BhP brāhmaṇo janmanā śreyān sarveṣām prāṇinām iha
BhP tapasā vidyayā tuṣṭyā kim u matkalayā yutaḥ
BhP na brāhmaṇān me dayitaṃ rūpam etac caturbhujam
BhP sarvavedamayo vipraḥ sarvadevamayo hy aham
BhP duṣprajñā aviditvaivam avajānanty asūyavaḥ
BhP guruṃ māṃ vipram ātmānam arcādāv ijyadṛṣṭayaḥ
BhP carācaram idaṃ viśvaṃ bhāvā ye cāsya hetavaḥ
BhP madrūpāṇīti cetasy ādhatte vipro madīkṣayā
BhP tasmād brahmaṛṣīn etān brahman macchraddhayārcaya
BhP evaṃ ced arcito 'smy addhā nānyathā bhūribhūtibhiḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa itthaṃ prabhunādiṣṭaḥ sahakṛṣṇān dvijottamān
BhP ārādhyaikātmabhāvena maithilaś cāpa sadgatim
BhP evaṃ svabhaktayo rājan bhagavān bhaktabhaktimān
BhP uṣitvādiśya sanmārgaṃ punar dvāravatīm agāt
BhP śrīparīkṣid uvāca
BhP brahman brahmaṇy anirdeśye nirguṇe guṇavṛttayaḥ
BhP kathaṃ caranti śrutayaḥ sākṣāt sadasataḥ pare
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP buddhīndriyamanaḥprāṇān janānām asṛjat prabhuḥ
BhP mātrārthaṃ ca bhavārthaṃ ca ātmane 'kalpanāya ca
BhP saiṣā hy upaniṣad brāhmī pūrveśāṃ pūrvajair dhṛtā
BhP śrraddhayā dhārayed yas tāṃ kṣemaṃ gacched akiñcanaḥ
BhP atra te varṇayiṣyāmi gāthāṃ nārāyaṇānvitām
BhP nāradasya ca saṃvādam ṛṣer nārāyaṇasya ca
BhP ekadā nārado lokān paryaṭan bhagavatpriyaḥ
BhP sanātanam ṛṣiṃ draṣṭuṃ yayau nārāyaṇāśramam
BhP yo vai bhāratavarṣe 'smin kṣemāya svastaye nṛṇām
BhP dharmajñānaśamopetam ākalpād āsthitas tapaḥ
BhP tatropaviṣṭam ṛṣibhiḥ kalāpagrāmavāsibhiḥ
BhP parītaṃ praṇato 'pṛcchad idam eva kurūdvaha
BhP tasmai hy avocad bhagavān ṛṣīṇāṃ śṛṇvatām idam
BhP yo brahmavādaḥ pūrveṣāṃ janalokanivāsinām
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP svāyambhuva brahmasatraṃ janaloke 'bhavat purā
BhP tatrasthānāṃ mānasānāṃ munīnām ūrdhvaretasām
BhP śvetadvīpaṃ gatavati tvayi draṣṭuṃ tadīśvaram
BhP brahmavādaḥ susaṃvṛttaḥ śrutayo yatra śerate
BhP tatra hāyam abhūt praśnas tvaṃ māṃ yam anupṛcchasi
BhP tulyaśrutatapaḥśīlās tulyasvīyārimadhyamāḥ
BhP api cakruḥ pravacanam ekaṃ śuśrūṣavo 'pare
BhP śrīsanandana uvāca
BhP svasṛṣṭam idam āpīya śayānaṃ saha śaktibhiḥ
BhP tadante bodhayāṃ cakrus talliṅgaiḥ śrutayaḥ param
BhP yathā śayānaṃ saṃrājaṃ vandinas tatparākramaiḥ
BhP pratyūṣe 'bhetya suślokair bodhayanty anujīvinaḥ
BhP śrīśrutaya ūcuḥ
BhP jaya jaya jahy ajām ajita doṣagṛbhītaguṇāṃ
BhP tvam asi yad ātmanā samavaruddhasamastabhagaḥ
BhP agajagadokasām akhilaśaktyavabodhaka te

BhP bṛhad upalabdham etad avayanty avaśeṣatayā
BhP yata udayāstamayau vikṛter mṛdi vāvikṛtāt
BhP ata ṛṣayo dadhus tvayi manovacanācaritaṃ
BhP katham ayathā bhavanti bhuvi dattapadāni nṛṇām
BhP iti tava sūrayas tryadhipate 'khilalokamala
BhP kṣapaṇakathāmṛtābdhim avagāhya tapāṃsi jahuḥ
BhP kim uta punaḥ svadhāmavidhutāśayakālaguṇāḥ
BhP parama bhajanti ye padam ajasrasukhānubhavam
BhP dṛtaya iva śvasanty asubhṛto yadi te 'nuvidhā
BhP mahadahamādayo 'ṇḍam asṛjan yadanugrahataḥ
BhP puruṣavidho 'nvayo 'tra caramo 'nnamayādiṣu yaḥ
BhP sadasataḥ paraṃ tvam atha yad eṣv avaśeṣam ṛtam
BhP udaram upāsate ya ṛṣivartmasu kūrpadṛśaḥ
BhP parisarapaddhatiṃ hṛdayam āruṇayo daharam
BhP tata udagād ananta tava dhāma śiraḥ paramaṃ
BhP punar iha yat sametya na patanti kṛtāntamukhe
BhP svakṛtavicitrayoniṣu viśann iva hetutayā
BhP taratamataś cakāssy analavat svakṛtānukṛtiḥ
BhP atha vitathāsv amūṣv avitathāṃ tava dhāma samaṃ
BhP virajadhiyo 'nuyanty abhivipaṇyava ekarasam
BhP svakṛtapureṣv amīṣv abahirantarasaṃvaraṇaṃ
BhP tava puruṣaṃ vadanty akhilaśaktidhṛto 'ṃśakṛtam
BhP iti nṛgatiṃ vivicya kavayo nigamāvapanaṃ
BhP bhavata upāsate 'ṅghrim abhavam bhuvi viśvasitāḥ
BhP duravagamātmatattvanigamāya tavāttatanoś
BhP caritamahāmṛtābdhiparivartapariśramaṇāḥ
BhP na parilaṣanti kecid apavargam apīśvara te
BhP caraṇasarojahaṃsakulasaṅgavisṛṣṭagṛhāḥ
BhP tvadanupathaṃ kulāyam idam ātmasuhṛtpriyavac
BhP carati tathonmukhe tvayi hite priya ātmani ca
BhP na bata ramanty aho asadupāsanayātmahano
BhP yadanuśayā bhramanty urubhaye kuśarīrabhṛtaḥ
BhP nibhṛtamarunmano'kṣadṛḍhayogayujo hṛdi yan

BhP striya uragendrabhogabhujadaṇḍaviṣaktadhiyo
BhP vayam api te samāḥ samadṛśo 'ṅghrisarojasudhāḥ
BhP ka iha nu veda batāvarajanmalayo 'grasaraṃ
BhP yata udagād ṛṣir yam anu devagaṇā ubhaye
BhP tarhi na san na cāsad ubhayaṃ na ca kālajavaḥ
BhP kim api na tatra śāstram avakṛṣya śayīta yadā
BhP janim asataḥ sato mṛtim utātmani ye ca bhidāṃ
BhP vipaṇam ṛtaṃ smaranty upadiśanti ta ārupitaiḥ
BhP triguṇamayaḥ pumān iti bhidā yad abodhakṛtā
BhP tvayi na tataḥ paratra sa bhaved avabodharase
BhP sad iva manas trivṛt tvayi vibhāty asad āmanujāt
BhP sad abhimṛśanty aśeṣam idam ātmatayātmavidaḥ
BhP na hi vikṛtiṃ tyajanti kanakasya tadātmatayā
BhP svakṛtam anupraviṣṭam idam ātmatayāvasitam
BhP tava pari ye caranty akhilasattvaniketatayā
BhP ta uta padākramanty avigaṇayya śiro nirṛteḥ
BhP parivayase paśūn iva girā vibudhān api tāṃs
BhP tvayi kṛtasauhṛdāḥ khalu punanti na ye vimukhāḥ
BhP tvam akaraṇaḥ svarāḍ akhilakārakaśaktidharas
BhP tava balim udvahanti samadanty ajayānimiṣāḥ
BhP varṣabhujo 'khilakṣitipater iva viśvasṛjo
BhP vidadhati yatra ye tv adhikṛtā bhavataś cakitāḥ
BhP sthiracarajātayaḥ syur ajayotthanimittayujo
BhP vihara udīkṣayā yadi parasya vimukta tataḥ
BhP na hi paramasya kaścid aparo na paraś ca bhaved

BhP aparimitā dhruvās tanubhṛto yadi sarvagatās
BhP tarhi na śāsyateti niyamo dhrava netarathā
BhP ajani ca yanmayaṃ tad avimucya niyantṛ bhavet
BhP samam anujānatāṃ yad amataṃ mataduṣṭatayā
BhP na ghaṭata udbhavaḥ prakṛtipūruṣayor ajayor

BhP sarita ivārṇave madhuni lilyur aśeṣarasāḥ
BhP nṛṣu tava mayayā bhramam amīṣv avagatya bhṛśaṃ
BhP tvayi sudhiyo 'bhave dadhati bhāvam anuprabhavam
BhP katham anuvartatāṃ bhavabhayaṃ tava yad bhrukuṭiḥ
BhP sṛjati muhus trinemir abhavaccharaṇeṣu bhayam
BhP vijitahṛṣīkavāyubhir adāntamanas turagaṃ
BhP ya iha yatanti yantum atilolam upāyakhidaḥ
BhP vyasanaśatānvitāḥ samavahāya guroś caraṇaṃ
BhP vaṇija ivāja santy akṛtakarṇadharā jaladhau

BhP sukhayati ko nv iha svavihate svanirastabhage

BhP dadhati sakṛn manas tvayi ya ātmani nityasukhe
BhP na punar upāsate puruṣasāraharāvasathān
BhP sata idaṃ utthitaṃ sad iti cen nanu tarkahataṃ
BhP vyabhicarati kva ca kva ca mṛṣā na tathobhayayuk
BhP vyavahṛtaye vikalpa iṣito 'ndhaparamparayā
BhP bhramayati bhāratī ta uruvṛttibhir ukthajaḍān
BhP na yad idam agra āsa na bhaviṣyad ato nidhanād

BhP ata upamīyate draviṇajātivikalpapathair

BhP sa yad ajayā tv ajām anuśayīta guṇāṃś ca juṣan

BhP tvam uta jahāsi tām ahir iva tvacam āttabhago

BhP asutṛpayoginām ubhayato 'py asukhaṃ bhagavann

BhP śrīnārada uvāca

BhP sabhājito bhagavatā kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ

BhP śrīrājovāca

BhP matparaiḥ kṛtamaitrasya kariṣye madanugraham

BhP vijñāyātmatayā dhīraḥ saṃsārāt parimucyate

BhP tatas ta āśutoṣebhyo labdharājyaśriyoddhatāḥ

BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP śāpaprasādayor īśā brahmaviṣṇuśivādayaḥ
BhP sadyaḥ śāpaprasādo 'ṅga śivo brahmā na cācyutaḥ
BhP atra codāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam

BhP dṛṣṭvāśutoṣaṃ papraccha deveṣu triṣu durmatiḥ
BhP sa āha devaṃ giriśam upādhāvāśu siddhyasi

BhP prīyeya toyena nṛṇāṃ prapadyatām aho tvayātmā bhṛśam ardyate vṛthā
BhP devaṃ sa vavre pāpīyān varaṃ bhūtabhayāvaham
BhP yasya yasya karaṃ śīrṣṇi dhāsye sa mriyatām iti
BhP tac chrutvā bhagavān rudro durmanā iva bhārata
BhP oṃ iti prahasaṃs tasmai dade 'her amṛtaṃ yathā
BhP sa tadvaraparīkṣārthaṃ śambhor mūrdhni kilāsuraḥ
BhP svahastaṃ dhātum ārebhe so 'bibhyat svakṛtāc chivaḥ
BhP tenopasṛṣṭaḥ santrastaḥ parādhāvan savepathuḥ
BhP yāvad antaṃ divo bhūmeḥ kaṣṭhānām udagād udak
BhP ajānantaḥ pratividhiṃ tūṣṇīm āsan sureśvarāḥ
BhP tato vaikuṇṭham agamad bhāsvaraṃ tamasaḥ param
BhP yatra nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣān nyāsināṃ paramo gatiḥ
BhP śāntānāṃ nyastadaṇḍānāṃ yato nāvartate gataḥ
BhP taṃ tathā vyasanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān vṛjinārdanaḥ
BhP dūrāt pratyudiyād bhūtvā baṭuko yogamāyayā
