BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP śākuneya bhavān vyaktaṃ śrāntaḥ kiṃ dūram āgataḥ
BhP kṣaṇaṃ viśramyatāṃ puṃsa ātmāyaṃ sarvakāmadhuk
BhP yadi naḥ śravaṇāyālaṃ yuṣmadvyavasitaṃ vibho
BhP bhaṇyatāṃ prāyaśaḥ pumbhir dhṛtaiḥ svārthān samīhate
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ bhagavatā pṛṣṭo vacasāmṛtavarṣiṇā
BhP gataklamo 'bravīt tasmai yathāpūrvam anuṣṭhitam
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP evaṃ cet tarhi tadvākyaṃ na vayaṃ śraddadhīmahi
BhP yo dakṣaśāpāt paiśācyaṃ prāptaḥ pretapiśācarāṭ
BhP yadi vas tatra viśrambho dānavendra jagadgurau
BhP tarhy aṅgāśu svaśirasi hastaṃ nyasya pratīyatām
BhP yady asatyaṃ vacaḥ śambhoḥ kathañcid dānavarṣabha
BhP tadainaṃ jahy asadvācaṃ na yad vaktānṛtaṃ punaḥ
BhP itthaṃ bhagavataś citrair vacobhiḥ sa supeśalaiḥ
BhP bhinnadhīr vismṛtaḥ śīrṣṇi svahastaṃ kumatir nyadhāt
BhP athāpatad bhinnaśirāḥ vrajāhata iva kṣaṇāt
BhP jayaśabdo namaḥśabdaḥ sādhuśabdo 'bhavad divi
BhP mumucuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi hate pāpe vṛkāsure
BhP devarṣipitṛgandharvā mocitaḥ saṅkaṭāc chivaḥ
BhP muktaṃ giriśam abhyāha bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ
BhP aho deva mahādeva pāpo 'yaṃ svena pāpmanā
BhP hataḥ ko nu mahatsv īśa jantur vai kṛtakilbiṣaḥ
BhP kṣemī syāt kim u viśveśe kṛtāgasko jagadgurau
BhP ya evam avyākṛtaśaktyudanvataḥ parasya sākṣāt paramātmano hareḥ
BhP giritramokṣaṃ kathayec chṛṇoti vā vimucyate saṃsṛtibhis tathāribhiḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sarasvatyās taṭe rājann ṛṣayaḥ satram āsata
BhP vitarkaḥ samabhūt teṣāṃ triṣv adhīśeṣu ko mahān
BhP tasya jijñāsayā te vai bhṛguṃ brahmasutaṃ nṛpa
BhP tajjñaptyai preṣayām āsuḥ so 'bhjagād brahmaṇaḥ sabhām
BhP na tasmai prahvaṇaṃ stotraṃ cakre sattvaparīkṣayā
BhP tasmai cukrodha bhagavān prajvalan svena tejasā
BhP sa ātmany utthitam manyum ātmajāyātmanā prabhuḥ
BhP aśīśamad yathā vahniṃ svayonyā vāriṇātmabhūḥ
BhP tataḥ kailāsam agamat sa taṃ devo maheśvaraḥ
BhP parirabdhuṃ samārebha utthāya bhrātaraṃ mudā
BhP naicchat tvam asy utpathaga iti devaś cukopa ha
BhP śūlam udyamya taṃ hantum ārebhe tigmalocanaḥ
BhP patitvā pādayor devī sāntvayām āsa taṃ girā
BhP atho jagāma vaikuṇṭhaṃ yatra devo janārdanaḥ
BhP śayānaṃ śriya utsaṅge padā vakṣasy atāḍayat
BhP tata utthāya bhagavān saha lakṣmyā satāṃ gatiḥ
BhP svatalpād avaruhyātha nanāma śirasā munim
BhP āha te svāgataṃ brahman niṣīdātrāsane kṣaṇam
BhP ajānatām āgatān vaḥ kṣantum arhatha naḥ prabho
BhP punīhi sahalokaṃ māṃ lokapālāṃś ca madgatān
BhP pādodakena bhavatas tīrthānāṃ tīrthakāriṇā
BhP adyāhaṃ bhagavaṃl lakṣmyā āsam ekāntabhājanam
BhP vatsyaty urasi me bhūtir bhavatpādahatāṃhasaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ bruvāṇe vaikuṇṭhe bhṛgus tanmandrayā girā
BhP nirvṛtas tarpitas tūṣṇīṃ bhaktyutkaṇṭho 'śrulocanaḥ
BhP punaś ca satram āvrajya munīnāṃ brahmavādinām
BhP svānubhūtam aśeṣeṇa rājan bhṛgur avarṇayat
BhP tan niśamyātha munayo vismitā muktasaṃśayāḥ
BhP bhūyāṃsaṃ śraddadhur viṣṇuṃ yataḥ śāntir yato 'bhayam
BhP dharmaḥ sākṣād yato jñānaṃ vairāgyaṃ ca tadanvitam
BhP aiśvaryaṃ cāṣṭadhā yasmād yaśaś cātmamalāpaham
BhP munīnāṃ nyastadaṇḍānāṃ śāntānāṃ samacetasām
BhP akiñcanānāṃ sādhūnāṃ yam āhuḥ paramāṃ gatim
BhP sattvaṃ yasya priyā mūrtir brāhmaṇās tv iṣṭadevatāḥ
BhP bhajanty anāśiṣaḥ śāntā yaṃ vā nipuṇabuddhayaḥ
BhP trividhākṛtayas tasya rākṣasā asurāḥ surāḥ
BhP guṇinyā māyayā sṛṣṭāḥ sattvaṃ tat tīrthasādhanam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itthaṃ sārasvatā viprā nṛṇām saṃśayanuttaye
BhP puruṣasya padāmbhoja sevayā tadgatiṃ gatāḥ
BhP śrīsūta uvāca
BhP ity etan munitanayāsyapadmagandha
BhP pīyūṣaṃ bhavabhayabhit parasya puṃsaḥ
BhP suślokaṃ śravaṇapuṭaiḥ pibaty abhīkṣṇam
BhP pāntho 'dhvabhramaṇapariśramaṃ jahāti
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ekadā dvāravatyāṃ tu viprapatnyāḥ kumārakaḥ
BhP jātamātro bhuvaṃ spṛṣṭvā mamāra kila bhārata
BhP vipro gṛhītvā mṛtakaṃ rājadvāry upadhāya saḥ
BhP idaṃ provāca vilapann āturo dīnamānasaḥ
BhP brahmadviṣaḥ śaṭhadhiyo lubdhasya viṣayātmanaḥ
BhP kṣatrabandhoḥ karmadoṣāt pañcatvaṃ me gato 'rbhakaḥ
BhP hiṃsāvihāraṃ nṛpatiṃ duḥśīlam ajitendriyam
BhP prajā bhajantyaḥ sīdanti daridrā nityaduḥkhitāḥ
BhP evaṃ dvitīyaṃ viprarṣis tṛtīyaṃ tv evam eva ca
BhP visṛjya sa nṛpadvāri tāṃ gāthāṃ samagāyata
BhP tām arjuna upaśrutya karhicit keśavāntike
BhP parete navame bāle brāhmaṇaṃ samabhāṣata
BhP kiṃ svid brahmaṃs tvannivāse iha nāsti dhanurdharaḥ
BhP rājanyabandhur ete vai brāhmaṇāḥ satram āsate
BhP dhanadārātmajāpṛktā yatra śocanti brāhmaṇāḥ
BhP te vai rājanyaveṣeṇa naṭā jīvanty asumbharāḥ
BhP ahaṃ prajāḥ vāṃ bhagavan rakṣiṣye dīnayor iha
BhP anistīrṇapratijño 'gniṃ pravekṣye hatakalmaṣaḥ
BhP śrībrāhmaṇa uvāca
BhP saṅkarṣaṇo vāsudevaḥ pradyumno dhanvināṃ varaḥ
BhP aniruddho 'pratiratho na trātuṃ śaknuvanti yat
BhP tat kathaṃ nu bhavān karma duṣkaraṃ jagadīśvaraiḥ
BhP tvaṃ cikīrṣasi bāliśyāt tan na śraddadhmahe vayam
BhP śrīarjuna uvāca
BhP nāhaṃ saṅkarṣaṇo brahman na kṛṣṇaḥ kārṣṇir eva ca
BhP ahaṃ vā arjuno nāma gāṇḍīvaṃ yasya vai dhanuḥ
BhP māvamaṃsthā mama brahman vīryaṃ tryambakatoṣaṇam
BhP mṛtyuṃ vijitya pradhane āneṣye te prajāḥ prabho
BhP evaṃ viśrambhito vipraḥ phālgunena parantapa
BhP jagāma svagṛhaṃ prītaḥ pārthavīryaṃ niśāmayan
BhP prasūtikāla āsanne bhāryāyā dvijasattamaḥ
BhP pāhi pāhi prajāṃ mṛtyor ity āhārjunam āturaḥ
BhP sa upaspṛśya śucy ambho namaskṛtya maheśvaram
BhP divyāny astrāṇi saṃsmṛtya sajyaṃ gāṇḍīvam ādade
BhP nyaruṇat sūtikāgāraṃ śarair nānāstrayojitaiḥ
BhP tiryag ūrdhvam adhaḥ pārthaś cakāra śarapañjaram
BhP tataḥ kumāraḥ sañjāto viprapatnyā rudan muhuḥ
BhP sadyo 'darśanam āpede saśarīro vihāyasā
BhP tadāha vipro vijayaṃ vinindan kṛṣṇasannidhau
BhP mauḍhyaṃ paśyata me yo 'haṃ śraddadhe klībakatthanam
BhP na pradyumno nāniruddho na rāmo na ca keśavaḥ
BhP yasya śekuḥ paritrātuṃ ko 'nyas tadaviteśvaraḥ
BhP dhig arjunaṃ mṛṣāvādaṃ dhig ātmaślāghino dhanuḥ
BhP daivopasṛṣṭaṃ yo mauḍhyād āninīṣati durmatiḥ
BhP evaṃ śapati viprarṣau vidyām āsthāya phālgunaḥ
BhP yayau saṃyamanīm āśu yatrāste bhagavān yamaḥ
BhP viprāpatyam acakṣāṇas tata aindrīm agāt purīm
BhP āgneyīṃ nairṛtīṃ saumyāṃ vāyavyāṃ vāruṇīm atha
BhP rasātalaṃ nākapṛṣṭhaṃ dhiṣṇyāny anyāny udāyudhaḥ
BhP tato 'labdhadvijasuto hy anistīrṇapratiśrutaḥ
BhP agniṃ vivikṣuḥ kṛṣṇena pratyuktaḥ pratiṣedhatā
BhP darśaye dvijasūnūṃs te māvajñātmānam ātmanā
BhP ye te naḥ kīrtiṃ vimalāṃ manuṣyāḥ sthāpayiṣyanti
BhP iti sambhāṣya bhagavān arjunena saheśvaraḥ
BhP divyaṃ svaratham āsthāya pratīcīṃ diśam āviśat
BhP sapta dvīpān sasindhūṃś ca sapta sapta girīn atha
BhP lokālokaṃ tathātītya viveśa sumahat tamaḥ
BhP tatrāśvāḥ śaibyasugrīva meghapuṣpabalāhakāḥ
BhP tamasi bhraṣṭagatayo babhūvur bharatarṣabha
BhP tān dṛṣṭvā bhagavān kṛṣṇo mahāyogeśvareśvaraḥ
BhP sahasrādityasaṅkāśaṃ svacakraṃ prāhiṇot puraḥ
BhP tamaḥ sughoraṃ gahanaṃ kṛtaṃ mahad
BhP vidārayad bhūritareṇa rociṣā
BhP manojavaṃ nirviviśe sudarśanaṃ
BhP guṇacyuto rāmaśaro yathā camūḥ
BhP dvāreṇa cakrānupathena tat tamaḥ paraṃ paraṃ jyotir anantapāram
BhP samaśnuvānaṃ prasamīkṣya phālgunaḥ pratāḍitākṣo pidadhe 'kṣiṇī ubhe
BhP tataḥ praviṣṭaḥ salilaṃ nabhasvatā balīyasaijadbṛhadūrmibhūṣaṇam
BhP tatrādbhutaṃ vai bhavanaṃ dyumattamaṃ bhrājanmaṇistambhasahasraśobhitam
BhP tasmin mahābhogam anantam adbhutaṃ
BhP sahasramūrdhanyaphaṇāmaṇidyubhiḥ
BhP vibhrājamānaṃ dviguṇekṣaṇolbaṇaṃ
BhP sitācalābhaṃ śitikaṇṭhajihvam
BhP dadarśa tadbhogasukhāsanaṃ vibhuṃ
BhP mahānubhāvaṃ puruṣottamottamam
BhP sāndrāmbudābhaṃ supiśaṅgavāsasaṃ
BhP prasannavaktraṃ rucirāyatekṣaṇam
BhP mahāmaṇivrātakirīṭakuṇḍala
BhP prabhāparikṣiptasahasrakuntalam
BhP pralambacārvaṣṭabhujaṃ sakaustubhaṃ
BhP śrīvatsalakṣmaṃ vanamālayāvṛtam
BhP mahāmaṇivrātakirīṭakuṇḍala
BhP prabhāparikṣiptasahasrakuntalam
BhP pralambacārvaṣṭabhujaṃ sakaustubhaṃ
BhP śrīvatsalakṣmaṃ vanamālayāvṛtam
BhP vavanda ātmānam anantam acyuto jiṣṇuś ca taddarśanajātasādhvasaḥ
BhP tāv āha bhūmā parameṣṭhināṃ prabhur beddhāñjalī sasmitam ūrjayā girā
BhP dvijātmajā me yuvayor didṛkṣuṇā mayopanītā bhuvi dharmaguptaye
BhP kalāvatīrṇāv avaner bharāsurān hatveha bhūyas tvarayetam anti me
BhP pūrṇakāmāv api yuvāṃ naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī
BhP dharmam ācaratāṃ sthityai ṛṣabhau lokasaṅgraham
BhP ity ādiṣṭau bhagavatā tau kṛṣṇau parameṣṭhinā
BhP oṃ ity ānamya bhūmānam ādāya dvijadārakān
BhP nyavartetāṃ svakaṃ dhāma samprahṛṣṭau yathāgatam
BhP viprāya dadatuḥ putrān yathārūpaṃ yathāvayaḥ
BhP niśāmya vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma pārthaḥ paramavismitaḥ
BhP yat kiñcit pauruṣaṃ puṃsāṃ mene kṛṣṇānukampitam
BhP itīdṛśāny anekāni vīryāṇīha pradarśayan
BhP bubhuje viṣayān grāmyān īje cātyurjitair makhaiḥ
BhP pravavarṣākhilān kāmān prajāsu brāhmaṇādiṣu
BhP yathākālaṃ yathaivendro bhagavān śraiṣṭhyam āsthitaḥ
BhP hatvā nṛpān adharmiṣṭhān ghāṭayitvārjunādibhiḥ
BhP añjasā vartayām āsa dharmaṃ dharmasutādibhiḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sukhaṃ svapuryāṃ nivasan dvārakāyāṃ śriyaḥ patiḥ
BhP sarvasampatsamṛddhāyāṃ juṣṭāyāṃ vṛṣṇipuṅgavaiḥ
BhP strībhiś cottamaveṣābhir navayauvanakāntibhiḥ
BhP kandukādibhir harmyeṣu krīḍantībhis taḍiddyubhiḥ
BhP nityaṃ saṅkulamārgāyāṃ madacyudbhir mataṅgajaiḥ
BhP svalaṅkṛtair bhaṭair aśvai rathaiś ca kanakojjvalaiḥ
BhP udyānopavanāḍhyāyāṃ puṣpitadrumarājiṣu
BhP nirviśadbhṛṅgavihagair nāditāyāṃ samantataḥ
BhP reme ṣoḍaśasāhasra patnīnāṃ ekavallabhaḥ
BhP tāvad vicitrarūpo 'sau tadgeheṣu maharddhiṣu
BhP protphullotpalakahlāra kumudāmbhojareṇubhiḥ
BhP vāsitāmalatoyeṣu kūjaddvijakuleṣu ca
BhP vijahāra vigāhyāmbho hradinīṣu mahodayaḥ
BhP kucakuṅkumaliptāṅgaḥ parirabdhaś ca yoṣitām
BhP upagīyamāno gandharvair mṛdaṅgapaṇavānakān
BhP vādayadbhir mudā vīṇāṃ sūtamāgadhavandibhiḥ
BhP sicyamāno 'cyutas tābhir hasantībhiḥ sma recakaiḥ
BhP pratiṣiñcan vicikrīḍe yakṣībhir yakṣarāḍ iva
BhP tāḥ klinnavastravivṛtorukucapradeśāḥ
BhP siñcantya uddhṛtabṛhatkavaraprasūnāḥ
BhP kāntaṃ sma recakajihīrṣayayopaguhya
BhP jātasmarotsmayalasadvadanā virejuḥ
BhP kṛṣṇas tu tatstanaviṣajjitakuṅkumasrak
BhP krīḍābhiṣaṅgadhutakuntalavṛndabandhaḥ
BhP siñcan muhur yuvatibhiḥ pratiṣicyamāno
BhP reme kareṇubhir ivebhapatiḥ parītaḥ
BhP naṭānāṃ nartakīnāṃ ca gītavādyopajīvinām
BhP krīḍālaṅkāravāsāṃsi kṛṣṇo 'dāt tasya ca striyaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇasyaivaṃ viharato gatyālāpekṣitasmitaiḥ
BhP narmakṣvelipariṣvaṅgaiḥ strīṇāṃ kila hṛtā dhiyaḥ
BhP ūcur mukundaikadhiyo gira unmattavaj jaḍam
BhP cintayantyo 'ravindākṣaṃ tāni me gadataḥ śṛṇu
BhP mahiṣya ūcuḥ
BhP kurari vilapasi tvaṃ vītanidrā na śeṣe
BhP svapiti jagati rātryām īśvaro guptabodhaḥ
BhP vayam iva sakhi kaccid gāḍhanirviddhacetā
BhP nalinanayanahāsodāralīlekṣitena
BhP netre nimīlayasi naktam adṛṣṭabandhus
BhP tvaṃ roravīṣi karuṇaṃ bata cakravāki
BhP dāsyaṃ gata vayam ivācyutapādajuṣṭāṃ
BhP kiṃ vā srajaṃ spṛhayase kavareṇa voḍhum
BhP bho bhoḥ sadā niṣṭanase udanvann alabdhanidro 'dhigataprajāgaraḥ
BhP kim vā mukundāpahṛtātmalāñchanaḥ prāptāṃ daśāṃ tvaṃ ca gato duratyayām
BhP tvaṃ yakṣmaṇā balavatāsi gṛhīta indo
BhP kṣīṇas tamo na nijadīdhitibhiḥ kṣiṇoṣi
BhP kaccin mukundagaditāni yathā vayaṃ tvaṃ
BhP vismṛtya bhoḥ sthagitagīr upalakṣyase naḥ
BhP kiṃ nv ācaritam asmābhir malayānila te 'priyam
BhP govindāpāṅganirbhinne hṛdīrayasi naḥ smaram
BhP megha śrīmaṃs tvam asi dayito yādavendrasya nūnaṃ
BhP śrīvatsāṅkaṃ vayam iva bhavān dhyāyati premabaddhaḥ
BhP atyutkaṇṭhaḥ śavalahṛdayo 'smadvidho bāṣpadhārāḥ
BhP smṛtvā smṛtvā visṛjasi muhur duḥkhadas tatprasaṅgaḥ
BhP priyarāvapadāni bhāṣase mṛtasañjīvikayānayā girā
BhP karavāṇi kim adya te priyaṃ vada me valgitakaṇṭha kokila
BhP na calasi na vadasy udārabuddhe kṣitidhara cintayase mahāntam artham
BhP api bata vasudevanandanāṅghriṃ vayam iva kāmayase stanair vidhartum
BhP śuṣyaddhradāḥ karaśitā bata sindhupatnyaḥ
BhP sampraty apāstakamalaśriya iṣṭabhartuḥ
BhP yadvad vayaṃ madhupateḥ praṇayāvalokam
BhP aprāpya muṣṭahṛdayāḥ purukarśitāḥ sma
BhP haṃsa svāgatam āsyatāṃ piba payo brūhy aṅga śaureḥ kathāṃ
BhP dūtaṃ tvāṃ nu vidāma kaccid ajitaḥ svasty āsta uktaṃ purā
BhP kiṃ vā naś calasauhṛdaḥ smarati taṃ kasmād bhajāmo vayaṃ
BhP kṣaudrālāpaya kāmadaṃ śriyam ṛte saivaikaniṣṭhā striyām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP itīdṛśena bhāvena kṛṣṇe yogeśvareśvare
BhP kriyamāṇena mādhavyo lebhire paramāṃ gatim
BhP śrutamātro 'pi yaḥ strīṇāṃ prasahyākarṣate manaḥ
BhP urugāyorugīto vā paśyantīnāṃ ca kiṃ punaḥ
BhP yāḥ samparyacaran premṇā pādasaṃvāhanādibhiḥ
BhP jagadguruṃ bhartṛbuddhyā tāsāṃ kim varṇyate tapaḥ
BhP evaṃ vedoditaṃ dharmam anutiṣṭhan satāṃ gatiḥ
BhP gṛhaṃ dharmārthakāmānāṃ muhuś cādarśayat padam
BhP āsthitasya paraṃ dharmaṃ kṛṣṇasya gṛhamedhinām
BhP āsan ṣoḍaśasāhasraṃ mahiṣyaś ca śatādhikam
BhP tāsāṃ strīratnabhūtānām aṣṭau yāḥ prāg udāhṛtāḥ
BhP rukmiṇīpramukhā rājaṃs tatputrāś cānupūrvaśaḥ
BhP ekaikasyāṃ daśa daśa kṛṣṇo 'jījanad ātmajān
BhP yāvatya ātmano bhāryā amoghagatir īśvaraḥ
BhP teṣām uddāmavīryāṇām aṣṭādaśa mahārathāḥ
BhP āsann udārayaśasas teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu
BhP pradyumnaś cāniruddhaś ca dīptimān bhānur eva ca
BhP sāmbo madhur bṛhadbhānuś citrabhānur vṛko 'ruṇaḥ
BhP puṣkaro vedabāhuś ca śrutadevaḥ sunandanaḥ
BhP citrabāhur virūpaś ca kavir nyagrodha eva ca
BhP eteṣām api rājendra tanujānāṃ madhudviṣaḥ
BhP pradyumna āsīt prathamaḥ pitṛvad rukmiṇīsutaḥ
BhP sa rukmiṇo duhitaram upayeme mahārathaḥ
BhP tasyāṃ tato 'niruddho 'bhūt nāgāyatabalānvitaḥ
BhP sa cāpi rukmiṇaḥ pautrīṃ dauhitro jagṛhe tataḥ
BhP vajras tasyābhavad yas tu mauṣalād avaśeṣitaḥ
BhP pratibāhur abhūt tasmāt subāhus tasya cātmajaḥ
BhP subāhoḥ śāntaseno 'bhūc chatasenas tu tatsutaḥ
BhP na hy etasmin kule jātā adhanā abahuprajāḥ
BhP alpāyuṣo 'lpavīryāś ca abrahmaṇyāś ca jajñire
BhP yaduvaṃśaprasūtānāṃ puṃsāṃ vikhyātakarmaṇām
BhP saṅkhyā na śakyate kartum api varṣāyutair nṛpa
BhP tisraḥ koṭyaḥ sahasrāṇām aṣṭāśītiśatāni ca
BhP āsan yadukulācāryāḥ kumārāṇām iti śrutam
BhP saṅkhyānaṃ yādavānāṃ kaḥ kariṣyati mahātmanām
BhP yatrāyutānām ayuta lakṣeṇāste sa āhukaḥ
BhP devāsurāhavahatā daiteyā ye sudāruṇāḥ
BhP te cotpannā manuṣyeṣu prajā dṛptā babādhire
BhP tannigrahāya hariṇā proktā devā yadoḥ kule
BhP avatīrṇāḥ kulaśataṃ teṣām ekādhikaṃ nṛpa
BhP teṣāṃ pramāṇaṃ bhagavān prabhutvenābhavad dhariḥ
BhP ye cānuvartinas tasya vavṛdhuḥ sarvayādavāḥ
BhP śayyāsanāṭanālāpa krīḍāsnānādikarmasu
BhP na viduḥ santam ātmānaṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛṣṇacetasaḥ
BhP tīrthaṃ cakre nṛponaṃ yad ajani yaduṣu svaḥsarit pādaśaucaṃ
BhP vidviṭsnigdhāḥ svarūpaṃ yayur ajitapara śrīr yadarthe 'nyayatnaḥ
BhP yannāmāmaṅgalaghnaṃ śrutam atha gaditaṃ yatkṛto gotradharmaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇasyaitan na citraṃ kṣitibharaharaṇaṃ kālacakrāyudhasya
BhP jayati jananivāso devakījanmavādo
BhP yaduvarapariṣat svair dorbhir asyann adharmam
BhP sthiracaravṛjinaghnaḥ susmitaśrīmukhena
BhP vrajapuravanitānāṃ vardhayan kāmadevam
BhP itthaṃ parasya nijavartmarirakṣayātta
BhP līlātanos tadanurūpaviḍambanāni
BhP karmāṇi karmakaṣaṇāni yadūttamasya
BhP śrūyād amuṣya padayor anuvṛttim icchan
BhP martyas tayānusavam edhitayā mukunda
BhP śrīmatkathāśravaṇakīrtanacintayaiti
BhP tad dhāma dustarakṛtāntajavāpavargaṃ
BhP grāmād vanaṃ kṣitibhujo 'pi yayur yadarthāḥ
